Fa edziban tɔ hɛn nye hɛn asaase, na hɛn nye hɛn asaase bɛyɛ asomfo ama Farao: na ma hɛn eduaba, ama yaatsena ase, na yeennwuwu, na amma asaase yi aannda pan.
Nna Josef tɔɔ Egypt asaase nyinara maa Farao; na Egyptfo nyinara tontɔɔn hɔn haban, osiandɛ ɔkɔm no mu yɛɛ dzen wɔ hɔn do: na asaase no bɛyɛɛ Farao dze.
Na nkorɔfo no dze, ɔdaan hɔn nkowaa otuu hɔn hɔ ma wɔkɛtsenatsenaa nkurow a ofi Egypt ɔhe no kurotsia kɛpem ne kurotsia no mu.
Asɔfo no hɔn asaase nko na ɔanntɔ: osiandɛ Farao maa asɔfo no kyɛfa bi, na wodzii hɔn kyɛfa a Farao dze maa hɔn no; dɛm ntsi wɔanntɔn hɔn asaase.
Nna Josef see nkorɔfo no dɛ, Hwɛ matɔ hom nye hom asaase ndɛ ama Farao: hwɛ, hom eduaba nye yi, na hom nkoduadua no wɔ asaase no do.
Na dza ɔbɛyɛ nye dɛ, hom dze ekuadze yi mu mbumu enum enum bɛma Farao, na anan no ayɛ homankasa homdze, ma wɔdze bi edua haban mu, na ɔayɛ hom, nye hom fifo nye hom mbofraba edziban.
Na wɔsee dɛ, Agye hɛn nkwa: ma yennya mo wura n’enyim enyimnyam, na yɛbɛyɛ Farao n’asomfo.
Na Josef dze yɛɛ mbra too hɔ wɔ Egypt asaase do ɔdze bɛpem ndɛ ara, dɛ wɔmfa mbumu enum enum mma Farao; gyedɛ asɔfo no hɔn asaase nkotsee na annyɛ Farao dze.
Na Israel tsenaa Egypt wɔ Gosen asaase do; na wonyaa egyapadze wɔ hɔ, na wɔwowoe, na wɔdɔɔr pii.
Jakob Ne Samansew Na Jakob tsenaa Egypt asaase do mfe duesuon: na Jakob ne nda, no nkwa ne mfe, yɛɛ mfe ɔha eduanan esuon.
Na mber a Israel dze bowu no bɛnee no: ɔfrɛɛ ne ba Josef, na ɔsee no dɛ, Sɛ afei menya w’enyim enyimnyam a, meserɛ wo, fa wo nsa to m’aserɛ ase, na enye me ndzi no ayamuyie mu nye nokwar mu; meserɛ wo, mma nnsie me wɔ Egypt: na sɛ mokɔ me nsamankyir a, ɔno soa me fi Egypt, na kesie me wɔ m’egyanom hɔn esiei.
Na ɔsee dɛ, Mebɛyɛ dɛ mbrɛ aka no ara.
Na Jakob see dɛ, Dzi nsew kyerɛ me: nna Josef dzii nsew kyerɛɛ no.
Na Israel bɔɔ no mu adze wɔ mpa no n’etsifi.
Jakob Hyira Efraim Na Manaasɛ Na ɔbaa dɛ iyinom ekyir no, wɔkaa kyerɛɛ Josef dɛ, Hwɛ, w’egya yar: na ɔfaa ne mbabanyin beenu no, Manaasɛ nye Efraim kaa no ho.
Na obi kaa kyerɛɛ Jakob dɛ, Hwɛ, wo ba Josef reba wo nkyɛn: na Israel miaa n’enyi, na ɔtsenaa mpa do.
Na Jakob see Josef dɛ, Otumfo Nyankopɔn yii noho kyerɛɛ me wɔ Luz wɔ Keenan asaase do, na ohyiraa me, na ɔsee me dɛ, Hwɛ, mebɛma awo, na adɔr, na mebɛyɛ wo aman asafo; na medze asaase yi ama w’asefo a wobedzi w’ekyir ma wɔdze ayɛ daa egyapadze.
Na afei wo mba beenu a ewoo hɔn wɔ Egypt asaase do ansaana mereba wo nkyɛn wɔ Egypt no, wɔyɛ medze; Efraim nye Manaasɛ, bɛyɛ medze, dɛ Reuben nye Simeon ara so.
Na wo mba a hɔn ekyir ebɔwo hɔn no, na wɔbɛyɛ wodze; wɔdze hɔn nuanom dzin bɛfrɛ hɔn wɔ hɔn egyapadze mu.
Na emi dze, mifi Paddan mebae no, Rahel wuu m’enyim wɔ kwan mu wɔ Keenan asaase do, aber a aka ɔkwan kakraabi ma edu Efrat no: na misiee no Efrat kwan mu hɔ (ɔnoara nye Bɛtlɛhɛm).
Na Israel hun Josef ne mba no, na ɔsee dɛ, Woananom nye yi?
Na Josef see n’egya dɛ, me mba a Nyankopɔn dze hɔn ama me wɔ ha a. Na ɔsee dɛ, Meserɛ wo, fa hɔn brɛ me, ma minhyira hɔn.
Nna onyin dodow ntsi Israel n’enyiwa do ayɛ no nkusunkusu, ma onntum nnhu adze.
Na Josef dze hɔn piin ne nkyɛn; na Israel feew hɔn ano, na ɔyɛɛ hɔn etuu.
Na Israel see Josef dɛ, Manndwen dɛ nkyɛ mubohu w’enyim: na hwɛ, Nyankopɔn ama mehu wo mba so.
Na Josef yii hɔn wɔ n’anan ntamu bae; na ɔbɔɔ no mu adze dze n’enyim boom famu.
Na Josef faa hɔn beenu nyina, ne nsa enyimfa dze Efraim mu wɔ Israel n’abankum, na ne nsa abankum dze Manaasɛ mu wɔ Israel n’enyimfa, na ɔdze hɔn piin ne nkyɛn.
Na Israel tseen ne nsa enyimfa, na ɔdze too Efraim a ɔyɛ kakraba no n’etsifi, na ɔdze ne nsa abankum too Manaasɛ n’etsifi, ɔboapa ara yɛɛ ne nsa dɛm; osiandɛ Manaasɛ nye abakan.
Na ohyiraa Josef, na ɔsee dɛ, Nyankopɔn no a m’egyanom Abraham nye Isaak wɔnantseew n’enyim no, Nyankopɔn no a ɔahwɛ me mo nkwaber nyinara mu ma ɔdze abɛpem ndɛ no, sor abɔfo no a oeyi me efi mbusu nyinara mu no, onhyira mbofra yi: na wɔmma wɔmfa me dzin nye m’egyanom Abraham nye Isaak hɔn dzin mfrɛ hɔn; na wɔmma wonnyin wɔnyɛ ɔdodow wɔ asaase do.
Na aber a Josef hun dɛ n’egya dze ne nsa enyimfa ato Efraim n’etsifi no, ɔannyɛ no abodwe: na osuoo n’egya ne nsa mu dɛ oriyi wɔ Efraim n’etsifi ato Manaasɛ n’etsifi.
Na Josef see n’egya dɛ, ɔnntse dɛm, m’egya: na abakan no nye yi; fa wo nsa enyimfa to n’etsifi.
Na n’egya ammpen, na ɔsee dɛ, Minyim, me ba, minyim: ɔno so bɛyɛ ɔman, na ɔno so bɛyɛ kɛse: naaso no nua kuma bɛyɛ kɛse asen no, na n’asefo bɛyɛ amanaman pii.
Na ohyiraa hɔn da no see dɛ, ɔwo na Israel dze wo behyira dɛ, Nyankopɔn mma yɛ dɛ Efraim nye dɛ Manaasɛ: na ɔdze Efraim dzii Manaasɛ ne kan. Na Israel see Josef dɛ, Hwɛ, muruwu: na Nyankopɔn bedzi hom ekyir, na ɔdze hom akɔ hom egyanom hɔn asaase do bio.
Nkyii so medze kyɛpɛn kor a ɔbor wo nuanom do a medze m’afona nye m’egyen megyee no wɔ Amorifo nsamu no ama wo.
Jakob Hyira Ne Mba Na Jakob frɛɛ ne mbabanyin, na ɔsee dɛ: Hom mboa hom ano, na menka dza ndaamba ɔbɛba hom do nkyerɛ hom.
Hom nhyia, na wontsie, hom Jakob mba; Na wontsie hom egya Israel.
Reuben, ɔwo nye m’abakan, mo tum, nye m’ahoɔdzen ahyɛse; Nyia ɔkyɛn wɔ enyidzi mu na nyia ɔkyɛn wɔ tum mu.
Ihihim dɛ nsu, ennkɛkyɛn; Osiandɛ efoow w’egya ne mpa: Nna iguu ho fi: efoow m’adae.
Simeon nye Levi wɔyɛ enuanom; Hɔn mfona yɛ enyiber akodze.
Ao me kra, mma mmba hɔn apam mu; M’enyimnyam, mma mmfora hɔn mboano mu; Osiandɛ hɔn ebufuw mu na wokum nyimpa, Na hɔn ahopɔw mu na wotwitwaa nantwi anantsir.
Ndom nka hɔn ebufuw, osiandɛ ɔyɛ hyew; Na hɔn enyiber, osiandɛ no mu yɛ dzen: Mebɛpaapaa hɔn mu wɔ Jakob mu, Na mabɔ hɔn apetse wɔ Israel mu.
Juda, ɔwo na wo nuanom beyi wo ayɛw: Wo nsa bɛhyɛ w’atamfo hɔn kɔn do; W’egya mba bɔbɔ hɔn mu adze wɔ w’enyim.
Juda yɛ ogyata ba; Abɔgyanam ara na edze enyin, me ba: ɔkotowee, obutuuw hɔ dɛ ogyata, Na dɛ ogyataber; woana na obekenyan no?
Ahempoma nnkefi Juda nsa, Nna mbrahyɛfo poma nnkefi n’anan ntamu, Kɛpem dɛ Siloh bɛba; Na ɔno na aman bɛyɛ setsie ama no.
Ɔdze n’asoasopɔnkɔba amontan wenyindua, Na n’asoasopɔnkɔber ba wɔ wenyindua pa ho; ɔahor ne ntar wɔ wenyin mu, Na n’akataho wɔ wenyinamba bɔgya mu: N’enyiwa yɛ dɛnn sen nsa memen, Na numfonsu ama ne se ho ahoa fitaa.
Zebulun bɛtsena po berekyir: Na ɔbɛyɛ mbrɛ ahɛn gyinagyina; Na ɔnye Zidon bɔbɔ ɔhe.
Isakar yɛ asoaso a no ho yɛ dzen, Obutuuw nguamban ntamu: Na ohun ahomgye bea dɛ oye, Na asaase no dɛ ɔyɛ fɛw; Na ɔbrɛɛ n’abatsir adze dze soae, Na ɔbɛyɛɛ ɔsomfo wɔ edwumadzen mu.
Dan bobua no nkorɔfo atsɛn, Dɛ Israel mbusuakuw mu kor.
Dan bɛyɛ ɔwɔ a ɔbew kwan mu, Ehurutsia a ɔda akwantsen, ɔsɔw ɔpɔnkɔ nantsir, na no do atsefo no obu dua n’ekyir.
EWURADZE, matweɔn wo nkwahosan.
Gad, dɔm bɛhyɛ no do: Na ɔno so bɛhyɛ hɔn etsia hɔn anantsir.
Aser n’edziban fi no mu bɔtɔ angoa, Na ɔbɛma ahemfo adɔkɔdɔkɔdze.
Naftali yɛ ɔtrɔmber a woegyaa no: ɔka ahomkasɛm.
Josef yɛ dua a ɔsow, Abaw a ɔsow wɔ nsunyiwa ho; No nkorbata tratra ban.
Egyentofo no eyi no awerɛhow kɛsenara, Na wɔatotow no, na wɔayɛ no enyienyi: Na n’egyen dze ɔwɔ hɔ pintsinn, Na ne nsa n’abasa no mu yɛ dzen, ɔnam Jakob no Tumfo Kor no ne nsa do, Hɔ na oguanhwɛfo no, Israel no bo no ofi.
Mekyerɛ w’egya ne Nyankopɔn a ɔbɔboa wo no, Na Otumfo a ɔdze ɔsor nhyira, Bun a ɔda daadzetsirmu ne nhyira, Enumfo mu, nye yafun mu nhyira, Behyira wo no, W’egya ne nhyira Akyɛn daa mbepɔw ne nhyira ɔdze kodu tsetse mbepɔw no n’ano no ho ara: ɔbɛtsena Josef n’etsifi, Nyia wɔtseew no fii no nuanom ho no n’etsifi pampamu.
Benjamin yɛ pataku a ɔtsetsew mbowa mu: Obedzi abɔgyanam anapa, Na ewimbir no ɔakyɛ asadze.
Jakob No Wu Woyinom nyinara nye Israel mbusuakuw duebien no: na iyi na hɔn egya kaa kyerɛɛ hɔn na ɔdze hyiraa hɔn no; hɔn nyinara mbrɛ hɔn nhyira tsetsee nkorkor, na ohyiraa hɔn.
Na Jakob hyɛɛ hɔn, na ɔsee hɔn dɛ, ɔwɔ dɛ wɔdze me kɛka mo nkorɔfo ho: wonsie me m’egyanom nkyɛn wɔ ɔbo tu a ɔwɔ Efron Hetnyi no, ne haban mu no mu, wɔ ɔbo tu a ɔwɔ Makepela haban mu no a, ɔwɔ Mamre enyim, wɔ Keenan asaase do no a Abraham dze kaa haban no ho tɔɔ no wɔ Hetnyi Efron hɔ, dze yɛɛ efunsiebea no no mu: hɔ na wosiee Abraham nye ne yer Sara; hɔ na wosiee Isaak nye ne yer Rebeka; na hɔ na misiee Leah: haban no nye ɔbo tu a ɔwɔ mu no a wɔtɔɔ no wɔ Hetmba hɔ no a. Na Jakob wiee ne nsamansew a ɔhyɛɛ ne mba no ara, nna ɔkaa n’anan boaa ano dze guu mpa no do, na ogyaa no sunsum mu, na otsiiw n’egyanom wɔ samanadze.
Na Josef twae hwee n’egya n’enyim, na osui guu no do, na ɔfeew n’ano.
Na Josef hyɛɛ no nkowaa a wɔhyɛ fun edur no dɛ wɔnhyɛ n’egya akyenkyendur: na wɔhyɛɛ Israel akyenkyendur.
Na wɔdze adaduanan dzii ho dwuma: nna mber a wɔdze wie akyenkyendur hyɛ nye no: na Egyptfo no suu no nda eduosuon.
Na nda a wɔdze suu no no twaa mu no, Josef kaa kyerɛɛ Farao ne fifo, dɛ, Sɛ afei menya hom enyim enyimnyam a, meserɛ hom, wɔnka no wɔ Farao n’asomu, dɛ, M’egya maa midzii nsew dɛ, Hwɛ, muruwu: na nda a mabɔ ama moho wɔ Keenan asaase do no mu hɔ na kesie me.
Dɛm ntsi, afei meserɛ wo, ma monkɔ, na minkesie m’egya, na membra bio.
Na Farao see dɛ, Kɔ, na kesie w’egya, dɛ mbrɛ ɔmaa idzii nsew no ara.
Na Josef kɔree dɛ orikesie n’egya: na Farao no nkowaa nyinara, ne fie mpanyimfo, nye Egypt asaase do mpanyimfo nyinara, nye Josef ne fifo nyinara, nye no nuanom, nye n’egya ne fifo, nyinara nye no kɔree.
Hɔn mbofraba, nye hɔn nguan, nye hɔn anantwi, nko na wɔdaan hɔn gyaa Gosen asaase do.
Na ntseaseanam nye mpɔnkɔdofo nyina nye no kɔree: na ɔyɛɛ kuw kɛsenara.
Na wɔbaa Atad ewuporoweebea a ɔwɔ Jordan egya no, na hɔ na wotwaa kwadwom kɛse a no mu yɛ dzen papanara: na Josef suu n’egya nda esuon.
Na hɔn a wɔtse asaase no do no, Keenanfo no, hun osu a wosuu no wɔ Atad ewuporoweebea no, wɔsee dɛ, Iyi yɛ eyi kɛse ma Egyptfo: dɛm ntsi wɔfrɛɛ ne dzin Abel-mizraim a ɔwɔ Jordan egya.
Na ne mba yɛɛ no dɛ mbrɛ ɔhyɛɛ hɔn no ara: na ne mba soaa no kɔr Keenan asaase do, na wokesiee no wɔ Makepela haban mu ɔbo tu no mu, dza Abraham dze kaa haban no ho tɔɔ no wɔ Hetnyi Efron hɔ, dze yɛɛ efunsiebea wɔ Mamre enyim no a. Na Josef siee n’egya wiei ekyir no, ɔnoara nye no nuanom no, nye hɔn a wɔnye no kɔree kesiee n’egya no nyinara sanee kɔr Egypt.
Josef Gye No Nuanom Anoyie Na Josef no nuanom no hun dɛ hɔn egya ewu no, wɔsee dɛ, Bɛyɛ na Josef atan hɛn, na bɔn a yɛdze yɛɛ no no nyinara oesusu mbrɛ ɔtse no ara atɔ hɛn do wer.
Na wɔsomae ma wɔkɛsee Josef dɛ, Ansaana w’egya ruwu no ɔhyɛɛ dɛ, Dɛm na hom nka nkyerɛ Josef, Afei meserɛ wo, fa wo nuanom hɔn mbrato, nye hɔn bɔn kyɛ hɔn, dɛ wɔyɛɛ wo bɔn: na afei yɛserɛ wo, fa w’egya ne Nyankopɔn no nkowaa hɔn bɔn kyɛ hɔn.
Na Josef sui wɔ aber a wɔkaa dɛm kyerɛɛ no no.
Na no nuanom no so kɔree, na wokotwitwae hwehwee n’enyim; na wɔsee dɛ, Hwɛ, yɛyɛ wo nkowaa.
Na Josef see hɔn dɛ, Mma hom nnsuro: ana migyina Nyankopɔn ananmu a?
Hom dze, hom dween dɛ wɔreyɛ me bɔn; na Nyankopɔn dze ɔdween dɛ oye, ma ɔaayɛ dɛ mbrɛ ndɛ ɔayɛ yi, ma wɔaagye nkorɔfo piinara nkwa.
Dɛm ntsi afei, mma hom nnsuro: mobɔhwɛ hom, nye hom mbofraba.
Na ɔkaa hɔn akoma too hɔn yamu, na ɔkasaa ayamuyie mu kyerɛɛ hɔn.
Josef No Wu Na Josef tsenaa Egypt, ɔnoara nye n’egya ne fifo: na Josef dzii mfe ɔha nye du.
Na Josef hun Efraim ne mbanana a otsia ebiasa: Manaasɛ ne babanyin Makir ne mba so wɔwoo hɔn guu Josef n’aserɛ do.
Na Josef see no nuanom no dɛ, Morobɔkɔ me nsamankyir: na ampaara Nyankopɔn bɛba abɛsera hom, na oebeyi hom efi asaase yi do akɔ asaase a ɔkaa ho ntam kyerɛɛ Abraham, Isaak nye Jakob no no do.
Na Josef maa Israelmba dzii nsew dɛ, Ampaara, Nyankopɔn bɛba abɛsera hom, na hom nsoa me mbiew mfi ha nkɔ.
Na Josef wui, nna oedzi mfe ɔha nye du: na wɔhyɛɛ no akyenkyendur, na wɔtoo no adaka mu wɔ Egypt.
NHƐNMU Nwoma no ne dzin “Eksodɔs” no ase kyerɛ dɛ Otukɔr.
Ɔka Israelfo abakɔsɛm no mu nsɛntsitsir bi a osii ho asɛm.
Ɔfa no Israelfo tu a wotui fii Egypt asaase do nkowaasom mu no ho.
Wobotum akyekyɛ nwoma yi mu ahorow ebiasa.
.
Wɔgyee Hebriwfo fii nkowaasom mu ma wotuu kwan fii Egypt kɔr Sinai Bepɔw ho.
.
Nyankopɔn n’ahyɛmu a ɔnye ne man dzii wɔ Sinai Bepɔw no ho.
Ahyɛmu yi fa abrabɔ, amanyɛ na Nyamesom ho mbra a ɔsɛ dɛ wodzi do ho.
.
Wosii dan siesiee mu dɛ Israelfo no nsom wɔ mu, hyehyɛɛ mbra maa asɔfodzi na mbrɛ wonsi nsom Nyankopɔn mfa.
Na no korakora nye dɛ, nwoma yi ka dza Nyankopɔn yɛe, dɛ ɔgyee ne man a nna wɔdze hɔn ayɛ nkowaa na mfonabaa, na ɔyɛɛ hɔn ɔman a woenya enyidado.
Nyimpa tsitsir a nwoma yi ka no ho asɛm nye Moses.
Ɔno na Nyankopɔn yii no dɛ onndzi ne man no enyim nyi hɔn mfi Egypt.
Nwoma no fa bi a ayɛ atsenka yie nye Mbrasɛm Du a ɔwɔ Tsir no mu no.
Dza Ɔwɔ Mu Wɔgyee Israelfo fii Egypt nkowaasom mu .—.
.
Wɔyɛɛ hɔn nkowaa wɔ Egypt .- .
Moses n’awoo na no mbofrase ho nsɛm .—.
.
Moses na Aaron kehyiaa Egypthen .—.
.
Apaho Afahyɛ na fi a Israelfo fii Egypt .—.
Wofii Mbɛw Po no ho kɔr Sinai Bepɔw ho .—.
Mbra no na ahyɛmu no .—.
Ehyiadzibuw no na ɔsom ho nhyehyɛɛ .—.
Wɔtseetsee Israelmba Wɔ Egypt Na Israel mbabanyin a wɔbaa Egypt no hɔn edzin nye yi; ɔbanyin biara nye ne fifo kaa Jakob ho bae.
Reuben, Simeon, Levi, nye Juda; Isakar, Zebulun, nye Benjamin; Dan nye Naftali, Gad nye Aser.
Na akra a wofi Jakob n’asen mu nyinara yɛ eduosuon: nna Josef wɔ Egypt dada.
Na Josef, nye no nuanom nyinara, nye ebusuasantsen no nyinara, wuwui.
Na Israelmba no wowoe, na wɔdɔɔr menyamenya, na hɔn dodow dɔɔ so, na hɔn ho yɛɛ dzen papaara; na wɔhyɛɛ asaase no do ma.
Na ɔhen fofor bi soɛree wɔ Egypt a nna onnyim Josef.
Na ɔkaa kyerɛɛ ne man dɛ, Hwɛ, Israelmba no dɔɔ so, na hɔn ho yɛ dzen sen hɛn: hom mbra ma yɛnye hɔn ndzi no nyansa mu, amma wɔaanndɔɔ so, na aammba dɛ sɛ ɔsa bi ba a, wɔaannkɛka hɛn atamfo ho nye hɛn ammbɔko, na woeenntu emmfi asaase yi do annkɔ.
Dɛm ntsi wɔhyehyɛɛ abɔmbaafo wɔ hɔn do dɛ wɔmma hɔn ndzesoadze nhyɛ hɔn do.
Na wɔkyekyeer adzekora nkurow, Pitom nye Raamses, maa Farao.
Na mber dodow a wɔtseetsee hɔn kɛse no mbom na wɔdɔɔr kɛse na wɔtrɛe.
Na Israelmba ho nketsenketse kyeer hɔn.
Na Egyptfo yɛɛ Israelmba ma wodzii suhia: na wɔmaa hɔn asetsena foon hɔn wɔ ndwumadzen mu, wɔ dɛtse nye ntayaa, nye hamudwuma ahorow nyinara mu.
Na wɔmaa wodzii suhia wɔ hɔn som nyinara mu.
Na Egypthen no kasaa kyerɛɛ Hebriwfo awogyefo a hɔn mu kor ne dzin dze Sifra, na ɔbaako so ne dzin dze Pua no: na ɔsee dɛ, Sɛ hom regye Hebriwfo mbaa no awoo, na hom hu wɔ awoo egua no do dɛ ɔyɛ ɔbanyin a, ɔno hom nku no; na sɛ ɔyɛ ɔbabaa a, ɔno ɔntsena ase.
Na awogyefo no suroo Nyankopɔn, na wɔannyɛ dɛ mbrɛ Egypthen no hyɛɛ hɔn no, na mbom wɔgyee mbanyimba no nkwa.
Na Egypthen no frɛɛ awogyefo no, na obisaa hɔn dɛ, Ɔyɛ dɛn ntsi na hom ayɛ dɛm adze yi, na hom agye mba mbanyimba no nkwa yi?
Na awogyefo no see Farao dɛ, Osiandɛ Hebriwfo mbaa no wɔnntse dɛ Egyptfo mbaa; na hɔn dze, wɔyɛ pirim pirim, na awogyefo nnyae nndur hɔn nkyɛn mpo nna wɔawo dada.
Na Nyankopɔn nye awogyefo no dzii no yie: na nkorɔfo no hɔn dodow dɔɔ so, na hɔn ho yɛɛ dzen pii.
Na osiandɛ, awogyefo no suroo Nyankopɔn ntsi, ɔkyekyeer efi maa hɔn.
Na Farao hyɛɛ no nkorɔfo nyinara dɛ, Ɔbabanyin biara a wɔbɔwo no no, hom nkɔtow no nkyen esutsen no mu, na ɔbabaa biara dze, hom mma ɔntsena ase.
Moses N’awoe Na ɔbanyin bi fi Levi fie kɔwaar Levi babaa bi.
Na ɔbaa no nyinsenii, na ɔwoo ɔbabanyin: na ohun dɛ ɔyɛ abofra a no ho yɛ fɛw no, ɔdze no sumaa abosoom ebiasa.
Na ɔdze no suma bio a ɔnnyɛ yie no, ɔfaa mbɛw adakaba, na ɔdze hua na aman seraam ho: na ɔdze abofra no too mu, na ɔdze kesii atsen no mu wɔ esutsen no no nkɔkɔnoa.
Na n’akyerɛbaa gyinaa ekyirekyir, dɛ ɔrohwɛ dza ɔbɛyɛ no.
Na Farao ne babaa sianee baa esutsen no ho dɛ oruboguar; na ne mbaawa pasaar esutsen no nkyɛn.
Ber a ohun adaka no wɔ atsen no mu no, ɔsomaa n’abaawa dɛ ɔnkɛfa mbra.
Na obuee do, na ohun abofra no: na, hwɛ, akɔkowaba no sui.
Na ohun no mbɔbɔr, na ɔsee dɛ, Hebriwfo mba no kor nye yi.
Nna abofra no n’akyerɛbaa no bisaa Farao babaa no dɛ, Ana monkɔ nkɛfrɛ Hebriwfo mbaa no mu onufomafo mbrɛ wo, ma ɔmma abofra no enumfo mma wo anaa?
Na Farao ne babaa no see no dɛ, Kɔ.
Na akataasia no kɔree kɛfrɛɛ abofra no ne na.
Na Farao ne babaa no see no dɛ, Fa abofra yi kɔ, na kɛma no enumfo ma me, na medze w’akatua bɛma wo.
Na ɔbaa no faa abofra no, na ɔkɛmaa no enumfo.
Na abofra no nyinii, na ɔdze no brɛɛ Farao ne babaa no, na ɔbɛyɛɛ ne babanyin.
Na ɔtoo no dzin Moses, na ɔsee dɛ, Osiandɛ mefaa no nsu mu.
Moses Guan Kɔ Midian Na ɔbaa dɛ nda no mu no, aber a Moses nyinii no, ofiir edzi kɔr no nuanom nkyɛn, na ɔkɔhwɛɛ hɔn ndzesoadze.
Ohun dɛ Egyptnyi bi robor Hebriwnyi bi, no nuanom mu baako.
Na ɔhwɛɛ ha hwɛɛ ha, na ohun dɛ nyimpa bi nnyi hɔ no, ɔbɔɔ Egyptnyi no kum no, na ɔdze no hyɛɛ anhwea mu.
Na n’adzekyee no ofiir edzi, na, hwɛ, Hebriwfo beenu roko: na obisaa nyia odzi fɔ no dɛ, Ɔyɛ dɛn ntsi na ebɔ wo nyɛnko yi?
Na obuaa no dɛ, Woana yɛɛ wo ɔpanyin nye ɔsɛndzifo wɔ hɛn do?
Edwen dɛ iruboku me dɛ mbrɛ ikum Egyptnyi no anaa?
Na Moses suroi, na ɔsee dɛ, Ampaara asɛm no epue.
Ber a Farao tsee asɛm yi no, ɔhwehwɛɛ dɛ nkyɛ oboku Moses.
Na Moses guanee fii Farao enyim, na ɔkɛtsenaa Midian asaase do: na ɔkɔkoo nsubura bi ho.
Nna Midian ɔsɔfo no wɔ mbabaa beesuon; na wɔbae bɔtoow nsu, na wɔdze hyehyɛɛ ndaasee no amaama dɛ wɔrema hɔn egya no nguan anom.
Na nguanhwɛfo bi bae beyii hɔn edzi: na Moses soɛree boaa hɔn, na ɔmaa hɔn nguan no nomee.
Na wɔbaa hɔn egya Reuel nkyɛn no, obisaa hɔn dɛ, Ɔyɛ dɛn na ndɛ hom aba ntsɛm dɛm yi?
Na wɔsee dɛ, Egyptnyi bi na oyii hɛn fii nguanhwɛfo no nsamu, na ɔtoow nsu mpo maa hɛn, na ɔmaa nguan no nomee.
Na obisaa ne mbabaa no dɛ, Na ɔwɔ hen?
Ɔyɛ dɛn ntsi na hom adan ɔbanyin no egya yi?
Wɔnkɛfrɛ no ma ombedzidzi.
Na Moses peen dɛ ɔnye ɔbanyin no bɛtsena: na ɔpanyin no dze ne babaa Zipora maa Moses awar.
Na ɔwoo ɔbabanyin, na ɔtoo no dzin Gersom: na ɔsee dɛ, Osiandɛ mayɛ ɔmamforanyi wɔ ananaben asaase do.
Na ɔbaa dɛ nda pii guu mu no, Egypthen no wui: na nkowaasom no ntsi Israelmba pempenee, na wosui, na hɔn su fowee kɔr Nyankopɔn nkyɛn.
Na Nyankopɔn tsee hɔn nkrumsi, na Nyankopɔn kaa n’ahyɛmu a ɔnye Abraham, Isaak, na Jakob dzii no.
Na Nyankopɔn hwɛɛ Israelmba no, na ohun hɔn haw.
Nyankopɔn Frɛ Moses Dabi a nna Moses rohwɛ n’asew Jetro, Midian ɔsɔfo no, no nguan no, ɔkaa hɔn kɔr sar no ekyir noho, na odur Nyankopɔn bepɔw Horeb ho.
Na EWURADZE bɔfoe beyii noho edzi kyerɛɛ no wɔ haban bi finimfin gyaframee mu: na ɔhwɛe, na, hwɛ, haban no redzɛw ogya, naaso haban no nnhyew.
Na Moses see dɛ, Iyi dze, mebɛman akɔhwɛ adzehu kɛse yi, siantsir a haban no nnhyew.
Na EWURADZE hun dɛ ɔaman rohwɛ no, Nyankopɔn fii haban no mu frɛɛ no, na ɔsee dɛ, Moses, Moses.
Na ɔgyee do dɛ, Emi nye yi.
Na ɔsee dɛ, Mma nntwe mmpin ha: yiyi w’ananadze mpaboa no, na bea a igyina do no yɛ asaase krɔnkrɔn.
Nkyii so ɔsee dɛ, Emi nye w’egyanom, Abraham, Isaak, nye Jakob Nyankopɔn no.
Na Moses dze n’enyim sumae; osiandɛ osuroo dɛ ɔbɔhwɛ Nyankopɔn.
Na EWURADZE see dɛ, Ampaara mehu me man a wɔwɔ Egypt hɔn amandzehu, na matse hɔn su a hɔn abɔmbaafo no ntsi wosu no; na minyim hɔn awerɛhow ntsi; na mesian dɛ miribeyi hɔn wɔ Egyptfo nsamu, na metutu hɔn mefi asaase no do makɔ asaase pa a ɔso do, asaase a numfonsu nye ewo pem wɔ do; Keenanfo, Hitifo, Amorifo, Perizfo, Hivifo, nye Jebusfo hɔn tsenabew no.
Na afei, hwɛ, Israel hɔn su edu m’enyim: nkyii so mehu ɔhaw a Egyptfo dze haw hɔn no.
Dɛm ntsi afei bra, na morosoma wo Farao hɔ, ma eekeyi me man Israelmba no efi Egypt efir.
Na Moses see Nyankopɔn dɛ, Woana nye emi, na maakɔ Farao nkyɛn ekeyi Israelmba efi Egypt efir?
Na ɔsee dɛ, Ampaara mibedzi w’ekyir; na iyi bɛyɛ wo asɛnkyerɛdze dɛ mara na masoma wo.
Na sɛ inya yi ɔman no fi Egypt ba a, hom bɔsom Nyankopɔn wɔ bepɔw yi do.
Na Moses see Nyankopɔn dɛ, Hwɛ, sɛ mudu Israelmba nkyɛn, na mese hɔn dɛ, Hom egyanom Nyankopɔn na ɔasoma me hom hɔ; na wobisa me dɛ, Ne dzin dze dɛn a, menka dɛn menkyerɛ hɔn?
Na Nyankopɔn see Moses dɛ, MARA NYE MARA NO: na ɔsee dɛ, Dɛm na ka kyerɛ Israelmba, MARA no na ɔasoma me hom hɔ.
Na nkyii so Nyankopɔn see Moses dɛ, Dɛm na ka kyerɛ Israelmba, EWURADZE, hom egyanom Nyankopɔn no, Abraham Nyankopɔn, Isaak Nyankopɔn, nye Jakob Nyankopɔn no, na ɔasoma me hom hɔ: iyi nye me dzin daa, na iyi nye me nkaadze kɔ ebusuasantsen nyinara mu.
Kɔ, na kɔboa Israel mpanyimfo ano, na ka kyerɛ hɔn dɛ, EWURADZE, hom egyanom Nyankopɔn no, Abraham, Isaak, nye Jakob Nyankopɔn no, eyi noho akyerɛ me, dɛ, Ɔsera na mabɛsera hom, na mehu dza wɔdze reyɛ hom wɔ Egypt no: na mase dɛ, Mibeyi hom efi Egypt amandzehu no mu akɔ Keenanfo, Hitifo, Amorifo, Perizfo, Hivifo, nye Jebusfo asaase do, asaase a numfonsu nye ewo pem wɔ do.
Na wobetsie wo ndze: na ɔwo, nye Israel mpanyimfo nkɔ Egypthen no nkyɛn, na hom nse no dɛ, EWURADZE, Hebriwfo Nyankopɔn no, nye hɛn ehyia mu: na afei yɛserɛ wo, ma yɛnkɔ sar do ndaansa kwan nkɔbɔ afɔr mma EWURADZE, hɛn Nyankopɔn.
Na minyim dɛ Egypthen remma hom kwan ma wɔnnkɔ, mpo, nnyɛ nsa a ɔyɛ dzen do a. Na mebɛtsen me nsa, na medze anwanwadze a mebɛyɛ wɔ no mu hɔ no mabɔ Egypt: na ɔno n’ekyir na ɔbɛma hom akɔ.
Na mebɛma ɔman yi enyim aba nyam wɔ Egyptfo enyim: na ɔbɛba dɛ, sɛ hom rokɔ a, hom nnkɔkɔ no nsapan: na ɔbaa biara bebisa ne fisamenanyi, na ne fie ɔmamforanyi dwetɛ edwindze, nye sika edwindze, nye atam: na hom dze ahyehyɛ hom mbabanyin nye hom mbabaa; na hom bɛfa Egyptfo no afo.
Nyankopɔn Ma Moses Anwanwatum Na Moses buae see dɛ, hwɛ, wɔnnkɛgye me edzi, eso wonketsie me ndze: na wɔbɛka dɛ, EWURADZE nnyii noho nnkyerɛɛ wo.
Na EWURADZE bisaa no dɛ, Ebɛnadze na ɔdze wo nsamu no?
Na ɔsee dɛ, Poma a. Na ɔsee dɛ, Tow kyen famu.
Na ɔtowee kyeen famu, na ɔdaan abowatsena; na Moses fii n’enyim guanee.
Na EWURADZE see Moses dɛ, Tsen wo nsa, na suo no dua mu: (na ɔtseen ne nsa suoo mu, na ɔdaan poma wɔ ne nsamu:) ama wɔaagye edzi dɛ EWURADZE, hɔn egyanom Nyankopɔn no, Abraham, Isaak nye Jakob Nyankopɔn no, eyi noho akyerɛ wo.
Na nkyii so EWURADZE see no dɛ, Afei fa wo nsa hyɛ wo bo mu.
Na ɔdze ne nsa hyɛɛ no bo mu: na oyii puei no, hwɛ, nna ne nsa ho egu kwata fitaa dɛ esukwankyɛba.
Na ɔsee dɛ, Fa wo nsa hyɛ wo bo mu bio.
(Na ɔdze ne nsa hyɛɛ no bo mu bio; na oyii fii no bo mu no, hwɛ, nna adan dɛ no honam ara bio.)
Na ɔbɛba dɛ, sɛ wɔanngye wo enndzi, nkyii so woenntsie asɛnkyerɛdze a odzi kan no ne ndze a, wɔbɛgye asɛnkyerɛdze a otsia ebien no ne ndze edzi.
Na ɔbɛba dɛ, sɛ wɔanngye nsɛnkyerɛdze ebien yi mpo enndzi, nkyii so woenntsie wo ndze a, ɔno kɛsaw esutsen no mu nsu bi, na hue gu asaase kɛsɛɛ do: na nsu a ebɛsaw no wɔ esutsen no mu no ɔbɛdan bɔgya wɔ asaase kɛsɛɛ no do.
Na Moses see EWURADZE dɛ, Ao, EWURADZE, m’ano nntsew, nkan no o, ofitsi aber a ɔwo enye w’akowaa kasae yi o: osiandɛ m’ano yɛ dur, na me tɛkyerɛma yɛ pembɔɔ.
Na EWURADZE see no dɛ, Woana na ɔyɛɛ nyimpa ano?
Anaa woana na ɔyɛ nyimpa mmum, anaa otsitsifo, anaa ɔdzehufo, anaa onyifurafo?
Ana nnyɛ emi EWURADZE bi a?
Dɛm ntsi afei kɔ, na mibedzi w’ano ekyir, na makyerɛ wo dza ebɛka.
Na ɔsee dɛ, Ao EWURADZE, mepa wo kyɛw, dua nyia woara epɛ dɛ esoma no, ne nsa do soma.
Na EWURADZE n’ebufuw dzɛɛw wɔ Moses do, na ɔsee dɛ, Ana wo nua Aaron Levinyi no nnyi hɔ bi a?
Minyim dɛ obotum akasa yie.
Na eso, hwɛ, orifi edzi nye wo ebehyia: na sɛ ohu wo a, n’akoma bɔtɔ ne yamu.
Na kasa kyerɛ no, na fa nsɛm no hyɛ n’ano: na mibedzi w’ano, na ɔnye n’ano ekyir, na makyerɛ hom dza hom nyɛ.
Na ɔbɛyɛ wo kyeame ama ɔman no: na ɔbɛba dɛ, ɔno na ɔbɛyɛ ano ama wo, na ɔwo aayɛ dɛ Nyankopɔn ama no.
Na fa poma yi a edze bɛyɛ nsɛnkyerɛdze no kitsa wo nsamu.
Moses San Kɔ Egypt Na Moses sanee kɔr n’asew Jetro nkyɛn, na ɔkɛsee no dɛ, Mepa wo kyɛw, ma monkɔ, na mensan nkɔ mo nuanom a wɔwɔ Egypt no nkyɛn, na monkɔhwɛ kyerɛ wɔda ho tse ase anaa.
Na Jetro see Moses dɛ, Kɔ no asomdwee mu.
Na EWURADZE see Moses wɔ Midian dɛ, Kɔ, san kɔ Egypt: na nyimpa a wɔhwehwɛ wo nkwa no nyinara ewuwu.
Na Moses faa ne yer nye ne mbabanyin no, na ɔdze hɔn tsenatsenaa asoaso do, na ɔsanee dɛ ɔrokɔ Egypt asaase do: na Moses faa Nyankopɔn no poma no kitsaa ne nsamu.
Na EWURADZE see Moses dɛ, Sɛ esan kɔ Egypt a, hwɛ na anwanwadze a medze mahyɛ wo nsa no nyinara yɛ no wɔ Farao enyim: na mibepirim n’akoma, na ɔnnkɛma ɔman no akɔ.
Na se Farao dɛ, Mbrɛ EWURADZE se nye yi, Israel yɛ me babanyin, m’abakan a: na mase wo dɛ, Ma me ba nkɔ nkɔsom me; na ɔwo ammpen ma ɔannkɔ: hwɛ, muboku wo babanyin, w’abakan no.
Na ɔbaa dɛ ɔkwan do asoɛe no, EWURADZE hyiaa no, na ɔpɛɛ dɛ oboku no.
Nna Zipora faa ɔtwerɛbo, na ɔdze twaa ne babanyin no twatsia, na ɔtowee kyeen Moses n’ananadze; na ɔsee dɛ, Ampaara ɔwo yɛ bɔgya ho kun fofor dze ma me.
Na Ewuradze gyaa Moses.
Na osian twatsiatwa no ntsi Zipora see dɛ, Bɔgya ho kun fofor nye wo no.
Moses Hyia Aaron Na EWURADZE see Aaron dɛ, Kɔ sar no do kehyia Moses.
Na ɔkɔree, kehyiaa no wɔ Nyankopɔn ne bepɔw no ho, na ɔfeew n’ano.
Na Moses kaa nsɛm a EWURADZE dze somaa no no nyinara, nye nsɛnkyerɛdze a ɔdze hyɛɛ no no nyinara kyerɛɛ Aaron.
Na Moses nye Aaron kɔree na wɔkɔboaboaa Israelmba mpanyimfo nyinara ano.
Na Aaron kaa nsɛm a EWURADZE kaa kyerɛɛ Moses no nyinara, na ɔyɛɛ nsɛnkyerɛdze no wɔ ɔman no enyim.
Na ɔman no gyee dzii: na aber a wɔtsee dɛ EWURADZE abɛsera Israelmba, na ɔahwɛ hɔn amandzehu no wɔbobɔɔ hɔn tsir adze na wɔsɔree.
Moses Na Aaron Kɔ Farao Enyim Na n’ekyir no Moses nye Aaron bae, na wɔbɛsee Farao dɛ, Mbrɛ EWURADZE, Israel Nyankopɔn no se nye yi, Ma me man nkɔ, na wɔnkɛhyɛ fa mma me wɔ sar no do.
Na Farao see dɛ, Woana nye EWURADZE a mibetsie ne ndze na mama Israel akɔ?
Minnyim EWURADZE, na nkyii so meremma Israel nnkɔ.
Na wɔsee dɛ, Hebriwfo Nyankopɔn nye hɛn ehyia: yɛpa wo kyɛw, ma yɛnkɔ sar no do ndaansa kwan, na yɛnkɔbɔ afɔr mma EWURADZE hɛn Nyankopɔn; mma ɔaammfa ɔyardɔm, anaa afona emmbotua hɛn.
Na Egypthen no see hɔn dɛ, Ɔyɛ dɛn ntsi na Moses nye Aaron, hom robɔ ɔman no ko wɔ hɔn ndwuma ho yi?
Hom nkɔ hom ndzesoadze ho.
Na Farao see dɛ, Hwɛ, afei asaase no do nkorɔfo no adɔɔ so, na hom ma wɔhom fi hɔn ndzesoadze ho yi.
Na da no ara Farao hyɛɛ ɔman no hɔn abɔmbaafo, nye hɔn ahwɛdofo no dɛ, Mma hom mma ɔman no sar a wɔdze bɛyɛ ntayaa no bio dɛ nkan no: wɔmma hɔnara wɔnkɔ na wɔnkɔboaboa sar ano mma hɔnho.
Na ntayaa dodow a wɔyɛ no dada no, hom ngye hɔn; mma hom nnyi do bi: na wɔyɛ enyihaw; dɛm ntsi na wosu dɛ, Wɔmma yɛnkɔ nkɔbɔ afɔr mma hɛn Nyankopɔn no.
Hom mma edwuma durdur nda nkorɔfo no do, ama wɔaayɛ mu edwuma aberɛ; na mma wonntsie nsɛnhun.
Na ɔman no hɔn abɔmbaafo, nye hɔn ahwɛdofo no fiir edzi, na wɔbɛkaa kyerɛɛ ɔman no dɛ, Mbrɛ Farao se nye yi, Meremma hom sar bio.
Homara nkɔ nkɛfa sar wɔ mbrɛ hom benya bi: na worinnyi hom edwuma do biribiara.
Nna ɔman no petsee Egypt asaase nyina do kɔboaboaa mburonan ano dze yɛɛ sar.
Na abɔmbaafo no piapiaa hɔn dɛ, Hom nwie hom da kor edwuma wɔ ne da mu, dɛ aber a sar wɔ hɔ no ara.
Na wɔhwee Israelmba ahwɛdofo no a Farao n’abɔmbaafo no dze hɔn esisi hɔn do no, na wobisaa dɛ, Ɔyɛ dɛn ntsi na hom ennwie ntayaa a wɔahyɛ hom no yɛ ndeda nye ndɛ dɛ nkan no yi?
Nna Israelmba ahwɛdofo no bae bosui tɔɔ Farao do dɛ, Ɔyɛ dɛn ntsi na enye wo nkowaa dzi no dɛm yi?
Wɔmmaa wo nkowaa sar, na wɔse hɛn dɛ, Hom nyɛ ntayaa: na, hwɛ, wɔahwe wo nkowaa dze; na wankasa wo man na wɔayɛ bɔn.
Na ɔsee dɛ, Enyiahafo nye hom, enyiahafo nye hom: dɛm ntsi na hom se dɛ, Ma yɛnkɔ nkɔbɔ afɔr mma EWURADZE a. Dɛm ntsi afei hom nkɔ nkɛyɛ edwuma; na sar dze wɔremma hom, naaso ntayaa no dodow dze hom mma.
Na Israelmba ahwɛdofo no hun dɛ wɔwɔ amandzenya mu wɔ aber a wɔkaa dɛ, Mma hom nnyi hom da kor edwuma mu ntayaa no do dabiarada no.
Na wofi Farao nkyɛn reba no, wɔbɔtoo Moses nye Aaron dɛ wogyina ɔkwan no mu hɔ: na wɔsee hɔn dɛ, EWURADZE nhwɛ hom, na ombua; dɛ hom ama hɛn ho abɔn wɔ Farao, nye no nkowaa enyim, na hom dze afona ahyɛ hɔn nsa dɛ wɔmfa nku hɛn ntsi.
Moses Kosu Kyerɛ EWURADZE Na Moses sanee kɔr EWURADZE nkyɛn kɛsee dɛ, EWURADZE, ɔyɛ dɛn ntsi na enye ɔman yi edzi no bɔn dɛm yi?
Ɔyɛ dɛn ntsi na esomaa me yi?
Na ofitsi aber ara a mebaa Farao nkyɛn dɛ medze wo dzin nye no kasae no, ɔayɛ ɔman yi bɔn; nkyii so enngyee wo man koraa.
Na EWURADZE see Moses dɛ, Afei na irubohu dza medze merebɛyɛ Farao: na nsa a ɔyɛ dzen do na ɔbɛma wɔakɔ, na nsa a ɔyɛ dzen do na ɔbɛpam hɔn efi n’asaase do.
Nyankopɔn Kasa Kyerɛ Moses Na Nyankopɔn kasaa kyerɛɛ Moses, na ɔsee no dɛ, Emi nye EWURADZE: na miyii moho mekyerɛɛ Abraham, Isaak, nye Jakob, dɛ Nyankopɔn Otumfo, na me dzin YHWH (EWURADZE) no dze mamma wɔammfa ennhu me.
Na eso mama m’ahyɛmu a menye hɔn dzii no etsim, dɛ medze Keenan asaase a ɔyɛ hɔn ahɔhobea asaase no a wɔyɛ do ahɔho no mebɛma hɔn.
Na nkyii so matse Israelmba a Egyptfo dzii hɔn nya no, hɔn apempen; na makaa m’ahyɛmu no.
Dɛm ntsi se Israelmba dɛ, Emi nye Jehova, na mibeyi hom mefi Egyptfo ndzesoadze no ase, na meyi hom efi hɔn nkowaasom no mu, na medze abasa a wɔatsɛw mu, nye ntsɛmbu akɛse agye hom: na mafa hom ayɛ me man, na mayɛ hom Nyankopɔn: na hom ehu dɛ emi nye Jehova hom Nyankopɔn a oyii hom fii Egyptfo ndzesoadze ase no.
Na medze hom bɔkɔ asaase a memaa me nsa do wɔ ho dɛ medze mebɛma Abraham, Isaak, nye Jakob no do, na medze bɛma hom dɛ egyapadze: emi nye Jehova.
Na Moses kaa dɛm kyerɛɛ Israelmba no: na ahomtsew nye nkowaasom dzendzen ntsi woenntsie Moses.
Na EWURADZE kaa kyerɛɛ Moses dɛ, Kɔ, kɛka kyerɛ Egypthen Farao, dɛ ɔmma Israelmba mfi asaase no do nkɔ.
Na Moses kasae wɔ EWURADZE enyim see dɛ, Hwɛ, Israelmba enntsie me; na ɔbɛyɛ dɛn na Farao betsie emi a wonntwaa m’anofamfa twatsia yi?
Na EWURADZE kasaa kyerɛɛ Moses nye Aaron, na ɔdze hyɛɛ hɔn nsa dɛ wɔnkɔ Israelmba, nye Egypthen Farao nkyɛn, nkeyi Israelmba no mfi Egypt asaase do.
Moses Na Aaron Hɔn Ebusua Iyinom nye hɔn egyanom efi mu etsitsir: Israel n’abakan Reuben ne mbabanyin; Hanok, Pallu, Hezron, nye Karmi: iyinom nye Reuben n’ebusuafo.
Na Simeon ne mbabanyin; Jemuel, Jamin, Ohad, Jakin, Zohar, nye Saul, Keenannyi ɔbaa bi ne babanyin no: iyinom nye Simeon n’ebusuafo.
Na iyinom nye Levi ne mbabanyin no hɔn edzin dɛ mbrɛ hɔn mbusuasantsen tsetsee; Gerson, Kohat, nye Merari: na Levi no nkwaber mu mfe yɛ mfe ɔha eduasa esuon.
Gerson ne mbabanyin nye Libni na Simei, dɛ mbrɛ hɔn ebusuafo tsetsee.
Kohat ne mbabanyin; Amram, nye Izhar, Hebron, Uziel: na Kohat no nkwamber mu mfe yɛ mfe ɔha eduasa ebiasa.
Merari ne mbabanyin nye Mahili nye Musi.
Iyinom nye Levifo ebusuafo dɛ mbrɛ hɔn ebusuasantsen tsetsee.
Na Amram faa n’egya akyerɛbaa Jokebed waar no; na ɔnye no woo Aaron nye Moses: na Amram no nkwaber mu mfe yɛ mfe ɔha eduasa esuon.
Izhar ne mbabanyin nye Kora, Nefeg, nye Zikri.
Uziel ne mbabanyin nye Misael, Elzafan, nye Sitri.
Na Aaron faa Eliseba, Aminadab ne babaa no, Nahson n’akyerɛbaa no waar no; na ɔnye no woo Nadab, Abihu, Eleazar nye Itamar.
Na Kora ne mbabanyin nye Assir, Elkana, na Abiasaf; iyinom nye Korafo ebusuafo.
Na Aaron ne babanyin Eleazar faa Putiel ne mbabaa mu baako waar no; na ɔnye no woo Finehas.
Iyinom nye Levifo egyanom efi mu etsitsir dɛ mbrɛ hɔn ebusuafo tsetsee.
Iyinom nye Aaron nye Moses no a EWURADZE see hɔn dɛ, wonnyi Israelmba mfi Egypt asaase do dɛ mbrɛ hɔn dɔm tsetsee no.
Moses na Aaron nye hɔn a wɔkasaa kyerɛɛ Egypthen Farao dɛ wobeyi Israelmba efi Egypt akɔ no.
EWURADZE N’asɛm Ba Moses Nye Aaron Hɔ Na ɔbaa dɛ da no a EWURADZE kasaa kyerɛɛ Moses wɔ Egypt asaase do no, EWURADZE kaa kyerɛɛ Moses dɛ, Emi nye EWURADZE: ka dza meka kyerɛ wo nyinara kyerɛ Egypthen Farao.
Na Moses kae wɔ EWURADZE enyim dɛ, Hwɛ, emi wonntwaa m’anofamfa twatsia, na Farao bɛyɛ dɛn etsie me?
Na EWURADZE see Moses dɛ, Hwɛ, mebɛma ayɛ dɛ Nyame wɔ Farao enyim; na wo nua Aaron bɛyɛ wo nkɔnhyɛnyi.
Ɔwo bɛka dza mehyɛ wo nyinara: na wo nua Aaron bɛka akyerɛ Farao ma ɔaama Israelmba efi n’asaase do akɔ.
Na mibepirim Farao n’akoma, na mama me nsɛnkyerɛdze nye m’anwanwadze adɔɔ so wɔ Egypt asaase do.
Na Farao rinntsie hom, na medze me nsa bɔto Egypt do, na meyi mo dɔm, me man Israelmba no, mefi Egypt asaase do wɔ atsɛmbu akɛse mu.
Na sɛ metsen me nsa wɔ Egypt do na miyi Israelmba fi hɔn mu fir a, nna Egyptfo bohu dɛ emi nye EWURADZE.
Na Moses nye Aaron yɛɛ dɛ mbrɛ EWURADZE hyɛɛ hɔn no ara.
Aber a wɔkasaa kyerɛɛ Farao no, nna Moses edzi mfe eduowɔtwe, na Aaron mfe eduowɔtwe ebiasa.
Aaron No Poma Dan Abowatsena Na EWURADZE kasaa kyerɛɛ Moses nye Aaron dɛ, Sɛ Farao ka kyerɛ hom dɛ, Hom nyi hom anwanwadze bi nkyerɛ a, ɔnodze ka kyerɛ Aaron dɛ, Yi wo poma no, na tow kyen famu wɔ Farao enyim, ma ɔndan abowatsena.
Na Moses nye Aaron kɔr Farao nkyɛn, na wɔyɛɛ dɛm, dɛ mbrɛ EWURADZE hyɛe no: na Aaron toow no poma kyeen famu wɔ Farao enyim nye no nkowaa enyim, na ɔdaan abowatsena.
Nna Farao so frɛfrɛɛ enyansafo no, na abayifo no: na hɔn so, Egypt akɔmfo no, dze hɔn nkaber yɛɛ dɛmara.
Na hɔn nyinara totoow hɔn mpoma guu famu, na ɔdandaan mbowatsena: na Aaron no poma no memeen hɔn mpoma no.
Na Farao n’akoma pirimii, na oenntsie hɔn; dɛ mbrɛ EWURADZE kae no.
Ɔhaw Ahorow Ba Egypt: Mbɔgya Na EWURADZE see Moses dɛ, Farao n’akoma epirim, ɔmmpen dɛ ɔman no kɔ.
Kɔ Farao nkyɛn ampa: hwɛ, orupue akɔ nsu mu: na ɔwo kegyina esutsen no no nkɔnkɔnoa hɔ hyia no; na poma no a ɔdaan abowatsena no fa kitsa wo nsamu.
Na se no dɛ, EWURADZE, Hebriwfo Nyankopɔn no, na ɔasoma me wo hɔ dɛ, Ma me man nkɔ nkɔsom me wɔ sar no do: na, hwɛ, enntsie ara dze ebodu sesei.
Mbrɛ EWURADZE se nye yi, Iyi mu na ibohu dɛ emi nye EWURADZE: Hwɛ, medze poma a ɔdze me nsamu yi mobɔbɔ esutsen yi mu nsu, na ɔbɛdan bɔgya.
Na nam a wɔwɔ esutsen no mu bowuwu, na esutsen no bɔbɔn; na Egyptfo bekyir dɛ wɔbɔnom esutsen no mu nsu.
Na EWURADZE see Moses dɛ, Se Aaron dɛ, Fa wo poma, na tsen wo nsa wɔ Egypt esuesu do, hɔn esutsen do, hɔn nsubansuba do, nye hɔn mbakansu nyina do, ma ɔndandan bɔgya; na bɔgya bɛba Egypt asaase nyinara do, ndua esupi nye abo esupi nyina mu.
Na Moses nye Aaron yɛɛ dɛm, dɛ mbrɛ EWURADZE hyɛe no; na ɔmaa poma no do, na ɔdze bɔɔ nsu a ɔwɔ esutsen no mu no wɔ Farao enyim, nye no nkowaa enyim; na nsu a ɔwɔ esutsen no mu nyinara daan bɔgya.
Na nam a wɔwɔ esutsen no mu wuwui, na esutsen no bɔnee, na Egyptfo enntum annom esutsen no mu nsu; na bɔgya no baa Egypt asaase nyinara do.
Na Egypt akɔmfo no dze hɔn nkaber no yɛɛ dɛmara: na Farao n’akoma pirimii, na oenntsie hɔn; dɛ mbrɛ EWURADZE kae no.
Na Farao daan noho na ɔkɔr ne fie, na ɔammfa iyi so mpo annto n’akoma mu.
Na Egyptfo nyina tutuu amona wɔ esutsen no ho dɛ wobenya nsu anom; osiandɛ wonntum nnom esutsen no mu nsu.
Na EWURADZE bɔɔ esutsen no ekyir no, nda esuon botwaa mu.
Ntwɛr Na EWURADZE kaa kyerɛɛ Moses dɛ, Kɔ Farao nkyɛn, na se no dɛ, Mbrɛ EWURADZE se nye yi, Ma me man nkɔ, na wɔnkɔsom me.
Na sɛ ammpen ma wɔaannkɔ a, hwɛ, medze ntwɛr bofura wo ntoaado nyinara: na esutsen no bɔdɔ ntwɛr menyamenya, na wɔbɔfofow aba wo fie, nye w’adankyir, nye wo mpa do, nye wo nkowaa fie, nye wo man do, nye wo mfononoo mu, nye wo mbɔrnkutu mu: na ntwɛr no bɔfow aba ɔwo, nye wo mamfo, nye wo nkowaa nyinara do.
Na EWURADZE see Moses dɛ, Se Aaron dɛ, Fa wo poma tsen wo nsa wɔ esutsen, nye nsubansuba, nye nsutaae do, na ma ntwɛr mbra Egypt asaase do.
Na Aaron tseen ne nsa wɔ Egypt nsu do; na ntwɛr no fowee bae, na wobofuraa Egypt asaase do.
Na akɔmfo no dze hɔn nkaber no yɛɛ dɛmara, na wɔmaa ntwɛr fowee baa Egypt asaase do.
Nna Farao frɛɛ Moses nye Aaron, na ɔsee dɛ, Hom mpa EWURADZE kyɛw ma onyi ntwɛr no mfi emi, nye me man do; na mebɛma ɔman no akɔ, ma wɔaakɔbɔ afɔr ama EWURADZE.
Na Moses see Farao dɛ, W’adaworom: ebɛn aber na mempa kyɛw memma ɔwo, nye wo nkowaa, nye wo man, ma wɔnsɛɛ ntwɛr no mfi ɔwo nye w’efi do, na wɔnka esutsen no nko mu?
Na ɔsee dɛ, Ɔkyena a. Na ɔsee dɛ, Ɔnyɛ dɛ dza aka no ara: ama eehu dɛ obiara nnyi hɔ a ɔtse dɛ EWURADZE hɛn Nyankopɔn.
Na ntwɛr no befi ɔwo, nye w’efi, nye wo nkowaa, nye wo man do; esutsen no mu nko na wɔbɛka.
Na Moses nye Aaron fii Farao nkyɛn kɔree: na Moses sui frɛɛ EWURADZE wɔ ntwɛr no a ɔdze baa Farao do no ho.
Na EWURADZE yɛɛ dɛ mbrɛ Moses kae no: na ntwɛr no wuwui wɔ efi mu, nye abangua do, nye haban mu.
Na wɔboaboaa hɔn ano ekuwekuw: na asaase no do bɔnee.
Na Farao hun dɛ ahotɔ aba mu no, opiriim n’akoma, na oenntsie hɔn: dɛ mbrɛ EWURADZE kae no.
Dwuw Na EWURADZE see Moses dɛ, Se Aaron dɛ, Tsen wo poma no, na fa bɔ asaase do huntuma, ma ɔndan dwuw wɔ Egypt asaase nyinara do.
Na wɔyɛɛ dɛm; na Aaron dze no poma no tseen ne nsa, na ɔdze bɔɔ asaase do huntuma, ma dwuw fɔɔr nyimpa nye mbowa: asaase no do huntuma nyinara daan dwuw wɔ Egypt asaase nyinara do.
Na akɔmfo no dze hɔn nkaber yɛɛ dɛmara dɛ wɔrema dwuw aba na woenntum: na dwuw no wɔ nyimpa nye mbowa ho.
Nna akɔmfo no see Farao dɛ, Nyankopɔn nsatseaba nye yi: na Farao n’akoma pirimii, na oenntsie hɔn; dɛ mbrɛ EWURADZE kae no.
Atsɛn Na EWURADZE see Moses dɛ, Soɛr anapaatu, na kegyina Farao enyim; hwɛ, ɔreba nsu no ho; na se no dɛ, Mbrɛ EWURADZE se nye yi, Ma me man nkɔ, ma wɔnkɔsom me.
Na sɛ ennkɛma me man akɔ a, hwɛ, mebɛma atsɛn menyamenya aba ɔwo, nye wo nkowaa, nye wo man, nye w’efi do: na Egyptfo efiefi mu, na asaase a wɔtse do no so atsɛn menyamenya bɛyɛ no amaama.
Na da no mubotwa Gosen asaase a me man tse do no egya, ma atsɛn menyamenya aannkɔ hɔ, ama eehu dɛ emi nye EWURADZE wɔ asaase finimfin.
Na medze ɔhe mobɔto me man nye wo man ntamu: ɔkyena na asɛnkyerɛdze yi bɛba.
Na EWURADZE yɛɛ dɛm; na atsɛn menyamenya a hɔn ano yɛ yaw baa Farao fi mu, nye no nkowaa efi mu: na osian atsɛn menyamenya no ntsi Egypt asaase no nyinara do sɛɛe.
Na Farao frɛɛ Moses nye Aaron, na ɔsee dɛ, Hom nkɔ nkɔbɔ afɔr mma hom Nyankopɔn wɔ asaase no do.
Na Moses dɛ, Ɔnnsɛ dɛ wɔyɛ no dɛm; osiandɛ Egyptfo ekyiwadze na yɛdze bɔbɔ afɔr ama EWURADZE hɛn Nyankopɔn no: hwɛ, ana yɛmfa Egyptfo ekyiwadze mbɔ afɔr wɔ hɔn enyiwa mu, na wonnkesiw hɛn abo bi a?
Yebotu ndaansa kwan akɔ sar no do, na yɛakɔbɔ afɔr ama EWURADZE hɛn Nyankopɔn, dɛ mbrɛ ɔbɛhyɛ hɛn no.
Na Farao see dɛ, mebɛma hom akɔ, ama hom aakɔbɔ afɔr ama EWURADZE hom Nyankopɔn no wɔ sar no do; na ekyir nko na hom nnkɔ: hom mpa kyɛw mma me.
Na Moses see dɛ, Hwɛ, mirifi wo nkyɛn akɔ, na makɛpa EWURADZE kyɛw ma atsɛn menyamenya no eefi Farao, nye no nkowaa, nye ne man do ɔkyena: na abrasɛm nko na mma Farao nndzi bio, dɛ ɔnnkɛma ɔman no akɔ akɔbɔ afɔr ama EWURADZE.
Na Moses fii Farao nkyɛn kɔree, na ɔkɛpaa EWURADZE kyɛw.
Na EWURADZE yɛɛ dɛ mbrɛ Moses kae no; na oyii atsɛn menyamenya no fii Farao, nye no nkowaa, nye ne man do; kor mpo annka.
Na Farao piriim n’akoma aber yi so, na ɔamma ɔman no annkɔ.
Mbowa Wu Nna EWURADZE see Moses dɛ, Kɔ Farao nkyɛn, na ka kyerɛ no dɛ, Mbrɛ EWURADZE Hebriwfo Nyankopɔn se nye yi, Ma me man nkɔ, ma wɔnkɔsom me.
Na sɛ ammpen ma wɔaannkɔ, na eda ho ara tsintsim hɔn do a, hwɛ, EWURADZE nsa wɔ wo mbowa a wɔwɔ haban mu do, na ɔdze mbowawu yayaayaw bɛba mpɔnkɔ, nsoasopɔnkɔ, efumpɔnkɔ, anantwikuw, nye nguankuw do.
Na EWURADZE dze sorbi bɔto Israel mbowa nye Egypt mbowa ntamu na dza ɔyɛ Israelmba dze no nyinara mu biara nnkowu.
Na EWURADZE hyɛɛ aber, dɛ, Ɔkyena na EWURADZE bɛyɛ adze yi wɔ asaase no do.
Na adze kyee no EWURADZE yɛɛ adze no, na Egypt mbowa nyinara wuwui: na Israelmba mbowa dze no mu kor mpo ennwu.
Na Farao somae, na hwɛ, nna Israelfo mbowa mu kor mpo nnwui.
Na Farao n’akoma sorowee, na ɔamma ɔman no annkɔ.
Mpɔmpɔ Na EWURADZE see Moses nye Aaron dɛ, Hom mfa fononoo mu nso nsama nsama, na Moses ntow mpetse wimu wɔ Farao enyim.
Na ɔbɛdan tutuw wɔ Egypt asaase nyinara do, na ɔayɛ mpɔmpɔ a ɔpaapaa tutu ekur wɔ nyimpa nye mbowa ho, wɔ Egypt asaase nyinara do.
Na wɔfaa fononoo mu nso, na wokegyinaa Farao enyim; na Moses towee petsee wimu; na ɔdaan pɔmpɔ a ɔpaapaa tutu ekur wɔ nyimpa nye mbowa ho.
Na osian mpɔmpɔ no ntsi akɔmfo no enntum enngyina Moses enyim; osiandɛ nna mpɔmpɔ no abobɔ akɔmfo no nye Egyptfo nyinara.
Na EWURADZE piriim Farao n’akoma, na oenntsie hɔn; dɛ mbrɛ EWURADZE kaa kyerɛɛ Moses no.
Ɔsorbo Na EWURADZE see Moses dɛ, Soɛr anapaatu, na kegyina Farao enyim, na se no dɛ, Mbrɛ EWURADZE, Hebriwfo Nyankopɔn no se nye yi, Ma me man nkɔ, ma wɔnkɔsom me.
Na afei dze merema me yardɔm nyinara aba w’akoma do, nye wo nkowaa do, nye wo man do; ama eehu dɛ obiara nnyi hɔ a ɔtse dɛ emi wɔ asaase nyinara do.
Na afei sɛ matsen me nsa, na medze owuyar abɔ ɔwo nye wo man a, nkyɛ woetwa wo efi asaase do: na ampaara iyi ntsi na mama egyina hɔ, dɛ mebɛkyerɛ wo mo tum, na wɔaabɔ me dzin akyerɛ wɔ asaase nyinara do.
Eda ho ara rema woho do wɔ me man do, dɛ eremma wɔnnkɔ anaa?
Hwɛ, ɔkyena siseber yi mebɛma ɔsorbo a n’ano yɛ dur dodoodow a ne saso mmbaa Egypt pɛn ofi da a wɔkyekyeree dze bodu ndɛ yi atɔ.
Dɛm ntsi afei soma na wɔnkɛfa wo mbowa nye biribiara a ewɔ wɔ haban mu nyina mbra ntsɛm; na nyimpa biara nye abowa biara a wobohu hɔn wɔ haban mu, na wɔammfa hɔn ammba fie no, ɔsorbo no bɔhwe hɔn, na wobowuwu.
Farao nkowaa mu nyia osuroo EWURADZE n’asɛm no maa no nkowaa nye ne fiembowa guanee baa fie.
Na nyia oemmbu EWURADZE n’asɛm bi no gyaa no nkowaa nye ne fiembowa wɔ haban mu.
Na EWURADZE see Moses dɛ, Tsen wo nsa wɔ sor, ma ɔsorbo mbra Egypt asaase nyinara do, nyimpa, nye abowa, nye haban mu efuw biara do, wɔ Egypt asaase nyinara do.
Na Moses tseen no poma no wɔ sor: na EWURADZE maa senaman nye ɔsorbo bae, na ogya porowee guu asaase do; na EWURADZE tɔɔ ɔsorbo guu Egypt asaase do.
Nna ɔsorbo no bae, na ogya a ɔdzɛw brambram toatoa mu a ɔfora ɔsorbo no mu a n’ano yɛ dzen dodoodow a ne saso mmbaa Egypt asaase nyinara do pɛn ofi da a ɔbɛyɛɛ ɔman no.
Na ɔsorbo no hwee Egypt asaase nyinara do dza ɔwɔ haban mu nyinara, nyimpa nye abowa nyina; na ɔsorbo no hwee haban mu efuw nyinara, na obubuu haban mu ndua nyinara.
Gosen asaase do mbrɛ Israelmba wɔ no nko na ɔsorbo no bi ammba.
Na Farao somae ma wɔkɛfrɛɛ Moses nye Aaron, na ɔsee hɔn dɛ, Afei dze mayɛ bɔn: EWURADZE dzi bem, na emi nye me man yɛyɛ afɔdzifo.
Hom mpa EWURADZE kyɛw; na asenaman dzendzen yi nye ɔsorbo no adɔɔ so; na mebɛma hom akɔ, na hom renntsena ha bio.
Na Moses see no dɛ, Mefi kurow mu akɔ ara a, nkyɛ matserɛw me nsamu akyerɛ EWURADZE; asenaman no begyaa, nkyii so ɔsorbo biara nnkɛba bio; ama eehu dɛ asaase yɛ EWURADZE dze.
Na ɔwo nye wo nkowaa dze, minyim dɛ hom nnyae nnsuroo EWURADZE Nyankopɔn bi.
Na ɔhwee asaaba nye atoko: osiandɛ atoko no ayɛ mbɛtsem, na asaaba no so abɔ nkukuduuduw.
Na ewifua nye ewu dze wɔannhwe hɔn: osiandɛ nna wonntuu mpon biara.
Na Moses fi Farao nkyɛn fii kurow no mu, na ɔkɛtserɛɛw ne nsamu kyerɛɛ EWURADZE, na nsenaman nye ɔsorbo no gyaae, na nyankom no woennhue enngu asaase no do.
Na Farao hun dɛ nyankom, nye ɔsorbo, nye asenaman no egyae no, ɔyɛɛ bɔn bio, na opiriim n’akoma, ɔno nye no nkowaa.
Na Farao n’akoma pirimii, na ɔamma Israelmba annkɔ; dɛ mbrɛ EWURADZE nam Moses do kae no.
Mbɛbɛw Na EWURADZE see Moses dɛ, Kɔ Farao nkyɛn: na mepirim n’akoma, nye no nkowaa akoma, ama meeyi me nsɛnkyerɛdze yi akyerɛ no wɔ hɔn mu: na aaka no wɔ wo ba, nye wo ba ne ba asomu, ndzɛmba a mayɛ no wɔ Egypt do, na me nsɛnkyerɛdze a mayɛ no wɔ hɔn mu; ama hom eehu dɛ emi nye EWURADZE.
Na Moses nye Aaron kɔr Farao nkyɛn, na wɔkɛsee no dɛ, Mbrɛ EWURADZE, Hebriwfo Nyankopɔn no se nye yi, Eropow dɛ ebrɛ woho adze wɔ m’enyim ma ekodu dabɛn?
Ma me man nkɔ, na wɔnkɔsom me.
Na sɛ ammpen ma me man aannkɔ a, hwɛ, ɔkyena medze mbɛbɛw bɛba wo ntoaado: na wɔbɛkata asaase enyi, dɛ obi nnkotum ehu asaase: na wobedzi edzinkaa a ɔsorbo no gyaae ma ɔkae maa hom no, na wobedzi dua biara a ɔrefefɛw wɔ haban mu ama hom no: na wɔbɛhyehyɛ w’efi mu, nye wo nkowaa nyinara efi mu, nye Egyptfo nyinara efi mu amaama; dɛ mbrɛ w’egyanom, nye w’egyanom hɔn egyanom nnhun bi pɛn ofi da a wɔdze baa asaase do dze bodu ndɛ da yi.
Na ɔdaan noho, na ofii Farao nkyɛn puei.
Na Farao no nkowaa see no dɛ, Nyimpa yi bɛtseetsee hɛn araa ma ekodu dabɛn?
Ma nkorɔfo no nkɔ, ma wɔnkɔsom EWURADZE hɔn Nyankopɔn no.
Ana Egypt asɛɛ yi innhu bi a?
Na wɔdze Moses nye Aaron baa Farao nkyɛn bio: na ɔsee hɔn dɛ, Hom nkɔ nkɔsom EWURADZE hom Nyankopɔn: na woananom ara na wɔbɔkɔ?
Na Moses see dɛ, Yɛnye hɛn mbofra nye hɛn mpanyin bɔkɔ, yɛnye hɛn mbabanyin na ɔnye hɛn mbabaa, yɛnye hɛn nguan na ɔnye hɛn anantwi bɔkɔ; osiandɛ otwar dɛ yɛhyɛ fa ma EWURADZE.
Na ɔsee hɔn dɛ, Hm, EWURADZE ndzi hom ekyir ɛ, ber a merema hom, nye hom mbofraba no akɔ yi: mutum hu dɛ bɔn na ɔwɔ hom adwen mu.
Dabida: hom a hom yɛ mbanyin no ara nkɔ, na wɔnkɔsom EWURADZE; na ɔnoara nye dza hom rohwehwɛ.
Na woyii hɔn edzi fii Farao enyim.
Na EWURADZE see Moses dɛ, Tsen wo nsa wɔ Egypt asaase do, wɔ mbɛbɛw no ntsi, ma wɔmbra Egypt asaase do, na wɔmbɔwe asaase no do efuw nyinara, mekyerɛ dza ɔsorbo no egyaa no nyinara.
Na Moses tseen no poma no wɔ Egypt asaase do, na EWURADZE dze boka mframa bɔɔ asaase no do da no nyinara, na anadwe no nyinara; na anapa no, boka mframa dze mbɛbɛw no bae.
Na mbɛbɛw no kɔr Egypt asaase nyinara do, na wɔkɛgyegyee Egypt ntoaado nyinara; wɔdɔɔ so dodow; mbɛbɛw biara a ɔtse dɛm mbaa pɛn, na hɔn ekyir so bi nnkɛba dɛm da.
Na wɔkataa asaase no nyinara enyi, ma isum gyee asaase no do; na wɔwee asaase no do efuw nyinara, nye ndua a ɔsorbo no gyaae no do aba nyinara: na adze momon biara annka a ɔyɛ dua anaa haban mu efuw, wɔ Egypt asaase nyinara do.
Nna Farao maa wɔkɛfrɛɛ Moses nye Aaron ntsɛmara; na ɔsee dɛ, Mayɛ bɔn etsia EWURADZE hom Nyankopɔn, nye hom.
Dɛm ntsi afei, mepa wo kyɛw, fa mo bɔn fir me prɛko yi ara, na hom mpa EWURADZE hom Nyankopɔn kyɛw, ma onyi owu yi ara mfi mo do.
Na ofii Farao nkyɛn kɔree, na ɔkɛpaa EWURADZE kyɛw.
Na EWURADZE dze daan anee mframa dzendzen mbordo a ɔbɛfaa mbɛbɛw no, na ɔdze hɔn koguu Mbɛw Po no mu; abɛbɛw kor mpo annka wɔ Egypt ntoaado nyinara.
Na EWURADZE piriim Farao n’akoma, na ɔamma Israelmba no annkɔ.
Sum Na EWURADZE see Moses dɛ, Tsen wo nsa wɔ sor, ma sum mbra Egypt asaase do, mekyerɛ sum a wosuo mu a ɔbɛyɛ a yie.
Na Moses tseen ne nsa wɔ sor; na sum kebii hyɛɛ Egypt asaase nyinara dze, do nda ebiasa; obiara ennhu ne nyɛnko, nkyii so obiara annsoɛr emmfi ne tsenabew nda ebiasa: na Israelmba nyinara wonyaa kan wɔ hɔn efiefi.
Na Farao frɛɛ Moses, na ɔsee dɛ, Hom nkɔ nkɔsom EWURADZE; hom nguan nye hom anantwi nko na wɔmma wɔnka: wɔmma hom mbofraba no so nye hom nkɔ.
Na Moses see dɛ, Ohia dɛ edze okum afɔrbɔdze nye ɔhyew afɔrbɔdze so hyɛ hɛn nsa ama yaabɔ afɔr ama EWURADZE hɛn Nyankopɔn.
Hɛn mbowa so nye hɛn bɔkɔ; ɔnnkɛka abowaanamɔn mpo wɔ ekyir; na ɔno mu bi na otwar dɛ yɛkɛfa som EWURADZE hɛn Nyankopɔn; na yennyim dza yɛdze bɔsom EWURADZE, gyedɛ yedu hɔ ana.
Na EWURADZE piriim Farao n’akoma, na ɔammpɛ dɛ ɔma wɔkɔ.
Na Farao see no dɛ, Fi mo do kɔ, hwɛ woho yie, mma nnhu m’enyim bio; na da a ibohu m’enyim no ibowu.
Na Moses see dɛ, Aka no yie; munnkohu w’enyim bio.
Moses Ka Mbakamba Hɔn Wu Ho Asɛm Na EWURADZE see Moses dɛ, Mebɛma ɔyardɔm kor so aba Farao, nye Egypt do bio; na n’ekyir no ɔbɛma hom efi ha akɔ: aber a ɔbɛma hom akɔ no, ampaara, ɔbɛpam hom efi ha koraa.
Afei kasa wɔ ɔman no asomu, na ma ɔbanyin biara mbisa wɔ ne nyɛnko hɔ, na ɔbaa mbisa wɔ ne nyɛnko hɔ, dwetɛ ndwindze, nye sika ndwindze.
Na EWURADZE maa ɔman no enyimpa wɔ Egyptfo enyim.
Nkyii so nna ɔyɛɛ Moses otsitsir paara wɔ Egypt asaase do, wɔ Farao nkowaa enyim, nye ɔman no enyim.
Na Moses see dɛ, Mbrɛ EWURADZE se nye yi, Bɛyɛ esuom na mibefir edzi mafa Egypt mu: na Egypt asaase do mbakan nyinara bowuwu, ofi Farao n’abakan a ɔtsena n’ahengua do do, dze kodu afonabaa mpo a ɔwɔ ewuyambo ekyir n’abakan do; nye ofiembowa mbakan nyinara.
Na su kɛse bɛba Egypt asaase nyinara do a ne saso bi mbaa da, eso ne saso bi nnkɛba bio.
Na Israelmba nyinara dze, ɔkraman mpo nnkɔtwe ne tɛkyerɛma ahye hɔn, ɔnnkɛhye nyimpa anaa abowa: ama hom eehu mbrɛ EWURADZE si dze ɔhe to Egyptfo nye Israel ntamu.
Na wo nkowaa yi nyinara besian aba mo hɔ, na wɔabɔbɔ hɔn mu adze ama me dɛ, Fir edzi kɔ, ɔwo nye ɔman a wɔka wo do nyinara: na ɔno ekyir no na mibefir edzi makɔ.
Na ɔdze ebufuhyew fii Farao nkyɛn kɔree.
Na EWURADZE see Moses dɛ, Farao nnketsie hom; ama m’anwanwadze aadɔɔ so wɔ Egypt asaase do.
Na Moses nye Aaron yɛɛ anwanwadze yi nyinara wɔ Farao enyim; na EWURADZE piriim Farao n’akoma, na ɔamma Israelmba emmfi n’asaase do annkɔ.
Apaho Na EWURADZE kasaa kyerɛɛ Moses nye Aaron wɔ Egypt asaase do dɛ, Bosoom yi bɛyɛ abosoom ahyɛse ama hom: ɔbɛyɛ afrenhyia mu bosoom a odzi kan ama hom.
Hom nkasa nkyerɛ Israel mboanofo no nyinara dɛ, Bosoom yi ne da a otsia du no mu, wɔmfefa nguambaa nkorkor, dɛ mbrɛ hom egyanom efiefi tsetsee, fie kor eguambaa kor: na sɛ ofidua no suar dodow dze ma eguambaa kor a, ɔno wɔmma ɔnye ne nyɛnko a ɔbɛn ne fi mfa kor dɛ mbrɛ akra no hɔn dodow tse; dɛ mbrɛ nyimpa biara n’edzidzi tse no, na hom mfa mbu eguambaa no ano.
Hom eguambaa nyɛ dza onndzi dzɛm, onyin a oedzi afrenhyia a: hom nyi no wɔ nkɔsɔw anaa mpɔnkye mu: na hom mfa no nsie ma onkodu bosoom kor no ara ne da a otsia duanan no: na Israel mboanofo kuw no nyina nkuku hɔn ewimbir.
Na wɔmfa bɔgya no bi, na wɔmfa nsera efi a wobedzi no wɔ mu no n’apondua ebien no nye mpondua etsifi no ho.
Na wondzi nam no anadwe no ara, wɔmfa gya ntoto, na wɔmfa epitsi boodoo, nye fan wenwen ndzi.
Mma wonndzi no amon, nkyii so mma wɔmmfa nsu nnoa, mbom wɔmfa gya ntoto; ne tsir nye no ntwɛr na ɔnye n’ayamudze no.
Na mma hom mma no ho biribiara nnka ma adze nnkye do; na dza ɔbɛka ma adze akye do no hom mfa gya nhyew.
Na mbrɛ hom ndzi no nye yi; hom mbobɔ hom asen do, hom mpaboa nhyehyɛ hom anan, na hom mpoma nkitsakitsa hom nsamu: na hom ndzi no ɔhar do: ɔyɛ EWURADZE apaho.
Osiandɛ mubotwa mu wɔ Egypt asaase do anadwe no, na muboku Egypt asaase do mbakan nyinara, nyimpa nye mbowa nyina; na mubobu Egypt enyame nyinara ntsɛn: emi nye EWURADZE.
Na bɔgya no bɛyɛ asɛnkyerɛdze ama hom wɔ efi a hom wɔ mu no ho: na sɛ muhu mbɔgya no a, mebɛpa hom ho, na ɔyardɔm bi nnkɛba hom do abɛsɛɛ hom, sɛ morobɔbɔ Egypt asaase no a. Na da yi nyɛ nkaa mma hom, na hom nhyɛ no fa mma EWURADZE: hom mfa mbra do nyɛ no afahyɛ wɔ hom ebusuasantsen mu daa.
Nda esuon na hom ndzi epitsi boodoo; da a odzi kan no ara na hom nyi mbɔrkaw mfi hom efiefi: na obiara a obedzi mbɔrkaw boodoo ofitsi da a odzi kan no do dze kodu da a otsia esuon no do no, ɔkra no wobotwa no efi Israel.
Na da a odzi kan no hom nyɛ no nhyiamu krɔnkrɔn, na da a otsia esuon no so nhyiamu krɔnkrɔn; mma wɔnnyɛ edwuma biara wɔ mu, gyedɛ dza nyimpa biara bedzi nko na hom nyɛ.
Na hom ndwen epitsi afahyɛ no do; na dɛm da yi ara so na miyii hom dɔm no mifii Egypt asaase do: dɛm ntsi hom ndwen da yi do wɔ hom ebusuasantsen mu nyɛ no mbra daa.
Bosoom a odzi kan no mu, bosoom no mu da a otsia duanan ewimbir no, na hom ndzi epitsi ma onkodu bosoom no mu da a otsia eduonu biako ewimbir.
Nda esuon na mma mma wonnhu mbɔrkaw wɔ hom efi mu: na obiara a obedzi dza ɔaka no, ɔkra no wobotwa no efi Israel mboanofo mu, sɛ ɔyɛ ɔmamforanyi o, obi a wɔwoo no wɔ asaase no do o. Mma hom nndzi biribiara a akaw; hom ndzi epitsi wɔ hom tsenabew nyinara.
Nna Moses frɛɛ Israel mpanyimfo nyinara, na ɔsee hɔn dɛ, Hom nkɔ nkeyiyi nguambaa dɛ mbrɛ hom ebusua tsetsee, na hom nku apaho no.
Na hom mfa odwonhataw (hisɔp) siaw, na hom mfa mbɔ bɔgya a ɔwɔ bɛɛsen no mu no mu, na hom mfa bɔgya a ɔwɔ bɛɛsen no mu no bi mpetse mpondua etsifi nye apondua ebien no ho; na mma hom mu obiara mmfir edzi mmfi ne fie abowano ma onkodu anapa.
Na EWURADZE botwa mu abɔbɔ Egyptfo; na sɛ ohu bɔgya no wɔ mpondua etsifi, nye apondua ebien no ho a, EWURADZE bɛpa ɔpon no ho, na ɔnnkɛma ɔsɛɛfo no kwan ma ɔaaba hom efi mu abɔbobɔ hom.
Na hom ndwen iyi do ma ɔnyɛ mbra mma ɔwo nye wo mba daa.
Na ɔbɛba dɛ, sɛ hom du asaase a EWURADZE dze bɛma hom no do, dɛ mbrɛ ɔabɔ anohoba no a, ɔno hom ndzi ɔsom yi do.
Na ɔbɛba dɛ, sɛ hom mba bisa hom dɛ, Hom som yi ase nye dɛn?
Ɔno hom nse dɛ, Ɔyɛ EWURADZE n’apaho afɔrbɔdze, nyia ɔpaa Israelmba hɔn efi ho wɔ Egypt, wɔ aber a ɔbɔɔ Egyptfo, na oyii hɛn efi fii mu no.
Na ɔman no bɔɔ hɔn tsir adze na wɔsɔree.
Na Israelmba kɔree kɛyɛɛ dɛ mbrɛ EWURADZE hyɛɛ Moses nye Aaron no.
Mbakamba Hɔn Wu Na ɔbaa dɛ esuom no, EWURADZE bɔbɔɔ Egypt asaase do mbakan nyinara, ofi Farao n’abakan a ɔtsena n’ahengua do no do dze kodu adaduadan mu ndɔmmum n’abakan do; nye ofiembowa mbakan nyinara.
Na Farao soɛɛr anadwe no ara, ɔno, nye no nkowaa nyinara, nye Egyptfo nyinara: na su kɛse baa Egypt; osiandɛ fie biara nnyi hɔ a obi ennwu wɔ mu.
Na ɔfrɛɛ Moses nye Aaron anadwe, na ɔsee dɛ, Hom nsoɛr, hom mfi me man mu mfir, hom nye Israelmba no nyina; na hom nkɔ nkɔsom EWURADZE, dɛ mbrɛ hom aka no.
Hom mfa hom nguan nye hom anantwi so, dɛ mbrɛ hom aka no, na hom nkɔ; na hom nhyira mo so.
Na Egyptfo no piapiaa ɔman no dɛ wɔrepam hɔn ntsɛm efi asaase no do; na wɔsee dɛ, Hɛn nyinara ayɛ ewufo ara nye no.
Na ɔman no fefaa hɔn mbɔr ansaana ɔrekaw, hɔn mbɔrakorow no wɔakyekyer no wɔ hɔn atam mu sisi hɔn kɔn ho.
Na Israelmba no yɛɛ dɛ mbrɛ Moses kae no; na wobisabisaa dwetɛ ndwindze, nye sika ndwindze, nye atam wɔ Egyptfo hɔ: na EWURADZE maa ɔman no enyimpa wɔ Egyptfo no enyim, ma wɔmaa hɔn nsa kaa dza wobisae no.
Na wɔfoom Egyptfo egyapadze kɔree.
Israelmba No Fi Egypt Na Israelmba no sii mu fii Rameses kɔr Sukɔt, mbanyin ara a wɔnam famu bɛyɛ mpem ahaesia, a mbofraba nnka ho.
Na aforafora dɔm so nye hɔn kɔree; na nguan, na anantwi, mekyerɛ ofiembowa piigyan.
Na wɔdze mbɔr a wɔdze fi Egypt bae no totoo epitsi tatar, nna ɔnnkawee; osiandɛ wɔpaam hɔn fii Egypt ntsi, na woenntum enntsinntsim, nkyii so woennsiesie edzidzidze biara amma hɔnho.
Afei tsena a Israelmba dze tsenaa Egypt no yɛ mfe ahaanan eduasa.
Na ɔbaa dɛ mfe ahaanan eduasa no n’ewiei no, mekyerɛ da kor no ara, EWURADZE no dɔm nyinara tui fii Egypt asaase do.
Ɔyɛ anadwe a ɔwɔ dɛ wɔhyɛ no nsew ma EWURADZE dɛ oyii hɔn fii Egypt asaase do: iyi nye EWURADZE n’anadwe no a wɔhyɛ no nsew wɔ Israelmba nyinara mu wɔ hɔn ebusuasantsen nyina mu no.
Apaho No Ho Nhyehyɛɛ Na EWURADZE see Moses nye Aaron dɛ, Iyi nye apaho no ho mbra no: ɔnanaben biara nndzi bi: na nyimpa biara n’akowaa a ɔdze sika atɔ no no dze, sɛ etwa no twatsia a, ɔno ondzi bi.
Mma ɔmamforanyi nye akowaa ɔpaanyi nndzi bi.
Ofi kor mu na wondzi; mma mmfa nam no bi mmfi fie no mu mmpue; nkyii so mma hom mmbu ne biew bi.
Israel mboanofo nyinara ndzi do.
Na sɛ ɔhɔho bi bɛnye wo tsena, na ɔpɛ dɛ odzi apaho no ma EWURADZE a, ma wontwa ne mbarimba nyinara twatsia, na nkyii ɔntwe mbɛn na ombedzi; na ɔnyɛ dɛ nyia wɔawo no asaase no do: monomonomnyi biara dze mma onndzi bi.
Mbra kor na ɔnda hɔ mma nyia ɔyɛ okuromnyi, nye ɔhɔho a ɔtsena hom mu.
Na Israelmba nyinara yɛɛ dɛm; dɛ mbrɛ EWURADZE hyɛɛ Moses nye Aaron no, dɛmara so na wɔyɛe.
Na ɔbaa dɛ da kor no ara, EWURADZE yii Israelmba no fii Egypt asaase do dɛ mbrɛ hɔn dɔm tsetsee.
Wotu Mbakan Si Hɔ Ma EWURADZE Na EWURADZE kaa kyerɛɛ Moses dɛ, Tu mbakan nyinara si nkyɛn ma me, adze biara a obue yafun mu, wɔ Israelmba mu, wɔ onyimpa nye abowa mu nyinara; yɛ medze.
Epitsi Afahyɛ Na Moses see ɔman no dɛ, Hom nkaa da yi a hom dze fii Egypt firii, fii nkowaasom fi mu no; na nsa a ɔyɛ dzen na EWURADZE dze yii hom fii bea no do: mma wonndzi mbɔrkaw boodoo.
Ndɛ da yi na hom rifir edzi wɔ bosoom Abib mu.
Na ɔbɛba dɛ sɛ EWURADZE nya dze wo du Keenanfo, Hitifo, Amorifo, Hivifo, nye Jebusfo asaase a ɔkaa ho ntam kyerɛɛ w’egyanom dɛ ɔdze bɛma wo no, asaase a numfonsu nye ewo pem wɔ do no do a, ɔno som ɔsom yi wɔ bosoom yi mu.
Nda esuon na dzi epitsi boodoo, na da a otsia esuon no bɛyɛ afahyɛ ama EWURADZE.
Wondzi epitsi boodoo nda esuon no mu nyina; na mma wonnhu mbɔrkaw boodoo wɔ wo nkyɛn, nkyii so mma wonnhu mbɔrkaw wɔ wo nkyɛn, wɔ wo ntoaado nyinara mu.
Na da no kyerɛ mu kyerɛ wo ba dɛ, Osian dza EWURADZE yɛe maa me wɔ ber a mirifi Egypt aba no ntsi a. Na ɔbɛyɛ wo wo nsa do asɛnkyerɛdze, na w’enyiwa ntamu nkaadze, ama EWURADZE mbra no aako w’anomu: na nsa a ɔyɛ dzen na EWURADZE dze eyi wo efi Egypt.
Dɛm ntsi dzi mbra yi do wɔ ne ber mu afrenhyia daa.
Na ɔbɛba dɛ sɛ EWURADZE dze wo du Keenanfo asaase do, dɛ mbrɛ ɔkaa ntam kyerɛɛ ɔwo nye w’egyanom no, na ɔdze ma wo a, ɔno yi dza obue yafun mu nyinara si nkyɛn ma EWURADZE, na abakan biara a ewɔ a ofi abowa mu: enyin no nyɛ EWURADZE dze.
Na asoasopɔnkɔ abakan biara fa eguambaa sesa; na sɛ annsesa a, ɔno bu no kɔn mu; na nyimpa mbakan a wɔwɔ wo mbabanyin mu nyinara dze sesa gye hɔn.
Na ɔbɛba dɛ sɛ ndaamba bi wo ba bisa wo dɛ, Ebɛnadze nye yi a, ase no dɛ, Nsa a ɔyɛ dzen na EWURADZE dze yii hɛn fii Egypt, fii nkowaasom fi no mu.
Na ɔbaa dɛ, aber a nna Farao mmpen dɛ ɔbɛma yɛakɔ no, EWURADZE kunkum Egypt asaase do mbakan nyinara, nyimpa abakan, nye mbowa abakan nyina: dɛm ntsi na mo so medze enyin nyinara a wobue yafun mu no mobɔ EWURADZE afɔr; na me mbabanyin mu mbakan nyinara dze medze mbowa sesa gye hɔn.
Na ɔbɛyɛ wo nsa do asɛnkyerɛdze, nye w’enyiwa ntamu nkaadze: na nsa a ɔyɛ dzen na EWURADZE dze yii hɛn fii Egypt.
Ogya Na Mununkum Fadum Na ɔbaa dɛ, Farao maa ɔman no kwan no, Nyankopɔn ammfa hɔn annkɛfa Filistiafo asaase do kwan do, kaansa ɔno ɔbɛn mpo a; na Nyankopɔn see dɛ, Bi a bɛyɛ na ɔman no ekehyia ɔsa, na woenu hɔnho, na wɔasan akɔ Egypt: mbom Nyankopɔn dze ɔman no danee faa Mbɛw Po no ho sar do ɔkwan do; na Israelmba no miae fii Egypt asaase do kɔree.
Na Moses faa Josef mbiew no kaa no ho: osiandɛ ɔaka Israelmba ntam dɛ, Ampaara Nyankopɔn bɛba abɛsera hom; na hom mfa me mbiew nka hom ho mfi ha nkɔ.
Na wotuu hɔn kwan fii Sukɔt, na wɔkɛkyeer nsera wɔ Etam, wɔ sar no ano.
Na EWURADZE dzii hɔn enyim ewimbir wɔ mununkum dum mu, dɛ ɔrekyerɛ hɔn kwan; na anadwe wɔ gya dum mu, dɛ ɔrema hɔn kan; ama wɔaanantsew ewiaber nye anadwe: ewiaber mununkum dum no, nye anadwe gya dum no, wɔanntwe hɔnho emmfi ɔman no enyim.
Mbɛw Po No Ntwae Na EWURADZE kaa kyerɛɛ Moses dɛ, Ka kyerɛ Israelmba dɛ wɔnsan hɔn ekyir na wɔnkɛkyer nsera wɔ Pi-hahirot a wɔ Migidɔl nye Mbɛw po no ntamu na ɔbɛn Baal-zefon no enyim: ne tsentsendo na hom nkyer nsera no wɔ po no ne nkyɛn.
Na Farao bɛse wɔ Israelmba ho dɛ, Wɔatoto wɔ asaase no do, sar no atow hɔn mu.
Na mibepirim Farao n’akoma, na obetsiw hom; na mebɛhyɛ m’enyim nyam wɔ Farao nye no dɔm nyinara do; na Egyptfo bohu dɛ emi nye EWURADZE.
Na wɔyɛɛ dɛm.
Na wɔkaa kyerɛɛ Egypthen no dɛ ɔman no eguan kɔ: na Farao nye no nkowaa no hɔn akoma sakyeree wɔ ɔman no ho, na wɔsee dɛ, Ebɛnadze na yɛayɛ yi, dɛ yɛama Israel egyaa hɛn som kɔ yi?
Na ɔhyehyɛɛ ne tseaseanam, na ɔfaa ne man kaa no ho: na ɔfaa ntseaseanam a wɔasan mu eyi ahaesia, na Egypt ntseaseanam nyinara, na hɔn nyinara hɔn do asafohemfo.
Na EWURADZE piriim Egypthen Farao n’akoma, na otsiiw Israelmba no: na Israelmba no dze ahosɛpɛw kɛse fiir edzi kɔree.
Na Egyptfo tsiiw hɔn, Farao no mpɔnkɔ nye ne ntseaseanam nyinara, nye no mpɔnkɔdofo, nye no dɔm no, na wɔbɔtoo hɔn dɛ wɔakyer nsera wɔ po no ano, Pi-hahirot nkyɛn, wɔ Baal-zefon enyim.
Na aber a Farao bɛnee no, Israel memaa hɔn enyi do, na, hwɛ, Egyptfo etu dzi hɔn ekyir reba; na wosuroo dodow; na Israelmba no sui frɛɛ EWURADZE.
Na wɔsee Moses dɛ, Osiandɛ ndakamona nnyi Egypt ntsi, na eyi hɛn hɔ ma yerubowuwu wɔ sar do yi?
Ebɛnadze ntsi na enye hɛn edzi no dɛm yi, dɛ iyii hɛn fii Egypt bae yi?
Ana nnyɛ yi nye asɛm a yɛkaa kyerɛɛ wo wɔ Egypt no, dɛ, Gyaa hɛn ma yɛnsom Egyptfo no?
Osiandɛ nkyɛ obeye ama hɛn dɛ yɛbɔsom Egyptfo mbom sen dɛ yebowuwu wɔ sar do.
Na Moses see ɔman no dɛ, Mma hom nnsuro, hom ngyina dzinn, na hom nhwɛ EWURADZE no nkwagye a ɔrebɛyɛ akyerɛ hom ndɛ da yi: na Egyptfo a hom ehu hɔn ndɛ da yi, hom nnkohu hɔn bio dabiarada.
EWURADZE bɔko ama hom, na hom nka hom ano nto mu.
Na EWURADZE bisaa Moses dɛ, Ebɛnadze ntsi na isu frɛ me yi?
Kasa kyerɛ Israelmba, ma wɔnkɔ kan. Na ma wo poma no do, na tsen wo nsa wɔ po no do, na paa mu: na Israelmba nnantsew mfa po no ne finimfin wɔ daadze kɛsɛɛ do.
Na emi, hwɛ, mibepirim Egyptfo akoma, na wobedzi hom ekyir: na mebɛhyɛ m’enyim nyam wɔ Farao do, nye no mpɔnkɔdofo do.
Na Egyptfo no bohu dɛ emi nye EWURADZE, aber a mahyɛ m’enyim nyam wɔ Farao do, ne ntseaseanam do, nye no mpɔnkɔdofo do no.
Na Nyankopɔn no bɔfoe a odzi Israel nseraban enyim no, ɔtwee noho na okedzii hɔn ekyir; na mununkum dum no twee fii hɔn enyim, na okegyinaa hɔn ekyir: na ɔbaa Egypt nseraban no nye Israel nseraban no ntamu; na ɔyɛɛ mununkum nye sum, naaso ɔmaa kan anadwe: na kor ammba kor nkyɛn anadwe ne nyinara.
Na Moses tseen ne nsa wɔ po no do; na EWURADZE dze boka mframa dzendzen maa po no kɔr ekyir anadwe no nyinara, na ɔyɛɛ po no asaase kɛsɛɛ, na nsu no mu paae.
Na Israelmba no nantsewee faa po no ne finimfin wɔ daadze kɛsɛɛ no do: na nsu no yɛɛ hɔn fadum wɔ hɔn nsa enyimfa, nye hɔn abankum.
Na Egyptfo no tsiiw hɔn, na wodzii hɔn ekyir kɔr po no ne finimfin, Farao no mpɔnkɔ, ne ntseaseanam, nye no mpɔnkɔdofo nyinara.
Na ɔbaa dɛ anapa dasu mu no, EWURADZE nam ogya nye mununkum dum no mu hwɛɛ Egyptfo dɔm no, na ɔkaa Egyptfo dɔm no gui.
Na ohuhuaan hɔn ntseaseanam n’anan hwiir ma no ntwee mu yɛɛ dzen: ma dɛm ntsi Egyptfo no see dɛ, Hom mma yemfi Israel enyim nguan; osiandɛ EWURADZE roko tsia Egyptfo dze ma hɔn.
Na EWURADZE see Moses dɛ, Tsen wo nsa wɔ po no do, ma nsu no mbra bio wɔ Egyptfo do, hɔn ntseaseanam do, nye hɔn mpɔnkɔdofo do.
Na Moses tseen ne nsa wɔ po no do, na adze kyee anapa no po no saan n’ekyir peem dɛ mbrɛ ɔtse no ara, na Egyptfo guanee behyiaa no; na EWURADZE toow Egyptfo guu po no ne finimfin.
Na nsu no saan ekyir, na ɔbɛkataa ntseaseanam, nye mpɔnkɔdofo no, mekyerɛ Farao no dɔm a wodzii hɔn ekyir kɔr po no ne finimfin no nyinara do; hɔn mu kor mpo annka.
Na Israelmba no dze, wɔnantseew asaase kɛsɛɛ do wɔ po no ne finimfin; na nsu no yɛɛ fadum maa hɔn wɔ hɔn nsa enyimfa, nye hɔn abankum.
Mbrɛ EWURADZE sii gyee Israel nkwa da no fii Egyptfo nsamu nye no: na Israel hun Egyptfo no dɛ woewuwu gu po no ano.
Na Israel hun dwuma kɛse a EWURADZE dzii no wɔ Egyptfo do, na ɔman no suroo EWURADZE: na wɔgyee EWURADZE, nye n’akowaa Moses dzii.
Moses No Ndwom Na Moses nye Israelmba no toow ndwom yi maa EWURADZE, na wɔkaa dɛ, Mobɔtow ndwom ama EWURADZE, osiandɛ ɔama noho do enyimnyam mu: Ɔpɔnkɔ nye no do tsefo no ɔatow hɔn egu po mu.
EWURADZE nye m’ahoɔdzen nye mo ndwom, Na ɔabɛyɛ mo nkwagye: Oyi nye me Nyankopɔn, na mibeyi no ayɛw; M’egya ne Nyankopɔn a, na mubohuhor no.
EWURADZE yɛ ɔsabarimba: EWURADZE nye ne dzin.
Farao ne ntseaseanam nye no dɔm no ɔatow hɔn egu po mu: Na n’asafohemfo a wɔasan mu eyi no wɔamemem Mbɛw Po no mu.
Ebun akata hɔn do: Wɔamemem kɔ ase too dɛ ɔbo.
EWURADZE, wo nsa enyimfa yɛ tum mu onyimnyamfo, EWURADZE, wo nsa enyimfa dwerew ɔtamfo no.
Na w’abɔso akɛseyɛ no mu ara na edze butuw hɔn a wɔsoɛr tsia wo no: Ɔwo soma w’ebufuhyew ba, ɔhyew hɔn dɛ eburonan.
Na wo hwen mu ehuw mu na nsu no ano boae, Nsuyirii no gyinaa bantsenn dɛ kuw: Ebun no kyekyeer wɔ po akoma mu.
Ɔtamfo no see dɛ, Mibetsiw hɔn, mobɔto hɔn, mebɛkyɛ asadze no mu: Wɔbɛmee me kra; Mobɔtwe m’afona, me nsa bɛsɛɛ hɔn.
Ɔwo dze wo mframa huwii, epo no kataa hɔn do: Wɔmeem dɛ sumbui wɔ nsu kɛse no mu.
EWURADZE, woana na ɔtse dɛ ɔwo, wɔ enyame mu?
Woana na ɔtse dɛ ɔwo, krɔnkrɔnyɛ mu onyimnyamfo, Ayɛyi mu ɔhoyifo, anwanwadzeyɛfo?
Ɔwo tseen wo nsa enyimfa, Asaase meen hɔn.
Ɔwo wo mbɔbɔrhu mu na egya ɔman a apon hɔn no kwan: Ɔwo w’ahoɔdzen mu na egya hɔn akɔ wo tsenabew krɔnkrɔn no.
Aman atsetse, hɔn ho rihim: Ahopopo aka hɔn a wɔtse Filistia.
Nna Edom asafohen mpanyimfo bɔɔ hu; Moab akatakyi no, ahohim aka hɔn: Hɔn a wɔtse Keenan nyinara anan anan.
Nketsenketse nye suro ekitsa hɔn; W’abasa ne kɛseyɛ ntsi wɔayeyɛ dzindzinn dɛ ɔbo; Kodu dɛ wo man botwa mu, EWURADZE, Kodu dɛ wo man a enya hɔn no botwa mu.
Ɔwo dze hɔn bɛba, na abɛtsɛw hɔn wɔ w’egyapadze bepɔw no do, Bea a, EWURADZE, edze ayɛ wo tsenabew no a, Krɔnkrɔnbea a, EWURADZE, edze wo nsa dze etsim hɔ no a. EWURADZE bedzi hen daa.
Miriam No Ndwom Na Farao no mpɔnkɔ nye ne ntseaseanam na ɔnye no mpɔnkɔdofo na wɔkɔr po no mu, na EWURADZE maa po no mu nsu no sanee bɛkataa hɔn do; na Israelmba no dze wɔnantseew asaase kɛsɛɛ do wɔ po ne finimfin.
Na nkɔnhyɛnyi Miriam, Aaron n’akyerɛbaa no, faa mfuaba kitsae: na mbaa no nyinara dze mfuaba na ɔnye asaw puei dzii n’ekyir.
Na Miriam gyee hɔn do dɛ, Hom ntow ndwom mma EWURADZE, na oedzi konyim wɔ enyimnyam mu; Ɔpɔnkɔ nye no do tsefo no ɔatow hɔn egu po mu.
Na Moses gyaa Israel fii Mbɛw Po no ho kɔr kan, na wɔkɔr Sur sar do, na wɔnantseew sar no do ndaansa, na woennhu nsu.
Na wɔbaa Mara no, woenntum annom Mara nsu no bi, osiandɛ ɔyɛ wen: dɛm ntsi wɔfrɛɛ ne dzin Mara.
Na ɔman no hwinhwiin Moses ho dɛ, Ebɛnadze na yɛnnom?
Na osui frɛɛ EWURADZE; na EWURADZE kyerɛɛ no dua bi, na ɔtowee kyeen nsu no mu, na nsu no yɛɛ dɛw.
Hɔ na ɔhyɛɛ hɔn ahyɛdze nye mbra, na hɔ so na ɔsɔɔ hɔn hwɛe; na ɔsee dɛ, Sɛ ibetsie EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn ne ndze yie, na ayɛ dza ɔtsen wɔ n’enyiwa do, na ayɛ aso wɔ ne mbransɛm do, na edzi n’ahyɛdze nyinara do a, ɔnodze mennkɛfa yarba biara a medze megu Egyptfo do no bi megu wo do: na emi nye EWURADZE a ɔsa wo yarba no.
Na wɔbaa Elim, mbrɛ nsunyiwa duebien, nye mbɛdua eduosuon wɔ: na wɔkyeer nsera wɔ hɔ wɔ nsu no ho.
Maana Na Nkokɔhwerew Na wotui fii Elim, na Israel mboanofo no nyinara baa Sin sar a ɔda Elim nye Sinai ntamu no do, nna wofii Egypt asaase do no, no bosoom a otsia ebien no mu da a otsia duenum nye no.
Na Israelmba mboanofo man mu nyinara hwinhwiin Moses nye Aaron ho wɔ sar no do: na Israelmba no see hɔn dɛ, Mbom nkyɛ EWURADZE mma yenwuwu ne nsaano wɔ Egypt asaase do, aber a yɛtsetse nam nkutu ho no, aber a yedzi edziban mee no; osiandɛ hom dze hɛn efir edzi aba sar yi do, dɛ hom dze akɔmfun rubokuku mboanofo man mu yi nyinara.
Nna EWURADZE see Moses dɛ, Hwɛ, mebɛma edziban efi sor atɔ ama hom; na ɔman no befir edzi akɛtase dza ɔbɔso hɔn ano da kor wɔ ne da mu, ma maasɔ hɔn mahwɛ kyerɛ dɛ wobedzi me mbra do anaa wonnkedzi do.
Na ɔbɛba dɛ da a otsia esia no, wobesiesie dza wɔdze ba no, na ɔbɛyɛ dza wɔtase no daa no no mbɔho ebien.
Na Moses nye Aaron see Israelmba no nyinara dɛ, Ewimbir nna hom bohu dɛ EWURADZE eyi hom efi Egypt asaase do: na anapa nna hom bohu EWURADZE n’enyimnyam; osiandɛ ɔtse hom ehwinhwin a hom hwinhwin EWURADZE ho no: na hɛn dze, ebɛnadze nye hɛn, na hom hwinhwin hɛn ho?
Na Moses see dɛ, Iyi bɛba, EWURADZE bɛma hom nam ewimbir ma woeedzi, na edziban anapa ma wɔaamee, osiandɛ EWURADZE tse hom ehwinhwin a hom dze hwinhwin no ho: na ebɛnadze nye hɛn?
Nnyɛ hɛn ho na hom hwinhwin, mbom EWURADZE ho a. Na Moses see Aaron dɛ, Se Israelmba mboanofo no nyinara dɛ, Hom ntwe mpin EWURADZE enyim: na ɔatse hom ehwinhwin no.
Na ɔbaa dɛ Aaron rekasa kyerɛ Israelmba mboanofo nyinara no, wɔdandaan hɔn enyi kɔr sar no do, na hwɛ, EWURADZE enyimnyam puei wɔ mununkum no mu.
Na EWURADZE kaa kyerɛɛ Moses dɛ, Matse Israelmba ehwinhwin no: ka kyerɛ hɔn dɛ, Ewimbir hom bedzi nam, na anapa hom edzi edziban amee; na hom ehu dɛ emi nye EWURADZE hom Nyankopɔn.
Na ɔbaa dɛ ewimbir no Nkokɔhwerɛw bae, na wɔbɛkataa nseraban no do: na anapa no ɔbɔw tɔr nseraban no ho hyiae.
Na ɔbɔw a ɔtɔree no kɔr sor no, hwɛ, adze bi nkorkorba nketsenketse deda sar no enyi, nketsenketse dɛ famu ɔbɔsu kyenkyenee.
Na aber a Israelmba hunii no, wɔsesee hɔnho nkorkor dɛ, Ebɛnadze nye yi?
Osiandɛ wonnyim adze kor no.
Na Moses see hɔn dɛ, Iyi nye edziban a EWURADZE dze ama hom dɛ hom ndzi.
Iyi nye adze a EWURADZE ahyɛ, Hom ntase bi dɛ mbrɛ nyimpa biara n’edzidzi tse; olonka nkorkor, dɛ mbrɛ hom nyimpa dodow tse, nna hom mfefa, nyimpa biara mfa mma hɔn a wɔwɔ n’asesee mu no.
Na Israelmba no yɛɛ dɛm, na wɔtasee, binom dze so, binom dze suar.
Na wɔdze olonka susui no, nyia ɔtasee pii no oennya bi ammbor do, na nyia ɔtasee kumaabi no annka no bi: wɔtasee dɛ mbrɛ nyimpa biara n’edzidzi tse.
Na Moses see hɔn dɛ, Mma obi nngya bi ma adze nnkye do.
Naaso woenntsie Moses; mbom hɔn mu binom gyaa bi ma adze kyee do, na ɔdɔɔ mbowaba, na ɔbɔnee; na Moses no bo fuuw hɔn.
Na wɔtasee no anapa anapa, nyimpa biara dɛ mbrɛ n’edzidzi tse: na ewia ano yɛɛ dzen no, ɔnanee.
Na ɔbaa dɛ, da a otsia esia no wɔtasee edziban no mbɔho, ɔbaako dze yɛ olonka ebien: na mboanofo no mu mpanyimfo nyinara baa bɛkaa kyerɛɛ Moses.
Na ɔsee hɔn dɛ, Iyi nye dza EWURADZE aka no, Ɔkyena yɛ awɔse ahomgye, ahomgyeda krɔnkrɔn ma EWURADZE: hom nto dza hom bɔto, na hom nnoa dza hom bɔnoa; na dza ɔka no nyinara hom mfa nsie ma adze nkye do.
Na wɔdze siee ma okodur anapa, dɛ mbrɛ Moses hyɛe no: na ɔammbɔn, nkyii so abowaba bi nnyi mu.
Na Moses see dɛ, Hom ndzi ɔno ndɛ; na ndɛ ɔyɛ ahomgyeda ma EWURADZE: ndɛ hom nnkohu bi wɔ haban mu.
Nda esia na hom ntase; na da a otsia esuon no dze ɔyɛ ahomgyeda, ɔno mu bi nnkɛba hɔ.
Na ɔbaa dɛ da a otsia esuon no, ɔman no mu bi fiir edzi dɛ wɔrekɛtase, na woennhu bi.
Na EWURADZE see Moses dɛ, Hom ropow dɛ wodzi me mbransɛm nye me mbra do ma ekodu dabɛn?
Hom nhwɛ, osiandɛ EWURADZE ama hom ahomgyeda ntsi, na da a otsia esia no ɔma hom nda ebien edziban: hom mu nyimpa biara ntsena ne tsenabew, mma obiara mmfir edzi mmfi ne tsenabew wɔ da a otsia esuon no mu.
Nna ɔman no hoom da a otsia esuon no.
Na Israel fi frɛɛ ne dzin Manna: nna ɔtse dɛ wusa aba, fitaa, na ne dɛw tse dɛ tatar ntrɛtraba a wɔdze ewo ayɛ.
Na Moses see dɛ, Iyi nye adze a EWURADZE ahyɛ, Wɔmfa bi nhyɛ esusudze olonka ma mfa nsie hom ebusuasantsen; ama woeehu edziban a medze menyɛɛn hom wɔ sar no do, aber a miyii hom fii Egypt asaase do no.
Na Moses see Aaron dɛ, Fa kutu bi, na fa manna esusudze olonka kor gu mu, na fa si EWURADZE enyim, ma wɔmfa nsie hom ebusuasantsen.
Dɛ mbrɛ EWURADZE hyɛɛ Moses no, dɛmara so na Aaron dze sii Adasehyɛdze no enyim, ma wɔdze eesie.
Na Israelmba dzii manna no mfe eduanan, dze kodur dɛ wɔbaa asaase a nyimpa tse do do; wodzii manna no, dze kodur dɛ wɔbaa Keenan asaase no ntoaado.
Afei esusudze olonka yɛ efa mu ebupɛn du mu kor.
Nsu Fi Bobaa Mu Ba Na Israelmba mboanofo no nyinara tui fii Sin sar no do, wɔ hɔn akwantu mu, dɛ mbrɛ EWURADZE mbrasɛm tse, na wɔkɛkyekyeer nsera wɔ Refidim: na nsu nnyi hɔ mma ɔman no dɛ wɔbɔnom.
Dɛm ntsi ɔman no nye Moses hamee, na wɔsee dɛ, Ma hɛn nsu ma yɛnnom.
Na Moses see hɔn dɛ, Ebɛnadze ntsi na hom nye me reham?
Ebɛnadze ntsi na hom rosɔ EWURADZE ahwɛ yi?
Na nsukɔm dzee ɔman no wɔ hɔ; na ɔman no hwinhwiin Moses ho, na wɔsee dɛ, Ebɛnadze ntsi na iyii hɛn fii Egypt bae, dɛ edze nsukɔm ruboku hɛn nye hɛn mba nye hɛn mbowa yi?
Na Moses sui frɛɛ EWURADZE see dɛ, Ebɛnadze na menyɛ memma ɔman yi?
Aka kakra ma woeesiw me abo.
Na EWURADZE see Moses dɛ, Pa ho kedzi ɔman no enyim, na fa Israel mpanyin no bi ka woho; na wo poma a edze bɔɔ esutsen no, fa kitsa wo nsamu, na kɔ.
Hwɛ, mibegyina w’enyim wɔ hɔ wɔ Horeb ɔbotan no do; na bɔ ɔbotan no, na nsu befi mu aba, ma ɔman no aanom.
Na Moses yɛɛ dɛm wɔ Israel mpanyin no enyim.
Na ɔfrɛɛ bea no ne dzin Massa, nye Meriba, osian Israelmba hɔn ham no ntsi, na EWURADZE a wɔsɔɔ no hwɛe see dɛ, Ana EWURADZE wɔ hɛn mu, anaa onnyi mu ntsi a?
Israel nye Amalek Ko Nna Amalek bae, na ɔnye Israel bɔkoe wɔ Refidim.
Na Moses see Josua dɛ, San mu yiyi mbanyin ma hɛn, na fir edzi kɔ, nye Amalek nkɔko: ɔkyena medze Nyankopɔn poma no bekitsa me nsamu mekegyina koko no etsifi.
Nna Josua yɛɛ dɛ mbrɛ Moses see no no, na ɔnye Amalek kɔkoe: na Moses, Aaron, nye Hur fowee kɔr koko no etsifi.
Na ɔbaa dɛ, sɛ Moses ma ne nsa do a, nna Israel edzi nyim: na sɛ ɔto ne nsa famu a, nna Amalek edzi nyim.
Na Moses ne nsa gyenee; na wɔfaa ɔbo, na wɔdze too n’ase, na ɔtsenaa do; na Aaron nye Hur susuoo ne nsamu gyinae, ɔbaako dze afa, na ɔbaako so dze afa so; na ne nsa gyinaa dzinn kodur witɔree.
Na Josua dwereew Amalek nye ne man afona ano.
Na EWURADZE see Moses dɛ, Kyerɛw iyi wɔ nwoma mu fa yɛ nkaa, na ka hyɛ Josua n’asomu: dɛ pepa ara na mebɛpepa Amalek ho nkaa mefi ɔsor ase.
Na Moses sii afɔrmbukyia, na ɔfrɛɛ ne dzin Yahweh-nissi, (a ase nye, EWURADZE nye me frankaa), na ɔsee dɛ, EWURADZE esua: EWURADZE nye Amalek bedzi ako fi ebusuasantsen do ekodu ebusuasantsen do.
Jetro Kɛsera Moses Afei Jetro, Midian ɔsɔfo no, Moses n’asew no, tsee dza Nyankopɔn ayɛ ama Moses, nye ne man Israel no nyinara, mbrɛ EWURADZE esi eyi Israel efi Egypt.
Na Jetro, Moses n’asew no, faa Zipora, Moses yer a ɔama ɔasan kɔ no, nye ne mbabanyin beenu a ɔbaako ne dzin dze Gersom; osiandɛ ɔkaa dɛ, Mayɛ amanandze hɔho: na kor no so ne dzin dze Eliezer, osiandɛ ɔsee dɛ, M’egya ne Nyankopɔn yɛɛ mo mboa, na oyii me fii Farao n’afona anomu: na Jetro, Moses n’asew no, dze ne mbabanyin no nye ne yer no baa Moses nkyɛn wɔ sar no do mbrɛ ɔkɛkyeer nsera no, wɔ Nyankopɔn bepɔw no ho: na ɔsee Moses dɛ, Emi w’asew Jetro, nye wo yer, nye wo mbabanyin beenu no ka no ho, aba wo nkyɛn.
Na Moses fiir edzi kehyiaa n’asew, na ɔkotowee, na ɔfeew n’ano; na wobisabisaa hɔn apɔwmu; na wɔbaa asese mu.
Na Moses kaa dza osian Israel ntsi EWURADZE dze ayɛ Farao nye Egyptfo nyinara kyerɛɛ n’asew, awoko a ɔbaa hɔn do wɔ ɔkwan no mu nyinara, na mbrɛ EWURADZE sii yii hɔn no.
Na Jetro dzii dɛw wɔ papa a EWURADZE ayɛ ama Israel, wɔ dɛ oyii hɔn fii Egyptfo nsamu no nyinara ho.
Na Jetro see dɛ, Nhyira nka EWURADZE a oeyi hom efi Egyptfo nsamu, na woefi Farao nsamu; ɔno a oeyi ɔman no efi Egyptfo nsaadze.
Afei na mehu dɛ EWURADZE yɛ kɛse kyɛn enyame nyinara: nyew, adze a wɔdze dzi hɔn do nkontompɔsɛm no ara mu a. Na Jetro, Moses n’asew no, faa ɔhyew afɔr nye okum afɔr kɛmaa Nyankopɔn: na Aaron nye Israel mpanyin nyinara baa dɛ wɔnye Moses n’asew no ribedzidzi wɔ Nyankopɔn enyim.
Moses Yi Atsɛmbuafo Na ɔbaa dɛ adze kyee no, Moses tsenaa famu dɛ orubu ɔman no atsɛn: na ɔman no gyinaa Moses do tsentsen fi anapa kodur ewimbir.
Na aber a Moses n’asew hun dza ɔyɛe maa ɔman no nyinara no, ɔsee dɛ, Ebɛnadze na ereyɛ ma ɔman yi?
Ɔyɛ dɛn ntsi na woara nko etse hɔ, na ɔman no nyinara gyinagyina wo do tsentsen fi anapa ebodu ewimbir yi?
Na Moses see n’asew no dɛ, Osiandɛ ɔman no ba me nkyɛn Nyankopɔn hɔ ebisa: sɛ wonya asɛm bi a, wɔba me nkyɛn; na mubu nyimpa nye ne nyɛnko ntamu atsɛn, na mema wohu Nyankopɔn n’ahyɛdze, nye ne mbra.
Na Moses n’asew no see no dɛ, Adze a eyɛ yi onnye.
Ampa ebɛberɛ, ɔwo nye ɔman a wɔka wo ho yi nyina, osiandɛ adze no yɛ dur dodow ma wo; ɔwo woara nko irunntum nnyɛ.
Afei tsie me ndze, mebɛma wo apam, na Nyankopɔn ndzi w’ekyir; ɔwo gyina Nyankopɔn afamu ma ɔman no, na fa nsɛm no brɛ Nyankopɔn: na kyerɛkyerɛ hɔn ahyɛdze no nye mbra no, na ma wonhu ɔkwan kor a ɔwɔ dɛ wɔnantsew mu, na edwuma a ɔwɔ dɛ wɔyɛ.
Afei so yiyi ɔman no nyinara mu mbanyin a wotum a wosuro Nyankopɔn a wɔyɛ anokwafo a wokyir enyikaber, na fa hɔn sisi hɔn do, ma wɔnyɛ apem apem do mpanyin, ɔha ɔha do mpanyin, eduonum eduonum do mpanyin, nye du du do mpanyin; na ma wombu ɔman no ntsɛn aber nyinara mu: na ɔmbra dɛ asɛnkɛse biara dze wɔmfa mbrɛ wo, na nsɛnketseaba nyinara dze, hɔnara wondzi: ama aayɛ wo do har, na wɔnye wo aasoa adzesoa no.
Sɛ eyɛ dɛm adze yi, na Nyankopɔn hyɛ wo dɛm a, ɔno na ibotum asɔw, na ɔman yi nyinara so bɔkɔ hɔn tsenabew dwudwoodwo.
Nna Moses tsiee n’asew ne ndze, na ɔyɛɛ dza ɔsee no nyinara.
Na Moses yiyii Israel nyinara mu nyimpa a wotum, na ɔyɛɛ hɔn etsitsir wɔ ɔman no do, apem apem do mpanyin, ɔha ɔha do mpanyin, eduonum eduonum do mpanyin, nye du du do mpanyin.
Na wobuu ɔman no ntsɛn aber nyinara mu: nsɛm a ɔyɛ dzen no wɔdze brɛɛ Moses, na nsɛnketseaba dze hɔnara wodzii.
Na Moses gyaa n’asew no kwan; na ɔfaa no kwan kɔr nankasa n’asaase do.
Israelmba No Ba Sinai Bosoom a otsia ebiasa a Israelmba sii mu fii Egypt asaase do no, da no ara na wɔbaa Sinai sar do.
Na aber a wotui fii Refidim, na wɔbaa Sinai sar do no, wɔkyeer nsera wɔ sar no do; na hɔ na Israel kyeer nsera wɔ bepɔw no enyim.
Na Moses fowee kɔr Nyankopɔn nkyɛn, na EWURADZE fii bepɔw no do frɛɛ no see dɛ, Dɛm na se Jakob fi, na ka kyerɛ Israelmba; Hom ehu dza medze mayɛ Egyptfo, na mbrɛ mosoaa hom nkɔr ntsaban do, na medze hom baa mara me nkyɛn.
Dɛm ntsi afei, sɛ hom betsie me ndze ara ampa, na woedzi m’ahyɛmu do a, ɔnodze, hom bɛyɛ egyapadze a ɔsom bo efi aman nyinara mu ama me: osiandɛ asaase nyinara yɛ medze: na hom bɛyɛ asɔfo ahendzi, nye ɔman krɔnkrɔn ama me.
Iyinom nye nsɛm a fa ka kyerɛ Israelmba no.
Na Moses bae na ɔbɛfrɛɛ ɔman mpanyimfo no, na ɔdze nsɛm yi a EWURADZE dze hyɛɛ no nyinara too hɔn enyim.
Na ɔman no nyinara bɔɔ mu buae, na wɔsee dɛ, Dza EWURADZE aka nyinara, yɛbɛyɛ.
Na Moses kɛkaa ɔman no hɔn nsɛm no kyerɛɛ EWURADZE.
Na EWURADZE see Moses dɛ, Hwɛ, mereba wo nkyɛn wɔ mununkum kebii mu, ama sɛ menye wo kasa a ɔman no aatse, na eso wɔaagye wo edzi daa.
Na Moses kaa ɔman no hɔn nsɛm no kyerɛɛ EWURADZE.
Na EWURADZE see Moses dɛ, Kɔ ɔman no nkyɛn, na tsew hɔn ho ndɛ nye ɔkyena, na ma wɔnhohor hɔn ntar, na wonsiesie hɔnho nsie da a otsia ebiasa no: na da a otsia ebiasa no EWURADZE besian wɔ ɔman no nyinara enyim aba bepɔw Sinai do.
Na bɔ ɔman no ho ɔheban hyia, se dɛ, Hom nhwɛ homho yie, ma hom aammfow bepɔw no, anaa hom annkɛka ne he: obiara a ɔbɛka bepɔw no oku na woboku no: nsa biara nnka no, mbom abo na wonsiw no, anaa tow na wɔntow no ma onhwira mu; sɛ abowa o, nyimpa o, orinnya nkwa: sɛ abɛn no hɛn kyɛr a, wɔmfow bepɔw no.
Na Moses sianee fi bepɔw no do kɔr ɔman no nkyɛn, na ɔtseew ɔman no ho; na wɔhohoor hɔn ntar.
Na ɔsee ɔman no dɛ, Hom nsiesie homho nsie da a otsia ebiasa no: mma wɔnnkɔ ɔbaa biara ho.
Na ɔbaa dɛ da a otsia ebiasa no, anapa no, asenaman nye enyinam, nye mununkum kebii baa bepɔw no do, na abɛn ndze dzendzen mbordo; na ɔman a wɔwɔ nseraban no mu nyinara ho popoe.
Na Moses dze ɔman no fir edzi fii nseraban no mu dɛ worikehyia Nyankopɔn; na wokegyinagyinaa bepɔw no ase afamu.
Na bepɔw Sinai no nyinara rupun wusiw, osiandɛ EWURADZE nam gya mu sianee baa do: na no wusiw no tui kɔr sor dɛ fononoo mu wusiw, na bepɔw no nyinara wosoow kɛsenara.
Na abɛn no ne ndze yɛɛ dzendzenndzen dodow no, Moses kasae, na Nyankopɔn dze ndze gyee no do.
Na EWURADZE sianee baa bepɔw Sinai do, wɔ bepɔw no etsifi: na EWURADZE frɛɛ Moses dɛ ɔnkɔ bepɔw no etsifi: na Moses fowee kɔree.
Na EWURADZE see Moses dɛ, Sian famu behyia ɔman no, amma wɔaanntsetsew mu ammba EWURADZE nkyɛn ammbɔhwɛ, ma hom mu pii aanntotɔ.
Na ma asɔfo no so a wɔba EWURADZE nkyɛn no ntsew hɔnho, amma EWURADZE eenntu annhyɛ hɔn do.
Na Moses see EWURADZE dɛ, Ɔman no runntum mmfow mmba bepɔw Sinai do: osiandɛ woara hyɛɛ hɛn dɛ, Bɔ bepɔw no ho ɔheban hyia, na tsew ho.
Na EWURADZE see no dɛ, Kɔ, sian famu; na fow bra, ɔwo, nye Aaron ka wo ho: na mma asɔfo no nye ɔman no nntsetsew mu mmfow mmba EWURADZE nkyɛn, amma oeenntu annhyɛ hɔn do.
Nna Moses sianee kɔr ɔman no nkyɛn, na ɔkɛkaa kyerɛɛ hɔn.
Mbrasɛm Du No Na Nyankopɔn kaa nsɛm yi nyinara, see dɛ, Emi nye EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn a miyii wo wɔ Egypt asaase do, wɔ nkowaasom fi mu no.
Mma nnya enyame fofor nnka mo ho.
Mma nnyɛ ohonyi bi, anaa adze a ɔwɔ wimu wɔ sor, anaa dza ɔwɔ asaase do wɔ famu, anaa dza ɔwɔ nsu mu wɔ asaase ase, ne saso mma woho: mma mmbɔ wo mu adze mma hɔn, na nnsom hɔn: na emi EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn meyɛ Nyame nyinkufo a medze egyanom hɔn emumuyɛ bɔhwɛ mba, ekodu ebusuasantsen ebiasa nye anan a wɔtan me do; na muhu mpempem a wɔdɔ me na wodzi me mbransɛm do mbɔbɔr.
Mma mmbɔ EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn dzin gyangyan, na EWURADZE nnkɛma nyia no a ɔbɔ ne dzin gyangyan afa noho tɔtrɔtɔ.
Kaa ahomgyeda no na sie no krɔnkrɔn.
Nda esia na yɛ edwuma, na dzi wo dwuma nyinara: na da a otsia esuon no yɛ EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn ahomgyeda: mma nnyɛ edwuma biara wɔ mu, ɔwo o, wo babanyin o, wo babaa o, w’akowaa o, w’afonabaa o, wo mbowa o, wo hɔho a ɔwɔ wo kuropon mu o: na nda esia na EWURADZE bɔɔ sor nye asaase, po, nye dza ɔwɔ mu nyinara, na ɔhoom da a otsia esuon no: dɛm ntsi na EWURADZE hyiraa ahomgyeda no, na ɔyɛɛ no krɔnkrɔn.
Dzi w’egya nye wo na nyi: ama wo nda aawar wɔ asaase a EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn dze rema wo no do.
Mma nndzi ewu.
Mma nnto awar.
Mma nnwia adze.
Mma nngye wo nyɛnko ho dasewia.
Mma w’enyi mmber wo nyɛnko fi, mma w’enyi mmber ne yer, anaa n’akowaa, anaa n’afonabaa, anaa ne nantwi, anaa n’asoaso, anaa biribiara a ɔyɛ wo nyɛnko dze.
Suro Ka Ɔman No Na aber a ɔman no nyinara hun asenaman no, nye enyinam no, nye bepɔw a orupun wusiw no, na wɔtsee abɛn ndze no, hɔn ho popoe, na wokegyinaa ekyirekyir.
Na wɔsee Moses dɛ, Woara nye hɛn nkasa, na yebetsie: na mma Nyankopɔn nnye hɛn nnkasa, ɔno yebowuwu.
Na Moses see ɔman no dɛ, Mma hom nnsuro: na Nyankopɔn aba dɛ ɔrobɔsɔ hom ahwɛ, ama no ho suro aaba hom enyi do, ma hom aannyɛ bɔn.
Na ɔman no gyinaa ekyirekyir, na Moses twee bɛɛn sum kadoo no mbrɛ Nyankopɔn wɔ no.
Afɔrmbukyia Ho Mbra Na EWURADZE see Moses dɛ, Mbrɛ se Israelmba nye yi, Homara hom ehu dɛ mifi ɔsor na menye hom akasa.
Mma hom nnyɛ me saso enyame bi mma hom ho; dwetɛ enyame, anaa sika enyame o, mma hom nnyɛ.
Dɛtse afɔrmbukyia na yɛ ma me, na dze wo hyew afɔr, nye w’asomdwee afɔr, wo nguan, nye w’anantwi no bɔ do afɔr: beebiara a mebɛma wɔakaa me dzin no, mebɛba wo nkyɛn na mebehyira wo.
Na sɛ ereyɛ abo afɔrmbukyia ama me: mma mmfa abo a woetwa nnsia osiandɛ sɛ ema w’edwindadze do bɔ do a, egu ho fi.
Nkyii so mma mmfow atwer nnkɔ afɔrmbukyia do, amma w’adagyaw aannda edzi wɔ do.
Nkowaa Ho Mbra Na iyinom nye ntsɛmbusɛm a fa to hɔn enyim.
Sɛ etɔ akowaa a ɔyɛ Hebriwnyi a, mfe esia na ɔnsom: na dza otsia esuon no mu ɔmfa no ho ndzi nkɔ kwa.
