Na mma wonngu Israelmba hɔn ndzɛmba krɔnkrɔn a wɔdze brɛ EWURADZE no ho fi; amma wɔaannsoa asodzi ho mbusu biara, sɛ wodzi hɔn ndzɛmba krɔnkrɔn no a: na emi nye EWURADZE a metsew hɔn ho no.
Na EWURADZE kasaa kyerɛɛ Moses dɛ, Kasa kyerɛ Aaron, nye ne mbabanyin no, nye Israelmba nyinara, na se hɔn dɛ, Obiara a ofi Israel ofi mu no, anaa ofi Israel mu ahɔho mu a ɔdze n’ayɛyɛdze ba, dɛ hɔn anohobadze mu biara, anaa hɔn ayamuyi afɔr mu biara a wɔdze brɛ EWURADZE bɔbɔ ɔhyew afɔr no; nyɛ onyin a onndzii dzɛm; anantwi mu o, nkɔsɔw mu o, anaa mpɔnkye mu o ama aasɔ enyi ama hom.
Mbom adze biara a odzi dzɛm no, mma hom mmfa mmba: na ɔrennyɛ enyisɔdze mma hom.
Na obiara a ɔdze asomdwee afɔr bɛbrɛ EWURADZE dɛ ɔdze rehyɛ anohoba ma, anaa ɔdze reyɛ ayamuyi afɔr no, ofi anantwikuw anaa nguankuw mu no, ɔmma ondzi mu na aasɔ enyi; dzɛm biara nnyi no ho.
Dza n’enyi efura, anaa oebubu, anaa oepira, anaa ɔahohon, anaa ntwem anaa ase egu no ho no, mma hom mmfa iyinom mmbrɛ EWURADZE, na mma mmfa hɔn mu bi mmbɔ ogya afɔr so wɔ afɔrmbukyia no do mma EWURADZE.
Na ɔnantwisaa anaa eguambaa a no ho biribi bor do anaa ɔtɔ sin wɔ ne beebi no, ayamuyi afɔr no fa no bɔ; na ɔyɛ anohobadze a ɔronnsɔ enyi.
Dza no ntɔhwɛbo ebubu, anaa adwerew, anaa abɔ, anaa etwa no, mma hom mmfa mmbrɛ EWURADZE; nkyii so mma hom nnyɛ dɛm wɔ hom asaase do.
Eso mma hom nngye iyinom mu biara wɔ ɔnanaben bi nsamu mmfa nnyɛ hom Nyankopɔn edziban mmba; osiandɛ hɔn sɛɛ wɔ hɔn ho, dzɛm bi wɔ hɔn ho: wɔrennyɛ enyisɔdze mma hom.
Na EWURADZE kasaa kyerɛɛ Moses dɛ, Sɛ wɔwo nantwisaa, ɔkɔsɔw, anaa apɔnkye, a, ɔno ɔnko ne na n’ase nda esuon; na ofi da a otsia awɔtwe no dze rokɔ no, ɔsɔ enyi dɛ ogya afɔr ayɛyɛdze ma EWURADZE.
Na sɛ ɔnantwiber o, oguamber o, mma hom nnku ɔno nye ne ba nyina da kor.
Na sɛ hom bɔ aseda afɔr ma EWURADZE a, hom mbɔ ma ɔnsɔ enyi mma hom.
Da no ara na wondzi; mma hom nngya mu bi mma adze nkye do: emi nye EWURADZE.
Dɛm ntsi hom nsie me mbra, na wondzi do: emi nye EWURADZE.
Na mma hom nngu me dzin krɔnkrɔn no ho fi: na mo ho bɛtsew wɔ Israelmba mu: emi nye EWURADZE a metsew hom ho no a medze hom fi Egypt asaase do bae, dɛ mebɛyɛ hom Nyankopɔn no: emi nye EWURADZE.
Afahyɛ Ahorow Na EWURADZE kasaa kyerɛɛ Moses dɛ, Kasa kyerɛ Israelmba, na se hɔn dɛ, EWURADZE n’afahyɛ a wɔahyehyɛ a, hom mpaa mu dɛ ɔyɛ nhyiamu krɔnkrɔn no, mekyerɛ iyinom nye m’afahyɛ a mahyehyɛ.
Nda esia na wɔnyɛ edwuma: na da a otsia esuon no yɛ ahomgye mu ahomgyeda, nhyiamu krɔnkrɔn a; mma hom nnyɛ edwuma biara: ɔyɛ ahomgyeda ma EWURADZE wɔ hom tsenabew nyina.
Iyinom nye EWURADZE n’afahyɛ a wɔahyehyɛ, mekyerɛ nhyiamu krɔnkrɔn a hom mpaa wɔ ne mber a wɔahyɛ mu no.
Bosoom a odzi kan no ne da a otsia duanan no n’ewimbir no yɛ EWURADZE apaho.
Na bosoom no ara mu da a otsia duenum no yɛ EWURADZE epitsi afahyɛ: nda esuon na hom ndzi epitsi.
Da a odzi kan no nyɛ nhyiamu krɔnkrɔn: mma hom nnyɛ edwumadzen biara.
Mbom hom mbɔ ogya afɔr mma EWURADZE nda esuon: da a otsia esuon no yɛ nhyiamu krɔnkrɔn; mma hom nnyɛ edwumadzen biara.
Na EWURADZE kasaa kyerɛɛ Moses dɛ, Kasa kyerɛ Israelmba, na se hɔn dɛ, Sɛ hom du asaase a medze rema hom no do, na wotwa no do ndɔbaa a, ɔno hom mfa hom ndɔbaa mu nduadzewakan no ifi mbrɛ ɔsɔfo no: na ɔntow ifi no wɔ EWURADZE enyim, ma ɔnsɔ enyi mma hom: ahomgyeda no n’adzekyee na ɔsɔfo no ntow.
Na da a hom tow ifi no, hom mfa eguambaanyin a onndzii dzɛm a oedzi afrenhyia mbɔ ɔhyew afɔr mma EWURADZE.
Na no ho edziban afɔr nyɛ isiam pa efa ebupɛn du mu ebien a wɔdze ngo afrɔw, ogya afɔr a oyi nka huanhuam ma EWURADZE: na no ho nom afɔr nyɛ wenyin, hin ebupɛn anan mu kor.
Na mma hom nndzi boodoo, anaa eburow totoe, anaa nomanoma, kɛpem dɛ hom dze hom Nyankopɔn ayɛyɛdze no bɛba ana: ɔyɛ daa ahyɛdze wɔ hom ebusuasantsen mu wɔ hom tsenabew nyinara mu.
Na hom mfitsi ahomgyeda no n’adzekyee nkan nda, mfa mfi da a hom dze ɔtow afɔr ifi baa no do; ma ahomgyeda esuon nwie du: hom nkan adaduenum ma onkesi ahomgyeda a otsia esuon no n’adzekyee; na hom mfa edziban afɔr fofor mbrɛ EWURADZE.
Hom mfa efa (efah) ebupɛn du mu ebien nyɛ ntɔwntɔwmu mfi hom tsenabew mbra: ɔnyɛ isiam pa, wɔmfa mbɔrkaw nto, ma ɔnyɛ nduadzewakan mma EWURADZE.
Na hom mfa nguambaa esuon a wonndzii dzɛm a woedzi afrenhyia afrenhyia, nye ɔnantwisaa eburwa kor, nye nguannyin ebien nka boodoo no ho mbra: wɔnyɛ ɔhyew afɔr mma EWURADZE, mfa nka hɔn edziban afɔr, nye hɔn ɔnom afɔr ho, mekyerɛ ogya afɔr a oyi nka huanhuam ma EWURADZE.
Na hom mfa apɔnkyenyin kor mbɔ ho afɔr, nye nguambaanyin ebien a woedzi afrenhyia afrenhyia mbɔ asomdwee afɔr.
Na ɔsɔfo no ntow hɔn nye nduadzewakan boodoo no nyɛ ɔtow afɔr wɔ EWURADZE enyim, nka nguambaa ebien no ho: ɔnyɛ krɔnkrɔn mma EWURADZE mfa mma ɔsɔfo no.
Na hom mbɔ dawur da no ara; ɔnyɛ nhyiamu krɔnkrɔn mma hom: mma hom nnyɛ edwumadzen biara: ɔyɛ daa ahyɛdze wɔ hom tsenabew nyinara mu wɔ hom ebusuasantsen mu.
Na sɛ hom twa hom asaase do ndɔbaa a, mma nntwa hanoa dze no korakora, nkyii so mma nndzi wo ndɔbaa no mpɛpɛw: gya no hɔ fa ma ohianyi, nye ɔhɔho: emi nye EWURADZE hom Nyankopɔn.
Na EWURADZE kasaa kyerɛɛ Moses dɛ, Kasa kyerɛ Israelmba dɛ, Bosoom a otsia esuon no ne da a odzi kan no, nyɛ ahomgye pa mma hom; wɔnhɛn totorobɛnto nyɛ nkaa, nhyiamu krɔnkrɔn.
Mma hom nnyɛ edwumadzen biara: na hom mbɔ ogya afɔr, mma EWURADZE.
Na EWURADZE kasaa kyerɛɛ Moses dɛ, Naaso bosoom a otsia esuon yi ara ne da a otsia du no nye mpata da: ɔnyɛ nhyiamu krɔnkrɔn mma hom, na hom mbrɛ homho adze; na hom mbɔ ogya afɔr mma EWURADZE.
Na mma hom nnyɛ edwuma biara wɔ no ara mu: na ɔyɛ mpata da, ma wɔaapata ama hom wɔ EWURADZE hom Nyankopɔn enyim.
Na obiara a ɔnnkɛbrɛ noho adze da no ara mu no, wobotwa no efi ne man mu akyen.
Na obiara a ɔyɛ edwuma biara wɔ dɛm da no ara mu no, wɔbɛsɛɛ no efi ne man mu.
Mma hom nnyɛ edwuma biara: ɔyɛ daa ahyɛdze wɔ hom ebusuasantsen mu wɔ hom tsenabew nyinara.
Ɔnyɛ ahomgye pa mu ahomgyeda mma hom, na hom mbrɛ hom akra adze: bosoom no ne da a otsia akron no n’ewimbir, ofi ewimbir kodu ewimbir, na hom ndzi hom ahomgyeda no.
Na EWURADZE kasaa kyerɛɛ Moses dɛ, Kasa kyerɛ Israelmba dɛ, Bosoom a otsia esuon no yi ara ne da a otsia duenum no ɔyɛ ntamadan afahyɛ nda esuon ma EWURADZE.
Da a odzi kan no yɛ nhyiamu krɔnkrɔn: mma hom nnyɛ edwumadzen biara.
Nda esuon na hom mbɔ ogya afɔr mma EWURADZE: da a otsia awɔtwe no nyɛ nhyiamu krɔnkrɔn mma hom; na hom mbɔ ogya afɔr mma EWURADZE: ɔyɛ nguabɔ ewiei; mma hom nnyɛ edwumadzen biara.
Iyinom nye EWURADZE n’afahyɛ a wɔahyehyɛ a hom mpaa mu dɛ ɔyɛ nhyiamu krɔnkrɔn no, ma wɔmfa ogya afɔr mbrɛ EWURADZE, ɔhyew afɔr, nye edziban afɔr, okum afɔr, nye ɔnom afɔr, kor wɔ nankasa ne da mu: ɔsor EWURADZE n’ahomgyeda no, na ɔsor hom ayɛyɛdze, na ɔsor hom anohoba, na ɔsor hom ayamuyi afɔr nyinara a hom dze ma EWURADZE no.
Naaso bosoom a otsia esuon no ne da a otsia duenum no mu, sɛ hom roboaboa asaase no do nduadzewa ano a, hom nhyɛ EWURADZE fa no nda esuon: da a odzi kan no nyɛ ahomgye pa, na da a otsia awɔtwe no nyɛ ahomgye pa. Na da a odzi kan no hom mfa ndua fɛɛfɛw do nduadzewa, nye menankɔnson, nye ndua wusuww n’abaw, nye esukɔn do ndua; na hom enyi ngye wɔ EWURADZE hom Nyankopɔn enyim nda esuon.
Na hom nhyɛ no fa mma EWURADZE nda esuon wɔ afrenhyia mu: ɔyɛ daa ahyɛdze wɔ hom ebusuasantsen mu: bosoom a otsia esuon no mu na hom nhyɛ.
Hom ntsenatsena asese mu nda esuon; hɔn a wɔyɛ amamba wɔ Israel nyinara ntsenatsena asese mu: ama hom ebusuasantsen eehu dɛ emi na memaa Israelmba tsenatsenaa asese mu wɔ aber a miyii hɔn fii Egypt asaase do no: emi nye EWURADZE hom Nyankopɔn.
Na Moses kaa EWURADZE n’afahyɛ a wɔahyehyɛ no kyerɛɛ Israelmba.
Nkandzea No Do Nhwɛe Na EWURADZE kasaa kyerɛɛ Moses dɛ, Hyɛ Israelmba ma wɔmbrɛ wo olive ngo krɔnkrɔn a woesiw a wɔdze sɔ gya, ma wɔmfa nsɔ kandzea nsi do daa.
Dase ntwamutam no ekyir, wɔ ehyiadzibuw no mu, na Aaron nsiesie mfi ewimbir nkodu anapa wɔ EWURADZE enyim daa: ɔnyɛ daa ahyɛdze wɔ ebusuasantsen mu.
Onsiesie nkandzea no wɔ sika mapa kandzeadua a no ho tsew no do wɔ EWURADZE enyim daa.
Kyerɛ Paanoo No Na fa isiam pa, na fa bi to tatar duebien; efa ebupɛn du mu ebien nyɛ tatar kor.
Na hyehyɛ no akyerɛpɛn ebien, esia nyɛ kyerɛpɛn kor, wɔ sika mapa pon a no ho tsew no do wɔ EWURADZE enyim.
Na fa krɔbɔw gyirengyirenn to kyerɛpɛn kor do, ma ɔnyɛ nkaadze wɔ boodoo no do, mekyerɛ ogya afɔr mma EWURADZE.
Ahomgyeda biara ɔnhyehyɛ no yie wɔ EWURADZE enyim daa: ɔyɛ Israelmba afamu daa ahyɛmu.
Na ɔnyɛ Aaron nye ne mbabanyin dze; na wondzi no wɔ mbrɛ ɔyɛ krɔnkrɔn: na ɔyɛ krɔnkrɔndze mu adzekrɔnkrɔn a ofi EWURADZE ogya afɔr do ma no wɔ daa ahyɛdze do.
Mbusu Ho Asotwe Na Israelnyi ɔbaa bi ne babanyin a n’egya yɛ Egyptnyi, fiir edzi wɔ Israelmba no mu: na Israelnyi ɔbaa no ne babanyin no ɔnye Israelnyi ɔbanyin bi dzii aperper wɔ nseraban no mu; na Israelnyi ɔbaa no ne babanyin no kaa Dzin no ho ebususɛm, na ɔdomee: na wɔdze no brɛɛ Moses.
Na ne na ne dzin dze Selomit, Dibri ne babaa a ofi Dan ebusuakuw mu.
Na wɔdze no siei, ama woeenya EWURADZE n’anomu asɛm ma wɔaaka akyerɛ hɔn ana.
Na EWURADZE kasaa kyerɛɛ Moses dɛ, Fa nyia wɔadom no fir edzi kɔ nseraban no ekyir; na ma hɔn a wɔtsee no nyinara mfa hɔn nsa ngu n’etsifi, na ma mboanofo no nyinara nsiw no abo.
Na kasa kyerɛ Israelmba dɛ, Obiara a ɔdom ne Nyankopɔn no ɔbɔsoa no bɔn.
Na nyia ɔka EWURADZE ne dzin ho ebususɛm no, oku na wonku no; osiw na mboanofo no nyinara nsiw no abo: ɔhɔho o, okuromnyi o, sɛ ɔka EWURADZE ne dzin ho ebususɛm a, wonku no.
Na nyia ɔbɔ nyimpa biara adze ma ɔtɔr no, oku na wonku no; na nyia ɔbɔ abowa adze ma owu no ɔnhyɛ ananmu: nkwa nhyɛ nkwa ananmu.
Na sɛ nyimpa ma ne nyɛnko dzi dzɛm a; dɛ mbrɛ ɔno ɔayɛ no, dɛmara na wɔmfa nyɛ no; Obu nhyɛ obu ananmu, enyiwa nhyɛ enyiwa ananmu, ese nhyɛ ese ananmu: dɛ mbrɛ ɔama nyimpa bi edzi dzɛm no, dɛmara na wɔnyɛ mma no.
Na nyia oku abowa no ɔnhyɛ ananmu: na nyia oku nyimpa no wonku no.
Mbra kor ara nda hɔ mma hom, dɛ mbrɛ ɔtse ma ɔhɔho no, ɔnyɛ dɛmara mma okuromnyi no: na emi nye EWURADZE hom Nyankopɔn.
Na Moses kasaa kyerɛɛ Israelmba, na wɔdze nyia ɔdomee no fiir edzi kɔr nseraban no ekyir, na wosiiw no abo.
Na Israelmba yɛɛ dɛ mbrɛ EWURADZE hyɛɛ Moses no.
Ahomgye Afe No Na EWURADZE kasaa kyerɛɛ Moses wɔ kokwaa Sinai do dɛ, Kasa kyerɛ Israelmba, na se hɔn dɛ, Sɛ hom du asaase a medze rema hom no do a, ɔno asaase no ndzi ahomgye afe mma EWURADZE.
Mfe esia na dua wo haban mu adze, na mfe esia na pempan wo wenyin ture mu ndua ho, na boaboa no mu nduadzewa ano; Mbom afe a otsia esuon no nyɛ ahomgye pa mu ahomgye afe mfa mma asaase no, nyɛ ahomgye afe mma EWURADZE: mma nndua wo haban mu adze, na mmpempan wo wenyin ture mu ndua ho so.
Wo ndɔbaa mu dza nankasa efifir no mma nntwa, na wo wenyindua a ennsiesie ho no mma nntsetsew no do esikyireamba: ɔnyɛ ahomgye pa afe mfa mma asaase no.
Na asaase no n’ahomgye afe no nyɛ edziban mma hom; ɔwo, nye w’akowaa nye w’afonabaa, nye wo paanyi nye wo hɔhoe a ɔabɔsoɛ wo; nye wo fiembowa, nye mbowa a wɔwɔ w’asaase no do, na no do ndɔbaa no nyinara nyɛ hɔn edziban.
Na kan ahomgye afe mfe esuon ma woho, mfe esuon esuon ahorow esuon; na ɔnyɛ ahomgye afe mfe esuon mu nda mma wo, mekyerɛ mfe eduanan akron.
Na nkyii bosoom a otsia esuon no ne da a otsia du no ma totorobɛnto ndze kɛse nkɔ aman do; mpata da no mu na hom mma totorobɛnto no nkɔ aman do ntwa mu wɔ hom asaase nyinara do.
Na hom ntsew afe a otsia eduonum no ho, na wɔmpaa fahodzi wɔ asaase no do mma no do atsefo nyinara: ɔnyɛ ahosɛpɛw afe mma hom; na hom nsan, nyimpa biara nkɔ n’ebusua mu.
Ahosɛpɛw afe na afe a otsia eduonum no nyɛ mma hom: mma hom nndua, nkyii so wonntwitwa dza nankasa efifir wɔ mu no, na wɔnntsetsew no mu wenyinndua a woennsiesie ho no do esikyireamba so.
Na ɔyɛ ahosɛpɛw afe; ɔnyɛ krɔnkrɔn mma hom: hom mfi haban no do ndzi do ndzɛmba a ɔba no.
Ahosɛpɛw afe yi mu no hom nsan, nyimpa biara nkɔ n’egyapadze ho.
Na sɛ etɔn biribi ma wo nyɛnko, anaa etɔ wɔ wo nyɛnko nsamu a, mma hom mu kor nndzi kor no emim: dɛ mbrɛ ahosɛpɛw afe no ekyir mfe dodow tse no na tɔ wɔ wo nyɛnko hɔ, dɛ mbrɛ ndɔbaa mfe dodow tse no na ɔntɔn mma wo.
Dɛ mbrɛ mfe no dɔɔ so pa no na to no bo mu, na dɛ mbrɛ mfe no suar pa no na yi no bo do, wɔ ndɔbaa dodow a ɔtɔn ma wo no ho.
Na mma hom mu kor nndzi kor emim; mbom suro wo Nyankopɔn: na emi nye EWURADZE hom Nyankopɔn.
Dɛm ntsi hom nyɛ m’ahyɛdze, na hom ndzi me mbrasɛm do, na wɔnyɛ; na hom ntsena asaase no do dwudwoodwo.
Na asaase no bɛma no nsowee, na hom edzi amee, na wɔatsena do dwudwoodwo.
Na sɛ hom se dɛ, Ebɛnadze na afe a otsia esuon no yebedzi?
Hwɛ, yerunndua, na yɛrommboaboa hɛn ndɔbaa ano a: ɔno mebɛhyɛ me nhyira wɔ hom do wɔ afe a otsia awɔtwe no mu, na wondzi nduadzewa no bi, akoradze dadaw no; nkodu afe a otsia akron no, hom ndzi akoradze dadaw araa nkodu dɛ no nduadzewa bɛba.
Na asaase no mma wɔnntɔn no korakora; osiandɛ asaase no yɛ medze: na hom yɛ ahɔho nye amamforafo wɔ me nkyɛn.
Egyapadze Mponee Na hom enyadze asaase no nyinara do na hom mma asaase no no mponee ho kwan.
Sɛ ohia wo nua, na ɔtɔn n’egyapadze mu bi a, ɔno no busuanyi a ɔbɛn no no mbra, na ɔmbɔpon dza no nua atɔn no.
Na sɛ nyimpa bi nnyi obi a ɔpon, na ne nsamu ba adze na onya dza ɔso pon a; ɔno wɔmma ombu no ntɔnee mu mfe dodow ano, na ɔnhyɛ dza ɔbor do no ananmu mma nyimpa no a ɔtɔnee maa no no; na ɔnsan nkɔ n’egyapadze ho.
Mbom sɛ orunntum nngye bio mma noho a, ɔno dza wɔatɔn no nko nyia ɔatɔ no nsamu nkodu ahosɛpɛw afe no: na ahosɛpɛw afe no mu na omfi hɔ, na ɔnsan nkɔ n’enyadze ho.
Na sɛ nyimpa bi tɔn ofi a wɔtsena mu wɔ kurow a afadum wɔ ho mu a, ɔno ɔmpon no wɔ no ntɔnee ekyir afrenhyia no mu; na afrenhyia mu na ɔwɔ mponee ho kwan.
Na sɛ wɔammpon no wɔ afrenhyia mu ntamu a, ɔno fie a ɔwɔ kurow a afadum wɔ ho mu no, ɔnko hɔ daa mma nyia ɔtɔe no korakora, wɔ n’ebusuasantsen mu: ommfi hɔ wɔ ahosɛpɛw afe no mu.
Na efiefi a ɔwowɔ nkuroba a onnyi fadum a ehyia ho mu dze, wombu nka ɔman no mu haban ho: wɔropon a wɔmpon, na ahosɛpɛw afe no mu omfi hɔ.
Naaso Levifo nkurow no, hɔn enyadze nkurow mu efi no dze, Levifo no mpon no aber biara.
Na sɛ Levifo mu kor pon a, ɔno fie no a wɔtɔnee, nye n’enyadze kurow no mfi hɔ wɔ ahosɛpɛw afe no mu: na Levifo nkurow mu efiefi no nye hɔn enyadze wɔ Israelmba mu.
Na nkurow no no kurotsia haban dze, mma wɔnntɔn, na ɔyɛ hɔn daa enyadze.
Adɔnkɔfo Ehiafo Mponee Na sɛ ohia wo nua, na ɔpa abaw wɔ wo nkyɛn a; ɔno suo no mu; na ɔntsena wo nkyɛn dɛ ɔhɔho nye ɔmamforanyi.
Mma nngye nsiho anaa ndɔree wɔ no hɔ; mbom suro wo Nyankopɔn: ma wo nua nye wo ntsena.
Mma mmfa wo sika anaa w’edziban mma no nsiho do, wɔ no ndɔree ntsi.
Emi nye EWURADZE hom Nyankopɔn a, miyii hom fii Egypt asaase do, dɛ medze Keenan asaase rema hom, na maayɛ hom Nyankopɔn.
Na sɛ ohia wo nua wɔ wo nkyɛn, na ɔtɔn noho ma wo a; mma mma ɔnnsom wo dɛ ɔdɔnkɔnyi: na ɔnyɛ wo nkyɛn dɛ mbrɛ ɔpaanyi nye ɔmamforanyi tse; ɔnsom wɔ wo nkyɛn araa ma onkodu ahosɛpɛw afe no mu: na nkyii omfi wo nkyɛn nkɔ, ɔno nye ne mba a wɔwɔ wo nkyɛn, na ɔnsan nkɔ nankasa n’ebusua mu, na n’egyanom enyadze ho na ɔnsan nkɔ.
Na wɔyɛ mo nkowaa a miyii hɔn fii Egypt asaase do: mma wɔnntɔn hɔn dɛ adɔnkɔfo.
Mma mmfa egyapadze nnhyɛ no do; mbom suro wo Nyankopɔn.
Na wo nkowaa nye wo mfonabaa a ibenya no; amanaman a woehyia hom ho no, hɔn mu na hom ntotɔ nkowaa nye mfonabaa.
Nkyii so ahɔho a wɔabɔsoɛ hom mu hɔn mba no, hɔn hɔ na hom ntɔ, nye hɔn ebusuafo a wɔwɔ hom nkyɛn a wɔawo hɔn wɔ hom asaase do no hɔ: na wɔnyɛ hom egyapadze.
Na hom nyɛ hɔn egyapadze mma hom mba wɔ hom ekyir, ma woeesuo mu ayɛ egyapadze; na hɔn mu na hom mfa hom adɔnkɔfo daa: hom nuanom Israelmba dze mma hom nnhyɛ hɔn do, mma obiara mmfa egyapadze do nnhyɛ no nua do.
Na sɛ ɔhɔho anaa ɔmamforanyi bi a ɔwɔ hom nkyɛn nya adze, na ohia wo nua a ɔnye no wɔ hɔ no, na ɔtɔn noho ma ɔhɔho no anaa ɔmamforanyi no a ɔwɔ wo nkyɛn no, anaa ɔhɔho no n’ebusua mu nyimpa bi a: no ntɔnee ekyir no wɔmpon no; na no nuanom mu baako mpon no: anaa no wɔfa, anaa no wɔfa ne babanyin mpon no, anaa n’ebusua mu bɔgya biara a ɔbɛn mpon no; anaa sɛ oenya adze a, ɔmpon noho.
Na ɔnye nyia ɔtɔ no no mbubu mfitsi afe a ɔtɔɔn noho maa no no do nkodu ahosɛpɛw afe no do: na no ntɔnee bo no nyɛ dɛ mbrɛ mfe no no dodow tse.
Sɛ mfe no da ho dɔɔ so a, ne tsisika mu mponee bo no a ɔbɛdan ama no so ndɔɔ so dɛmara.
Na sɛ aka mfe kumaabi ma edu ahosɛpɛw afe no do a, ɔno ɔnye no mbubu; dɛ mbrɛ ne mfe no tse no na ɔmfa no mponee sika no ndan mma.
Ɔnye no ntsena dɛ akowaa a wɔbɔ no paa afrenhyia afrenhyia: mma ɔmmfa egyapadze do nnhyɛ no do wɔ w’enyim.
Na sɛ woenndua iyinom do ammpon no a, ɔno omfir edzi nkɔ wɔ ahosɛpɛw afe no mu, ɔno nye ne mba nka no ho.
Osiandɛ Israelmba yɛ nkowaa ma me; wɔyɛ mo nkowaa a miyii hɔn fii Egypt asaase do: emi nye EWURADZE hom Nyankopɔn.
Setsie Mu Nhyira Mma hom nnyɛ abosom, nkyii so wɔnnsen ohonyi, anaa dum bi mma homho, nkyii so mma hom mmfa ɔbo a woedzi no akye nnsi hom asaase mu, mmbɔ hom mu adze mma no: na emi nye EWURADZE hom Nyankopɔn.
Hom ndzi m’ahomgye afe no, na wondzi m’ahotseweebea no nyi: emi nye EWURADZE.
Sɛ hom nantsew m’ahyɛdze mu, na hom sie me mbra, na hom yɛ a; ɔno mebɛma hom nyankom atotɔ wɔ n’aber mu, na asaase no ama no ndɔbaa, na haban mu ndua asow n’aba.
Na hom ewuporow bokodu wenyinaba tsetsew mu, na wenyinaba tsetsew no bokodu odua ber mu: na hom bedzi hom edziban amee, na wɔatsena hom asaase do dwudwoodwo.
Na mebɛma asomdwee aba asaase no do, na hom ada, na obiara rinnyi hom hu: na mebɛma mbowa bɔn tun do etwa wɔ asaase no do, nkyii so nkrantsee remmfa hom asaase do.
Na hom betsiw hom atamfo, na wɔbɔtotɔr hom enyim wɔ nkrantsee ano.
Na hom mu beenu betsiw ɔha, na hom mu ɔha betsiw mpem du: na hom atamfo bɔtotɔr hom enyim wɔ nkrantsee ano.
Na mebɛdan m’enyim ama hom, na mama hom awowo, na hom adɔr, na mama menye hom ahyɛmu no etsim.
Na hom bedzi akoradze dadaw a wɔdze esie ma akyɛr no, na hom beyi dadaw no aba wɔ fofor no ntsi.
Na mibesi me ntamadan wɔ hom mu: na me kra rinnkyir hom.
Na mebɛnantsew hom mu, na mayɛ hom Nyankopɔn, na hom ayɛ me man.
Emi nye EWURADZE hom Nyankopɔn a miyii hom fii Egypt asaase do dɛ mma hom nnyɛ hɔn nkowaa; na mebubu hom kɔndua, na memaa hom sii nkyiremben nantsewee no.
Asoɔdzen Ho Ntsea Mbom sɛ hom enntsie me, na wɔannyɛ me mbrasɛm nyinara a; na sɛ hom pow m’ahyɛdze, na hom kra kyir me mbrasɛm, na hom annyɛ me mbransɛm nyinara, na mbom hom sɛɛ m’ahyɛmu a; mo so mebɛyɛ hom iyi; mebɛma nketsenketse akyer hom, mekyerɛ sasawaw nye etsiridii a ɔbɛsɛɛ enyiwa, na ɔbɛma ɔkra atsetsew: na hom bodua hom nduaba kwa, na hom atamfo bedzi.
Na mebɛma m’enyi asa hom, na hom edzi hom atamfo enyim nkogu: hɔn a wokyir hom bɛhyɛ hom do; na hom boguan aber a obi nntsiw hom.
Na sɛ hom enntsie me wɔ iyinom mpo ntsi a, ɔno mebɛtsea hom mpɛn esuon bio wɔ hom bɔn ntsi.
Na mubobubu hom tum ahokyerɛ no; na mayɛ hom sor dɛ dadze, nye hom asaase dɛ boran: na hom ahoɔdzen bɛsa kwa: na asaase remma ndɔbaa, nkyii so asaase no do ndua ronnsow n’aba.
Na sɛ hom nantsew tsia me, na woenntsie me a; medze ɔhaw mpɛn esuon so mebɛba hom do dɛ mbrɛ hom bɔn tse no.
Na mobɔsoma haban mu mbowa wɔ hom mu a wɔbɛgye hom nsamu mba, na wɔasɛɛ hom fiembowa, na wɔama hom dodow esuar; na hom akwan ayɛ akwamfo.
Na sɛ hom amma iyinom annsakyer hom amma me, na mbom wɔnantsew tsia me a: ɔno mo so mebɛnantsew etsia hom; na emi mara mabɔ hom mpɛn esuon wɔ hom bɔn ntsi.
Na medze awerdzi nkrantsee a obedzi ahyɛmu no ho wer mebɛba hom do; na hom aboaboa hom ano wɔ hom nkurow mu: na mobɔsoma ɔyardɔm wɔ hom mu; na woeyi hom ahyɛ ɔtamfo no nsa.
Sɛ mububu hom edziban dua a, mbaa du bɔto hɔn boodoo wɔ fononoo kor mu, na woeyi hom boodoo ama hom bio wɔ nsɛn do: na hom bedzi, na wɔremmee.
Na sɛ iyi nyinara mu so hom enntsie me, na wɔnantsew tsia me a; ɔno mebɛnantsew etsia hom ebufuw mu; na mo so matsea hom mpɛn esuon wɔ hom bɔn ntsi.
Na hom bedzi hom mbabanyin nam, na hom mbabaa nam so hom edzi.
Na mebɛsɛɛ hom sorɔnsorɔmbea, na metwitwa hom iwihonyi no egu, na matotow hom efun egu hom abosom efun no do; na me kra bekyir hom.
Na mebɛyɛ hom nkurow amamfo, na medze hom ahotseweebea akɔ ɔsɛɛ mu, na merenngye hom nduhuam ne nka.
Na medze asaase no bɔkɔ ɔsɛɛ mu: na hom atamfo a wɔtse do no ayɛ hɔn nwanwa.
Na hom dze mobɔbɔ hom apetse amanaman mu, na matwe nkrantsee no edzi hom ekyir: na hom asaase ayɛ ɔsɛɛ, na hom nkurow ayɛ amamfo.
Ɔno na asaase no benya n’ahomgye mber ho enyigye, mber tsentsen a ɔda hɔ kɔnn no nyinara, na hom wɔ hom atamfo asaase do no; mekyerɛ ɔno na asaase no bɔhom, na woenya n’ahomgye mber ho enyigye.
Mber tsentsen a ɔda hɔ kɔnn no nyinara obenya ahomgye; mekyerɛ ahomgye a woennya no wɔ hom ahomgyenda no mu, aber a hom tsenaa do no.
Na hom mu hɔn a wɔaka no dze, medze abawpa bɛhɛn hɔn akoma mu wɔ hɔn atamfo asaase do; na ahataw a atsew ne ndze etsiw hɔn; na woeguan dɛ obi ruguan nkrantsee ano; na wɔahwehwe ase aber a obi rinntsiw hɔn.
Na wobefintsiw hɔnho nkorkor, dɛ nkrantsee enyim, aber a obi rinntsiw hɔn: na hom rinnya tum nngyina hom atamfo enyim.
Na hom bɛsɛɛ wɔ amanaman mu, na hom atamfo asaase bɛmemen hom.
Na hom mu hɔn a wɔaka no bɛtsetsew wɔ hɔn emumuyɛ mu wɔ hom atamfo asaase do; na eso hɔn egyanom emumuyɛ mu na wɔnye hɔn bɛtsetsew.
Na wɔbɛka hɔn emumuyɛ, nye hɔn egyanom emumuyɛ, wɔ hɔn mfom a wɔfom mu no mu, na eso dɛ wɔanantsew etsia me ntsi, mo so menantsewee tsiaa hɔn, na medze hɔn baa hɔn atamfo asaase do: sɛ nkyii hɔn akoma monomonomyɛ no brɛ adze, na nkyii wɔpen hɔn emumuyɛ ho ntsea do a; ɔno na mebɛkaa menye Jakob ahyɛmu no; na menye Isaak ahyɛmu no so, na menye Abraham ahyɛmu no so mebɛkaa; na mebɛkaa asaase no.
Na asaase no so wobegya no hɔ, na woenya n’ahomgye mber mu enyigye, aber a woekwetsi hɔn ada hɔ kɔnn no; na wɔbɛpen hɔn emumuyɛ ho ntsea do: osiandɛ wɔpoow me mbrasɛm, na hɔn kra kyiir m’ahyɛdze.
Na iyi nyinara so mpo ekyir, sɛ wɔwɔ hɔn atamfo asaase do a morommpow hɔn, nkyii so mirinnkyir hɔn, dɛ meresɛɛ hɔn korakora, na matsetsew menye hɔn ntamu ahyɛmu no mu; na emi nye EWURADZE hɔn Nyankopɔn: mbom hɔn ntsi mebɛkaa hɔn nananom ahyɛmu no, hɔn a miyii hɔn fii Egypt asaase do wɔ amanaman enyim, dɛ mebɛyɛ hɔn Nyankopɔn no: emi nye EWURADZE.
Iyinom nye ahyɛdze nye ntsɛmbu nye mbra a EWURADZE dze nam Moses ne nsa do hyɛe too ɔno nye Israelmba ntamu wɔ kokwaa Sinai do.
EWURADZE Akyɛdze No Mponee Na EWURADZE kasaa kyerɛɛ Moses dɛ, Kasa kyerɛ Israelmba, na se hɔn dɛ, Sɛ nyimpa bi hyɛ anohoba ma a, nkorɔfo no nyɛ EWURADZE dze dɛ mbrɛ w’abotwa tse.
Na w’abotwa wɔ banyin a oedzi mfe eduonu do dze kodu nyia oedzi mfe eduosia do no ho nyɛ dwɛɛtɛɛ dwetɛbona eduonum, dɛ mbrɛ krɔnkrɔnbea dwetɛbona tse.
Na sɛ ɔyɛ ɔbaa a, ɔno w’abotwa nyɛ dwetɛbona eduasa.
Na sɛ ofi nyia oedzi mfe enum do dze kodu nyia oedzi mfe eduonu do a, ɔno w’abotwa wɔ ɔbanyin ho nyɛ dwetɛbona eduonu, na ɔbaa ho so dwetɛbona du.
Na sɛ ofi nyia oedzi bosoom do dze kodu nyia oedzi mfe enum do a, ɔno w’abotwa wɔ ɔbanyin ho nyɛ dwɛɛtɛɛ dwetɛbona enum, na ɔbaa ho so w’abotwa nyɛ dwɛɛtɛɛ dwetɛbona ebiasa.
Na sɛ ofi nyia oedzi mfe eduosia nye ekyir do a; sɛ ɔbanyin a, ɔno w’abotwa nyɛ dwetɛbona duenum, na ɔbaa ho so dwetɛbona du.
Mbom sɛ ɔyɛ ohianyi dodow kyɛn w’abotwa no a, ɔno wɔmfa no mbegyina ɔsɔfo no enyim, na ɔsɔfo no ntwa no bo; dɛ mbrɛ nyia ɔbɔɔ anohoba no ne nsa bɔso do no ara na ɔsɔfo no ntwa no bo.
Na sɛ ɔyɛ abowa a adasa dze bi yɛ ayɛyɛdze brɛ EWURADZE a, dza nyimpa biara dze mu bi ma EWURADZE no nyinara nyɛ krɔnkrɔn.
Mma ɔnndan no, nkyii so ɔnnsakyer no, ɔmmfa papa nnsesa bɔn, anaa ɔmmfa bɔn nnsesa papa: na sɛ koraa ɔdze abowa bɛsesa abowa a, ɔno emu ebien nyina ɔno nye dza wɔdze sesaa no no nyɛ krɔnkrɔn.
Na sɛ ɔyɛ abowa biara a no ho nntsew a wɔmmfa bi nnyɛ ayɛyɛdze mmbrɛ EWURADZE a, ɔno ɔmfa abowa no mbegyina ɔsɔfo no enyim: na ɔsɔfo no ntwa no bo, sɛ oye o, omuo o: dɛ mbrɛ woara ɔsɔfo no botwa no bo no, dɛmara na ɔnyɛ.
Mbom sɛ pon ara na ɔbɔpon no a, ɔno ɔmfa no mu ebupɛn enum mu kor nto wo bo a itwae no do.
Na sɛ nyimpa bi tsew ne fi ho dɛ ɔnyɛ krɔnkrɔn mma EWURADZE a, ɔno ɔsɔfo no ntwa no bo, sɛ oye o, omuo o: dɛ mbrɛ ɔsɔfo no botwa no bo no, dɛmara na ongyina.
Na sɛ nyia ɔtsew ho no bɔpon ne fi a, ɔno ɔmfa wo bo a itwae no ne sika no mu ebupɛn enum mu kor nto do, na ɔnyɛ nedze.
Na sɛ nyimpa bi tsew n’asaase mu haban mu bi ho ma EWURADZE a, ɔno w’abotwa nyɛ dɛ mbrɛ no nduae tse: atoko a woedua no homer kor no bo yɛ dwɛɛtɛɛ dwetɛbona eduonum.
Sɛ ahosɛpɛw afe no do na ɔtsew ne haban ho a, ontua dɛ mbrɛ bo a woetwa no tse no ara.
Mbom sɛ ahosɛpɛw afe no ekyir na ɔtsew ne haban ho a, ɔno ɔsɔfo no mbubu sika no ano mma no dɛ mbrɛ mfe a aka ma akɔso ahosɛpɛw afe no tse no, na wɔntsew bo a itwae no do.
Na sɛ pon ara na nyia ɔtsew haban no ho no bɔpon a, ɔno ɔmfa wo bo a itwae no ne sika no mu ebupɛn enum mu kor nto do, na wonsi no pi mma no.
Na sɛ ɔammpon haban no, anaa sɛ ɔatɔn haban no ama nyimpa bi so a, mma wɔmmpon bio; mbom haban no, sɛ ofir edzi ahosɛpɛw afe no mu kɔ a, ɔnyɛ krɔnkrɔn mma EWURADZE, dɛ haban a woehyira do ama; ɔnyɛ ɔsɔfo no n’enyadze.
Na sɛ ɔtsew haban a ɔatɔ a ɔnnyɛ n’enyadze haban no bi ho ma EWURADZE a; ɔno ɔsɔfo no mbubu w’abotwa a ɔdze kodu ahosɛpɛw afe no do no, no bo a ɔsom no mma no: na ɔmma wo bo a itwae no da no ara, dɛ adzekrɔnkrɔn mma EWURADZE.
Ahosɛpɛw afe no mu haban no nsan nkɔ nyia wɔtɔɔ no no hɔ, mekyerɛ nyia ɔyɛ n’enyadze asaase no no hɔ.
Na w’abotwitwa nyinara nyɛ dɛ mbrɛ krɔnkrɔnbea dwetɛbona no tse: gera eduonu yɛ dwetɛbona kor.
Mbowa mu abakan a wɔayɛ no abakan ama EWURADZE no, noara nkotoo na nyimpa bi nntsew ho; sɛ ɔnantwinyin o, ɔkɔsɔw o, EWURADZE dze a. Na sɛ ɔyɛ abowa a no ho nntsew bi a, ɔno ɔmma n’apondze dɛ mbrɛ w’abotwa tse no, na ɔmfa no mu ebupɛn enum mu kor nto do: anaa sɛ wɔammpon no no a, ɔno wɔntɔn no dɛ mbrɛ w’abotwa tse no.
Naaso ehyiradze biara a nyimpa bi behyira do ama EWURADZE wɔ adze a ɔwɔ nyinara mu no, sɛ nyimpa o, abowa o, n’enyadze mu haban o, mma wɔnntɔn anaa wɔmmpon: ehyiradze biara yɛ krɔnkrɔndze mu adzekrɔnkrɔn ma EWURADZE.
Na mpo, nyimpa biara a woebu no kumfɔ no, mma wɔmmpon no; oku na wonku no.
Na asaase no do ebupɛn du du nyinara, sɛ ofi asaase no do o, nduadzewa mu o, dua n’aba mu o, ɔyɛ EWURADZE dze; ɔyɛ krɔnkrɔn ma EWURADZE.
Na sɛ nyimpa bi bɔpon n’ebupɛn du du no mu bi a, ɔmfa no mu ebupɛn enum mu kor nto do.
Na anantwi anaa nguan mu ebupɛn du du nyinara, adze a ɔfa poma ase nyinara mu dza otsia du du no nyɛ krɔnkrɔn mma EWURADZE.
Mma ɔnnhwehwɛ mu dɛ ɔyɛ papa anaa bɔn, nkyii so mma ɔnnsesa bi: na sɛ koraa ɔbɛsesa bi a, ɔno emu ebien nyina, ɔno nye dza wɔdze sesa no no nyɛ krɔnkrɔn; mma wɔmmpon no.
Iyinom nye mbransɛm a EWURADZE dze hyɛɛ Moses wɔ bepɔw Sinai do ma ɔdze maa Israelmba no.
NHƐNMU Nkanee anaadɛ Sar Do Akwantu nwoma no ka abakɔsɛm a ɔfa Israelmba no hɔn mfe eduanan a wɔdze twaa kwan fii Sinai Bepɔw ho dze kodur anohoba asaase no ne he do wɔ boka afamu no ho asɛm.
Sar Do Akwantu nwoma no ka Israelmba hɔn abakɔsɛm no mu fa tsitsir bi ho asɛm.
Ɔfa kan a Moses kaan Israelmba no hun hɔn dodow wɔ Sinai Bepɔw no ho ana worutu efi hɔ akɔ no ho.
Ɔsanee kaan hɔn bio wɔ Moab asaase do wɔ esutsen Jordan afamu mfe eduasa ekyir.
Israelmba dze mber a ɔda nyimpakan a odzi kan na dza otsia ebien no ntamu no kodur Kades Barnea wɔ Keenan anaafo afamu tɔnn; naaso woenntum ammfa hɔ annkɔ anohoba asaase no do.
Wɔtsenaa Kades Barnea kyɛree ara yie ana worututu do akɔ asaase a ɔda esutsen Jordan no boka afamu no do.
Ha na hɔn mu binom tsenaa afebɔɔ, na hɔn a wɔaka no so boaboaa hɔn ho twaa esutsen no kɔr Keenan.
Sar Do Akwantu nwoma no ka ɔman bi a mpɛn pii wohyiaa amandzehu ma wosuroo yie ma wɔpaa abaw no ho asɛm.
Wɔtseew Nyankopɔn na Moses a Nyankopɔn yii no dɛ ondzi hɔn enyim no do etua.
Israelmba hɔn mberɛwyɛ na asoɔdzen nyina ekyir no, Nyankopɔn dzii nokwar maa hɔn hwɛɛ hɔn do daa nyina.
Ɔka Moses no nokwardzi ho asɛm dɛmara.
Ɔwɔ mu dɛ ɔtɔfabi a, Moses nntum nnya abotar dze, naaso oyii ne yamu soom Nyankopɔn na ne mamfoo wɔ nokwar mu.
Dza Ɔwɔ Mu Israelmba boaboa hɔn ho tu fi Sinai Bepɔw no ho .—.
.
Nyimpakan no .—.
.
Mbra na nhyehyɛɛ ahorow .—.
.
Apaho Afahyɛ a ɔtɔ do ebien .- Ofi Sinai Bepɔw do kɔ Moab .—.
Dza osii wɔ Moab asaase do .—.
Akwantu a ofi Egypt kɔ Moab mu nsɛm no mbubudo .- Dza wɔkyerɛɛ hɔn dɛ wɔnyɛ ana woetwa esutsen Jordan .—.
Israel Nyimpakan A Odzi kan Na Israelfo fii Egypt asaase do firii no n’ekyir afe a otsia ebien no mu bosoom a otsia ebien no ne da a odzi kan no, EWURADZE kasaa kyerɛɛ Moses wɔ Sinai sar do wɔ ehyiadzibuw no mu dɛ, Ɔwo na Aaron mbu Israelmba mboanofo no nyinara ano, dɛ mbrɛ hɔn ebusua ebusua tsetsee, na mbrɛ hɔn egyanom efi tsetsee, na dɛ mbrɛ hɔn banyin biara ne dzin tse nkorkor.
Israel mu hɔn a woedzi mfe eduonu na ekyir a wotum kɔ ɔsa nyinara no hom nkan hɔn dɛ mbrɛ hɔn dɔm no tse.
Na ebusuakuw biara mu banyin bi nka hom ho; kor biara a ɔyɛ n’egyanom fi mu otsitsir.
Na mbanyin a womfo a ebusuakuw no mu mboa hom no hɔn edzin nye yi: Reuben dze; Sedeur ne babanyin Elizur.
Simeon dze; Zurisadai ne babanyin Selumiel.
Juda dze; Amminadab ne babanyin Nahson.
Isakar dze; Zuar ne babanyin Netanel.
Zebulun dze; Helon ne babanyin Eliab.
Josef ne mba no dze; Efraim dze; Ammihud ne babanyin Elisama: Manaasɛ dze; Pedazur ne babanyin Gamaliel.
Benjamin dze; Gideoni ne babanyin Abidan.
Dan dze; Ammisaddai ne babanyin Ahiezer.
Aser dze; Okran ne babanyin Pagiel.
Gad dze; Deutel ne babanyin Eliasaf.
Naftali dze; Enan ne babanyin Ahira.
Iyinom nye hɔn a wɔfrɛɛ hɔn wɔ mboanofo no mu, hɔn egyanom ebusuakuw mu mbapɔmba no; wɔyɛ Israel mpem mpem mu etsitsir.
Na Moses nye Aaron faa mbanyin a wɔabobɔ hɔn edzin yi: na wohyiaa mboanofo no nyinara boaa ano wɔ bosoom a otsia ebien no ne da a odzi kan no mu, na wɔkyerɛɛ hɔn asefo dɛ mbrɛ hɔn ebusua ebusua na hɔn egyanom efi tsetsee, dɛ mbrɛ edzin no no dodow tse, hɔn a woedzi mfe eduonu na ekyir, dɛ mbrɛ wɔtse nkorkor.
Dɛ mbrɛ EWURADZE hyɛɛ Moses no, dɛmara na ɔkaan hɔn wɔ Sinai sar no do.
Na Israel n’abakan Reuben, ne mba, hɔn ebusuasantsen, dɛ mbrɛ hɔn ebusua ebusua na hɔn egyanom efi tsetsee, dɛ mbrɛ edzin no no dodow tse no, ɔbanyin biara a oedzi mfe eduonu na ekyir, na hɔn a wotum kɔ ɔsa a wɔkaan hɔn wɔ Reuben ebusuakuw mu, nyinara yɛ mpemeduanan esia na ahaenum.
Simeon ne mba, hɔn ebusuasantsen, dɛ mbrɛ hɔn ebusua ebusua na hɔn egyanom efi tsetsee, dɛ mbrɛ edzin no no dodow tse no, ɔbanyin biara a oedzi mfe eduonu na ekyir, na hɔn a wotum kɔ ɔsa nyinara; a wɔkaan hɔn wɔ Simeon ebusuakuw mu no, nyinara mpemeduonum akron na ahaasa.
Gad ne mba, hɔn ebusuasantsen, dɛ mbrɛ hɔn ebusua ebusua, na hɔn egyanom efi tsetsee, dɛ mbrɛ edzin no no dodow tse, hɔn a woedzi mfe eduonu na ekyir a wotum kɔ ɔsa a wɔkaan hɔn wɔ Gad ebusuakuw mu, nyinara yɛ mpemeduanan enum ahaesia na eduonum.
Juda ne mba, hɔn ebusuasantsen, dɛ mbrɛ hɔn ebusua ebusua, na hɔn egyanom efi tsetsee, dɛ mbrɛ edzin no no dodow tse, hɔn a woedzi mfe eduonu na ekyir na hɔn a wotum kɔ ɔsa nyinara a wɔkaan hɔn wɔ Juda ebusuakuw mu no nyinara mpemeduosuon anan na ahaesia.
Isakar ne mba, hɔn ebusuasantsen, dɛ mbrɛ hɔn ebusua ebusua na hɔn egyanom efi tsetsee, dɛ mbrɛ edzin no no dodow tse no hɔn a woedzi mfe eduonu na ekyir, hɔn a wotum kɔ ɔsa nyinara a wɔkaan hɔn wɔ Isakar ebusuakuw mu no yɛ mpemeduonum anan na ahaanan.
Zebulun ne mba, hɔn ebusuasantsen, dɛ mbrɛ hɔn ebusua ebusua, na hɔn egyanom efi tsetsee, dɛ mbrɛ edzin no no dodow tse no, hɔn a woedzi mfe eduonu na ekyir a wotum kɔ ɔsa a wɔkaan hɔn wɔ Zebulun ebusuakuw mu nyinara, wɔyɛ mpemeduonum esuon na ahaanan.
Josef n’asefo a wɔyɛ, Efraim ne mba, hɔn ebusuasantsen, dɛ mbrɛ hɔn ebusua ebusua, na hɔn egyanom efi tsetsee, dɛ mbrɛ edzin no no dodow tse no hɔn a woedzi mfe eduonu na ekyir a wotum kɔ ɔsa a wɔkaan hɔn wɔ Efraim ebusuakuw mu no yɛ mpemeduanan na ahaenum.
Manaasɛ ne mba, hɔn ebusuasantsen, dɛ mbrɛ hɔn ebusua ebusua na hɔn egyanom efi tsetsee, dɛ mbrɛ edzin no no dodow tse no, hɔn a woedzi mfe eduonu na ekyir a wotum kɔ ɔsa a wɔkaan hɔn wɔ Manaasɛ ebusuakuw mu nyinara, yɛ mpemeduasa ebien na ahaenu.
Benjamin ne mba, hɔn ebusuasantsen, dɛ mbrɛ hɔn ebusua ebusua na hɔn egyanom efi tsetsee, dɛ mbrɛ edzin no no dodow tse, hɔn a woedzi mfe eduonu na ekyir a wotum kɔ ɔsa nyinara; hɔn a wɔkaan hɔn wɔ Benjamin ebusuakuw mu no, yɛ mpemeduasa enum na ahaanan.
Dan ne mba, hɔn ebusuasantsen, dɛ mbrɛ hɔn ebusua ebusua na hɔn egyanom efi tsetsee, dɛ mbrɛ edzin no no dodow tse no, hɔn a woedzi mfe eduonu na ekyir a wotum kɔ ɔsa a wɔkaan hɔn, wɔ Dan ebusuakuw mu no nyinara yɛ mpemeduosia ebien na ahaesuon.
Aser ne mba, hɔn ebusuasantsen, dɛ mbrɛ hɔn ebusua ebusua, na hɔn egyanom efi tsetsee, dɛ mbrɛ edzin no no dodow tse no hɔn a woedzi mfe eduonu na ekyir a wotum kɔ ɔsa wɔkaan hɔn wɔ Aser ebusuakuw mu no nyinara, wɔyɛ mpemeduanan biako na ahaenum.
Naftali ne mba, hɔn ebusuasantsen, dɛ mbrɛ hɔn ebusua ebusua, na hɔn egyanom efi tsetsee, dɛ mbrɛ edzin no no dodow tse, hɔn a woedzi mfe eduonu na ekyir a wotum kɔ ɔsa nyinara a wɔkaan hɔn wɔ Naftali ebusuakuw mu no nyinara, wɔyɛ mpemeduonum ebiasa na ahaanan.
Iyinom nye hɔn a Moses na Aaron nye Israel mbapɔmba no a wɔyɛ mbanyin duebien no kanee no: wogyinagyinaa hɔn egyanom efi ananmu nkorkor.
Dɛm ntsi hɔn a wɔkaan hɔn wɔ Israelmba mu dɛ mbrɛ hɔn egyanom efi tsetsee nyinara, hɔn a woedzi mfe eduonu na ekyir a wotum kɔ ɔsa wɔ Israel mu a wɔkaan hɔn nyinara no yɛ mpemahaesia na ebiasa na ahaenum eduonum.
Levifo No Hɔn Ahyɛdze Levifo no dze, dɛ mbrɛ hɔn egyanom ebusuakuw tse no, wɔannkan hɔn ammfora hɔn.
Na EWURADZE kasaa kyerɛɛ Moses dɛ, Levi ebusuakuw nkotsee na mma nnkan, nkyii so mma mmbu hɔn dodow ano mmfora Israelmba: mbom woara fa Levifo no si dase ntamadan no na no ho ndzɛmba nyinara na dza odzi wɔ no nyinara do: hɔn na wɔnsoa ntamadan no, na no ho ndzɛmba nyinara; na wɔnyɛ ho edwuma, na wɔmbɔ nseraban nhyia ntamadan no ho.
Na sɛ worutu ntamadan no akɔ kan a, Levifo no na wontutu: na sɛ wɔrekyer ntamadan no nsera a, Levifo no na wonsi: na sɛ ɔhɔho ba ho a wonku no.
Na Israelmba no mbɔ hɔn asesee, nyimpa biara wɔ nankasa ne nseraban do, na nyimpa biara wɔ nankasa ne frankaa ho, dɛ mbrɛ hɔn dɔm no tse.
Levifo no dze wɔnkyer nsera wɔ dase ntamadan no ho nhyia, amma ebufuw bi aammba Israelmba mboanofo no do: na Levifo no nhwɛ dase ntamadan ahwɛdze no do.
Na Israelmba no yɛe; dɛ mbrɛ EWURADZE hyɛɛ Moses no nyinara, dɛmara na wɔyɛe.
Ebusuakuw Nserakyer Ho Nhyehyɛɛ Na EWURADZE kasaa kyerɛɛ Moses na Aaron dɛ, Israelmba no nkyer nsera wɔ nyimpa biara nankasa ne frankaa ho, wɔ hɔn egyanom efi nsɛnkyerɛdze do: ehyiadzibuw no ne tsentsendo na wɔnkyer hɔn nsera no nhyia.
Na hɔn a wɔnkyer nsera wɔ boka afamu a odzi kɔ wipuei no nye hɔn a wɔwɔ Juda nseraban do frankaa ho no dɛ mbrɛ hɔn dɔm no tse: na Amminadab ne babanyin Nason na ɔnyɛ Judamba no hɔn safohen panyin.
Na no dɔm, na hɔn a wɔkaan hɔn wɔ mu no, wɔyɛ mpemeduosuon anan na ahaesia.
Na hɔn a wɔnkyer nsera ntoa no do nye Isakar ebusuakuw.
Zuar ne babanyin Netanel na ɔnyɛ Isakarmba no hɔn safohen panyin: na no dɔm, na hɔn a wɔkaan hɔn wɔ mu no, wɔyɛ mpemeduonum anan na ahaanan.
Zebulun ebusuakuw ntoa do: na Helon ne babanyin Eliab na ɔnyɛ Zebulunmba no hɔn safohen panyin: na no dɔm, na hɔn a wɔkaan hɔn wɔ mu no, wɔyɛ mpemeduonum esuon na ahaanan.
Hɔn a wɔkaan hɔn wɔ Juda nseraban do nyinara yɛ mpem ɔha eduowɔtwe esia na ahaanan, dɛ mbrɛ hɔn dɔm no tse.
Hɔn na wondzi kan ntu.
Pomu afamu na Reuben nseraban do frankaa ndzi dɛ mbrɛ hɔn dɔm no tse: na Sedeur ne babanyin Elizur na ɔnyɛ Reubenmba ɔsafohen panyin.
Na no dɔm, na hɔn a wɔkaan hɔn wɔ mu no yɛ mpemeduanan esia na ahaenum.
Hɔn a wɔnkyer nsera ntoa no do nye Simeon ebusuakuw: na Zurisadai ne babanyin Selumiel na ɔnyɛ Simeonmba no hɔn safohen panyin: na no dɔm a wɔkaan hɔn wɔ mu no, wɔyɛ mpemeduonum akron na ahaasa.
Gad ebusuakuw no ntoa hɔn do: na Reuel ne babanyin Eliasaf na ɔnyɛ Gadmba no hɔn safohen panyin: na no dɔm a wɔkaan hɔn wɔ mu no yɛ mpemeduanan enum na ahaesia eduonum.
Hɔn a wɔkaan hɔn wɔ Reuben nseraban do nyinara wɔyɛ mpem ɔha eduonum biako na ahaanan eduonum, dɛ mbrɛ hɔn dɔm no tse.
Na hɔn na wɔntɔ do ebien ntu.
Nkyii so ehyiadzibuw no, nye Levifo nseraban no ntu ndzi nseraban nseraban no ne finimfin: dɛ mbrɛ wɔbɔ nseraban no, dɛmara na wontu, nyimpa biara wɔ ne dzibew, dɛ mbrɛ hɔn mfrankaa no tse.
Efraim ne nseraban do frankaa ndzi anee afamu dɛ mbrɛ hɔn dɔm no tse: na Ammihud ne babanyin Elisama na ɔnyɛ Efraimmba no hɔn safohen panyin.
Na no dɔm, na hɔn a wɔkaan hɔn wɔ mu no, wɔyɛ mpemeduanan na ahaenum.
Na Manaasɛ ebusuakuw ntoa no do: na Pedazur ne babanyin Gamaliel na ɔnyɛ Manaasɛmba no hɔn safohen panyin.
Na no dɔm, na hɔn a wɔkaan hɔn wɔ mu no yɛ mpemeduasa ebien na ahaenu.
Benjamin ebusuakuw no, Gideoni ne babanyin Abidan na ɔnyɛ hɔn safohen panyin: na no dɔm, na hɔn a wɔkaan hɔn wɔ mu no yɛ mpemeduasa enum na ahaanan.
Hɔn a wɔkaan hɔn wɔ Efraim nseraban do nyinara yɛ mpem ɔha nye awɔtwe na ɔha, dɛ mbrɛ hɔn dɔm no tse.
Na hɔn na wɔntɔ do ebiasa ntu.
Dan ne nseraban do frankaa ndzi kwaamu afamu dɛ mbrɛ hɔn dɔm no tse: na Ammisaddai ne babanyin Ahiezer na ɔnyɛ Danmba no hɔn safohen panyin.
Na no dɔm a wɔkaan hɔn wɔ mu no yɛ mpemeduosia ebien na ahaesuon.
Na hɔn a wɔnkyer nsera ntoa no do nye Aser ebusuakuw: na Okran ne babanyin Pagiel na ɔnyɛ Asermba no hɔn safohen panyin.
No dɔm na hɔn a wɔkaan hɔn wɔ mu no, wɔyɛ mpemeduanan biako na ahaenum.
Naftali ebusuakuw no, Enan ne babanyin Ahira na ɔnyɛ Naftalimba no hɔn safohen panyin: na no dɔm a wɔkaan hɔn wɔ mu no, yɛ mpemeduonum ebiasa na ahaanan.
Hɔn a wɔkaan hɔn wɔ Dan ne nseraban do nyinara yɛ mpem ɔha na eduonum esuon na ahaesia.
Hɔn na wondzi ekyir ntu dɛ mbrɛ hɔn mfrankaa no tse.
Iyinom nye Israelmba mu hɔn a wɔkaan hɔn dɛ mbrɛ hɔn egyanom efi tsetsee: hɔn a wɔkaan hɔn wɔ nseraban nseraban do dɛ mbrɛ hɔn dɔm no tse nyinara yɛ mpemahaesia nye ebiasa na ahaenum eduonum.
Levifo no dze, wɔannkan hɔn ammfora Israelmba no; dɛ mbrɛ EWURADZE hyɛɛ Moses no.
Na Israelmba no yɛɛ dɛ mbrɛ EWURADZE hyɛɛ Moses no nyinara, na wɔkyeer nsera dɛ mbrɛ hɔn mfrankaa no tse, na dɛmara so na wotui, obiara dɛ mbrɛ hɔn ebusua na hɔn egyanom efi tsetsee.
Levi Ebusuakuw Afei iyinom nye Aaron nye Moses hɔn ebusuasantsen wɔ da a EWURADZE nye Moses kasae, wɔ kokwaa Sinai do no.
Na iyinom nye Aaron ne mbabanyin no hɔn edzin; Nadab a ɔyɛ abakan no, nye Abihu, Eleazar, nye Itamar.
Iyinom nye Aaron ne mbabanyin, asɔfo a wɔseraa hɔn ngo a wotuu hɔn sii nkyɛn dɛ wondzi asɔfo no, hɔn edzin.
Na Nadab nye Abihu wuwui wɔ EWURADZE enyim, aber a wɔdze ananagya baa EWURADZE enyim, wɔ Sinai sar do no, na woennya mba ntsi Eleazar nye Itamar nko na wodzii asɔfo wɔ hɔn egya Aaron enyim.
Na EWURADZE kasaa kyerɛɛ Moses dɛ, Fa Levi ebusuakuw no bɛn, na fa hɔn begyina ɔsɔfo Aaron enyim ma wɔnsom me.
Na wɔnhwɛ n’ahwɛdze do, nye mboanofo no nyinara ahwɛdze no do wɔ ehyiadzibuw no enyim, mfa nyɛ ntamadan no ho edwuma no.
Na wɔnhwɛ ehyiadzibuw no ne ndzɛmba no nyinara, nye Israelmba ahwɛdze no do, mfa nyɛ ntamadan no ho edwuma no.
Na fa Levifo no ma Aaron nye ne mbabanyin no: wɔdze hɔn ama no koraa wɔ Israelmba no afamu.
Na yi Aaron nye ne mbabanyin no si hɔ, na wɔnhwɛ hɔn asɔfodzi no do: na sɛ ɔhɔho ba ho a wonku no.
Na EWURADZE kasaa kyerɛɛ Moses dɛ, Hwɛ, emi, mafa Levifo no efi Israelmba mu ahyɛ Israelmba mu mbakan a wobue yafun mu no nyinara no ananmu; na Levifo no nyɛ medze: no mbakan nyinara yɛ medze.
Da a mobobɔɔ Egypt asaase do mbakan nyinara no na metseew Israel mu mbakan nyinara ho maa moho, nyimpa nye abowa nyina: wɔyɛ medze; emi nye EWURADZE.
Levifo No Hɔn Nkanee Na EWURADZE kasaa kyerɛɛ Moses wɔ Sinai sar do dɛ, Kan Levimba no dɛ mbrɛ hɔn egyanom efi, nye hɔn ebusua ebusua tsetsee: banyin biara a oedzi bosoom nye ekyir no kan no.
Na Moses kaan hɔn dɛ mbrɛ EWURADZE n’asɛm a ɔhyɛɛ no no tse.
Na iyinom nye Levi mbabanyin dɛ mbrɛ hɔn edzin no tse; Gerson, Kohat, nye Merari.
Na iyinom nye Gerson ne mbabanyin edzin dɛ mbrɛ hɔn ebusua ebusua tsetsee; Libni nye Simei.
Na Kohat mbabanyin dɛ mbrɛ hɔn ebusua ebusua tsetsee; Amram, Izhar, Hebron, nye Uziel.
Na Merari mbabanyin dɛ mbrɛ hɔn ebusua ebusua tsetsee; Mahili nye Musi.
Iyinom nye Levifo ebusua ebusua no dɛ mbrɛ hɔn egyanom efi no tsetsee.
Gerson dze nye Libnifo, nye Simeifo ebusua: iyinom nye Gersonfo ebusua ebusua no.
Hɔn a wɔkaan hɔn wɔ mu no, dɛ mbrɛ mbanyin no nyinara a woedzi bosoom nye ekyir no hɔn dodow tse no, wɔyɛ mpemesuon nye ahaenum.
Gersonfo ebusua ebusua no nkyer nsera wɔ ntamadan no ekyir anee afamu.
Na Lael ne babanyin Eliasaf na ɔnyɛ Gersonfo egyanom efi mu safohen panyin.
Na Gerson ne mbabanyin no hɔn ahwɛdze wɔ ehyiadzibuw no mu nye ntamadan no, nye Buw no, n’akatado, nye ehyiadzibuw no n’abowano nkataano, nye dampan no ne nsensɛnho, nye dampan no n’abowano nkataano no, dza ɔwɔ ntamadan no ho, na otwa afɔrmbukyia no ho hyia no, nye ne ntampehoma wɔ no ho edwuma nyinara ho.
Na Kohat dze nye Amramfo ebusua, Izharfo ebusua, Hebronfo ebusua, nye Uzielfo ebusua: iyinom nye Kohatfo ebusua ebusua no.
Dɛ mbrɛ mbanyin nyinara a woedzi bosoom nye ekyir no hɔn dodow tse no, wɔyɛ mpemawɔtwe nye ahaesia a wɔhwɛ ahotseweebea ahwɛdodze no do.
Kohat ne mbabanyin ebusua ebusua no nkyer nsera wɔ ntamadan no nkyɛn wɔ pomu afamu.
Na Uziel ne mbabanyin Elizafan na ɔnyɛ ɔsafohen panyin wɔ Kohatfo ebusua ebusua no hɔn egyanom fie mu.
Na ahwɛdze nye adaka no, nye pon no, nye kandzeadua no, nye afɔrmbukyia no, nye ahotseweebea ndzɛmba no a wɔdze som no, nye nkataano no, nye no ho edwuma nyinara.
Na ɔsɔfo Aaron ne babanyin Eleazar na nyɛ ɔsafohen panyin wɔ Levifo asafohemfo mu, na ɔnhwɛ hɔn a wɔhwɛ ahotseweebea no do ahwɛdodze do no do.
Merari dze nye Mahilifo ebusua, nye Musfo ebusua: iyinom nye Merari ebusua ebusua no.
Na hɔn a wɔkaan hɔn wɔ mu no, dɛ mbrɛ mbanyin no nyinara a woedzi bosoom nye ekyir no hɔn dodow tse no, wɔyɛ mpemesia nye ahaenu.
Abihail ne babanyin Zuriel nye Merari ebusua ebusua no mu egyanom fi mu safohen panyin: hɔn na wɔnkyer nsera wɔ ntamadan no nkyɛn wɔ kwaamu afamu.
Na ahwɛdodze a wɔahyɛ ama Merari ne mbabanyin no nye ntamadan no ne ntaabow, nye ne ndaban, nye n’edum, nye ne ntaataase, nye no ho ndzɛmba nyinara, nye no ho edwuma nyinara; na dampan no n’edum a ehyia ho no, nye ne ntaease no, nye no mbɔfondua, nye ne ntampehoma.
Na hɔn a wɔnkyer nsera wɔ ntamadan no enyim wɔ boka afamu, wɔ ehyiadzibuw no enyim a odzi kɔ wipuei no, nye Moses, nye Aaron nye ne mbabanyin a wɔhwɛ ahotseweebea ahwɛdodze no ma Israelmba no; na ɔhɔho biara a ɔbɛba ho no wonku no.
Hɔn a wofi Levifo mu a Moses nye Aaron nam EWURADZE ne mbrasɛm do kaan hɔn nyinara, dɛ mbrɛ hɔn ebusua ebusua no tse no, mbanyin a woedzi bosoom nye ekyir no nyinara, wɔyɛ mpemeduonu ebien.
Wɔdze Levifo Pon Mbakan Na EWURADZE see Moses dɛ, Kan Israelmba mu mbakan mbanyin a woedzi bosoom nye ekyir no nyinara, na bu hɔn edzin no dodow ano.
Na fa Levifo no ma me (emi nye EWURADZE) fa hyɛ Israelmba mu mbakan no nyinara ananmu; nye Levifo fiembowa no hyɛ Israelmba fiembowa mu mbakan no nyinara ananmu.
Na Moses kaan Israelmba mu mbakan no nyinara, dɛ mbrɛ EWURADZE hyɛɛ no no.
Na mbakan mbanyin a woedzidzi bosoom nye ekyir, dɛ mbrɛ edzin dodow no tse wɔ hɔn a wɔkaan hɔn wɔ mu no mu no, wɔyɛ mpemeduonu ebien ahaenu eduosuon ebiasa.
Na EWURADZE kasaa kyerɛ, Moses dɛ, Fa Levifo no hyɛ Israelmba mu mbakan no nyinara ananmu, na fa Levifo fiembowa no hyɛ hɔn fiembowa no ananmu: na Levifo no nyɛ medze; emi nye EWURADZE.
Na Israelmba mbakan ahaenu eduosuon ebiasa a wɔbor Levifo no hɔn dodow do no hɔn apondze no dze, gyegye hɔn tsir sika dwetɛbona enum enum dɛ mbrɛ wɔtse nkorkor; mbrɛ ahotseweebea nhyehyɛɛ tse no na gye hɔn (dwetɛbona yɛ gera enum): na fa sika no a wɔdze poon hɔn a wɔbor hɔn do no ma Aaron nye ne mbabanyin no.
Na Moses gyegyee apondze sika no wɔ hɔn a wɔbor hɔn a Levifo poon hɔn no hɔ: Israelmba mbakan hɔ na ɔgyegyee sika no; dwetɛbona apem ahaasa eduosia enum, dɛ mbrɛ ahotseweebea dwetɛbona tse: na Moses dze apondze sika no maa Aaron nye ne mbabanyin no, dɛ mbrɛ EWURADZE n’asɛm a ɔhyɛɛ Moses no tse no.
Kohatfo No Na EWURADZE kasaa kyerɛɛ Moses nye Aaron dɛ.
Bu Kohat ne mbabanyin no ano fa fi Levi mbabanyin no mu, dɛ mbrɛ hɔn ebusua ebusua, nye hɔn egyanom efi tsetsee, ofi hɔn a woedzi mfe eduasa nye ekyir do kodu hɔn a woedzi mfe eduonum do, hɔn a wɔhɛn ɔsom no mu kɛyɛ edwuma wɔ ehyiadzibuw no mu no nyinara.
Iyi nye Kohat ne mbabanyin no hɔn edwuma wɔ ehyiadzibuw no mu, wɔ krɔnkrɔndze mu adzekrɔnkrɔn ho: sɛ nseraban no rubotu a, Aaron nye ne mbabanyin no na wɔnkɔ mu, na wonkeyi ntwamutam nkataano no, na wɔmfa nkata dasedaka no do: na wɔmfa esukraman nwoma akatado nto do, na wɔmfa tam a ne nyinara yɛ bibir nkata do, na wɔmfa no mpoma no nhyehyɛ mu.
Na wɔmfa tam bibir nkata ɔkyerɛpaanoo pon no do, na wɔmfa nkwansɛn no, nye ntser no, nye nkora, nye nkɔɔpow a wɔdze hue no nsisi do: na daa daa paanoo no nsi do: na wɔmfa tam memen nkata do, na wɔmfa esukraman nwoma akatado nkata ho, na wɔmfa no mpoma no nhyehyɛ mu.
Na wɔmfa tam bibir, nkata kandzea no ne kandzeadua nye ne nkandzea, nye n’adabaa, nye no nsompokuwa no, nye no ngo ntoaba nyinara a wɔdze som no ho: na wɔmfa ɔno nye no ho adze nyinara nhyɛ esukraman nwoma akatado mu, na wɔmfa nto pata no do.
Wɔmfa tam bibir nkata sika afɔrmbukyia no do, na wɔmfa esukraman nwoma akatado nkata do, na wɔmfa no mpoma no nhyehyɛ mu: na wɔmfa ɔsom ho ndzɛmba nyinara a wɔdze som wɔ ahotseweebea no nhyɛ tam bibir mu, na wɔmfa esukraman nwoma akatado nkata ho, na wɔmfa nto pata no do.
Na wɔnsesaw nso no wɔ afɔrmbukyia no do, na wɔmfa tam ɔberdum nkata do: na wɔmfa no ho ndzɛmba nyinara a wɔdze som wɔ ho no ngu do, ogyasɛn, edzinam, nye nsofi, nye mbɛɛsen, afɔrmbukyia no ho ndzɛmba no nyinara; na wɔmfa esukraman nwoma akatado nkata do, na wɔmfa no mpoma no nhyehyɛ mu.
Na sɛ nseraban no rubotu, na Aaron nye ne mbabanyin no wie ahotseweebea no, nye ahotseweebea no ho ndzɛmba no nyinara do kata a; nna nkyii Kohat ne mbabanyin no mbra mbɔsoa: ahotseweebea no dze mma wɔnnka, amma woeennwuwu.
Ndzɛmba yi nye Kohat ne mbabanyin no hɔn adzesoa wɔ ehyiadzibuw no mu.
Na ɔsɔfo Aaron ne babanyin Eleazar n’ahwɛdodze nye kandzea no ho ngo no, nduhuanhuam no, daa daa edziban afɔr no, ɔserango no, ntamadan no nye dza ɔayɛ no krɔnkrɔn a ɔwɔ mu no nyinara.
Na EWURADZE kasaa kyerɛɛ Moses nye Aaron dɛ, Hom nhwɛ ma wontwa Kohatfo ebusua ebusua mu ebusuakuw no mmfi Levifo no mu: na dza hom nyɛ mma hɔn ama woeenya nkwa na woeennwuwu, sɛ wɔbɛn krɔnkrɔndze mu adzekrɔnkrɔn no a: Aaron nye ne mbabanyin no nhɛn mu, na wɔmfa hɔn nsisi obiara n’edwuma nye n’adzesoa ho: na hɔn dze, mma wɔnnhɛn mu nnkɔhwɛ ahotseweebea no dɛ enyi robɔ do mpo, amma woeennwuwu.
Gersonfo Na EWURADZE kasaa kyerɛɛ Moses dɛ, Bu Gerson mbabanyin no so ano, dɛ mbrɛ hɔn egyanom efi, nye hɔn ebusua ebusua tsetsee; ofi hɔn a woedzi mfe eduasa nye ekyir do kodu hɔn a woedzi mfe eduonum do na kan hɔn; hɔn a wɔhɛn mu kɔsom dɛ wɔkɛyɛ edwuma wɔ ehyiadzibuw no mu no nyinara.
Iyi nye Gersonfo ebusua ebusua hɔn som wɔ ɔsom nye ndzesoa soa mu.
Hɔn na wɔnsoa ntamadan no ne nsensɛnho atam no, nye ehyiadzibuw no, ne nkatado, nye esukraman nwoma akatado no a ɔwɔ do wɔ sor no, nye ehyiadzibuw no n’abowano nkataano; nye pampan no ne nsensɛnho no, nye pampan no n’abotsen abowano nkataano, dza etwa ntamadan no nye afɔrmbukyia no ho ehyia no, nye ne ntampehoma, nye no ho edwuma ho ndzɛmba nyinara, nye biribiara a wɔdze bɛyɛ no, no mu na wɔnsom.
Aaron nye ne mbabanyin mbrasɛm do na Gersonfo mbabanyin no nyɛ hɔn edwuma nyinara, wɔ hɔn adzesoa nyinara, nye hɔn edwuma nyinara mu: na hom mfa hɔn adzesoa nyinara nhyɛ hɔn nsa ma wɔnhwɛ do.
Iyi nye Gersonfo mbabanyin ebusua ebusua no hɔn edwuma wɔ ehyiadzibuw no mu: na hɔn ahwɛdodze wɔ ɔsɔfo Aaron ne babanyin Itamar nsamu.
Merarifo Merari ne mbabanyin no dze, kan hɔn dɛ mbrɛ hɔn ebusua ebusua, nye hɔn egyanom efi tsetsee; ofi hɔn a woedzi mfe eduasa nye ekyir do kodu hɔn a woedzi mfe eduonum do no mu, obiara a ɔhɛn ɔsom no mu, dɛ ɔkɛyɛ edwuma wɔ ehyiadzibuw no mu no.
Na iyi nye hɔn adzesoa ahwɛdodze, dɛ mbrɛ hɔn edwuma nyinara tse wɔ ehyiadzibuw no mu; ntamadan no ne ntaabow, nye n’adaban, nye n’edum, nye ne ngyinado na kan hɔn; na pampan no n’edum a etwa ho ehyia no, nye ne ngyinado, nye no mbɔfondua, nye ne ntampehoma, ɔnye no ho ndzɛmba nyinara, na ɔnye n’edwuma nyinara: na hom mfa hɔn adzesoa ahwɛdodze ndzɛmba no mbɔ dzin nhyɛ hɔn nsa.
Iyi nye Merari mbabanyin ebusua ebusua edwuma, dɛ mbrɛ hɔn edwuma nyinara tse, wɔ ehyiadzibuw no mu, wɔ ɔsɔfo Aaron ne babanyin Itamar nsamu.
Na Moses nye Aaron nye mboanofo no mu mbapɔmba no kaan Kohatfo mbabanyin no dɛ mbrɛ hɔn ebusua ebusua, nye hɔn egyanom efi tsetsee, ofi hɔn a woedzi mfe eduasa nye ekyir do kodu hɔn a woedzi mfe eduonum do, dɛ ɔkɛyɛ edwuma wɔ ehyiadzibuw no mu no: na hɔn a wɔkaan hɔn wɔ mu dɛ mbrɛ hɔn ebusua ebusua tsetsee no wɔyɛ mpemebien ahaesuon eduonum.
Iyinom nye hɔn a wɔkaan hɔn wɔ Kohatfo ebusua ebusua mu, hɔn a wɔsoom wɔ ehyiadzibuw no mu nyinara a Moses nye Aaron nam EWURADZE mbrasɛm a ɔwɔ Moses nsamu no do kanee no.
Na hɔn a wɔkaan hɔn wɔ Gerson mbabanyin mu, dɛ mbrɛ hɔn ebusua ebusua, nye hɔn egyanom efi tsetsee, ofi hɔn a woedzi mfe eduasa nye ekyir do kodu hɔn a woedzi mfe eduonum do, obiara a ɔhɛn ɔsom no mu, dɛ ɔkɛyɛ edwuma wɔ ehyiadzibuw no mu no, dɛ mbrɛ hɔn ebusua, nye hɔn egyanom efi tsetsee no, wɔyɛ mpemebien nye ahaesia eduasa.
Iyinom nye hɔn a wɔkaan hɔn wɔ Gerson ne mbabanyin ebusua ebusua mu, hɔn a wɔsomee wɔ ehyiadzibuw no mu nyinara a Moses nye Aaron nam EWURADZE mbrasɛm do kanee no.
Na hɔn a wɔkaan hɔn wɔ Merari mbabanyin ebusua ebusua mu, dɛ mbrɛ ebusua ebusua nye hɔn egyanom efi tsetsee, ofi hɔn a woedzi mfe eduasa nye ekyir kodu hɔn a woedzi mfe eduonum do, obiara a ɔhɛn ɔsom no mu, dɛ ɔkɛyɛ edwuma wɔ ehyiadzibuw no mu no, dɛ mbrɛ hɔn ebusua ebusua tse a wɔkaan hɔn no, wɔyɛ mpemebiasa nye ahaenu.
Iyinom nye hɔn a wɔkaan hɔn wɔ Merari ne mbabanyin ebusua ebusua a Moses nye Aaron nam EWURADZE mbrasɛm a ɔwɔ Moses nsamu no do kanee no.
Hɔn a wɔkaan hɔn wɔ Levifo mu nyinara a Moses nye Aaron nye Israel mbapɔmba no kanee, dɛ mbrɛ hɔn ebusua ebusua, nye hɔn egyanom efi tsetsee, ofi hɔn a woedzi mfe eduasa nye ekyir do kodu hɔn a woedzi mfe eduonum do, obiara a ɔhɛn mu dɛ ɔkɛyɛ ɔsom edwuma, nye ndzesoa soa mu edwuma wɔ ehyiadzibuw no mu a wɔkaan hɔn no, wɔyɛ mpemawɔtwe ahaenum eduawɔtwe.
Dɛ mbrɛ EWURADZE mbrasɛm tse na wɔnam Moses nsa do kaan hɔn, obiara dɛ mbrɛ no som tse, nye mbrɛ n’adzesoa tse no ara: dɛm na kaan hɔn, dɛ mbrɛ EWURADZE hyɛɛ no no.
Nkorɔfo A Hɔn Ho Nntsew Na EWURADZE kasaa kyerɛɛ Moses dɛ, Hyɛ Israelmba ma wontu ɔkwatanyi biara, nye obiara a ɔwɔ ahosen, nye onyia biara a ɔdze fun egu noho fi, mfi nseraban no mu: ɔbanyin o ɔbaa o hom ntu no.
Nseraban no ekyir na hom ntu hɔn nkogu amma woeenngu hɔn nseraban a metse ne finimfin no ho fi.
Na Israelmba no yɛɛ dɛmara, na wotuu hɔn koguu nseraban ekyir: na dɛ mbrɛ EWURADZE kasaa kyerɛɛ Moses no, dɛmara na Israelmba no yɛe.
Mfom Ho Asɛm Na EWURADZE kasaa kyerɛɛ Moses dɛ, Kasa kyerɛ Israelmba dɛ, Sɛ ɔbanyin anaa ɔbaa yɛ bɔn tsia nyimpa bi, dze fom EWURADZE, na ɔkra no dzi so a; ɔno ɔmpaa mu nka hɔn bɔn a wɔayɛ no: na ontua n’asodzidze no imu, na ɔmfa no mu ebupɛn enum mu kor nto do, na ɔmfa mma nyia ɔafom no edzi so no.
Mbom sɛ nyimpa no ewu na onnyi bɔgya bi a ɔbɛn no a wɔdze asodzidze bɛma no wɔ asodzi no ntsi a, asodzi no ho asodzidze no yɛ EWURADZE dze na ɔnyɛ ɔsɔfo no dze; nka mpata oguannyin no a wɔdze rebɛpata ama no no ho.
Na ɔtow afɔr biara a ɔwɔ Israelmba adzekrɔnkrɔn nyinara mu a wɔdze brɛ ɔsɔfo no, nyɛ nedze.
Na nyimpa biara n’adzekrɔnkrɔn a ɔdze ba no yɛ ɔsɔfo no dze: biribiara a nyimpa biara dze ma ɔsɔfo no, nedze ara na ɔnyɛ.
Nyinkun Ho Asɛm Na EWURADZE kasaa kyerɛɛ Moses dɛ, Kasa kyerɛ Israelmba, na se hɔn dɛ, Sɛ ɔbanyin bi ne yer fi ne nkyɛn, na ɔkɔfom no, na ɔbanyin bi nye no da dze no ho nsu ma no, na wɔdze suma no kun, na wosiw do, na ogu noho fi, na no ho ɔdasefo bi nnyi hɔ, nkyii so wɔannkyer no wɔ do; na nyinkun sunsum ba no do, na ɔtwe ne yer no ho nyinkun, na sɛ basia no egu noho fi ampa: anaa sɛ nyinkun sunsum ba no do, na ɔtwe ne yer no ho nyinkun, na sɛ basia no nguu noho fi a: ɔno ɔbanyin no mfa ne yer no mbrɛ ɔsɔfo no, na ɔmfa no ho ayɛyɛdze mbra, atoko isiam efa ebupɛn du mu kor; mma ɔmmfa ngo nngu do, na ɔmmfa krɔbɔw so nnto do; osiandɛ ɔyɛ nyinkun ho edziban afɔr na nkaa ho edziban afɔr, a wɔdze kaa emumuyɛ.
Na ɔsɔfo no mfa no mbɛn, na ɔmfa no mbegyina EWURADZE enyim: na ɔsɔfo no mfa nsu krɔnkrɔn ngu dɛtse kɔɔpow bi mu; na ɔsɔfo no mfa ntamadan no ne daadze huntuma no bi, ngu nsu no mu: na ɔsɔfo no mfa ɔbaa no ngyina EWURADZE enyim, na ontutu ɔbaa no ne tsinhwi ngu do, na ɔmfa nkaa edziban afɔr no a ɔyɛ nyinkun edziban afɔr no nhyɛ ne nsamu: na ɔsɔfo no nkitsa nsu wenwen a ɔdze ndom ba no wɔ ne nsamu.
Na ɔsɔfo no mma ondzi nsew, na ɔnse ɔbaa no dɛ, Sɛ banyin bi nnye wo nndae, na sɛ immfii wo kun nkyɛn nnkoguu woho fi a, wo ho nyɛ tɔtrɔtɔ wɔ nsu wenwen a ɔdze ndom ba yi ho: mbom sɛ efi wo kun nkyɛn, ber a ewar wo kun yi na sɛ ekogu woho fi, na banyin bi nye wo ada ka wo kun ho a: ɔno ɔsɔfo no mma ɔbaa no mfa ndom ntam ndzi nsew, na ɔsɔfo no nse ɔbaa no dɛ, EWURADZE nyɛ wo dzin ndom nye ntam wɔ wo man mu, aber a EWURADZE bɛma w’aserɛ atotɔ mu, na wo yafun ahon.
Na nsu a ɔdze ndom ba yi akɛhɛn wo nson mu, na ɔama wo yafun ahon, na w’aserɛ atotɔ mu: na ɔbaa no nse dɛ, Amen, Amen.
Na ɔsɔfo no nkyerɛw ndom yi wɔ nwoma mu, na ɔmpepa ngu nsu wenwen no mu: na ɔmma ɔbaa no nnom nsu wenwen a ɔdze ndom ba no: na nsu a ɔdze ndom ba no nkɔ no mu nkɛyɛ wenwen.
Na ɔsɔfo no ngye nyinkun ho edziban afɔr no wɔ ɔbaa no nsamu, na ɔntow edziban afɔr no wɔ EWURADZE enyim, na ɔmfa mbra afɔrmbukyia no ho; na ɔsɔfo no mfa edziban afɔr no mu nsapuw, dɛ ne nkaadze, na ɔnhyew no wɔ afɔrmbukyia no do, na n’ekyir no ɔmma ɔbaa no nnom nsu no.
Na ɔbɛba dɛ aber a ɔama ɔanom nsu no, sɛ oegu noho fi na ɔayɛ bɔn etsia no kun a, nsu no a ɔdze ndom ba no bɛhɛn no mu akɛyɛ wenwen, na ne yafun ahon, na n’aserɛ atotɔ mu: na ɔbaa no ayɛ ndom wɔ ne man mu.
Na sɛ ɔbaa no ho enngu fi, na no ho tsew dze a; ɔno no ho bɛyɛ tɔtrɔtɔ, na oenyinsen ɔba.
Iyi nye nyinkun ho mbra, sɛ ɔyer bi fi no kun nkyɛn na okogu noho fi; anaa sɛ nyinkun sunsum ba banyin bi do, na ɔtwe ne yer ho nyinkun a; ɔno ɔmfa ɔbaa no mbegyina EWURADZE enyim, na ɔsɔfo no nyɛ no mbra yi mu adze nyinara.
Na ɔbanyin no ho bɛyɛ tɔtrɔtɔ wɔ emumuyɛ ho, na ɔbaa no asoa n’emumuyɛ.
Nazirinyiyɛ Ho Mbra Na EWURADZE kasaa kyerɛɛ Moses dɛ, Kasa kyerɛ Israelmba, na se hɔn dɛ, Sɛ ɔbanyin anaa ɔbaa bi bɔ anohoba soronko, Nazirinyi anohoba, dɛ orutu noho dze ama EWURADZE a: ɔnkam noho wɔ wenyin nye nsa dzendzen ho: mma ɔnnom wenyin kawee, anaa nsa dzendzen kawee, nkyii so mma ɔnnom esikyireamba nsa biara, na onndzi esikyireamba momon anaa guanee so.
Noho nkamee nda nyinara mu mma onndzi biribiara a wɔdze wenyindua ho biribi ayɛ, no nsowee mu aba o, no ho ahon o. Noho nkamee anohoba nda nyinara mu no mma oyindam bi nnka ne tsir: ɔnyɛ krɔnkrɔn nkodu dɛ nda a ɔkaam noho maa EWURADZE wɔ mu no bɔso, onsie etsimum.
Nda a ɔakam noho ama EWURADZE no nyinara mma ɔnnkɔ nyimpa bi fun ho.
Sɛ n’egya, anaa ne na, no nua anaa n’akyerɛbaa mpo wuwu a, mma onnkogu noho fi: osiandɛ noho nkamee a ɔdze ma Nyankopɔn no wɔ n’etsifi.
Noho nkamee nda nyinara ɔyɛ krɔnkrɔn ma EWURADZE.
Na sɛ nyimpa bi wu awerɛfir mu wɔ ne nkyɛn, na ogu noho nkamee tsir ho fi a; ɔno da a otsia esuon no onyi ne tsir wɔ n’ahoguar da no mu.
Na da a otsia awɔtwe no ɔmfa ntamram ebien, anaa mborɔnomamba ebien, mbrɛ ɔsɔfo no, wɔ ehyiadzibuw no n’abowano: na ɔsɔfo no mfa kor mbɔ bɔn ho afɔr, na kor no so ɔmfa nyɛ ɔhyew afɔr, na ɔmpata mma no, dɛ ɔafom wɔ fun no ho, na ɔntsew ne tsir ho da no ara.
Na ɔnsan nkam noho mma EWURADZE, na ɔmfa eguambaanyin a oedzi afrenhyia mbra mbɔbɔ asodzi ho afɔr: mbom nkan no nda no ayɛ kwa, osiandɛ noho nkamee no ho egu fi.
Na iyi nye Nazirinyi ho mbra, aber a noho nkamee nda ewie du no: wɔmfa no mbra ehyiadzibuw no n’abowano: na ɔmfa ayɛyɛdze mbrɛ EWURADZE, eguambaanyin a oedzi afrenhyia a onndzii dzɛm kor mbɔbɔ ɔhyew afɔr, na eguambaaber a oedzi afrenhyia a onndzii dzɛm kor mbɔbɔ bɔn ho afɔr, nye oguannyin a onndzii dzɛm kor mbɔbɔ asomdwee afɔr, nye epitsi boodoo kɛntsɛn no, nye isiam pa tatar a wɔdze ngo afrɔw, nye epitsi tatar ntrɛtraba a wɔdze ngo egu do, nye n’edziban afɔr, nye no nom afɔr.
Na ɔsɔfo no mfa mbra EWURADZE enyim, na ɔmbɔ no bɔn ho afɔr, nye ne hyew afɔr: na ɔmfa oguannyin no mbɔ asomdwee afɔr mma EWURADZE, nka epitsi boodoo kɛntsɛn no ho: ɔsɔfo no mbɔ n’edziban afɔr, nye no nom afɔr no so.
Na Nazirinyi no nyi ne tsir no wɔ ehyiadzibuw no n’abowano, na ɔmfa ne tsinhwi no ngu ogya no a ɔwɔ asomdwee afɔr ase no mu.
Na oeyi ne tsir no ekyir no, ɔsɔfo no mfa oguannyin abasa a wɔanoa, nye kɛntsɛn no mu epitsi tatar kor, na epitsi tatar ntrɛtraba kor ngu Nazirinyi no nsamu, na ɔsɔfo no ntow no ɔtow afɔr wɔ EWURADZE enyim; iyi yɛ krɔnkrɔn ma ɔsɔfo no dze ka ɔtow nyan nye ohim aserɛ no ho: na ɔno ekyir no Nazirinyi no nnom wenyin.
Iyi nye mbra a ɔwɔ hɔ ma Nazirinyi na mbom sɛ ɔbɔ anohoba bi ka dza Nazirinyi yɛ no ho a, otwar dɛ ɔpon dɛm anohoba no ka dza noho nkamee nhyehyɛɛ no kyerɛ no.
Mbrɛ Asɔfo No Nsi Nhyira Na EWURADZE kasaa kyerɛɛ Moses dɛ, Kasa kyerɛ Aaron nye ne mbabanyin no dɛ, Mbrɛ hom nsi nhyira Israelmba no nye yi; hom nse hɔn dɛ, EWURADZE nhyira wo, na ɔnhwɛ wo do: EWURADZE ntsew n’enyim nkyerɛ wo, na ɔndom wo: EWURADZE mma n’enyi do nhwɛ wo, na ɔmma wo asomdwee.
Na wɔmfa me dzin nto Israelmba do dɛm; na mibehyira hɔn.
Mbapɔmba No Hɔn Ayɛyɛdze Na ɔbaa dɛ da a Moses wiee ntamadan no si, na ɔseraa ho ngo na ɔtseew ɔno, nye no ho ndzɛmba nyinara, nye afɔrmbukyia no no ho ndzɛmba nyinara ho, na ɔseraa ho ngo na ɔtseew ho no; nna Israel mbapɔmba, hɔn egyanom efi mu etsitsir no, bɔɔ afɔr; iyinom nye ebusuakuw ebusuakuw do asafohen mpanyin, iyinom nye hɔn a wɔhwɛɛ hɔn a wɔkaan hɔn no do no: na wɔdze hɔn ayɛyɛdze baa EWURADZE enyim, ntseaseanam a wɔakata do esia, nye anantwi duebien; mbapɔmba beenu dze tseaseanam kor, na ɔbaako ɔnantwi kor: na wɔdze baa ntamadan no enyim.
Na EWURADZE kasaa kyerɛɛ Moses dɛ, Gye no wɔ hɔn nsamu, ma wɔmfa nyɛ ehyiadzibuw no ho edwuma; na fa ma Levifo no, dɛ mbrɛ nyimpa biara n’edwuma tse.
Na Moses gyee ntseaseanam no nye anantwi no na ɔdze maa Levifo no.
Ntseaseanam ebien nye anantwi anan na ɔdze maa Gerson mbabanyin no, dɛ mbrɛ hɔn edwuma tse: na ɔdze ntseaseanam anan nye anantwi awɔtwe maa Merari mbabanyin no, dɛ mbrɛ hɔn edwuma tse, wɔ ɔsɔfo Aaron ne babanyin Itamar nsamu.
Na Kohat mbabanyin no dze ɔamma hɔn bi: osiandɛ ahotseweebea edwuma no yɛ hɔndze; hɔn na wɔsoa no wɔ hɔn mbatsir do.
Na mbapɔmba no dze afɔrmbukyia oyimadze bae wɔ da a wɔseraa ho ngo no mu, mekyerɛ mbapɔmba no dze hɔn ayɛyɛdze baa afɔrmbukyia no enyim.
Na EWURADZE see Moses dɛ, Wɔmfa hɔn ayɛyɛdze mbra, ɔbapɔmba kor biara wɔ ne da mu, mfa mbɛyɛ afɔrmbukyia oyimadze.
Na nyia ɔdze n’ayɛyɛdze baa da a odzi kan no nye Aminadab a ofi Juda ebusuakuw mu no ne babanyin Nahson: na n’ayɛyɛdze nye dwetɛboyaa kor, n’ano tow dwetɛbona ɔha eduasa, dwetɛkora kor a ɔyɛ dwetɛbona eduosuon, dɛ mbrɛ ahotseweebea dwetɛbona tse: na ebien nyina isiam pa a wɔdze ngo afrɔw dze rekɛyɛ edziban afɔr ayeyɛ no amaama; sika atser kor a ɔyɛ dwetɛbona du a eduhuam ayɛ no ma; ɔnantwisaa eburwa kor, oguannyin kor, eguambaanyin kor a oedzi afrenhyia a wɔdze rokɔbɔ ɔhyew afɔr; mpɔnkye mu onyin kor a wɔdze rokɔbɔ bɔn ho afɔr; nye asomdwee afɔr dze, anantwi ebien, nguannyin enum, mpɔnkyenyin enum, nguambaanyin enum a woedzi afrenhyia afrenhyia: iyi nye Aminadab ne babanyin Nahson n’ayɛyɛdze.
Da a otsia ebien no Zuar ne babanyin Netanel, Isakar ɔbapɔmba no, dze n’ayɛyɛdze bae.
N’ayɛyɛdze a ɔdze bae nye dwetɛboyaa kor, n’ano tow dwetɛbona ɔha eduasa, dwetɛkora kor a ɔyɛ dwetɛbona eduosuon, dɛ mbrɛ ahotseweebea dwetɛbona tse; ebien nyina isiam pa a wɔdze ngo afrɔw dze rekɛyɛ edziban afɔr ayeyɛ no amaama; sika atser kor a ɔyɛ dwetɛbona du a eduhuam ayɛ no ma; ɔnantwisaa eburwa kor, oguannyin kor, eguambaanyin kor a oedzi afrenhyia a wɔdze rokɔbɔ ɔhyew afɔr; mpɔnkye mu onyin kor a wɔdze rokɔbɔ bɔn ho afɔr: nye asomdwee afɔr dze, anantwi ebien, nguannyin enum, mpɔnkyenyin enum, na nguambaanyin enum a woedzi afrenhyia afrenhyia: iyi nye Zuar ne babanyin Netanel n’ayɛyɛdze.
Da a otsia ebiasa no Helon ne babanyin Eliab, Zebulunmba mu ɔbapɔmba no dze n’ayɛyɛdze bae.
N’ayɛyɛdze nye dwetɛboyaa kor a n’ano tow dwetɛbona ɔha eduasa, dwetɛkora kor a ɔyɛ dwetɛbona eduosuon, dɛ mbrɛ ahotseweebea dwetɛbona tse: ebien nyina isiam pa a wɔdze ngo afrɔw dze rekɛyɛ edziban afɔr ayeyɛ no amaama; sika atser kor a ɔyɛ dwetɛbona du a eduhuam ayɛ no ma; ɔnantwisaa eburwa kor, oguannyin kor, eguambaanyin kor a oedzi afrenhyia a wɔdze rokɔbɔ ɔhyew afɔr; mpɔnkye mu onyin kor a wɔdze rokɔbɔ bɔn ho afɔr; nye asomdwee afɔr dze, anantwi ebien, nguannyin enum, mpɔnkyenyin enum na nguambaanyin enum a woedzi afrenhyia afrenhyia: iyi nye Helon ne babanyin Eliab n’ayɛyɛdze.
Da a otsia anan no yɛ Sedeur ne babanyin Elizur, Reubenmba mu ɔbapɔmba: n’ayɛyɛdze nye dwetɛboyaa kor, n’ano tow dwetɛbona ɔha eduasa, dwetɛkora a ɔyɛ dwetɛbona eduosuon, dɛ mbrɛ ahotseweebea dwetɛbona tse; n’ebien nyina isiam pa a wɔdze ngo afrɔw dze rekɛyɛ edziban afɔr ayeyɛ no amaama; sika atser kor a ɔyɛ dwetɛbona du a eduhuam ayɛ no ma; ɔnantwisaa eburwa kor, oguannyin kor, eguambaanyin kor a oedzi afrenhyia a wɔdze rokɔbɔ ɔhyew afɔr; mpɔnkye mu onyin kor a wɔdze rokɔbɔ bɔn ho afɔr; nye asomdwee afɔr dze, anantwi ebien, nguannyin enum, mpɔnkyenyin enum na nguambaanyin enum a woedzi afrenhyia afrenhyia: iyi nye Sedeur ne babanyin Elizur n’ayɛyɛdze.
Da a otsia enum no Zurisadai ne babanyin Selumiel, Simeonmba mu ɔbapɔmba na ɔbae: n’ayɛyɛdze nye dwetɛboyaa kor, n’ano tow dwetɛbona ɔha eduasa, dwetɛkora kor a ɔyɛ dwetɛbona eduosuon, dɛ mbrɛ ahotseweebea dwetɛbona tse; na ebien nyina isiam pa a wɔdze ngo afrɔw dze rekɛyɛ edziban afɔr ayeyɛ no amaama; sika atser kor a ɔyɛ dwetɛbona du a eduhuam ayɛ no ma; ɔnantwisaa eburwa kor, oguannyin kor, eguambaanyin kor a oedzi afrenhyia a wɔdze rokɔbɔ ɔhyew afɔr; mpɔnkye mu onyin kor a wɔdze rokɔbɔ bɔn ho afɔr; nye asomdwee afɔr dze, anantwi ebien, nguannyin enum, mpɔnkyenyin enum na nguambaanyin enum a woedzi afrenhyia afrenhyia: iyi nye Zurisadai ne babanyin Selumiel n’ayɛyɛdze.
Da a otsia esia no yɛ Deutel ne babanyin Eliasaf, Gadmba mu ɔbapɔmba no da: n’ayɛyɛdze nye dwetɛboyaa kor a n’ano tow dwetɛbona ɔha eduasa, dwetɛkora kor a ɔyɛ dwetɛbona eduosuon, dɛ mbrɛ ahotseweebea dwetɛbona tse; na ebien nyina isiam pa a wɔdze ngo afrɔw dze rekɛyɛ edziban afɔr ayeyɛ no amaama; sika atser kor a ɔyɛ dwetɛbona du a eduhuam ayɛ no ma; ɔnantwisaa eburwa kor, oguannyin kor, eguambaanyin kor a oedzi afrenhyia a wɔdze rokɔbɔ ɔhyew afɔr; mpɔnkye mu onyin kor a wɔdze rokɔbɔ bɔn ho afɔr; nye asomdwee afɔr dze, anantwi ebien, nguannyin enum, mpɔnkyenyin enum na nguambaanyin enum a woedzi afrenhyia afrenhyia: iyi nye Deutel ne babanyin Eliasaf n’ayɛyɛdze.
Da a otsia esuon no Ammihud ne babanyin Elisama, Efraimmba mu ɔbapɔmba no na ɔbae: n’ayɛyɛdze nye dwetɛboyaa kor, n’ano tow dwetɛbona ɔha eduasa, dwetɛkora kor a ɔyɛ dwetɛbona eduosuon, dɛ mbrɛ ahotseweebea dwetɛbona tse; na ebien nyina isiam pa a wɔdze ngo afrɔw dze rekɛyɛ edziban afɔr ayeyɛ no amaama; sika atser kor a ɔyɛ dwetɛbona du a eduhuam ayɛ no ma; ɔnantwisaa eburwa kor, oguannyin kor, eguambaanyin kor a oedzi afrenhyia a wɔdze rokɔbɔ ɔhyew afɔr; mpɔnkye mu onyin kor a wɔdze rokɔbɔ bɔn ho afɔr; nye asomdwee afɔr dze, anantwi ebien, nguannyin enum, mpɔnkyenyin enum na nguambaanyin enum a woedzi afrenhyia afrenhyia: iyi nye Ammihud ne babanyin Elisama n’ayɛyɛdze.
Da a otsia awɔtwe no Pedazur ne babanyin Gamaliel, Manaasɛmba mu ɔbapɔmba no na ɔbae: n’ayɛyɛdze nye dwetɛboyaa kor, n’ano tow dwetɛbona ɔha eduasa, dwetɛkora kor a ɔyɛ dwetɛbona eduosuon, dɛ mbrɛ ahotseweebea dwetɛbona tse; na ebien nyina isiam pa a wɔdze ngo afrɔw dze rekɛyɛ edziban afɔr ayeyɛ no amaama; sika atser kor a ɔyɛ dwetɛbona du a eduhuam ayɛ no ma; ɔnantwisaa eburwa kor, oguannyin kor, eguambaanyin kor a oedzi afrenhyia a wɔdze rokɔbɔ ɔhyew afɔr; mpɔnkye mu onyin kor a wɔdze rokɔbɔ bɔn ho afɔr; nye asomdwee afɔr dze, anantwi ebien, nguannyin enum, mpɔnkyenyin enum na nguambaanyin enum a woedzi afrenhyia afrenhyia: iyi nye Pedazur ne babanyin Gamaliel n’ayɛyɛdze.
Da a otsia akron no Gideoni ne babanyin Abidan, Benjaminmba mu ɔbapɔmba no na ɔbae: n’ayɛyɛdze nye dwetɛboyaa kor, n’ano tow dwetɛbona ɔha eduasa, dwetɛkora kor a ɔyɛ dwetɛbona eduosuon, dɛ mbrɛ ahotseweebea dwetɛbona tse; ebien nyina isiam pa a wɔdze ngo afrɔw dze rekɛyɛ edziban afɔr ayeyɛ no amaama; sika atser a ɔyɛ dwetɛbona du a eduhuam ayɛ no ma; ɔnantwisaa eburwa kor, oguannyin kor, eguambaanyin kor a oedzi afrenhyia a wɔdze rokɔbɔ ɔhyew afɔr; mpɔnkye mu onyin kor a wɔdze rokɔbɔ bɔn ho afɔr; nye asomdwee afɔr dze, anantwi ebien, nguannyin enum, mpɔnkyenyin enum na nguambaanyin enum a woedzi afrenhyia afrenhyia: iyi nye Gideoni ne babanyin Abidan n’ayɛyɛdze.
Da a otsia du no Ammisaddai ne babanyin Ahiezer, Danmba mu ɔbapɔmba: n’ayɛyɛdze nye dwetɛboyaa kor, n’ano tow dwetɛbona ɔha eduasa, dwetɛkora kor a ɔyɛ dwetɛbona eduosuon, dɛ mbrɛ ahotseweebea dwetɛbona tse; n’ebien nyina isiam pa a wɔdze ngo afrɔw dze rekɛyɛ edziban afɔr ayeyɛ no amaama; sika atser kor a ɔyɛ dwetɛbona du a eduhuam ayɛ no ma; ɔnantwisaa eburwa kor, oguannyin kor, eguambaanyin kor a oedzi afrenhyia a wɔdze rokɔbɔ ɔhyew afɔr; mpɔnkye mu onyin kor a wɔdze rokɔbɔ bɔn ho afɔr; nye asomdwee afɔr dze, anantwi ebien, nguannyin enum, mpɔnkyenyin enum na nguambaanyin enum a woedzi afrenhyia afrenhyia: iyi nye Ammisaddai ne babanyin Ahiezer n’ayɛyɛdze.
Da a otsia dubiako no Okran ne babanyin Pagiel, Asermba mu ɔbapɔmba: n’ayɛyɛdze nye dwetɛboyaa kor, n’ano tow dwetɛbona ɔha eduasa, dwetɛkora kor a ɔyɛ dwetɛbona eduosuon, dɛ mbrɛ ahotseweebea dwetɛbona tse; ebien nyina isiam pa a wɔdze ngo afrɔw dze rekɛyɛ edziban afɔr ayeyɛ no amaama; sika atser kor a ɔyɛ dwetɛbona du a eduhuam ayɛ no ma; ɔnantwisaa eburwa kor, oguannyin kor, eguambaanyin kor a oedzi afrenhyia a wɔdze rokɔbɔ ɔhyew afɔr; mpɔnkye mu onyin kor a wɔdze rokɔbɔ bɔn ho afɔr; nye asomdwee afɔr dze, anantwi ebien, nguannyin enum, mpɔnkyenyin enum na nguambaanyin enum a woedzi afrenhyia afrenhyia: iyi nye Okran ne babanyin Pagiel n’ayɛyɛdze.
Da a otsia duebien no Enam ne babanyin Ahira, Naftalimba mu ɔbapɔmba no ne da a: n’ayɛyɛdze nye dwetɛboyaa kor, n’ano tow dwetɛbona ɔha eduasa, dwetɛkora kor a ɔyɛ dwetɛbona eduosuon, dɛ mbrɛ ahotseweebea dwetɛbona tse; n’ebien nyina isiam pa a wɔdze ngo afrɔw dze rekɛyɛ edziban afɔr ayeyɛ no amaama; sika atser kor a ɔyɛ dwetɛbona du a eduhuam ayɛ no ma; ɔnantwisaa eburwa kor, oguannyin kor, eguambaanyin kor a oedzi afrenhyia a wɔdze rokɔbɔ ɔhyew afɔr; mpɔnkye mu onyin kor a wɔdze rokɔbɔ bɔn ho afɔr; nye asomdwee afɔr dze, anantwi ebien, nguannyin enum, mpɔnkyenyin enum na nguambaanyin enum a woedzi afrenhyia afrenhyia: iyi nye Enam ne babanyin Ahira n’ayɛyɛdze.
Iyi nye afɔrmbukyia no ho oyimadze a ofi Israel mbapɔmba no hɔ bae wɔ da a wɔseraa hɔn ngo no: ndwetɛboyaa duebien, ndwetɛkora duebien, sika ntser duebien: dwetɛboyaa kor n’ano tow dwetɛbona ɔha eduasa, na kora kor biara so yɛ eduosuon: ndzɛmba no no dwetɛ nyinara yɛ dwetɛbona mpemebien ahaanan, dɛ mbrɛ ahotseweebea dwetɛbona tse; sika ntser a eduhuam ayeyɛ no amaama duebien, kor n’ano tow dwetɛbona du, dɛ mbrɛ ahotseweebea dwetɛbona tse: ntser no ne sika nyinara yɛ dwetɛbona ɔha eduonu: ɔhyew afɔr anantwi no nyinara yɛ anantwisaa duebien, nguannyin no duebien, nguambaanyin a woedzi afrenhyia afrenhyia no duebien; mpɔnkye mu enyin a wɔdze rokɔbɔ bɔn ho afɔr duebien: Na asomdwee afɔr anantwi no nyinara yɛ anantwisaa eduonu anan, nguannyin no eduosia, mpɔnkyenyin no eduosia na nguambaanyin a woedzi afrenhyia afrenhyia no eduosia.
Iyi nye afɔrmbukyia no no ngosera ekyir oyimadze.
Na aber a Moses hɛɛn ehyiadzibuw no mu dɛ ɔnye no rekɛkasa no, nna ɔtsee ndze a ɔrekasa kyerɛ no fi mbɔbɔrhu egua a ɔwɔ dasedaka no do no do, wɔ kerobim ebien no ntamu: na ɔkasaa kyerɛɛ no.
Nkandzea No Ne Nsisii Na EWURADZE kasaa kyerɛɛ Moses dɛ, Kasa kyerɛ Aaron na se no dɛ, Sɛ esosɔ nkandzea no a, nkandzea esuon no ngyegye kandzeadua no enyim.
Na Aaron yɛɛ dɛm; ɔsosɔɔ ne nkandzea ma ɔgyegyee kandzeadua no enyim, dɛ mbrɛ EWURADZE hyɛɛ Moses no.
Na iyi nye kandzeadua no ne yɛbea, sika a ɔabor ara nko; fi n’ase dze kodu ne nhyiren do nyinara yɛ ɔbor edwuma: dɛ mbrɛ nsusudo a EWURADZE dze kyerɛɛ Moses no tse no, dɛmara na ɔyɛɛ kandzeadua no.
Levifo No Ho Ntsewee Na EWURADZE kasaa kyerɛɛ Moses dɛ, Yi Levifo no wɔ Israelmba mu, na tsew hɔn ho.
Dɛm na yɛ hɔn fa tsew hɔn ho: fa bɔnyi ho nsu petse hɔn do, na ma wɔmfa oyindam nyiyi hɔnho nyinara, na ma wɔnhor hɔn ntar mfa ntsew hɔnho.
Nna ma wɔmfa ɔnantwisaa eburwa, nye n’edziban afɔr, isiam pa a wɔdze ngo afrɔw, na fa ɔnantwisaa eburwa kor so bɔ bɔn ho afɔr.
Na fa Levifo no bra ehyiadzibuw no enyim: na ma Israelmba mboanofo no nyinara mbɔbɔ ngua: na fa Levifo no bra EWURADZE enyim: na Israelmba mfa hɔn nsa ngu Levifo no do.
Afei Aaron ntu Levifo no nsi hɔ dɛ ɔtow afɔr wɔ EWURADZE enyim, mfa ngyina Israelmba no ananmu, ma wɔntsena hɔ nyɛ EWURADZE n’edwuma.
Na Levifo no mfa hɔn nsa ngu anantwisaa no etsifi: na fa kor bɔ bɔn ho afɔr, na fa kor so bɔ ɔhyew afɔr ma EWURADZE, ma ɔnyɛ mpata mma Levifo no.
Na fa Levifo no gyina Aaron nye ne mbabanyin no enyim, na tu hɔn si hɔ dɛ ɔtow afɔr ma EWURADZE.
Dɛm na tsew Levifo no fi Israelmba mu: na Levifo no mbɛyɛ medze.
Na n’ekyir no Levifo no nkɔ nkɛyɛ ehyiadzibuw no ho edwuma: na tsew hɔn ho, na tu hɔn si hɔ dɛ ɔtow afɔr.
Osiandɛ wɔdze hɔn ama me koraa efi Israelmba no mu; medze hɔn ahyɛ dza obue yafun nyinara, mekyerɛ Israelmba mu mbakan nyinara ananmu mafa.
Na Israelmba mu mbakan nyinara yɛ medze, nyimpa nye mbowa nyina da a mobobɔɔ Egypt asaase do mbakan nyinara no na metseew hɔn ho maa moho.
Na mafa Levifo no ahyɛ Israelmba mu mbakan nyinara ananmu.
Na medze Levifo no ama Aaron nye ne mbabanyin no dɛ akyɛdze a ofi Israelmba mu dɛ wɔnyɛ edwuma wɔ ehyiadzibuw no mu, na wɔmpata mma Israelmba ama sɛ Israelmba no rotwe bɛn ahotseweebea no a, ɔyardɔm bi aammba Israelmba no mu.
Dɛm na Moses, nye Aaron, nye Israelmba mboanofo no nyinara, yɛɛ Levifo no.
Dɛ mbrɛ EWURADZE hyɛɛ Moses wɔ Levifo no ho nyinara no, dɛmara na Israelmba no yɛɛ hɔn.
Na Levifo no tseew hɔnho fii bɔn ho, na wɔhoor hɔn ntar; na Aaron tuu hɔn sii hɔ yɛɛ ɔtow afɔr wɔ EWURADZE enyim; na Aaron patae maa hɔn dze tseew hɔn ho.
Na n’ekyir no Levifo no kɔree kɛyɛɛ hɔn edwuma wɔ ehyiadzibuw no mu wɔ Aaron, nye ne mbabanyin no enyim: na dɛ mbrɛ EWURADZE hyɛɛ Moses wɔ Levifo no ho no, dɛmara na wɔyɛɛ hɔn.
Na EWURADZE kasaa kyerɛɛ Moses dɛ, Dza ɔyɛ Levifo dze no nye yi: hɔn a woedzi mfe eduonu enum nye ekyir no nkɔ nkɔsom wɔ ehyiadzibuw no edwuma no mu: na ofi hɔn a woedzi mfe eduonum do no ngyaa edwuma yɛ, na mma wɔnnkɔsom bio; mbom wɔnye hɔn nuanom nsom wɔ ehyiadzibuw no mu, nhwɛ ahwɛdodze no, na ɔsom edwuma no na mma wɔnnyɛ.
Dɛm na yɛ ma Levifo no wɔ hɔn ahwɛdodze ho afamu.
Apaho A Otsia Ebien No Na EWURADZE kasaa kyerɛɛ Moses wɔ Sinai sar do, wofii Egypt asaase do firii no n’ekyir afe a otsia ebien no no bosoom a odzi kan no mu dɛ, Nkyii so ma Israelmba ndzi apaho no wɔ n’aber a wɔahyɛ mu, bosoom yi ne da a otsia duanan no mu ewimbir, na hom ndzi: dɛ mbrɛ n’ahyɛdze nyinara tse, na mbrɛ no ho mmom nyinara tse no, na hom ndzi.
Na Moses kasaa kyerɛɛ Israelmba no dɛ wondzi apaho no.
Na wodzii apaho no wɔ bosoom a odzi kan no ne da a otsia duanan no mu, ewimbir, wɔ Sinai sar do: dɛ mbrɛ EWURADZE hyɛɛ Moses no nyinara, dɛmara na Israelmba no yɛe.
Na mbanyin bi wɔ hɔ a hɔn ho egu fi wɔ nyimpa bi no fun ho, ma dɛm ntsi woenntum enndzi apaho no da no ara: na mbanyin no see no dɛ, Hɛn ho egu fi wɔ nyimpa bi no fun ho: ɔyɛ dɛn ntsi na wɔakam hɛn, dɛ mma yɛmmfa EWURADZE ayɛyɛdze mmba wɔ n’aber a wɔahyɛ mu wɔ Israelmba no mu?
Na Moses see hɔn dɛ, Hom ngyina hɔ; ma minketsie dza EWURADZE bɛhyɛ wɔ hom ho.
Na EWURADZE kasaa kyerɛɛ Moses dɛ, Kasa kyerɛ Israelmba dɛ, Sɛ nyimpa bi no ho gu fi wɔ fun bi ho, anaa ɔwɔ ekyirekyir akwantu mu, wɔ hom mu, anaa hom ebusuasantsen mu a, ondzi apaho no mma EWURADZE ara: bosoom a otsia ebien no mu da a otsia duanan no ewimbir na wondzi; epitsi boodoo nye fan wenwen na wɔmfa ndzi: mma wonngya mu bi mma onnkodu anapa, na mma wommbu ne biew bi mu so: na dɛ mbrɛ apaho no no ho ahyɛdze no nyinara tse na wondzi.
Mbom nyimpa no a no ho tsew, na orunntu kwan, na ogyaa dɛ odzi apaho no dze, ɔkra no wobotwa no efi ne man mu akyen osiandɛ ɔammfa EWURADZE ayɛyɛdze no ammba wɔ n’aber a wɔahyɛ mu, dɛm nyimpa no nsoa no bɔn.
Na sɛ ɔhɔho bi bɔsoɛ hom mu na oridzi apaho no ama EWURADZE a ɔno dɛ mbrɛ apaho ahyɛdze no tse, na mbrɛ no ho mbra no tse no, na ɔnyɛ: hom nya ahyɛdze kor mfa mma ɔhɔho nye nyia wɔawo no wɔ asaase no do nyina.
Ogya Na Mununkum Fadum No Na da a wɔmaa ntamadan no do sii hɔ no mununkum no bɛkataa ntamadan no do, mekyerɛ dasebuw no: na ewimbir no na ɔwɔ ntamadan no do epue tse dɛ ogya dze kodu anapa.
Dɛm na ɔtse daa: mununkum no kataa do, na ogya no puee anadwe.
Na aber biara a wɔma mununkum no do ma ɔma noho do fi Buw no do no, ɔno n’ekyir no Israelmba tu kwan, na beebi mbrɛ mununkum no gyinae no, hɔ na Israelmba kyeer nsera.
EWURADZE mbrasɛm do na Israelmba nam tuu kwan, na EWURADZE mbrasɛm do na wɔnam kyeer nsera: aber tsentsen biara a mununkum no tsena ntamadan no do no nyinara wɔtsena nserakyer mu.
Na sɛ mununkum no kyinkyim ntamadan no do nda pii a, ɔno Israelmba hwɛ EWURADZE ahwɛdodze no do, na wonntu kwan.
Na ɔtɔfabi a mununkum no dzi nda kakrabaa bi wɔ ntamadan no do; nna dɛ mbrɛ EWURADZE mbrasɛm tse no wɔatsena nsera no mu, na dɛ mbrɛ EWURADZE mbrasɛm tse no, nna wɔnam do etu.
Na ɔtɔfabi so a mununkum no wɔ hɔ araa fi ewimbir kodu anapa; na sɛ mununkum no ma noho do anapa a, na woetu: anaa sɛ ɔwɔw do adzekyee nye adzesaa, na sɛ mununkum no ma no ho do a, na woetu.
Sɛ nda ebien o, bosoom o, afrenhyia o, nna mununkum no kyinkyim wɔ ntamadan no do tsena do a, Israelmba no tsena nsera no mu, na wonntu: na sɛ ɔma no ho do a, nna woetu.
EWURADZE ne mbrasɛm na wɔnam do kyeer nsera, na EWURADZE ne mbrasɛm na wɔnam do tui: wɔhwɛɛ EWURADZE n’ahwɛdodze do, wɔ EWURADZE ne mbrasɛm a ɔnam Moses ne nsa do hyɛɛ no do.
Dwetɛ Ntotorobɛnto No Na EWURADZE kasaa kyerɛɛ Moses dɛ, Yɛ dwetɛ ntotorobɛnto ebien fa ma woho: ɔbor edwuma na fa yɛ: na dze aafrɛ mboanofo no aba, na dze ama woeetutu nseraban no akɔ.
Na sɛ wɔhɛn n’ebien nyina a, mboanofo no nyinara hɔn ano nhyia wo nkyɛn wɔ ehyiadzibuw no n’abowano.
Na sɛ wɔhɛn kor a, ɔno mbapɔmba no, Israel mpempem mu etsitsir no, hɔn ano nhyia wo nkyɛn.
Na sɛ hom hɛn ewubɔ a, nseraban a ɔdeda boka afamu no ntutu nkɔ.
Na sɛ hom hɛn ewubɔ toa do ebien a, nseraban a ɔdeda pomu afamu no ntutu nkɔ: worubotu no, wɔnhɛn ewubɔ.
Mbom sɛ bagua no ribehyia a, hom nhɛn, na mma hom nnhɛn ewubɔ.
Na Aaron ne mbabanyin asɔfo no, na wɔmfa ntotorobɛnto no nhɛn; na ɔnyɛ daa ahyɛdze mma hom wɔ hom ebusuasantsen nyinara mu.
Na sɛ hom rokɔ ɔsa wɔ hom asaase do nye ɔtamfo a ohiahia hom ho akɔko a, ɔno hom mfa ntotorobɛnto no nhɛn ewubɔ; na wɔnkaa hom wɔ EWURADZE hom Nyankopɔn enyim, na wɔngye hom nkwa wɔ hom atamfo nsamu.
Na hom enyigye nda mu, nye hom afahyɛ a wɔahyehyɛ mu, na hom abosoom ahyɛse mu so, hom mfa ntotorobɛnto no nhɛn no wɔ hom ɔhyew afɔr nye hom asomdwee afɔr no do; na ɔnyɛ nkaa mma hom wɔ hom Nyankopɔn enyim: emi nye EWURADZE hom Nyankopɔn.
Israelmba no Tu Fi Sinai Asaase Do Na ɔbaa dɛ afe a otsia ebien no, bosoom a otsia ebien no, wɔ bosoom no ne da a otsia eduonu no mu no, mununkum no maa noho do fii dase ntamadan no do.
Na Israelmba no sii mu fii Sinai sar do dɛ mbrɛ hɔn akwantu no tse: na mununkum no kegyinaa Paran sar do.
Na wodzii kan tuu hɔn akwantu no dɛ mbrɛ EWURADZE mbrasɛm a ɔwɔ Moses nsamu no tse.
Na Judamba nseraban do frankaa na odzii kan tui dɛ mbrɛ hɔn dɔm no tsetsee: na Aminadab ne babanyin Nahson na ɔhwɛɛ no dɔm no do.
Na Zuar ne babanyin Netanel na ɔhwɛɛ Isakarmba ebusuakuw dɔm no do.
Na Helon ne babanyin Eliab na ɔhwɛɛ Zebulunmba ebusuakuw dɔm no do.
Na wɔpaa ntamadan no; na Gerson ne mbabanyin nye Merari ne mbabanyin a wɔsoasoaa ntamadan no tui.
Na Reuben nseraban do frankaa tui dɛ mbrɛ hɔn dɔm no tsetsee: na Sedeur ne babanyin Elizur na ɔhwɛɛ no dɔm no do.
Na Zurisadai ne babanyin Selumiel na ɔhwɛɛ Simeonmba ebusuakuw dɔm no do.
Na Deutel ne babanyin Eliasaf na ɔhwɛɛ Gadmba ebusuakuw dɔm no do.
Na Kohatfo no soasoaa ahotseweebea no dze tui: na binom so sii ntamadan no dze kodur dɛ wɔbae.
Na Efraimmba nseraban do frankaa tui dɛ mbrɛ hɔn dɔm no tsetsee: na Ammihud ne babanyin Elisama na ɔhwɛɛ no dɔm no do.
Na Pedazur ne babanyin Gamaliel na ɔhwɛɛ Manaasɛmba ebusuakuw dɔm no do.
Na Gideoni ne babanyin Abidan na ɔhwɛɛ Benjaminmba ebusuakuw dɔm no do.
Na Danmba nseraban do frankaa a ɔyɛ nseraban nseraban nyinara ne nkyidɔm no, tui dɛ mbrɛ hɔn dɔm no tsetsee: na Ammisaddai ne babanyin Ahiezer na ɔhwɛɛ no dɔm no do.
Na Okran ne babanyin Pagiel na ɔhwɛɛ Asermba ebusuakuw dɔm no do.
Na Enan ne babanyin Ahira na ɔhwɛɛ Naftalimba ebusuakuw dɔm no do.
Israelmba akwantu a wotui dɛ mbrɛ hɔn dɔm no tsetsee no nye yi; na wotui.
Na Moses see Hobab, a ɔyɛ n’asew Midiannyi Reuel ne babanyin no, dɛ, Yerutu akɔ beebi mbrɛ EWURADZE kasaa ho dɛ, Medze mebɛma hom no: bra ma yɛnkɔ, na yɛbɛyɛ wo yie: na EWURADZE aka Israel ho asɛm pa. Na ɔsee no dɛ, Moronnkɔ; mbom mobɔkɔ mankasa m’asaase do, nye m’ebusua mu.
Na ɔsee dɛ, Mepa wo kyɛw, mma nngya hɛn; susuampa dɛ ɔwo inyim mbrɛ yebesi akyer nsera wɔ sar no do ntsi, ɔwo yɛ enyiwa fa ma hɛn.
Na ɔbɛba dɛ, sɛ ɔwo nye hɛn kɔ a, ampa, ɔbɛba dɛ papa kor a EWURADZE dze bɛyɛ hɛn no, ɔnoara na yɛdze bɛyɛ wo.
Na wotutui fii EWURADZE bepɔw no ho tuu ndaansa kwan; na EWURADZE ahyɛmudaka no tui dzii hɔn enyim kɔr ndaansa kwan, dɛ ɔrokɔhwehwɛ ahomgyebea ama hɔn.
Na sɛ wotu fi nseraban no mu a, nna EWURADZE mununkum no wɔ hɔn do adzekyee.
Na ɔbaa dɛ, sɛ adaka no rutu a, Moses ka dɛ, EWURADZE, soɛr ɛ, na ma w’atamfo mbɔ mpetse; na ma hɔn a wokyir wo nguan w’enyim.
Na sɛ ɔsoɛ a, ɔka dɛ, EWURADZE, san bra Israel mpempem no nkyɛn.
Manna Fon Ɔman No Na ɔman no tse dɛ ehwinhwimfo a wɔkasa bɔn wɔ EWURADZE asomu: na EWURADZE tsee no, n’ebufuw dzɛwee; na EWURADZE ogya hyewee wɔ hɔn mu, na ɔmeen nseraban no ano noho.
Na ɔman no sui tɔɔ Moses do; na Moses paa EWURADZE kyɛw, na ogya no dumii.
Na wɔfrɛɛ bea no dzin dɛ Tabera: osiandɛ EWURADZE ogya hyewee wɔ hɔn mu.
Na aforafora nyimpa dodow a wɔwɔ hɔn mu no hɔn kɔn dɔɔ adze: Na Israelmba no so suu bio, na wɔsee dɛ, Woana na ɔbɛma hɛn nam ma yeedzi?
Yɛkaakaa esunam a yedzii no wɔ Egypt no kwa; efer, nye anamuna, nye fan, nye anwew, nye galik no: afei dze hɛn kra etwintwam; biribi biribiara nnyi hɔ: yennyi hwee gyedɛ manna yi ara na yɛahwɛ.
Na manna no tse dɛ korianda aba, na no ho tse dɛ bedula hyɛ ho.
Ɔman no kekyinii, na wɔtasetasee, na wɔnyaam no wɔ nwuyambo do, anaa wosiiw no nwɔdur mu, na wɔnoaa no wɔ asɛn mu, na wɔyɛɛ no tatar: na ne dɛw tse dɛ ngo momon ne dɛw.
Na sɛ ɔbɔsu tɔ gu nseraban no do anadwe a, manna no so tɔ gu do.
Na Moses tsee dɛ ɔman no worususu wɔ hɔn ebusua ebusua mu: nyimpa biara ɔwɔ no buw abowano: na EWURADZE n’ebufuw dzɛɛw kɛsenara; na ɔyɛɛ Moses ahomtsew.
Na Moses see EWURADZE dɛ, Ɔyɛ dɛn ntsi na ɔwo nye w’akowaa edzi no bɔn?
Na ɔyɛ dɛn ntsi na mennya w’enyim enyimnyam, dɛ edze ɔman yi nyinara adzesoa ato mo do yi?
Ana emi na minyinseen ɔman yi nyinara?
Emi na mowoo hɔn, na esee me dɛ Tur hɔn wɔ wo koko do, dɛ mbrɛ egya bagyegyefo tur enumfoanoba, fa kɔ asaase a ekaa ho ntam maa hɔn egyanom no do?
Henfa na minya nam mema ɔman yi nyinara?
Osiandɛ wosu gu mo do, dɛ, Ma hɛn nam, ma yendzi.
Mo nko murunntum nnkora ɔman yi nyinara, osiandɛ ɔyɛ dur dodow ma me.
Na sɛ dɛm na enye me bedzi no a, mepa wo kyɛw, sɛ menya w’enyim enyimnyam a, ɔnodze oku mbom na ku me; na mma munnhu m’awerɛhow.
Moses Pa Akandzifo Eduosuon Na EWURADZE see Moses dɛ, Boa Israel mpanyimfo mu eduosuon ano ma me hɔn a inyim dɛ wɔyɛ ɔman no mpanyimfo, nye hɔn do asafohemfo; na fa hɔn bra ehyiadzibuw no ho, ma wɔnye wo ngyina hɔ.
Na mibesian na menye wo abɛkasa wɔ hɔ: na mebɛfa sunsum a ɔwɔ wo do no bi, na medze egu hɔn do; na wɔnye wo aasoa ɔman no adzesoa no, amma woara nko aannsoa.
Na se ɔman no dɛ, Hom ntsew homho nsie ɔkyena, na hom bedzi nam: osiandɛ hom ekosu egu EWURADZE asomu dɛ, Woana na ɔbɛma hɛn nam ma yeedzi?
Oye ma hɛn wɔ Egypt mbom: dɛm ntsi EWURADZE bɛma hom nam, na hom eedzi.
