Nnyɛ da kor na hom bedzi, anaa nda ebien anaa nda enum, nnyɛ dadu, anaa adaduonu.
Mbom bosoom ara mu, ekodu dɛ obefifir hom ahwentokura mu, na ayɛ hom mfon: osiandɛ hom apow EWURADZE a ɔwɔ hom mu no, na hom esu wɔ n’enyim aka dɛ, Ebɛn ntsi na yefii Egypt bae?
Na Moses see dɛ, Ɔman a mowɔ hɔn mu yi yɛ anamɔnmufo mpemahaesia; na ɔwo ese dɛ, Mebɛma hɔn nam ma woeedzi no bosoom ara mu.
Aso wobokuku nguan nye anantwi ama hɔn ma aaso hɔn?
Anaa wɔbɔboaboa po mu nam nyinara ano ama hɔn, ma aaso hɔn?
Na EWURADZE see Moses dɛ, Ana woetwa EWURADZE nsa do a?
Afei na ibohu kyerɛ dɛ m’asɛm bɛba mu ama wo, anaa ɔnnkɛba mu.
Na Moses fiir edzi, na ɔkɛkaa EWURADZE n’asɛm no kyerɛɛ ɔman no: na ɔboaa ɔman mpanyimfo no mu mbanyin eduosuon ano, na ɔdze hɔn begyinaa Buw no ho hyiae.
Na EWURADZE sianee wɔ mununkum no mu, na ɔkasaa kyerɛɛ no, na ɔfaa sunsum a ɔwɔ no do no bi, na ɔdze guu mpanyimfo eduosuon no do: na ɔbaa dɛ, sunsum no baa hɔn do no, wɔhyɛɛ nkɔm, naaso wɔannyɛ dɛm bio.
Mbom ɔkaa mbanyin beenu wɔ nseraban no mu, ɔbaako ne dzin nye Eldad, na kor no so ne dzin dze Medad: na sunsum no baa hɔn do; na wɔfora hɔn a wɔkyerɛɛw hɔn no mu dze, na wonnyae nnkɔr Buw no ho: na wɔhyɛɛ nkɔm wɔ nseraban no mu.
Na aberantsɛ bi tutuu mbirika kɛkaa kyerɛɛ Moses, na ɔsee dɛ, Eldad nye Medad rehyɛ nkɔm wɔ nseraban no mu.
Na Nun ne babanyin Josua, Moses no somfo no, ɔyɛ ne mbanyin mpamufo mu kor no, buae see dɛ, Mo wura Moses, bra hɔn.
Na Moses see no dɛ, Ana emi ntsi erotwe nyinkun a?
Ɔka mo nko a nkyɛ Nyankopɔn aama EWURADZE ne man nyinara ayɛ nkɔnhyɛfo, ma EWURADZE dze no sunsum eegu hɔn do.
Na Moses sanee baa nseraban no mu, ɔno nye Israel mpanyimfo no.
Na mframa fi EWURADZE nkyɛn bɔe, na ɔdze Nkokɔhwerew fi po no ho boguu nseraban no ho, bɛyɛ da kor akwantu wɔ afa ha, nye da kor akwantu wɔ afa ha so, dze hyiaa nseraban no ho, na hɔn krɔn bɛyɛ basafa kor wɔ asaase enyi.
Na ɔman no soɛɛr adzekyee no nyinara, nye anadwe no nyinara, na wɔkɔboaboaa Nkokɔhwerew no ano: nyia ɔboaa kumaabi ano mpo, onyaa homer du: na wɔhatahatae araa dze twaa nseraban no ho hyiae maa hɔnho.
Aber a nam no da ho wowɔ hɔn se mu a wonnyae nnkosae no, EWURADZE ebufuw fraam ɔman no do, na EWURADZE dze ɔyardɔm kɛsenara bobɔɔ ɔman no.
Na wɔfrɛɛ bea no dzin dɛ Kibrot-hataava, osiandɛ hɔ na wosiee ɔman a hɔn kɔn dɔɔ adze no.
Na ɔman no tui fii Kibrot-hataava kɔr Hazerot; na wɔtsenaa Hazerot.
Miriam Nye Aaron Kasa Tsia Moses Na Miriam nye Aaron kasaa tsiaa Moses wɔ Kusnyi ɔbaa bi a ɔawar no no ntsi: osiandɛ nna ɔawar Kusnyi ɔbaa bi.
Na wɔsee dɛ, Ana ampaara dɛ Moses nko na EWURADZE nye no akasa?
Ana ɔnnye hɛn so nnkasae?
Na EWURADZE tsee.
Afei ɔbarimba Moses dze nna ɔdwe dodoodow, ɔbor nyimpa a wɔwɔ asaase do nyinara do.
Na EWURADZE kasaa awerɛfir mu kyerɛɛ Moses, nye Aaron, nye Miriam dɛ, Hom baasa hom mfir edzi mbra ehyiadzibuw no ho.
Na hɔn baasa no fiir edzi bae.
Na EWURADZE sianee wɔ mununkum dum mu, na obegyinaa Buw no n’abowano, na ɔfrɛɛ Aaron nye Miriam: na hɔn beenu no fiir edzi bae.
Na ɔsee dɛ, Afei hom ntsie me nsɛm: sɛ nkɔnhyɛfo bi wɔ hom mu a, emi EWURADZE mibeyi moho akyerɛ no wɔ enyido adzehu mu, adaaso mu na menye no bɛkasa.
M’akowaa Moses nntse dɛm; ɔno na medze me fie nyinara ahyɛ ne nsa.
Ano nye ano na menye no rekasa, mekyerɛ petee mu a, na nnyɛ abɛbu mu a; na ɔbɔhwɛ EWURADZE no su: na ɔyɛ dɛn ntsi na hom ennsuro dɛ hom bɛkasa etsia m’akowaa Moses?
Na EWURADZE ebufuw fraam hɔn do; na ofii hɔ kɔree.
Na mununkum no twee fii Buw no do; na, hwɛ, Miriam ayar kwata, ɔhoa dɛ esukwankyɛba: na Aaron hwɛɛ Miriam no, hwɛ, nna ɔayar kwata.
Na Aaron see Moses dɛ, Ao mo wura, mepa wo kyɛw, mma mmfa bɔn nnto hɛn do, na yɛayɛ nkwaseadze, na ɔno ho yɛayɛ bɔn.
Me kyɛw ara nye yi, mma ɔnnyɛ dɛ obi a oewu fi ne na yamu aba a woedzi no honam fa dada.
Na Moses sui frɛɛ EWURADZE dɛ, Ao Nyankopɔn, meserɛ wo, sa no yarba.
Na EWURADZE see Moses dɛ, Sɛ n’egya hina n’enyi do ntafi a, ana nkyɛ n’enyi nnwu nda esuon bi a?
Ma wɔntow no mu nda esuon wɔ nseraban no ekyir, na n’ekyir no na wɔmfa no mbra mu bio.
Na wɔtoow Miriam mu wɔ nseraban no ekyir nda esuon: na ɔman no enntu araa kodur dɛ wɔfaa Miriam baa mu bio.
Na n’ekyir no na ɔman no tui fii Hazerot, na wɔkɛkyeer nsera wɔ Paran sar do.
Akwanserafo Duebien No Na EWURADZE kasaa kyerɛɛ Moses dɛ, Soma mbanyin ma wɔnkɛsera Keenan asaase a medze rema Israelmba no: hɔn egyanom ebusuakuw biara mu no hom nsoma mu banyin kor, na hɔn nyina nyɛ hɔn mu mbapɔmba no bi.
Na Moses somaa hɔn fi Paran sar do dɛ mbrɛ EWURADZE mbrasɛm tse: hɔn nyinara wɔyɛ mbanyin a wɔyɛ Israelmba mu etsitsir.
Na hɔn edzin nye yi: Reuben ebusuakuw dze, Zakur ne babanyin Sammua.
Simeon ebusuakuw dze, Hori ne babanyin Safat.
Juda ebusuakuw dze, Jefune ne babanyin Kaleb.
Isakar ebusuakuw dze, Josef ne babanyin Igal.
Efraim ebusuakuw dze, Nun ne babanyin Hosea.
Benjamin ebusuakuw dze, Rafu ne babanyin Palti.
Zebulun ebusuakuw dze, Sodi ne babanyin Gaddiel.
Josef ebusuakuw dze, mekyerɛ Manaasɛ ebusuakuw dze, Susi ne babanyin Gaddi.
Dan ebusuakuw dze, Gemali ne babanyin Ammiel.
Aser ebusuakuw dze, Maekɛl ne babanyin Setur.
Naftali ebusuakuw dze, Vofsi ne babanyin Nahibi.
Gad ebusuakuw dze, Maki ne babanyin Geuel.
Iyinom nye mbanyin a Moses somaa hɔn dɛ wɔnkɛsera asaase no hɔn edzin.
Na Moses frɛɛ Nun ne babanyin Hosea no dɛ Josua.
Na Moses somaa hɔn dɛ wɔnkɛsera Keenan asaase no, na ɔsee hɔn dɛ, Hom mfa pomu afamu ɔkwan yi do, na hom nkɔfow mbepɔw no: na wɔnhwɛ asaase no, mbrɛ ɔtse; nye ɔman a wɔtse do no, kyerɛ dɛ wɔyɛ dzen anaa wɔyɛ mberɛw, dɛ wosuar anaa wɔdɔɔ so; nye mbrɛ asaase a wɔtse do no tse, dɛ oye anaa omuo; na mbrɛ nkurow a wɔtsetse mu no tsetsee, dɛ wɔtsetse nseraban mu, anaa akoban mu; na mbrɛ asaase no tse, dɛ ɔyɛ sɔɔsɔɔ anaa etwee, dɛ ndua wɔ do anaa ɔnntse dɛm.
Na hom nnya akokodur, na wɔmfa asaase no do aba bi mbra.
Nna aber no yɛ esikyireamba ababer a odzi kan n’aber.
Nna wosii mu kɔree, na wɔkɛseraa asaase no fi Zin sar do kodur Rehob, wɔ mbrɛ wɔnam kɔ Hamat no.
Na wɔfowee faa Pomu afamu, na wodur Hebron; na hɔ na Anakmba no, Ahiman, Sesai, nye Talmai, wɔwɔ.
(Na Hebron yi wɔkyekyeer no mfe esuon ansaana wɔrekyekyer Zoan a ɔwɔ Egypt.)
Na wodur Eskol ɔbɔn no mu, na wotwaa abaw a esikyireamba siaw kor wɔ do wɔ hɔ, na beenu wuraa no dua soae; na wɔdze pɔmegranate eduaba, nye adɔmba so bi bae.
Wɔfrɛɛ bea no Eskol ɔbɔn no mu, osian siaw no a Israelmba twaa no wɔ hɔ no ntsi.
Na adaduanan soe no, wɔsanee fii asaase no ne nserae mu bae.
Na wosii mu na wɔbaa Moses, nye Aaron, nye Israelmba mboanofo no nyinara nkyɛn, wɔ Paran sar do, wɔ Kades; na wɔbɔɔ hɔn amandzɛɛ kyerɛɛ hɔn, nye mboanofo no nyinara, na wɔdze asaase no do aba no kyerɛɛ hɔn.
Na wɔkaa kyerɛɛ no, na wɔsee dɛ, Yɛkɔr asaase a esomaa hɛn do no do, na numfonsu nye ewo pem wɔ do ampa; na no do aba nye yi.
Naaso ɔman a wɔtse asaase no do no na wɔyɛ dzen, na nkurow no wɔabɔ ho ban, ɔsoso dodow: na nkyii so yehun Anakmba wɔ hɔ.
Amalek tse Pomu afamu asaase no do: na Hitifo, nye Jebusfo, nye Amorifo, tsetse mbepɔw no do: na Keenanfo tse po no ho, nye Jordan nkyɛn.
Na Kaleb dwedwee ɔman no wɔ Moses enyim, na ɔsee dɛ, Hom mma yɛnkɔfow nkɔ prɛko, na yɛnkɛfa, na yebotum edzi hɔn do nyim.
Na mbanyin a wɔnye no kɔree no dze see dɛ, Yerunntum nnkɔfow nnkɔ nnkɛhyɛ ɔman no do; osiandɛ wɔyɛ dzen sen hɛn.
Na wɔdze asaase a wɔkɛserae no ho atsenka bɔn brɛɛ Israelmba no dɛ, Asaase a yɛakɛfa mu akɛsera no, ɔyɛ asaase a odzi no do atsefo no; na nkorɔfo a yehun hɔn wɔ do no nyinara wɔyɛ nyimpa a wɔyɛ akraban.
Na hɔ na yehun abran akɛse no, Anak ne mbabanyin no a wofi Nefilfo mu no: na yɛyɛɛ dɛ mbɛbɛw wɔ hɛnankasa hɛn enyi do, na dɛmara na yɛyɛe wɔ hɔn enyi do.
Ɔman No Hwinhwin Na mboanofo no nyinara memaa hɔn ndze do, na wɔkekaa mu; na ɔman no suu anadwe no.
Na Israelmba no nyinara hwinhwiin Moses nye Aaron ho: na mboanofo no nyinara see hɔn dɛ, Ka hɛn nko a nkyɛ Nyankopɔn maa yewuwui wɔ Egypt asaase do!
Anaa sar yi do ha ara mpo, ka hɛn nko a nkyɛ Nyankopɔn maa yewuwui!
Na ebɛn ntsi na EWURADZE dze hɛn reba asaase yi do, dɛ yɛmbɔtotɔr nkrantsee ano?
Hɛn yernom nye hɛn mbofraba bɛyɛ afonam: ana onnye mma hɛn dɛ yɛbɛsan akɔ Egypt bi a?
Na wɔsesee hɔnho dɛ, Wɔmma yɛnhyɛ ɔpanyin, na yɛnsan nkɔ Egypt.
Nna Moses nye Aaron dze hɔn enyim butubutuuw famu wɔ Israelmba mboanofo bagua no nyinara enyim.
Na Nun ne babanyin Josua nye Jefune ne babanyin Kaleb a wofi hɔn a wɔkɛseraa asaase no mu no, sunsuaan hɔn ntar mu: na wɔkasaa kyerɛɛ Israelmba mboanofo no nyinara dɛ, Asaase a yetwaa mu kɔree kɛserae no, ɔyɛ asaase pa mbordo.
Sɛ yɛsɔ EWURADZE enyi a, ɔno ɔdze hɛn bodu asaase no do, na ɔdze ama hɛn; asaase a numfonsu nye ewo pem do.
EWURADZE do etua ara nko na mma hom nntsew, nkyii so mma hom nnsuro asaase no do nkorɔfo no; na wɔyɛ edziban ma hɛn: hɔn akataman efi hɔn do, na hɛn dze EWURADZE nye hɛn wɔ hɔ: mma wonnsuro hɔn.
Na mboanofo no nyinara kaa dɛ wonsiw Josua na Kaleb abo.
Na EWURADZE enyimnyam puee ehyiadzibuw no mu kyerɛɛ Israelmba no nyinara.
Na EWURADZE see Moses dɛ, Ɔman yi rubu me enyimtsia ekodu dabɛn?
Na dabɛn na wɔrenngye me nndzi, wɔ nsɛnkyerɛdze a mayɛ wɔ hɔn mu nyinara mu no ekodu?
Medze owuyarba mobɔbɔ hɔn, na masɛɛ hɔn, na medze wo mayɛ ɔman kɛse a ɔwɔ dzin sen hɔn.
Na Moses see dɛ, Ɔno Egyptfo bɛtse; na ɔwo dze wo tum na edze eyi ɔman yi efi hɔn mu; na wɔbɛka akyerɛ asaase yi do atsefo: wɔatse dɛ ɔwo EWURADZE ewɔ ɔman yi mu; na ɔwo EWURADZE wohu wo enyim nye enyim, na wo mununkum gyina hɔn do, na ɔwo na idzi hɔn enyim, wɔ mununkum dum mu adzekyee, nye ogya dum mu adzesaa.
Afei sɛ iku ɔman yi dɛ nyimpa kor a, ɔno amanaman a wɔatse wo nka no bɛka dɛ, Osiandɛ EWURADZE enntum dɛ ɔdze ɔman yi kɔ asaase a ɔkaa hɔn ho ntam no do no, ntsi na oeku hɔn wɔ sar no do no.
Na afei, mepa wo kyɛw, ma EWURADZE no tum nyɛ kɛse, dɛ mbrɛ ɔwo aka dɛ, EWURADZE fa ebufuw nyaa, na n’adɔyɛ so, ɔdze emumuyɛ nye mbrato kyɛ, na bem bi na onnkobu ɔfɔdzinyi no; ɔdze egyanom hɔn emumuyɛ hwɛ mba, kodu ebusuasantsen ebiasa nye anan do.
Mepa wo kyɛw, fa ɔman yi hɔn emumuyɛ fir hɔn dɛ mbrɛ w’adɔyɛ ne kɛse tse, na dɛ mbrɛ ɔwo dze efir ɔman yi, efi Egypt araa ebodu sesei.
Na EWURADZE see dɛ, Medze akyɛ dɛ mbrɛ w’asɛm tse no: mbom nokwar ara, dɛ metse ase, na dɛ EWURADZE enyimnyam bɛhyɛ asaase nyinara ma yi; osiandɛ nyimpa nyina a woehu m’enyimnyam, nye me nsɛnkyerɛdze a meyɛe wɔ Egypt nye sar no do no, naaso wɔasɔ me ahwɛ mpɛn du nye yi, na woenntsie me ndze no; ampaara wonnkohu asaase a mekaa ho ntam mekyerɛɛ hɔn egyanom no, nkyii so hɔn mu biara a obu me enyimtsia no runnhu: na m’akowaa Kaleb dze, osiandɛ ɔwɔ sunsum bi so wɔ no mu, na oedzi m’ekyir koraa no ntsi, medze no mubodu asaase a ɔkɔr do no do; na n’asefo afa.
Afei Amalekfo nye Keenanfo tse ɔbɔn no mu: ɔkyena hom ndan, na hom ntu nkɔ sar no do wɔ Mbɛw Po kwan do.
Ehwinhwin No Ho Asehwe Na EWURADZE kasaa kyerɛɛ Moses nye Aaron dɛ, Dabɛn na memma mboanofo bɔn yi a wohwinhwin tsia me yi kwan ma onkodu?
Israelmba hɔn ehwinhwin a wohwinhwin tsia me no matse.
Se hɔn dɛ, Metse ase yi, EWURADZE na ɔse, ampaara dɛ mbrɛ hom akasa wɔ m’asomu no, dɛmara so na mebɛyɛ hom: sar yi do ara na hom efun bɛdeda; nye hɔn a wɔkaan hɔn wɔ hom mu no nyinara, dɛ mbrɛ hom dodow nyina tse, ofi hɔn a woedzi mfe eduonu nye ekyir do no a woehwinhwin etsia me no, ampaara hom runndu asaase a memaa me nsa do mekyerɛɛ dɛ mebɛma hom atsena do no do, gyedɛ Jefune ne babanyin Kaleb, nye Nun ne babanyin Josua.
Mbom hom mbofraba a hom see dɛ wɔbɛyɛ afonam no, hɔn na medze hɔn bɔkɔ do, na wobohu asaase a hom apow no.
Na hom dze, sar yi do ara na hom efun bɛdeda.
Na hom mba ayɛ aworamafo wɔ sar no do mfe eduanan, na wɔasoa hom ndwamanyɛ, ekodu dɛ hom efun bɛsa wɔ sar no do.
Nda a hom dze kɛseraa asaase no, no dodow mbrɛ ɔtse no, mekyerɛ adaduanan na da kor nye afe kor, nna hom nsoa hom emumuyɛ, mekyerɛ mfe eduanan, na hom ehu mbrɛ me pa tse.
Emi EWURADZE na maka, ampaara iyi na medze bɛyɛ mboanofo bɔn yi nyinara a woedzi ehyia etsia me yi: sar yi do ara na wɔbɛsa, na hɔ na wobowuwu.
Na mbanyin no a Moses somaa hɔn ma wɔkɛseraa asaase no a wɔsanee bae, na wɔmaa mboanofo no nyinara hwinhwinii tsiaa me no, dɛ wɔdze asaase no ho atsenka bɔn bae no, mekyerɛ mbanyin no a wɔdze asaase no ho atsenka bɔn bae no, wowuu owuyar wu wɔ EWURADZE enyim.
Mbom Nun ne babanyin Josua, nye Jefune ne babanyin Kaleb, na wonyaa nkwa wɔ mbanyin a wɔkɔree kɛseraa asaase no mu.
Na Moses kaa nsɛm yi kyerɛɛ Israelmba no nyinara: na ɔman no gyaam kɛsenara.
Na wɔsoɛɛr ahanamakye, na wɔfowee kɔr bepɔw no etsifi, dɛ, Hwɛ hɛn nye yi, yɛbɔfow akɔ beebi mbrɛ EWURADZE abɔ ho anohoba no: na yɛayɛ bɔn.
Na Moses see dɛ, Ɔyɛ dɛn ntsi na afei hom to EWURADZE mbrasɛm yi, na iyi dze ɔrennyɛ yie?
Mma hom mmfow nnkɔ, na EWURADZE nnyi hom mu; mma hom aanntotɔr wɔ hom atamfo enyim.
Na Amalekfo nye Keenanfo wɔ hom enyim hɔ, na hom bɔtotɔr wɔ nkrantsee ano: osiandɛ hom asan efi EWURADZE ekyir ntsi EWURADZE so rinndzi hom ekyir.
Na wotsitsii hɔn enyiwa ho ara dɛ wɔrofow akɔ bepɔw no etsifi: naaso EWURADZE n’ahyɛmudaka na Moses dze, woemmfi nseraban no mu emmfi.
Nna Amalekfo, nye Keenanfo a wɔtse bepɔw no do no sianee bae bokunkum hɔn na wɔbɔɔ hɔn petsee araa kodur Horma.
Afɔr Ho Mbra Na EWURADZE kasaa kyerɛɛ Moses dɛ, Kasa kyerɛ Israelmba, na se hɔn dɛ, Sɛ hom du hom tsenabew asaase a medze rema hom no do, na wɔrobɔ ogya afɔr ama EWURADZE, ɔhyew afɔr, anaa okum afɔr, dze ahyɛ anohoba bi ma, anaa dɛ ayamuyi afɔr, anaa hom afahyɛ a wɔahyɛ no mu, dze eyi nka huanhuam ama EWURADZE a ofi anantwi, anaa nguan mu a: ɔno nyia ɔdze n’ayɛyɛdze ba no, ɔmfa edziban afɔr isiam pa efa ebupɛn du mu kor nka ngo hin ebupɛn anan mu kor ho mbrɛ EWURADZE: na ɔnom afɔr wenyin, hin ebupɛn anan mu kor, na fa ka ɔhyew afɔr, anaa okum afɔr eguambaa kor ho siesie.
Na oguannyin dze, fa isiam pa efa ebupɛn du mu ebien a wɔdze ngo hin ebupɛn ebiasa mu kor afrɔw, siesie yɛ edziban afɔr: na ɔnom afɔr no fa wenyin hin ebupɛn ebiasa mu kor bra, ma onyi nka huanhuam mma EWURADZE.
Na sɛ ɔnantwisaa na irisiesie abɔ ɔhyew afɔr, anaa okum afɔr, dze ahyɛ anohoba bi ma, anaa edze robɔbɔ asomdwee afɔr ama EWURADZE a: ɔno edziban afɔr a ɔmfa nka ɔnantwisaa no ho nye isiam pa efa ebupɛn du mu ebiasa a wɔdze ngo hin ɔfa afrɔw.
Na fa wenyin hin ɔfa yɛ ɔnom afɔr no bra bɔbɔ ogya afɔr a oyi nka huanhuam ma EWURADZE.
Dɛm na wɔnyɛ ɔnantwisaa kor, anaa oguannyin kor, anaa nguambaanyin no, anaa mpɔnkyemba no nkorkor.
Dɛ mbrɛ dodow a hom besiesie no tse no, dɛmara na hom nyɛ no nkorkor dɛ mbrɛ hɔn dodow tse.
Ekuromfo nyinara nyɛ ndzɛmba yi dɛm mfa mbɔ ogya afɔr a oyi nka huanhuam mma EWURADZE.
Na sɛ ɔhɔho bi soɛ hom mu, anaa obiara a ɔwɔ hom mu wɔ hom ebusuasantsen nyina mu no, na ɔbɔbɔ ogya afɔr a oyi nka huanhuam ama EWURADZE no; dɛ mbrɛ hom yɛ no, dɛmara so na ɔnyɛ.
Bagua no, ahyɛdze kor na ɔnda hɔ mma hom na ɔhɔho a ɔbɔsoɛ hom mu no, ɔnyɛ daa ahyɛdze wɔ hom ebusuasantsen nyina mu: dɛ mbrɛ hom tse no, dɛmara so na ɔhɔho no nyɛ wɔ EWURADZE enyim.
Mbra kor nye ɔmom kor na ɔnda hɔ mma hom, nye ɔhɔho a ɔabɔsoɛ hom mu nyina.
Na EWURADZE kasaa kyerɛɛ Moses dɛ, Kasa kyerɛ Israelmba, na se hɔn dɛ, Sɛ hom du asaase a medze hom rokɔ do no do a, ɔno ɔba dɛ, sɛ hom ridzi asaase no do edziban no bi a, hom mbɔ ohim afɔr mma EWURADZE.
Hom mbɔrkan no bi ne tatar na hom mfa nyɛ ohim afɔr: dɛ mbrɛ hom yɛ ewuporoweebea ohim afɔr no, dɛmara so na hom nhim no.
Hom mbɔrkan no bi na hom mfa mma EWURADZE dɛ ohim afɔr wɔ hom ebusuasantsen nyina mu.
Na sɛ hom fom, na hom annhyɛ mbransɛm yi a EWURADZE aka akyerɛ Moses no nyinara nsew, mekyerɛ dza EWURADZE nam Moses nsa do ahyɛ hom nyinara, ofi da a EWURADZE hyɛɛ mbra no, na ɔdze ba yi wɔ hom ebusuasantsen nyina mu no a; ɔno ɔba dɛ, sɛ wɔyɛ no ntɔgon mu, dɛ mboanofo no nnyim a, mboanofo no nyinara mfa ɔnantwisaa eburwa kor mbɔ ɔhyew afɔr a oyi nka huanhuam ma EWURADZE, nka n’edziban afɔr, nye no nom afɔr no ho dɛ mbrɛ mbra no tse, nye apɔnkyenyin kor na ɔnyɛ bɔn ho afɔr.
Na ɔsɔfo no mpata mma Israelmba mboanofo no nyina, na wɔdze bɛkyɛ hɔn; na ɔyɛ mfom, na hɔn mfom no ntsi, wɔdze hɔn ayɛyɛdze aba dɛ EWURADZE ogya afɔr, nye hɔn bɔn ho afɔr wɔ EWURADZE enyim: na wɔdze befir Israelmba mboanofo no nyinara, nye ɔhɔho a ɔabɔsoɛ hɔn mu no; na ɔman no nyinara afamu na wɔyɛɛ no ntɔgon mu.
Na sɛ nyimpa kor bi annhyɛ da na ɔyɛ bɔn a, ɔno ɔmfa apɔnkyeber a oedzi afrenhyia mbra mbɔbɔ bɔn ho afɔr.
Na ɔsɔfo no mpata mma ɔkra a ɔfom no, sɛ ɔyɛ bɔn no ber a ɔnndze enyidaho wɔ EWURADZE enyim a, ɔmpata mma no; na wɔdze bɛkyɛ no.
Hom nnya mbra kor nto hɔ mma nyia ɔyɛ biribi a ɔnndze enyidaho dɛ ɔyɛ okuromnyi wɔ Israelmba mu, anaa ɔhɔho a ɔbɔsoɛ hom mu no.
Ɔkra a ɔhyɛ da ara yɛ bɔn no dze, sɛ ɔyɛ okuromnyi bi o, ɔhɔho bi o, oedzi etsia EWURADZE; na dɛm ɔkra no wobotwa no efi ne man mu akyen.
Osiandɛ oebu EWURADZE n’asɛm enyimtsia, na ɔato ne mbra no; otwa ara na wobotwa ɔkra no akyen, n’emumuyɛ nda no do.
Na aber a Israelmba wɔwɔ sar no do no, wohun ɔbanyin bi a ɔrepɛ nyena ahomgyeda.
Na hɔn a wohun no dɛ ɔrepɛ nyena no wɔdze no brɛɛ Moses nye Aaron, nye mboanofo no nyinara.
Na wɔbɔɔ no dua mu, osiandɛ wonnyae nnkyerɛɛ dza wɔmfa nyɛ no.
Na EWURADZE see Moses dɛ, Oku na wonku banyin no: mboanofo no nyinara nsiw no abo wɔ nseraban no ekyir.
Na mboanofo no nyinara dze no baa nseraban no ekyir na wosiiw no abo ma owui; dɛ mbrɛ EWURADZE hyɛɛ Moses no.
Ntar No Ndwow Ho Mbra Na EWURADZE kasaa kyerɛɛ Moses dɛ, Kasa kyerɛ Israelmba, na hyɛ hɔn ma wɔnyɛ hɔn ntar ano ndwow wɔ hɔn ebusuasantsen nyina mu, na wɔmfa bibir ahoma nsusuo n’ano n’ano ndwow no mu: na ɔnyɛ ndwow mma hom, ma hom aahwɛ, na wɔaakaa EWURADZE mbrasɛm nyinara, na wɔaayɛ; na hom eennkekyin enndzi hom akoma nye hom enyiwa ekyir, dza hom tɔ dɛ wodzi ekyir ndwamanyɛ mu no: ama hom aakaa na wɔayɛ me mbransɛm nyinara, na hom ayɛ krɔnkrɔn ama hom Nyankopɔn.
Emi nye EWURADZE hom Nyankopɔn a miyii hom fii Egypt asaase do dɛ mebɛyɛ hom Nyankopɔn no: emi nye EWURADZE hom Nyankopɔn.
Kora, Datan Na Abiram Soɛr Tsia Moses Afei Kora a n’egya nye Izhar a ɔyɛ Kohat a n’egya nye Levi ne babanyin no na Eliab ne mbabanyin Datan na Abiram na Pelet ne babanyin on (Eliab na Pelet yɛ Reuben ne mbabanyin) na wɔsoɛree tsiaa Moses.
Wɔnye Israelmba no mu bi, mboanofo no mu mbapɔmba ahaenu eduonum a wɔfrɛ hɔn bagua mu, nyimpa a wɔwɔ dzin: na wɔpoon hɔnho hyiae bɔɔ Moses nye Aaron do ngua, na wɔsee hɔn dɛ, Hom yɛ dodow, na mboanofo nyinara yɛ krɔnkrɔn, hɔn mu obiara, na EWURADZE wɔ hɔn mu: ɔyɛ dɛn ntsi mbɔ na hom mema hom ho do wɔ EWURADZE ne baguaa do?
Na Moses tsee no, ɔdze n’enyim butuuw famu: na ɔkasaa kyerɛɛ Kora nye no kuw no nyinara dɛ, Anapa EWURADZE bɛkyerɛ hɔn a wɔyɛ nedze, nye nyia ɔyɛ krɔnkrɔn, na ɔbɛma ɔaba ne nkyɛn: mekyerɛ nyia ɔbɛsan mu eyi no no nna ɔbɛma ɔaba ne nkyɛn.
Iyi na hom nyɛ; hom mfa nduhuam asɛn, Kora nye no kuw nyinara; na wɔmfa ogya ngu mu, na wɔmfa eduhuam ngu do wɔ EWURADZE enyim ɔkyena: na ɔbɛba dɛ nyimpa a EWURADZE bɛfa no no, ɔbɛyɛ krɔnkrɔn: hom yɛ dodow, hom Levi mbabanyin.
Na Moses see Kora dɛ, Afei hom ntsie, hom Levi mbabanyin: ana ɔyɛ hom adze ketseaba, dɛ Israel Nyankopɔn no atsew hom efi Israel mboanofo mu dɛ ɔdze hom rebɛn noho; ma hom aayɛ EWURADZE ntamadan no ho edwuma, na hom egyina mboanofo no enyim asom hɔn; Na ɔdze nuanom, Levi ne mbabanyin no nyinara ho abɛn, na hom rohwehwɛ asɔfodzi so yi?
Dɛm ntsi na ɔwo nye wo kuw nyinara ehyia wɔ EWURADZE do: na Aaron dze, woana nye no na hom hwinhwin tsia no?
Na Moses somae ma wɔkɛfrɛɛ Datan nye Abiram, Eliab ne mbabanyin no: na wɔsee dɛ, Yɛremmba: ana ɔyɛ adze ketseaba dɛ eyi hɛn efi asaase a numfonsu nye ewo pem wɔ do do, ruboku hɛn wɔ sar do, na kyenkyennkyen iridzi hɛn do ahenmbasɛm so yi?
Nkyii so emmfaa hɛn mmbaa asaase a numfonsu nye ewo pem wɔ do no do, na emmfaa haban nye wenyin nture enyadze no so mmaa hɛn; ana mbanyin yi enyiwa na irubotutu?
Yɛremmba.
Na Moses no bo fuuw kɛsenara, na ɔsee EWURADZE dɛ, Mma w’enyi nnsɔ hɔn afɔrbɔ: menngyee hɔn nsamu asoaso kor, nkyii so mennyɛɛ hɔn mu kor biara bɔn.
Na Moses see Kora dɛ, Ɔwo nye wo mboanofo no nyinara mbra EWURADZE enyim, ɔwo, nye hɔn, nye Aaron, mbra ɔkyena: na hom mu nyimpa biara mfa n’eduhuamsɛn, na hom mfa eduhuam ngugu mu, na hom mu nyimpa biara mfa n’eduhuamsɛn mbra EWURADZE enyim, nduhuamsɛn ahaenu eduonum; ɔwo so, nye Aaron, obiara mfa n’eduhuamsɛn.
Na wɔfefae, nyimpa biara nye n’eduhuamsɛn, na wɔdze ogya guguu mu, na wɔnye Moses nye Aaron kegyinagyinaa ehyiadzibuw no n’abowano.
Na Kora poon mboanofo no nyinara hyiae bɔɔ hɔn do ngua wɔ ehyiadzibuw no n’abowano: na EWURADZE enyimnyam yii noho edzi kyerɛɛ mboanofo no nyinara.
Na EWURADZE kasaa kyerɛɛ Moses nye Aaron dɛ, Hom ntsew homho mfi mboanofo yi mu, ma menhyew hɔn amon mu.
Na wɔdze hɔn enyim butubutuuw famu, na wɔsee dɛ, Ao Nyankopɔn, honam nyinara hɔn esunsum Nyankopɔn, ana nyimpa kor bɛyɛ bɔn, na wo bo efuw mboanofo no nyinara?
Na EWURADZE kasaa kyerɛɛ Moses dɛ, Kasa kyerɛ mboanofo no dɛ, Hom ntwe hom ho do mfi Kora, Datan, nye Abiram ntamadan ho.
Na Moses soɛree na ɔkɔr Datan nye Abiram nkyɛn; na Israel mpanyimfo no dzii n’ekyir kɔree.
Na ɔkasaa kyerɛɛ ɔman no dɛ, Mepa hom kyɛw, hom ntwe hom ho mfi nyimpa bɔn yi hɔn asesee ho, na mma hom nnka hɔn biribiara, bɛyɛ na hom ahyew wɔ hɔn bɔn nyinara mu.
Nna wɔtwee hɔnho fii Kora, Datan, nye Abiram ntamadan ho wɔ afa nyina: na Datan nye Abiram fiir edzi, na wobegyinagyinaa hɔn asesee abowano, hɔn yernom, nye hɔn mbabanyin, nye hɔn mbɔtoaba so.
Na Moses see dɛ, Iyi na hom dze bohu dɛ EWURADZE na ɔasoma me dɛ mindzi dwuma yi nyinara; na mommbɔɔ mankasa me tsir mu yɛ.
Sɛ nyimpa nyinara wu ara na iyinom bowuwu, anaa sɛ dza ɔto nyimpa nyinara na ɔbɔtɔ hɔn a, ɔnodze na nnyɛ EWURADZE na ɔasoma me.
Na sɛ adze fofor bi dze na EWURADZE bɛyɛ, na asaase bobue n’ano, na ɔamen hɔn, nye dza odzi wɔ hɔn nyinara, na wɔnam enyikan akɔ samanadze a; ɔnodze hom ntse ase dɛ mbanyin yi ebu EWURADZE enyimtsia.
Na ɔbaa dɛ owiee nsɛm yi nyinara ka no, asaase a ɔwɔ hɔn ase no paae: na asaase buee n’ano, na ɔmeen hɔn, nye hɔn efifo, nye nyimpa a wodzi wɔ Kora nyinara, nye hɔn adze nyinara.
Nna hɔn, nye dza odzi wɔ hɔn nyinara, nam enyikan sianee kɔr samanadze: na asaase no seraam hɔn do, na wɔherae wɔ bagua no mu.
Na Israelfo a woetwa hɔnho ehyia no nyinara guanee wɔ hɔn nkekamu no ntsi: na wɔsee dɛ, Bɛyɛ na asaase amen hɛn.
Na ogya fii EWURADZE hɔ bae, na ɔbɛhyeew mbanyin ahaenu eduonum a wɔdze eduhuam bae no.
Na EWURADZE kasaa kyerɛɛ Moses dɛ, Kasa kyerɛ ɔsɔfo Aaron ne babanyin Eleazar dɛ, ɔntase nduhuam asɛn no mfi ogyahyewee no mu, na fa ogya no petsepetse enyim noho; na ɔyɛ krɔnkrɔn: mekyerɛ ndzebɔnyɛfo yi a wɔayɛ hɔnankasa hɔn nkwa ho bɔn nduhuam asɛn no, na ma wɔnyɛ no ɔborntɛrba mfa nyɛ afɔrmbukyia no ho nkataho: osiandɛ wɔdze baa EWURADZE enyim, dɛm ntsi ɔyɛ krɔnkrɔn: na ɔnyɛ asɛnkyerɛdze mma Israelmba.
Na ɔsɔfo Eleazar faa boran nduhuam asɛn no a hɔn a wɔhyewee no dze bae no; na wɔboree dze yɛɛ afɔrmbukyia no ho nkataho: dɛ ɔnyɛ nkaadze mma Israelmba, amma ɔhɔho bi a ommfi Aaron n’asefo mu aammba ho ammbɛhyew eduhuam wɔ EWURADZE enyim; mma ɔaannyɛ dɛ Kora, nye no kuw no: dɛ mbrɛ EWURADZE nam Moses do kaa kyerɛɛ no no.
Na n’adzekyee no Israelmba mboanofo no nyinara hwinhwinii tsiaa Moses nye Aaron dɛ, Hom na hom eku EWURADZE ne man.
Na ɔbaa dɛ, aber a mboanofo no boaboaa hɔn ano tsiaa Moses nye Aaron no, wɔdandaan hɔn enyi wɔ ehyiadzibuw no do: na, hwɛ, mununkum no akata do, na EWURADZE enyimnyam no yii noho edzi.
Na Moses nye Aaron baa ehyiadzibuw no enyim.
Na EWURADZE kasaa kyerɛɛ Moses dɛ, Hom mma hom ho do mfi mboanofo yi mu, ma menhyew hɔn amon mu.
Na wɔdze hɔn enyim butubutuuw famu.
Na Moses see Aaron dɛ, Fa w’eduhuamsɛn, na sɔ afɔrmbukyia no do ogya gu mu, na fa eduhuam to do, na suo mu nantsew ntsɛmara kɔ mboanofo no nkyɛn, na kɛpata ma hɔn: na ebufuhyew efi EWURADZE hɔ efir; ɔyardɔm no ahyɛ ase.
Na Aaron fae dɛ mbrɛ Moses kae no, na otuu mbirika kɔr bagua no finimfin; na, hwɛ, ɔyardɔm no ahyɛ ase wɔ ɔman no mu: na ɔdze eduhuam no gui, na ɔpatae maa ɔman no.
Na ogyinaa ewufo nye enyikamfo no ntamu; na wosiankaa ɔyardɔm no.
Afei hɔn a wowuwui wɔ ɔyardɔm no mu wɔyɛ mpemduanan nye ahaesuon, ɔsor hɔn a Kora asɛm no ntsi wowuwui no.
Na ɔyardɔm no siankaa no, Aaron sanee baa Moses nkyɛn wɔ ehyiadzibuw no n’abowano.
Aaron No Poma No Na EWURADZE kasaa kyerɛɛ Moses dɛ, Kasa kyerɛ Israelmba, na gyegye hɔn hɔ mpoma, egyanom ofi kor mu kor, wɔ hɔn mbapɔmba no nyinara hɔ dɛ mbrɛ hɔn egyanom efi tsetsee, mpoma duebien: kyerɛw nyimpa biara ne dzin wɔ no poma do.
Na kyerɛw Aaron ne dzin wɔ Levi poma do: na poma kor nyɛ hɔn egyanom efi do tsitsir kor dze.
Na gyaa mu gu ehyiadzibuw no mu wɔ Dase no enyim, mbrɛ menye hom hyia no.
Na ɔbɛba dɛ banyin a mibeyi no no, no poma bɛfefɛw: na mebɛma mo ho ehwinhwin a Israelmba hwinhwin tsia hom no egyaa.
Na Moses kasaa kyerɛɛ Israelmba, na hɔn mbapɔmba no nyinara memaa no mpoma, ɔbapɔmba kor nedze kor, dɛ mbrɛ hɔn egyanom efi tsetsee no, mekyerɛ mpoma duebien: na Aaron no poma wɔ hɔn mpoma no mu.
Na Moses gyaa mpoma no mu guu EWURADZE enyim wɔ Dasebuw no mu.
Na ɔbaa dɛ adze kyee no, Moses kɔr Dasebuw no mu no; na, hwɛ, Aaron no poma no a ɔyɛ Levi ofi dze no afefɛw, ayɛ frɔmfrɔm, na egu nhyiren, na asow almɔnd aba beree.
Na Moses dze mpoma no nyinara fi EWURADZE enyim brɛɛ Israelmba no nyinara: na wɔhwɛe, na nyimpa biara faa no poma.
Na EWURADZE see Moses dɛ, Fa Aaron no poma no san to Dase no enyim, ma wɔmfa nsie nyɛ asɛnkyerɛdze mma mba asoɔdzenfo no; ama eetwa hɔn ehwinhwin a wohwinhwin tsia me no do, amma woeennwuwu.
Dɛm na Moses yɛe: dɛ mbrɛ EWURADZE hyɛɛ no no, dɛmara na ɔyɛe.
Na Israelmba no kasaa kyerɛɛ Moses dɛ, Hwɛ yeruwu, yɛreyera, hɛn nyinara rehera.
Obiara a ɔba ho, nyia ɔba EWURADZE ntamadan no ho, owu: ana hɛn nyinara yenwuwu?
Asɔfo Ma Levifo Hɔn Som Ho Kyɛfa Na EWURADZE see Aaron dɛ, Ɔwo nye wo mbabanyin nye w’egyanom fi a wɔka wo ho no nsoa ahotseweebea no ho emumuyɛ: na ɔwo nye wo mbabanyin a wɔka wo ho no nsoa hom asɔfodzi ho emumuyɛ.
Na wo nuanom no so, Levi ebusuakuw no, w’egya n’ebusuakuw no, fa hɔn ka woho bra ho, ma wɔmboa wo wɔ ɔsom no mu: mbom ɔwo nye wo mbabanyin a wɔka wo ho no nsom wɔ dasebuw no enyim.
Na wɔnhwɛ w’ahwɛdodze, nye Buw no nyinara ahwɛdodze no: ahotseweebea ndzɛmba ho nye afɔrmbukyia no ho nko ara na mma wɔmmba, amma woeennwuwu, hɔn o, hom o. Na wɔnka wo ho, na wɔnhwɛ ehyiadzibuw no n’ahwɛdodze, dɛ mbrɛ Buw no no ho edwuma nyinara tse: na mma ɔhɔho bi mmba hom nkyɛn.
Na hom nhwɛ ahotseweebea ahwɛdodze no, nye afɔrmbukyia no ahwɛdodze no: amma ebufuhyew bi aammba Israelmba do bio.
Na mara, hwɛ, mafa wo nuanom Levifo no mefi Israelmba no mu: mama hom dɛ wɔyɛ akyɛdze a wɔdze ama EWURADZE, dɛ wɔnyɛ ehyiadzibuw no ho edwuma.
Na ɔwo nye wo mbabanyin a wɔka wo ho no nhwɛ hom asɔfodzi no wɔ afɔrmbukyia no n’adze biara mu, na ntwamutam no mu dze no mu; na hom mfa nsom: medze asɔfodzi no mema hom dɛ akyɛdze dwuma: na ɔhɔho a ɔba ho no wonku no.
Na EWURADZE kasaa kyerɛɛ Aaron dɛ, Hwɛ, emi dze, medze me mado afɔr ahwɛdodze ama wo, mekyerɛ Israelmba adzekrɔnkrɔn nyinara, medze ama ɔwo nye wo mbabanyin no osian ngosera no ntsi, dɛ daa ahyɛdze.
Iyi na ɔnyɛ wodze wɔ krɔnkrɔndze mu adzekrɔnkrɔn a wɔdze esie efi ogya no mu no mu: hɔn ayɛyɛdze biara, mekyerɛ hɔn edziban afɔr biara, nye hɔn bɔn ho afɔr biara, nye hɔn asodzi ho afɔr biara a wɔdze brɛ me no, ɔnyɛ krɔnkrɔndze mu adzekrɔnkrɔn mma ɔwo nye wo mbabanyin no.
Dzi no wɔ bea a hɔ yɛ krɔnkrɔn: ɔbanyin biara ndzi bi; ɔnyɛ krɔnkrɔn mma wo.
Na iyi nyɛ wodze; hɔn ayɛyɛdze mu ɔmado afɔr, mekyerɛ Israelmba hɔn ohim afɔr nyinara; medze ama ɔwo, nye wo mbabanyin, nye wo mbabaa a wɔka wo ho, dɛ daa ahyɛdze: obiara a no ho tsew wɔ wo fi mu no ndzi bi.
Ngo mu papa nyinara, nye wenyin nye eburow mu papa nyinara no mu nduadzewakan a wɔdze ma EWURADZE no, ɔwo na medze ama wo.
Hɔn asaase do nduadzewa nyinara mu edziban beree a wɔdze brɛ EWURADZE no, ɔnyɛ wodze; obiara a no ho tsew wɔ wo fi mu no ndzi bi.
Israel mu adze biara a woehyira do ama nyɛ wodze.
Adze biara a obue ɔyafun, wɔ honam a wɔdze brɛ EWURADZE no nyinara mu, nyimpa nye abowa nyina, nyɛ wodze: naaso ɔpon na pon nyimpa mbakan, nye abowa a hɔn ho nntsew mbakan so pon hɔn.
Na hɔn a wɔrobɔpon hɔn a woedzi bosoom no, pon hɔn, dɛ mbrɛ w’abotwa tse, sika dwetɛbona enum, dɛ mbrɛ ahotseweebea dwetɛbona a ɔnoara nye gera eduonu.
Na ɔnantwi abakan, anaa apɔnkye abakan dze, mma mmpon; wɔyɛ krɔnkrɔn: fa hɔn bɔgyaa no petse afɔrmbukyia no do, na hyew hɔn seradze yɛ ogya afɔr a oyi nka huanhuam ma EWURADZE.
Na hɔn nam nyɛ wodze, dɛ mbrɛ ohim nyan nye aserɛ nyimfa no yɛ wodze no.
Ndzɛmba krɔnkrɔn mu ɔmado afɔr nyinara a Israelmba dze brɛ EWURADZE no, medze mama ɔwo, nye wo mbabanyin, nye wo mbabaa a wɔka wo ho no, dɛ daa ahyɛdze: ɔyɛ EWURADZE enyim daa nkyen ahyɛmu dze ma ɔwo nye w’asefo a wɔka wo ho no.
Na EWURADZE see Aaron dɛ, Mma nnya egyapadze wɔ hɔn asaase mu, nkyii so mma nnya kyɛfa bi wɔ hɔn mu: emi nye wo kyɛfa nye w’egyapadze wɔ Israelmba mu.
Na Levimba no dze, hwɛ, medze Israel mu ebupɛn du du nyinara ama hɔn dɛ egyapadze, ahyɛ hɔn som a wɔsom no ananmu, mekyerɛ ehyiadzibuw no ho ɔsom no a. Na ɔdzekɔr yi mma Israelmba no mmba ehyiadzibuw no ho, bɛyɛ na wɔasoa bɔn, na woewuwu.
Na Levifo no dze wɔnyɛ ehyiadzibuw no ho ɔsom edwuma, na wɔnsoa no ho mbusu: ɔnyɛ daa ahyɛdze wɔ hom ebusuasantsen nyina mu, na Israelmba mu dze worinnya egyapadze.
Na Israelmba ebupɛn du du a wɔdze ma dɛ ɔmado afɔr ma EWURADZE no, medze ama Levifo no dɛ egyapadze: dɛm ntsi na mase hɔn dɛ, Israelmba mu dze worinnya egyapadze no.
Na EWURADZE kasaa kyerɛɛ Moses dɛ, Afei so kasa kyerɛ Levifo no, na se hɔn dɛ, Sɛ hom regyegye Israelmba no hɔ ebupɛn du du no a medze fi hɔn hɔ ama hom dɛ hom egyapadze no a, ɔno hom mfa no mu ebupɛn du du mu ebupɛn du nyɛ no ɔmado afɔr mma EWURADZE.
Na wombu hom ɔmado afɔr mma hom dɛ ewuporoweebea eburow, nye wenyintwer mayɛ.
Dɛm na hom so mbɔ ɔmado afɔr mma EWURADZE wɔ hom ebupɛn du du a, hom gyegye no wɔ Israelmba hɔ nyinara mu; na hom mfa no mu EWURADZE ɔmado afɔr no mma ɔsɔfo Aaron.
Hom akyɛdze nyinara mu na hom mfa mu EWURADZE ɔmado afɔr biara mbra, no mu papa nyinara, mekyerɛ no mu adzekrɔnkrɔn no.
Dɛm ntsi se hɔn dɛ, Sɛ hom rema no mu papa no do a, ɔno wombu mma Levifo no dɛ ewuporoweebea ndɔree, nye wenyintwer ndɔree.
Na hom ndzi no beebiara, hom nye hom efifo: na ɔyɛ hom akatua a ɔhyɛ hom ehyiadzibuw ho ɔsom edwuma ananmu.
Na sɛ hom ma no mu papa no do a, hom ronnsoa bɔn bi wɔ ne ntsi: na mma hom nnhura Israelmba adzekrɔnkrɔn ho, mma hom eennwuwu.
Ahoguar Nsu No Na EWURADZE kasaa kyerɛɛ Moses nye Aaron dɛ, Iyi nye mbra ahyɛdze a EWURADZE ahyɛ, dɛ, Kasa kyerɛ Israelmba no, ma wɔmfa ɔnantwiber memen a nkekaa nnyi ho a onndzi dzɛm a kɔndua nnkɔr no do pɛn: na hom mfa no mma ɔsɔfo Eleazar, na ɔmfa no mpue mbra nseraban no ekyir, na obi nku no wɔ n’enyim: na ɔsɔfo Eleazar mfa ne nsatseaba mfa no bɔgyaa bi, na ɔmpetse no bɔgyaa no bi ngu ehyiadzibuw no enyim afamu mpɛn esuon: na obi nhyew ɔnantwiber no wɔ n’enyim; no nwoma, nye ne nam, nye no bɔgyaa, nye n’egyanan no: na ɔsɔfo no mfa kyindur dua, nye odwonhataw, nye serdaa, na ɔntow ngu ɔnantwiber a ɔrehyew no do.
Na afei ɔsɔfo no nhor ne ntar, na onguar wɔ nsu mu, na n’ekyir no na ɔmbra nseraban no mu, na ɔsɔfo no ho nntsew araa kodu ewimbir.
Na nyia ɔhyew no no nhor ne ntar wɔ nsu mu, na onguar no honam wɔ nsu mu, na no ho nntsew araa kodu ewimbir.
Na ɔbanyin bi a no ho tsew nsesaw ɔnantwiber no nso no, na ɔmfa nkogu nseraban no ekyir beebi a ɔtsew, na wɔmfa nsie nyɛ Israelmba mboanofo ahoguar nsu: ɔyɛ bɔn ho afɔr.
Na nyia ɔsesaw ɔnantwiber no nso no ɔnhor ne ntar, na no ho nntsew araa kodu ewimbir: na ɔnyɛ Israelmba no, nye ɔhɔho a ɔsoɛ hɔn mu no, daa ahyɛdze.
Nyia ɔka nyimpa biara no fun no no ho nntsew araa nda esuon: ɔnoara na ɔmfa iyi nguar noho da a otsia ebiasa no, na da a otsia esuon no na no ho atsew: na sɛ oennguar noho da a otsia ebiasa no, nye da a otsia esuon no a, no ho renntsew.
Obiara a ɔka nyimpa biara a oewu no fun no, na onnguar noho no, ogu EWURADZE ntamadan no ho fi; na ɔkra no wobotwa no efi Israel akyen: osiandɛ wɔammpetse ahoguar nsu no enngu no do ntsi no ho nntsew; n’ahoɔfi da ho wɔ no do.
Sɛ nyimpa wu asese mu a no ho mbra nye yi: obiara a ɔba asese no mu, na obiara a ɔwɔ asese no mu no, no ho nntsew araa nda esuon.
Na kɔɔpow biara a n’ano da hɔ a onnyi ebuado wɔ do no, no ho nntsew.
Na obiara a ɔka obi a ɔatɔr nkrantsee ano, anaa fun bi, anaa nyimpa biew bi, anaa nda bi wɔ haban mu no, no ho nntsew araa nda esuon.
Na nyia no ho nntsew no wɔmfa bɔn ho afɔr nhyewee no no nso no bi, na wɔmfa mbasu ngu do wɔ kɔɔpow mu mma no: na nyimpa a no ho tsew bi mfa odwonhataw, na ɔmfa mbɔ nsu no mu, na ɔmfa mpetse asese no, nye ndzɛmba no nyinara, nye nyimpa a wɔwɔ hɔ no, nye nyia ɔka biew, anaa ɔtɔfo, anaa fun, anaa nda bi no do: na nyimpa a no ho tsew no mfa mpetse nyia no ho nntsew no do da a otsia ebiasa no, nye da a otsia esuon no: na da a otsia esuon no onguar no; na ɔnhor ne ntar, na onguar wɔ nsu mu, na no ho ntsew ewimbir no.
Na nyimpa a no ho nntsew, na oennguar noho no, ɔkra no wobotwa no efi bagua no mu, osiandɛ oegu EWURADZE krɔnkrɔn bea ho fi: wɔmmpetsee ahoguar nsu no wɔ no do; no ho nntsew.
Na ɔnyɛ daa ahyɛdze mma hɔn: na nyia ɔpetse ahoguar nsu no nhor ne ntar; na nyia ɔka ahoguar nsu no no ho nntsew araa kodu ewimbir.
Na adze biara a nyimpa a no ho nntsew no ka no, no ho nntsew; na ɔkra a ɔka no no ho nntsew araa kodu ewimbir.
Nsɛm A Osisii Wɔ Kades Na Israelmba no, mekyerɛ mboanofo no nyina, baa Zin sar do wɔ bosoom a odzi kan no mu: na ɔman no tsenaa Kades; na Miriam wui wɔ hɔ, na wosiee no wɔ hɔ.
Nna nsu nnyi hɔ mma mboanofo no: na wohyiaa hɔnho hyiae tsiaa Moses nye Aaron.
Na ɔman no nye Moses hamee, na wɔkaa dɛ, Ka hɛn nko a nkyɛ ber a hɛn nuanom wuwui wɔ EWURADZE enyim no hɛn so yewuwui!
Na ebɛn ntsi na hom dze EWURADZE bagua aba sar yi do, dɛ yembowuwu wɔ ha, hɛn nye hɛn mbowa?
Na ɔyɛ dɛn ntsi na hom ayɛ ma yeefi Egypt efir, dɛ hom dze hɛn reba bea bɔn yi do yi?
Ɔnnyɛ abadua, anaa adɔmba, anaa wenyindua, anaa pɔmegranate eduaba bea: nkyii so nsu mpo a wɔnom bi nnyi hɔ.
Na Moses nye Aaron fii bagua no enyim kɔr ehyiadzibuw no n’abowano, na wɔdze hɔn enyim butubutuuw hɔ: na EWURADZE enyimnyam yii noho edzi kyerɛɛ hɔn.
Na EWURADZE kasaa kyerɛɛ Moses dɛ, Fa poma no, na boa mboanofo no ano, ɔwo, nye wo nua Aaron, na hom nkasa nkyerɛ ɔbotan no wɔ hɔn enyim, ma ɔmma no nsu; na yi ɔbotan no mu nsu ma hɔn: ma mboanofo no nye hɔn mbowa nnom.
Na Moses faa poma no fii EWURADZE enyim, dɛ mbrɛ ɔhyɛɛ no no.
Na Moses nye Aaron boaboaa bagua no ano wɔ ɔbotan no enyim, na ɔsee hɔn dɛ, Afei hom ntsie, hom asoɔdzenfo; ana yɛntwe ɔbotan yi mu nsu mma hom?
Na Moses maa ne nsa do, na ɔdze no poma no bɔɔ ɔbotan no mpɛn ebien: na nsu fiir edzi baa pii, na mboanofo no nye hɔn mbowa nomee.
Na EWURADZE see Moses nye Aaron dɛ, Osiandɛ hom anngye me enndzi, ammfa anntsew mo ho wɔ Israelmba enyim mu ntsi, hom remmfa bagua yi nndu asaase a medze ama hɔn no do.
Iyi nye Meriba nsu no; osiandɛ Israelmba nye EWURADZE hamee, na ɔtseew noho wɔ hɔn mu.
Na Moses somaa abɔfo fii Kades kɔr Edomhen hɔ dɛ, Mbrɛ wo nua Israel se nye yi, Woara inyim ɔhaw a aba hɛn do nyinara: mbrɛ hɛn egyanom dze sianee kɔr Egypt, na yɛdze tsenaa Egypt mber tsentsen; na Egyptfo yɛɛ hɛn, nye hɛn egyanom bɔn: na yesui frɛɛ EWURADZE a, otsiee hɛn ndze, na ɔsomaa ɔbɔfo, na oyii hɛn fii Egypt no: na, hwɛ yɛwɔ Kades, kurow a ɔwɔ wo ntoaado noho no mu: meserɛ wo, ma yentwa mu mfa w’asaase do: yerunntwa mu mmfa haban anaa wenyin ture mu, nkyii so yɛronnom bura mu nsu bi: yɛbɛfa ɔhen ne tsempɔn do ara akɔ, yɛremman enyimfa anaa abankum, ekodu dɛ yeetwa mu wɔ wo ntoaado.
Na Edom see no dɛ, Mma mmbɛfa mo mu, bɛyɛ na medze nkrantsee efir edzi ebehyia wo.
Na Israelmba no see no dɛ, Yɛrebɛfa ɔtsempɔn do akɔ: na sɛ hɛn nye hɛn mbowa nom wo nsu bi a, ɔno yebotua kaw: ɔnnyɛ biribiara, ma yɛmfa hɛn anamɔn ara mbotwa mu.
Na ɔsee dɛ, Mma hom nntwa mu.
Na Edom dze nkorɔfo pii, nye nsa a ɔyɛ dzen fiir edzi behyiaa hɔn.
Dɛm na Edom poow dɛ ɔma Israel kwan wɔ no ntoaado: dɛm ntsi Israel danee fii noho.
Na wotui fii Kades: na Israelmba no, mekyerɛ mboanofo no nyina, baa bepɔw Hor ho.
Na EWURADZE kasaa kyerɛɛ Moses nye Aaron wɔ bepɔw Hor ho, wɔ Edom asaase ntoaado dɛ, Ɔnnkɛkyɛr na Aaron akɛka no nkorɔfo ho wɔ nsamankyir: na ɔronnkɔ asaase a medze ama Israelmba no do, osiandɛ hom yɛɛ asoɔdzen wɔ m’asɛm do wɔ Meriba nsu ho.
Fa Aaron nye ne babanyin Eleazar, na fa hɔn fow bepɔw Hor: na pɔr Aaron ne ntar no, na fa hyɛ ne babanyin Eleazar: na onwu wɔ hɔ nkɛka no nkorɔfo ho.
Na Moses yɛɛ dɛ mbrɛ EWURADZE hyɛe no: na wɔfoow bepɔw Hor wɔ mboanofo no nyinara enyim.
Na Moses pɔɔr Aaron ne ntar no, na ɔdze hyɛɛ ne babanyin Eleazar; na Aaron wui wɔ bepɔw no etsifi hɔ: na Moses nye Eleazar fii bepɔw no do sianee.
Na aber a mboanofo no nyinara hun dɛ Aaron ewu no, wosuu Aaron adaduasa, mekyerɛ Israel fi no nyinara.
Israelfo Sɛɛ Keenanfo Na Aradhen, Keenannyi no a, ɔtse Pomu afamu no, tsee dɛ wɔreka dɛ Israel nam Atarim ɔkwan do aba no; nna ɔnye Israel bɔkoe, na ɔfaa hɔn mu binom ndɔmmum.
Na Israelfo bɔɔ EWURADZE anohoba see dɛ, Sɛ ɔwo dze ɔman yi rehyɛ hɛn nsa dze a, nkyɛ yɛbɛsɛɛ hɔn nkurow huntuhuntu.
Na EWURADZE tsiee Israelfo ndze, na oyii Keenanfo no mae; na wɔsɛɛ hɔn nye hɔn nkurow no huntuhuntu: na wɔtoo bea no dzin Horma.
Boran Abowatsena Na wotui fi bepɔw Hor ho dze faa Mbɛw Po kwan do, dɛ wɔrobɔ Edom asaase ho aprɔw akɔ: na ahomtsew kaa ɔman no hɔn kra pii wɔ ɔkwan no ntsi.
Na ɔman no kasaa tsiaa Nyankopɔn, nye Moses, dɛ, Ɔyɛ dɛn ntsi na hom eyi hɛn efi Egypt dɛ yembowuwu wɔ sar do yi?
Na edziban bi nnyi hɔ; na nsu bi nnyi hɔ; na edzibanhun yi afon hɛn kra.
Na EWURADZE somaa mbowatsena a wɔsɔw wɔ ɔman no mu, na wɔkɔsosɔɔw ɔman no; na Israel mu nkorɔfo pii wuwui.
Na ɔman no baa Moses nkyɛn bɛsee dɛ, Yɛayɛ bɔn, osiandɛ yɛakasa etsia EWURADZE, nye ɔwo; pa EWURADZE kyɛw, ma ombeyi mbowatsena no mfi hɛn do.
Na Moses paa kyɛw maa ɔman no.
Na EWURADZE see Moses dɛ, Yɛ boran abowatsena, na fa si dua do: na ɔbɛba dɛ, obiara a abowatsena asɔw no no, sɛ ɔhwɛ a, obenya nkwa.
Na Moses yɛɛ boran abowatsena, na ɔdze sii dua no do: na ɔbaa dɛ, sɛ abowatsena ka nyimpa bi a, ɔhwɛ boran abowatsena no a, onya nkwa.
Israelmba Sow Hɔn Akwantu Do Na Israelmba no tui, na wɔkɛkyeer nsera wɔ Obot.
Na wotui fii Obot, na wɔkɛkyeer nsera wɔ Iye-abarim, wɔ sar a ɔwɔ Moab enyim, wɔ wipuei afamu no do.
Hɔ na wofi tui, na wɔkɛkyeer nsera wɔ Zered bɔnsa mu.
Hɔ na wofi tui, na wɔkɛkyeer nsera wɔ Arnon a ɔwɔ sar do a ofi Amorifo ntoaado ba no, n’egya: na esutsen Arnon Moab ntoaado a, ɔda Moab nye Amorifo ntamu.
Dɛm ntsi wɔka no EWURADZE Akodzi nwoma no mu dɛ, Vaheb wɔ Sufa, Nye Arnon mbɔnsa no, Nye mbɔnsa no a ɔtserew no a Ɔkom kɔ Ar tsenabew afamu no, Na ɔtwer Moab ntoaado ho no.
Na hɔ na wofi tui kɔr Beer, nsubura a EWURADZE kaa ho asɛm kyerɛɛ Moses dɛ, Boa ɔman no ano, na mebɛma hɔn nsu.
Aber no mu na Israel toow ndwom yi dɛ: Nsubura tue ɛ; hom ngye no do: Nsubura a ahenmba tui no, Ɔman no mu ekunyin no fumfunii, Wɔdze ahempoma, ɔnye hɔn mpoma.
Na wofi sar no do tui kɔr Mattana: na wofi Mattana kɔr Nahaliel: na wofi Nahaliel kɔr Bamot: na wofi Bamot kɔr bɔnsa a ɔwɔ Moab haban mu wɔ Pisga etsifi a ɔhwɛ sar yiredede no enyi no mu.
Wodzi Sihon Na Og Do Konyim Na Israel somaa abɔfo ma wɔkɔr Amorifo hen Sihon nkyɛn, dɛ, Ma muntwa mu mfa w’asaase do: yɛremman haban mu, anaa wenyin ture mu; yɛronnom nsubura mu nsu bi: yɛrefa ɔhen tsempɔn do akɔ, ekodu dɛ yeetwa mu wɔ wo ntoaado.
Na Sihon amma Israel kwan ma woeenntwa mu wɔ no ntoaado: na mbom ɔboaa ne man nyinara ano, na ofiir edzi kehyiaa Israel wɔ sar no do, na ɔbaa Jahaz: na ɔnye Israel bɔkoe.
Na Israel dze nkrantsee ano kum no, na ɔfaa n’asaase ofi Arnon do dze kɔ Jabbok do, mekyerɛ okodu Ammonmba ho: osiandɛ Ammonmba ntoaado no ɔyɛ dzen.
Na Israel faa nkurow yi nyinara: na Israel tsenaa Amorifo nkurow no nyinara mu, wɔ Hesbon, nye no ho nkuroba nyinara mu.
Na Hesbon yɛ Amorifo hen Sihon kurow, ɔno na ɔnye nkan no Moabhen no ako, na ɔagye ne nsamu n’asaase nyinara kodu Arnon ho.
Dɛm ntsi hɔn a wɔkasa wɔ mbɛbu mu no ka dɛ, Hom mbra Hesbon, Ma wɔnkyekyer na wontsintsim Sihon kurow no: Na ogya bi efi Hesbon, Ogyaframee efi Sihon kurow mu: Ɔamen Moab Ar, Arnon mbea sorɔnsorɔm do ekunyin no Ɔwo Moab, due!
Kemos ɔman, ɔwo ayera: Oeyi ne mbabanyin ama dɛ eguamfo, Na ne mbabaa akɔ ndɔmmum mu, Wɔ Amorifo hen Sihon hɔ.
Yɛatotow hɔn; Hesbon ayera araa ekodu Dibon, Yɛasɛɛ hɔn araa akɔ Nofa a Ɔdze kodu Medeba.
Na Israel tsenaa Amorifo asaase do.
Na Moses somae ma wɔkɛseraa Jazer, na wɔfaa no nkuroba no, na wotuu Amorifo a wɔwɔ hɔ no.
Na wɔdanee na wɔkɔ fowee kɔr Basan ɔkwan do: na Basanhen Ɔge fiir edzi kehyiaa hɔn, ɔno nye ne man nyinara, dɛ wɔrokɔ ko wɔ Edrei.
Na EWURADZE see Moses dɛ, Mma nnsuro no: na meyi ɔno, nye ne man nyinara, nye n’asaase mahyɛ wo nsa; na yɛ no dɛ mbrɛ eyɛɛ Amorifo hen Sihon a ɔtsenaa Hesbon no.
Nna wokunkum ɔno, nye ne mbabanyin, nye ne man nyinara, kodur dɛ woenngyaa obi amma no: na wɔfaa n’asaase no.
Moabhen Balak Soma Kɔ Balaam Hɔ Na Israelmba no tui, na wɔkɛkyeer nsera wɔ Moab tɛtɛr mu wɔ Jeriko Jordan egya.
Na Zipor ne babanyin Balak hun dza Israel ayɛ Amorifo no nyinara.
Na Moab suroo ɔman no dodow, osiandɛ wɔdɔɔ so: na nketsenketse kitsaa hɔn wɔ Israelmba no ntsi.
Na Moab see Midian mpanyimfo dɛ, Afei nyimpadodow yi bɛsɛɛ dza etwa ehyia hɛn ho nyinara, dɛ mbrɛ ɔnantwi we haban mu efuw.
Na Zipor ne babanyin Balak nna aber no mu ɔyɛ Moabhen.
Na ɔsomaa abɔfo ma wɔkɔr Beor ne babanyin Balaam hɔ, wɔ Petor a ɔwɔ Esutsen no ho wɔ ne man mba asaase do dɛ wonkehyia no, dɛ, Hwɛ, ɔman bi efi Egypt aba: hwɛ, wɔkata asaase enyi, na wogu me tsentsendo: dɛm ntsi afei, meserɛ wo, bra bɛpaa ɔman yi ma me; na wɔyɛ dzen dodow ma me: dɛ bi a mibedzi nyim, ma meekuku hɔn, na maapam hɔn mefi asaase no do: na minyim dɛ nyia ɔwo ihyira no no woehyira no, na nyia ɔwo edom no no wɔadom no.
Na Moab mpanyin nye Midian mpanyin no sii mu dze ebisa no ho akatua no wɔ hɔn nsamu kɔree; na wɔbaa Balaam hɔ, na wɔbɛkaa Balak ne nsɛm no kyerɛɛ no.
Na ɔsee hɔn dɛ, Hom nsoɛ ha anadwe yi, na mebɛbrɛ hom mbuae, dɛ mbrɛ EWURADZE bɛka akyerɛ me no: na Moab mbapɔmba no nye Balaam tsenae.
Na Nyankopɔn baa Balaam nkyɛn, na ɔsee dɛ, Mbanyin bɛn na wɔnye wo wɔ hɔ yi?
Na Balaam see Nyankopɔn dɛ, Zipor ne babanyin Balak, Moabhen no, na ɔasoma ma wɔaba mo hɔ dɛ, Hwɛ, ɔman a woefi Egypt aba no, akata asaase enyi: afei, bra bɛpaa hɔn ma me; dɛ bi a mubotum menye hɔn ako, na mapam hɔn.
Na Nyankopɔn see Balaam dɛ, Mma nnye hɔn nnkɔ, mma mmpaa ɔman no: na woehyira hɔn.
Na Balaam soɛɛr anapa no, na ɔsee Balak mbapɔmba no dɛ, Hom nkɔ hom asaase do: na EWURADZE mmpen dɛ ɔbɛma me kwan ma menye hom akɔ.
Na Moab mbapɔmba no soɛree, na wɔbaa Balak nkyɛn, na wɔsee dɛ, Balaam ammpen dɛ ɔnye hɛn bɛba.
Na Balak somaa mbapɔmba a wɔdɔɔ so, na hɔn enyim wɔ nyam sen hɔn so bio.
Na wɔbaa Balaam nkyɛn, na wɔsee no dɛ, Mbrɛ Zipor babanyin Balak se nye yi, Mepa wo kyɛw, mma biribi nnsiw wo me nkyɛn ba ho kwan: na mebɛhyɛ wo enyimnyam kɛsenara, na biribiara a ebɛse me no mebɛyɛ: dɛm ntsi bra, meserɛ wo, bɛpaa ɔman yi ma me.
Na Balaam buae na ɔsee Balak no nkowaa no dɛ, Sɛ Balak dze dwetɛ nye sika ne fi ma mpo bɛma me a, murunntum mummbu EWURADZE me Nyankopɔn n’asɛm do, mennkɛyɛ biribi, dɛ osuar anaa ɔyɛ kɛse.
Afei dɛm ntsi, mɛserɛ hom, hom so ntsintsim ha anadwe yi, ma munhu dza EWURADZE bɛka akyerɛ me bio.
Na Nyankopɔn baa Balaam nkyɛn anadwe, na ɔsee no dɛ, Sɛ mbanyin no ba behyia wo a, Soɛr, nye hɔn nkɔ; mbom dza meka mekyerɛ wo no nko na yɛ.
Na Balaam soɛɛr anapa no, na ɔhyehyɛɛ n’asoasopɔnkɔ, na ɔnye Moab mbapɔmba no kɔree.
Balaam N’asoasopɔnkɔ Gye No Nkwa Na Nyankopɔn n’ebufuw dzɛwee dɛ ɔkɔree: na EWURADZE bɔfoe begyinaa ɔkwan no do dɛ ɔyɛfo bi a otsia no.
Na ɔnodze ɔtse n’asoaso do reba, na no nkowaa beenu ka no ho.
Na asoaso no hun EWURADZE no bɔfoe no dɛ ogyina ɔkwan no mu, ɔatwe ne nkrantsee kitsa ne nsamu: na asoaso no danee fii ɔkwan no mu faa nkyɛn, na ɔkɔr haban mu: na Balaam bɔɔ asoaso no dɛ ɔdze redan no aba ɔkwan mu.
Nna EWURADZE no bɔfoe no kegyinaa wenyin nture ntamu ɔkwan tokur bi mu, ban wɔ afa ha, na ban wɔ afa ha.
Na asoaso no hun EWURADZE no bɔfoe no, na ɔdze noho miaa ɔfadum no ho, na ɔdze Balaam n’anan miaa ɔfadum no: na ɔbɔɔ no bio.
Na EWURADZE no bɔfoe no kɔr kan, na okegyinaa beebi a ɔmoa, mbrɛ ɔkwan bi nnyi a wɔdan fa enyimfa anaa abankum.
Na asoaso no hun EWURADZE no bɔfoe no, na obutuuw famu wɔ Balaam n’ase: na Balaam n’ebufuw dzɛwee, na ɔdze n’abaa bɔɔ asoaso no.
Na EWURADZE buee asoaso no ano, na ɔsee Balaam dɛ, Ebɛnadze na mayɛ wo, na abɔ me mpɛn ebiasa yi?
Na Balaam see asoaso no dɛ, Osiandɛ esi me atwetwe: kɛtseankyɛ nkrantsee kitsa me nsamu, nkyɛ sisei meku wo.
Na asoaso no see Balaam dɛ, Ana nnyɛ w’asoaso nye me a atsena mo do wo nkwa tsentsen nyinara dze ebodu ndɛ da yi?
Ana menya wo dɛm nyɛe pɛn?
Na ɔsee dɛ, Oho.
Nna EWURADZE buee Balaam n’enyiwa, na ohun EWURADZE no bɔfoe no dɛ ogyina ɔkwan no mu, wɔatwe ne nkrantsee kitsa ne nsamu: na ɔbɔɔ ne tsir adze, na ɔdze n’enyim butuuw famu.
Na EWURADZE no bɔfoe no see no dɛ, Ɔyɛ dɛn ntsi na abɔ w’asoaso mpɛn ebiasa yi?
Hwɛ, emi na mefir edzi abɛyɛ wo ɔyɛfo osiandɛ wo kwan no akyea wɔ m’enyim: na asoaso no hun me, na ɔdanee fii m’enyim mpɛn ebiasa yi: sɛ wɔanndan emmfi m’enyim dze a, nkyɛ wo so sisei meku wo, na magye no nkwa.
Na Balaam see EWURADZE no bɔfoe no dɛ, Mayɛ bɔn; na minnyim dɛ ɔwo na igyinaa ɔkwan no mu tsiaa me: dɛm ntsi afei, sɛ emmpɛ a, mebɛsan m’ekyir bio.
Na EWURADZE no bɔfoe no see Balaam dɛ, Nye mbanyin no nkɔ: na mbom asɛm a mebɛka makyerɛ wo no nko na ka.
Nna Balaam nye Balak mbapɔmba no kɔree.
Na aber a Balak tsee dɛ Balaam reba no, ofiir edzi kehyiaa no wɔ Moab Kurow a ɔda Arnon ntoaado a ɔwɔ ntoaado ano no.
Na Balak see Balaam dɛ, Ana nnyɛ enyiberdo ara na mosomaa dɛ wombehyia wo ma bra?
Ɔyɛ dɛn ntsi na ammba me nkyɛn?
Egye dzi dɛ murunntum mennhyɛ wo enyimnyam a?
Na Balaam see Balak dɛ, Hwɛ, maba wo nkyɛn: ana afei mowɔ tum biara a medze meka asɛm bi?
Asɛm a Nyankopɔn dze bɛhyɛ m’anomu no, ɔno na mebɛka.
Na Balaam nye Balak kɔree, na wɔbaa Kiriat-huzoth.
Na Balak dze anantwi nye nguan bɔɔ okum afɔr, na ɔdze kɛmaa Balaam nye mbapɔmba a wɔnye no wɔ hɔ no.
Na ɔbaa dɛ anapa no, Balak faa Balaam, na ɔdze no fowee kɔr Baal ne mbea sorɔnsorɔm no do, na ofi hɔ hun ɔman no ano.
Balaam Ne Nkɔnhyɛ a Odzi Kan Na Balaam see Balak dɛ, Sisi afɔrmbukyia esuon ma me wɔ ha, na siesie anantwisaa esuon nye nguannyin esuon ma me wɔ ha.
Na Balak yɛɛ dɛ mbrɛ Balaam kae no; na Balak nye Balaam dze ɔnantwisaa kor nye oguannyin kor bobɔɔ afɔr wɔ afɔrmbukyia biara do.
Na Balaam see Balak dɛ, Gyina wo hyew afɔr no ho, na monkɔ, anyanyanbiara EWURADZE bɛba ebehyia me a: na biribiara a ɔdze bɛkyerɛ me no mebɛka makyerɛ wo.
Na osii mu kɔr sorɔnsorɔm pataa bi do.
Na Nyankopɔn behyiaa Balaam: na Balaam see no dɛ, Mesiesie afɔrmbukyia esuon no, na medze ɔnantwisaa nye oguannyin nkorkor abobɔ afɔr wɔ afɔrmbukyia biara do.
Na EWURADZE dze asɛm hyɛɛ Balaam anomu, see dɛ, San kɔ Balak nkyɛn, na dza ka nye yi.
Na ɔsanee kɔr ne nkyɛn, na, hwɛ, ogyina ne hyew afɔr no ho, ɔno nye Moab mbapɔmba no nyinara.
Na ɔkasaa no abɛbu mu see dɛ, Aram na Balak kɛfaa me bae, Moabhen no faa me fi Boka mbepɔw no mu dɛ: Bra, bɛpaa Jakob ma me, Na bra, bɛhyɛ Israel enyimguase.
Meyɛ dɛn na mepaa nyia Nyame mmpaa no?
Na meyɛ dɛn na mehyɛ nyia EWURADZE nnhyɛɛ no enyimguase?
Abotan etsifi na mifi muhun no, Na akoko do na mifi megyeen no: Hwɛ, ɔman a no nko bɛtsena a, Na worummbu no mmfora amanaman.
Woana botum akan Jakob huntuma, Anaa Israel ebupɛn anan mu kor no dodow?
Ma munwu ɔtseneneenyi wu, Na ma m’ewiei nyɛ dɛ nedze!
Na Balak see Balaam dɛ, Ebɛnadze na edze ayɛ me yi?
Mekɛfaa wo dɛ bɔdom m’atamfo, na, hwɛ, ehyira hɔn koraa.
Na obuae see dɛ, Ana onnhia dɛ mohwɛ yie na meka dza EWURADZE dze hyɛɛ m’anomu no bi a?
Balaam Ne Nkɔnhyɛ A Otsia Ebien Na Balak see no dɛ, Mepa wo kyɛw, bra ma yɛnkɔ beebi fofor, mbrɛ ifi bohu hɔn; ibohu hɔn ano nko, na innkohu hɔn nyinara: na paa hɔn ma me wɔ hɔ.
Na ɔfaa no kɔr Zofim haban mu, wɔ Pisga etsifi, na osisii mbukyia esuon, na ɔdze ɔnantwisaa, nye oguannyin bobɔɔ ɔhyew afɔr wɔ afɔrmbukyia biara do.
Na ɔsee Balak dɛ, Gyina wo hyew afɔr ho ha, ber a mirikehyia EWURADZE wɔ enyim noho yi.
Na EWURADZE behyiaa Balaam, na ɔdze asɛm hyɛɛ n’anomu, see dɛ, San kɔ Balak nkyɛn, na mbrɛ ka nye yi.
Na ɔbaa ne nkyɛn, na, hwɛ, ogyina ne hyew afɔr no ho, na Moab mbapɔmba ka no ho.
Na Balak see no dɛ, EWURADZE aka dɛn?
Na ɔkasaa abɛbu mu see dɛ, Soɛr, Balak, na tsie; Yɛ aso ma me, Zipor babanyin: Nyankopɔn nnyɛ nyimpa, na oeedzi ator; Anaaso nyimpa ba, na oeenu noho: Ana ɔase, na ɔrennyɛ?
Ana ɔakasa, na ɔremma onntsim?
Hwɛ, nhyira ho mbra na menya: Na oehyira, na murunntum menndan enyi.
Onnhun emumuyɛ wɔ Jakob mu, Nkyii so onnhun nkontompɔ wɔ Israel mu: EWURADZE ne Nyankopɔn nye no wɔ hɔ, Na ɔhen ho esebɔ wɔ hɔn mu.
Nyame eyi hɔn wɔ Egypt; Ɔwɔ ahoɔdzen dɛ ɔnantwi bɔyafo.
Ampaara nkaber bi nnyi Jakob mu, Nkyii so ebisa bi nnyi Israel mu: Afei na wɔbɛka no wɔ Jakob nye Israel ho dɛ, Ebɛnadze na Nyame ayɛ yi!
Hwɛ, ɔman no soɛr dɛ ogyataber, Na ɔma noho do dɛ ogyata: Orummbutuw gyedɛ oedzi afonam, Na ɔanom ɔtɔfo bɔgyaa ana.
Na Balak see Balaam dɛ, Mpaa na eremmpaa hɔn a, na nhyira so innhyira hɔn.
Na Balaam buae na ɔsee Balak dɛ, Ana mannka mannkyerɛ wo dɛ, dza EWURADZE bɛka no nyinara, nna mebɛyɛ?
Balaam No Nkɔnhyɛ A Otsia Ebiasa Na Balak see Balaam dɛ, Afei bra, ma memfa wo monkɔ beebi fofor; anyanyanbiara ɔbɔsɔ Nyankopɔn enyi ma efi hɔ adom hɔn ama me.
Na Balak faa Balaam kɔr Peor etsifi a ɔhwɛ sar pradada no enyi no.
Na Balaam see Balak dɛ, Sisi afɔrmbukyia esuon ma me wɔ ha, na siesie anantwisaa esuon nye nguannyin esuon ma me wɔ ha.
Na Balak yɛɛ dɛ mbrɛ Balaam see no, na ɔdze ɔnantwisaa nye oguannyin bobɔɔ ɔhyew afɔr wɔ afɔrmbukyia biara do.
Na aber a Balaam hun dɛ asɔ EWURADZE enyi dɛ ohyira Israel no, ɔannkɔ ebisa bio, dɛ nkan no, mbom ɔdze n’enyi kedzii sar no do.
Na Balaam maa n’enyi do, na ohun Israel dɛ wogu hɔ dɛ mbrɛ hɔn ebusuakuw ebusuakuw tsetsee; na Nyankopɔn sunsum baa no do.
Na ɔkasae see dɛ, Beor babanyin Balaam se dɛ, Ɔbanyin a n’enyi hu adze yie no se dɛ: Nyia otsie Nyame ne nsɛm no, Nyia ohu Twerammpon enyido adze no, Ɔrohwe ase a, wɔtseew n’enyi do no, ɔse dɛ: Ao Jakob, mbrɛ wo tsenabea dua yɛ fɛw a, Wo ntamadan no, Ao Israel!
Wɔtserɛw dɛ mbɔnsa, Dɛ esutsen ho nture, Dɛ alɔe ndua a EWURADZE atsetsɛw, Dɛ nsu ho kyindur ndua.
No mbokitsi mu nsu bobu do, Na n’asefo bɛtsena nsu pii mu, Na ne hen bɔkrɔn asen Agag, Na wɔbɛma n’ahendzi do.
Nyame eyi no efi Egypt; Ɔwɔ ahoɔdzen dɛ ɔnantwi bɔyafo: Ɔbɛmen amanaman a wɔyɛ n’atamfo, Na woebubu hɔn mbiew esinesin, Na ɔdze n’egyen menaba ehwirahwira hɔn mu.
Ɔkotowee, ɔdaa famu dɛ ogyata, Na dɛ ogyataber; woana na obopusuw no?
Nhyira nka obiara a ohyira wo, Na mpaa nka obiara a ɔpaa wo.
Balak Gya Balaam Kwan Na Balak n’ebufuw dzɛɛw Balaam do, na ɔbɔɔ ne nsamu: na Balak see Balaam dɛ, Mibehyiaa wo dɛ bɛpaa m’atamfo, na, hwɛ, ɔwo ehyira hɔn mpɛn ebiasa nye yi.
Dɛm ntsi afei guan kɔ mbrɛ ifi: modween dɛ nkyɛ mebɛhyɛ wo enyimnyam kɛse; na, hwɛ, EWURADZE esiw w’enyimnyam ho kwan.
Na Balaam see Balak dɛ, Ana mannka annkyerɛ w’abɔfoe a esomaa hɔn me nkyɛn no so dɛ, Sɛ Balak dze dwetɛ nye sika ne fi ma mpo bɛma me a, murunntum mummbu EWURADZE n’asɛm do mommbɔ me tsir mu nnkɛyɛ papa anaa bɔn: dza EWURADZE bɛka no, ɔno na mebɛka?
Na afei, hwɛ, morokɔ me man mu: bra, na memma hu dza ɔman yi dze bɛyɛ wo man wɔ nda a odzi ekyir no mu.
Na obuu no bɛ see dɛ, Beor babanyin Balaam se dɛ, Ɔbanyin a n’enyi emua no se dɛ: Nyia otsie Nyame ne nsɛm no, Na onyim Abɔso no ho nyimdzee no, Nyia ohu Twerammpon enyido adze no, Ɔrohwe ase a, wɔtseew n’enyi do no ɔse dɛ: Muhu no, nnyɛ sesei dze a: Mohwɛ no, ɔmmbɛn dze: Nworaba bi fi Jakob mu bopue, Na ahempoma befi Israel mu asoɛr, Na wɔabɔ afa Moab nkukuwa mu, Na wɔadwerew ɔko mba gyigyeegye no nyinara.
Na Edom bɛyɛ adzenyadze, Seir so a wɔyɛ n’atamfo bɛyɛ n’adzenyadze; Na Israel bɛyɛ mbanyindze ara.
Na obi fi Jakob mu bedzi tum, Na ɔasɛɛ kurow no mu dza aka no.
Na ɔhwɛɛ Amalek, na ɔsɔɔw ne kasaa no do see dɛ Amalek nye amanaman mu odzikamfo; Na n’ewiei bowie no ɔsɛɛ mu.
Na ɔhwɛɛ Kennyi, na ɔkasaa bio see dɛ, Wo tsenabew si hɔ pintsinn, Na wɔdze wo berɛbuw ahyɛ ɔbotan mu.
Naaso Kain bɔhwer, Ekodu dɛ Assur bɛfa wo ndɔmmum.
Na owiee ne kasaa no obuu no bɛ see dɛ, Ebei, Nyame reyɛ iyi no woana bɛtsena ase?
Na ahɛn befi Kittim mbew do aba, Na wɔabɛhaw Assur, na wɔahaw Eber, Na ɔnoara so ewie no ɔsɛɛ mu.
Na Balaam soɛree, na osii mu sanee kɔr ne tsenabew: na Balak so faa no kwan kɔree.
Israelmba Hɔn Edwamambɔ Na Abosonsɔr Na Israel tsenaa Sittim, na ɔman no hyɛɛ ase nye Moab mbabaa no yɛɛ ehuhudze: na wohyiahyiaa ɔman no kɔr hɔn enyame okum afɔr ho; na ɔman no dzidzii, na wɔbɔɔ hɔn mu adze maa hɔn enyame no.
Na Israel dze noho bɔɔ Baal-peor ho: na EWURADZE ebufuw dzɛɛw Israel do.
Na EWURADZE see Moses dɛ, Fa ɔman no mu etsitsir nyinara, na sensɛn hɔn ma EWURADZE wɔ ewia do, ma EWURADZE ebufuhyew no ndan mfi Israel do.
Na Moses see Israel atsɛmbuafo no dɛ, Hom mu obiara nkuku ne mbanyin a wɔdze hɔnho akɔbɔ Baal-peor ho no.
Na, hwɛ, Israelmba no mu kor dze Midiannyi ɔbaa bi baa no nuanom no nkyɛn wɔ Moses n’enyim, nye Israelmba mboanofo no nyinara enyim, aber a worususu wɔ ehyiadzibuw no n’abowano.
Na aber a ɔsɔfo Aaron ne babanyin Eleazar, ne babanyin Finehas, hunii no, ɔsoɛree fii mboanofo no mu, na ɔfaa nkambaa kitsaa ne nsamu; na odzii Israelnyi no ekyir kɔr pia no mu, na ɔdze wowɔɔ hɔn beenu nyina hwira hwiraa hɔn mu, Israelnyi no, nye ɔbaa no ohwiraa no fur mu.
Nna ɔyardɔm no siankae fii Israelmba no do.
Na hɔn a wowuwui wɔ ɔyardɔm no mu no wɔyɛ mpemeduonu anan.
Na EWURADZE kasaa kyerɛɛ Moses dɛ, Ɔsɔfo Aaron ne babanyin Eleazar, ne babanyin Finehas, adan m’ebufuw efi Israelmba do, wɔ dɛ ɔatwe me nyinkuntwe no nyinkun wɔ hɔn mu, ma mannhyew Israelmba no wɔ me nyinkuntwe mu.
Dɛm ntsi se dɛ, Hwɛ, medze m’asomdwee ahyɛmu mema no: ɔnyɛ ɔno, nye n’asefo a wobedzi n’ekyir no daa asɔfodzi ahyɛmu; osiandɛ ɔatwe ne Nyankopɔn ho nyinkun, na ɔapata ama Israelmba no.
Na Israelnyi no a wokum no no, nyia wokum no kaa Midiannyi ɔbaa no ho no, ne dzin dze Zimri, Salu ne babanyin a, ɔyɛ Simeonfo egyanom ofi mu ɔbapɔmba.
Na Midiannyi ɔbaa no a wokum no no, ne dzin dze Kozbi, Zur a ɔyɛ otsitsir wɔ Midian egyanom ofi bi mu nkorɔfo do no, ne babaa a. Na EWURADZE kasaa kyerɛɛ Moses dɛ, Hom nhiahia Midianfo no ho, na hom nku hɔn: osiandɛ hɔn so wɔdze hɔn ndaadaa a wɔdze tseetsee hom wɔ Peor ho asɛm no mu, nye hɔn akyerɛbaa Kozbi, Midian ɔsafohen no ne babaa no a wokum no wɔ ɔyardɔm da no mu wɔ Peor ho asɛm no mu no, ehiahia hom ho.
Wɔkan Israelmba Na ɔbaa dɛ ɔhaw no ekyir no, EWURADZE kasaa kyerɛɛ Moses nye ɔsɔfo Aaron ne babanyin Eleazar dɛ, Hom nkan Israelmba mboanofo no nyinara, ofi hɔn a woedzi mfe eduonu do dze rokɔ no, dɛ mbrɛ hɔn egyanom efi tsetsee, hɔn a wotum ɔsa kɔ wɔ Israel nyinara.
Na Moses nye ɔsɔfo Eleazar nye hɔn kasae wɔ Moab tɛtɛr mu wɔ Jeriko Jordan nkyɛn dɛ, Hom nkan ɔman no, ofi hɔn a woedzi mfe eduonu do dze rokɔ no; dɛ mbrɛ EWURADZE hyɛɛ Moses nye Israelmba a wofi Egypt asaase do bae no.
Reuben, Israel n’abakan no: Reuben ne mbabanyin; Hanok dze, Hanokfo ebusua: Pallu dze, Pallufo ebusua: Hezron dze, Hezronfo ebusua: Karmi dze, Karmifo ebusua.
Iyinom nye Reubenfo ebusua ebusua: na hɔn a wɔkaan hɔn wɔ mu wɔyɛ mpemeduanan ebiasa nye ahaesuon eduasa.
Na Pallu ne ba; Eliab.
Na Eliab ne mbabanyin; Nemuel, nye Datan, nye Abiram.
Iyinom nye Datan, nye Abiram no a wɔfrɛɛ hɔn wɔ mboanofo no mu no a wɔhaam Moses nye Aaron ho wɔ Kora no kuw no mu, wɔ aber a wɔhaam EWURADZE ho: na asaase buee n’ano, na ɔmemeen hɔn dze kaa Kora ho, aber a kuw no wuwui no; wɔ aber a ogya memeen nyimpa ahaenu eduonum, dze yɛɛ asɛnkyerɛdze no.
Naaso Kora ne mbabanyin no dze, woennwuwu.
Simeon ne mbabanyin dɛ mbrɛ hɔn ebusua tsetsee: Nemuel dze, Nemuelfo ebusua: Jamin dze, Jaminfo ebusua: Jakin dze, Jakinfo ebusua: Zera dze, Zerafo ebusua: Saul dze, Saulfo ebusua.
Iyinom nye Simeonfo ebusua, mpemeduonu ebien nye ahaenu.
Gad ne mbabanyin dɛ mbrɛ hɔn ebusua tsetsee: Zefon dze, Zefonfo ebusua: Hagi dze, Hagifo ebusua: Suni dze, Sunifo ebusua: Ozni dze, Oznifo ebusua: Eri dze, Erifo ebusua: Arod dze, Arodfo ebusua: Areli dze, Arelifo ebusua.
Iyinom nye Gad ne mbabanyin ebusua ebusua dɛ mbrɛ hɔn a wɔkaan hɔn wɔ mu tse, mpemeduanan nye ahaenum.
Juda ne mbabanyin, Er nye Onan: na Er nye Onan wowui wɔ Keenan asaase do.
Na Juda ne mbabanyin dɛ mbrɛ hɔn ebusua tsetsee nye yi; Sela dze, Selafo ebusua: Perez dze, Perezfo ebusua: Zera dze, Zerafo ebusua.
Na Perez ne mbabanyin nye yi; Hezron dze, Hezronfo ebusua: Hamul dze, Hamulfo ebusua.
Iyinom nye Juda ebusua ebusua dɛ mbrɛ hɔn a wɔkaan hɔn wɔ mu tse, mpemeduosuon esia nye ahaenum.
Isakar ne mbabanyin: Tola dze, Tolafo ebusua: Puva dze, Punifo ebusua: Jasub dze, Jasubfo ebusua: Simron dze, Simronfo ebusua.
Iyinom nye Isakar ebusua ebusua dɛ mbrɛ hɔn a wɔkaan hɔn wɔ mu tse, mpemeduosia anan nye ahaasa.
Zebulun ne mbabanyin dɛ mbrɛ hɔn ebusua ebusua tsetsee: Sered dze, Seredfo ebusua: Elon dze, Elonfo ebusua: Jahleel dze, Jahleelfo ebusua.
Iyinom nye Zebulunfo ebusua ebusua dɛ mbrɛ hɔn a wɔkaan hɔn wɔ mu tse, mpemeduosia nye ahaenum.
Josef ne mbabanyin dɛ mbrɛ hɔn ebusua ebusua tsetsee: Manaasɛ nye Efraim.
Manaasɛ ne mbabanyin: Makir dze, Makirfo ebusua: na Makir woo Gilead: Gilead dze, Gileadfo ebusua.
Iyinom nye Gilead ne mbabanyin: Iezer dze, Iezerfo ebusua: Helek dze, Helekfo ebusua: na Asriel dze, Asrielfo ebusua: na Sekem dze, Sekemfo ebusua: na Semida dze, Semidafo ebusua: na Hefer dze, Heferfo ebusua.
Na Hefer ne babanyin Zelofehad ennya mbabanyin, na onyaa mbabaa: na Zelofehad ne mbabaa edzin nye Mahala, nye Noa, Hogla, Milka, nye Tirza.
Iyinom nye Manaasɛ ebusua: na hɔn a wɔkaan hɔn wɔ mu wɔyɛ mpemeduonum ebien nye ahaesuon.
Iyinom nye Efraim ne mbabanyin dɛ mbrɛ hɔn ebusua ebusua tsetsee: Sutela dze, Sutelafo ebusua: Beker dze, Bekerfo ebusua: Tahan dze, Tahanfo ebusua.
Na iyinom nye Sutela ne mbabanyin: Eran dze, Eranfo ebusua.
Iyinom nye Efraim ne mbabanyin ebusua ebusua dɛ mbrɛ hɔn a wɔkaan hɔn wɔ mu tse, mpemeduasa ebien nye ahaenum.
Iyinom nye Josef ne mbabanyin dɛ mbrɛ hɔn ebusua tsetsee.
Benjamin ne mbabanyin dɛ mbrɛ hɔn ebusua ebusua tsetsee: Bela dze, Belafo ebusua: Asbel dze, Asbelfo ebusua: Ahiram dze, Ahiramfo ebusua: Sefufam dze, Sufafo ebusua: Hufam dze, Hufamfo ebusua.
Na Bela ne mbabanyin nye Ard nye Naaman: Ard dze, Ardfo ebusua: Naaman dze, Naamanfo ebusua.
Iyinom nye Benjamin ne mbabanyin dɛ mbrɛ hɔn ebusua ebusua tsetsee: na hɔn a wɔkaan hɔn wɔ mu wɔyɛ mpemeduanan enum nye ahaesia.
Iyinom nye Dan ne mbabanyin dɛ mbrɛ hɔn ebusua ebusua tsetsee: Suham dze, Suhamfo ebusua.
Iyinom nye Dan ebusua dɛ mbrɛ hɔn ebusua ebusua tsetsee.
Suhamfo ebusua nyinara, dɛ mbrɛ hɔn a wɔkaan hɔn wɔ mu tse, wɔyɛ mpemeduosia anan nye ahaanan.
Aser ne mbabanyin dɛ mbrɛ hɔn ebusua ebusua tsetsee: Imna dze, Imnafo ebusua: Isvi dze, Isvifo ebusua: Beria dze, Beriafo ebusua.
Beria ne mbabanyin dze: Heber dze, Heberfo ebusua: Malkiel dze, Malkielfo ebusua.
Na Aser ne babaa ne dzin dze Sera.
Iyinom nye Aser ne mbabanyin ebusua ebusua dɛ mbrɛ hɔn a wɔkaan hɔn wɔ mu tse, mpemeduonum ebiasa nye ahaanan.
Naftali ne mbabanyin dɛ mbrɛ hɔn ebusua ebusua tsetsee: Jahzeel dze, Jahzeelfo ebusua: Guni dze, Gunifo ebusua: Jezer dze, Jezerfo ebusua: Sillem dze, Sillemfo ebusua.
Iyinom nye Naftali ebusua dɛ mbrɛ hɔn ebusua ebusua tsetsee: na hɔn a wɔkaan hɔn wɔ mu wɔyɛ mpemeduanan enum nye ahaanan.
Iyinom nye hɔn a wɔkaan hɔn wɔ Israelmba mu, mpemahaesia nye kor ahaesuon eduasa.
Asaase No Ne Nkyɛɛ Ho Nhyehyɛɛ Na EWURADZE kasaa kyerɛɛ Moses dɛ, Iyinom na wɔnkyɛ asaase no mma hɔn dɛ egyapadze dɛ mbrɛ edzin no no dodow tse.
Nyia ɔso no ma no egyapadze a ɔso, na nyia osuar no ma no egyapadze a osuar: obiara dɛ mbrɛ hɔn a wɔkaan hɔn no mu tse no na wɔmfa n’egyapadze mma no.
Naaso asaase no wɔmfa tonto nkyɛ: dɛ mbrɛ hɔn egyanom ebusuakuw ebusuakuw edzin tsetsee no na wonnya egyapadze no.
Dɛ mbrɛ tonto no tse no na wɔmfa nkyɛ hɔn egyapadze no mma hɔn a wɔso nye hɔn a wosuar.
Levifo Ebusua Na iyinom nye hɔn a wɔkaan hɔn wɔ Levifo mu dɛ mbrɛ hɔn ebusua ebusua tsetsee: Gerson dze, Gersonfo ebusua: Kohat dze, Kohatfo ebusua: Merari dze, Merarifo ebusua.
Iyinom nye Levi ebusua ebusua: Libnifo ebusua, Hebronfo ebusua, Mahilifo ebusua, Korafo ebusua.
Na Kohat woo Amram.
Na Amram ne yer dzin dze Jokebed, Levi ne babaa a wɔwoo no ma Levi wɔ Egypt no a: na ɔwoo Aaron nye Moses nye hɔn akyerɛbaa Miriam maa Amram.
Na Aaron so wɔwoo Nadab nye Abihu, Eleazar nye Itamar maa no.
Na Nadab nye Abihu wuwui, wɔ aber a wɔdze ananagya baa EWURADZE enyim no.
Na hɔn a wɔkaan hɔn wɔ mu wɔyɛ mpemeduonu ebiasa, banyin biara a oedzi bosoom nye ekyir no: na wɔannkan hɔn ammfora Israelmba, osiandɛ wɔamma hɔn egyapadze wɔ Israelmba no mu.
Kaleb Na Josua Iyinom nye hɔn a Moses nye ɔsɔfo Eleazar kaan hɔn no; hɔn a wɔkaan Israelmba wɔ Moab tɛtɛr mu wɔ Jeriko Jordan ho no a. Na iyinom mu dze ɔbanyin biara nnyi mu a ofi hɔn a Moses nye ɔsɔfo Aaron kaan hɔn wɔ aber a wɔkaan Israelmba wɔ Sinai sar do no mu.
Na EWURADZE aka no wɔ hɔn ho dɛ, Owu na wobowuwu wɔ sar no do.
Na hɔn mu nyimpa biara annka, gyedɛ Jefune ne babanyin Kaleb, nye Nun ne babanyin Josua.
Zelofehad Mbabaa Ho Asɛm Nna Zelofehad, Hefer ne babanyin no, Gilead ne babanyin no Makir ne babanyin no, Manaasɛ ne babanyin no, ne mbabaa a wofi Josef ne babanyin Manaasɛ ebusua mu no, twee bɛnee: na ne babaa no hɔn edzin nye yi; Mahala, Noa, nye Hogla, nye Milka, nye Tirza.
Na wobegyinaa Moses, nye ɔsɔfo Eleazar, nye mbapɔmba no nye mboanofo no nyinara enyim, wɔ ehyiadzibuw no n’abowano dɛ, Hɛn egya wui wɔ sar no do, nna onnyi kuw no a wohyiahyiaa hɔnho dze tsiaa EWURADZE wɔ Kora kuw no mu no mu: mbom owui wɔ nankasa no bɔn mu: na oennya mbabanyin.
Ebɛnadze ntsi na hɛn egya ne dzin mpepa mfi n’ebusua mu, dɛ oennya ɔbanyin ntsi?
Ma hɛn egyapadze wɔ hɛn egya no nuanom mu.
Na Moses dze hɔn asɛm no baa EWURADZE enyim.
Na EWURADZE kasaa kyerɛɛ Moses dɛ, Zelofehad ne mbabaa no aka no tsenn: ɔma na ma hɔn egyapadze wɔ hɔn egya no nuanom mu; na ma hɔn egya n’egyapadze no nkɔ hɔn hɔ.
Na kasa kyerɛ Israelmba dɛ, Sɛ ɔbanyin bi wu, na onnyi ɔbabanyin a, ɔno hom mma n’egyapadze nkɔ ne babaa hɔ.
Na sɛ onnyi ɔbabaa a, ɔno hom mfa n’egyapadze mma no nuanom.
Na sɛ onnyi nuanom a, ɔno hom mfa n’egyapadze mma n’egya no nuanom.
Na sɛ n’egya nnyi nuanom a, ɔno hom mfa n’egyapadze mma no bɔgyaa a ɔbɛn no wɔ n’ebusua mu, na ɔmfa: na iyi nyɛ atsɛmbu ahyɛdze mma Israelmba, dɛ mbrɛ EWURADZE hyɛɛ Moses no.
Wɔpa Josua Dɛ Israel Kandzifo Na EWURADZE see Moses dɛ, Fow Abarim bepɔw yi, na kɔhwɛ asaase a medze ama Israelmba no.
Na sɛ inya hu a, wo so akɛka wo nkorɔfo ho, dɛ mbrɛ wo nua Aaron akɛka hɔn ho no: osiandɛ hom yɛɛ asoɔdzen wɔ m’asɛm ho wɔ Zin sar do, wɔ mboanofo ham no mu, dɛ nkyɛ hom tsew mo ho wɔ nsu no ho wɔ hɔn enyim.
(Iyi nye Meriba nsu no wɔ Kades wɔ Sin sar do no.)
Na Moses kasaa kyerɛɛ EWURADZE dɛ, Ma EWURADZE, honam nyinara esunsum Nyankopɔn, nhwehwɛ ɔbanyin bi nsi mboanofo no do a obedzi hɔn enyim efir edzi, na obedzi hɔn enyim aba mu a obegya hɔn epue, na ɔdze hɔn bɛba mu; amma EWURADZE no mboanofo aannyɛ dɛ nguan a wonnyi oguanhwɛfo.
Na EWURADZE see Moses dɛ, Fa Josua, Nun ne babanyin no, ɔbanyin a sunsum no wɔ no mu no, na fa wo nsa gu no do; na fa no gyina ɔsɔfo Eleazar, nye mboanofo no nyinara enyim; na hyɛ no mbra wɔ hɔn enyim.
Na fa w’enyimnyam no bi ma no, ma Israelmba mboanofo no nyinara ntsie no.
Na onkegyina ɔsɔfo Eleazar enyim, ɔno na obebisa Urim a ase nye kan no, atsɛmbu ama no wɔ EWURADZE enyim: na n’asɛm do na womfir edzi, na n’asɛm do na wɔmbra mu, ɔno nye Israelmba nyinara a wɔka no ho nyina, mekyerɛ mboanofo no nyinara.
Na Moses yɛɛ dɛ mbrɛ EWURADZE hyɛɛ no no nyinara: na ɔfaa Josua, na ɔdze no kegyinaa ɔsɔfo Eleazar, nye mboanofo no nyinara enyim: na ɔdze ne nsa guu no do, na ɔhyɛɛ no mbra, dɛ mbrɛ EWURADZE nam Moses do kae no.
Daa Afɔrbɔ Ho Nhyehyɛɛ Na EWURADZE kasaa kyerɛɛ Moses dɛ, Hyɛ Israelmba no, na se hɔn dɛ, M’ayɛyɛdze, me gya afɔr edziban a oyi nka huanhuam ma me no, hom ndwen do mfa mbrɛ me wɔ ne ber mu.
Na se hɔn dɛ, Ogya afɔr a hom mfa mbrɛ EWURADZE nye yi; nguambaanyin a woedzi afrenhyia afrenhyia a wonndzii dzɛm, na wɔmfa ebien da kor mbɔ ɔhyew afɔr daa.
Eguambaa kor na fa bɔ afɔr anapa na eguambaa kor so fa bɔ afɔr ewimbir; na fa isiam pa efa ebupɛn du mu kor yɛ edziban afɔr a wɔdze ngo a woesiw hin ebupɛn anan mu kor afrɔw.
Ɔyɛ daa afɔr a wɔhyehyɛe wɔ bepɔw Sinai do a oyi nka huanhuam a ɔyɛ ogya afɔr ma EWURADZE.
Na no nom afɔr wɔ eguambaa kor ho nyɛ hin ebupɛn anan mu kor: na bea krɔnkrɔn no do na hue ɔnom afɔr nsadzen no ma EWURADZE.
Na eguambaa kor no so fa bɔ afɔr ewimbir no: dɛ mbrɛ anapa edziban afɔr no tse, na mbrɛ no nom afɔr no tse no, na fa bɔ ne gya afɔr a oyi nka huanhuam ma EWURADZE.
Ahomgyeda Afɔrbɔ Ho Nhyehyɛɛ Na ahomgyeda no nguambaanyin ebien a woedzi afrenhyia afrenhyia a wonndzii dzɛm, nye edziban afɔr isiam pa efa ebupɛn du mu ebien a wɔdze ngo afrɔw nye no nom afɔr: iyi nye ahomgyeda biara ne hyew afɔr a ɔka daa ɔhyew afɔr, nye no nom afɔr ho.
Na hom abosoom ahyɛse no hom mbɔ ɔhyew afɔr mma EWURADZE; anantwisaa mburwa ebien, nye oguannyin kor, nguambaanyin esuon a woedzi afrenhyia afrenhyia a wonndzii dzɛm; na edziban afɔr isiam pa efa ebupɛn du mu ebiasa a wɔdze ngo afrɔw, nka ɔnantwisaa kor ho; na edziban afɔr isiam pa ebupɛn du mu ebien a wɔdze ngo afrɔw nka oguannyin kor no ho; na edziban afɔr isiam pa ebupɛn du mu nkorkor a wɔdze ngo afrɔw, nka eguambaa biara ho; nyɛ ɔhyew afɔr a oyi nka huanhuam, ogya afɔr mma EWURADZE.
Na no nom afɔr nyɛ wenyin hin ɔfa nka ɔnantwisaa kor ho, na hin ebupɛn ebiasa mu kor nka oguannyin no ho, na hin ebupɛn anan mu kor nka eguambaa kor ho: iyi nye bosoom biara ne hyew afɔr wɔ afrenhyia abosoom no nyina mu.
Na wɔmfa apɔnkyenyin kor mbɔ bɔn ho afɔr mma EWURADZE; mfa nka daa ɔhyew afɔr no, nye no nom afɔr no ho.
Apaho Afahyɛ Afɔrbɔ Ho Nhyehyɛɛ Na bosoom a odzi kan no mu, bosoom no ne da a otsia duanan no, ɔyɛ EWURADZE apaho.
Na bosoom no ara ne da a otsia duenum no, nyɛ afahyɛ da: nda esuon na wondzi epitsi boodoo.
Da a odzi kan no nyɛ nhyiamu krɔnkrɔn; mma mma hom nnyɛ edwumadzen biara: mbom hom mbɔ ogya afɔr, ɔhyew afɔr mma EWURADZE; anantwisaa mburwa ebien, nye oguannyin kor, nye nguambaanyin esuon a woedzi afrenhyia afrenhyia: wɔnyɛ dza wonndzii dzɛm mma hom: nye n’edziban afɔr, isiam pa a wɔdze ngo afrɔw: ebupɛn du mu ebiasa na hom mfa nka ɔnantwisaa kor ho, na ebupɛn du mu ebien nka oguannyin no ho mbra; ebupɛn du mu nkorkor na fa ka nguambaa esuon no mu eguambaa biara ho bra; na bɔn ho afɔr apɔnkyenyin kor, ma wɔmfa mpata mma hom.
Hom nyɛ iyinom nka anapa ɔhyew afɔr a ɔyɛ daa ɔhyew afɔr no ho.
Dɛm yi ara na hom nyɛ ogya afɔr edziban a oyi nka huanhuam ma EWURADZE no, daa daa, nda esuon: wɔnyɛ nka daa ɔhyew afɔr no, na no nom afɔr no ho.
Na da a otsia esuon no hom nyɛ nhyiamu krɔnkrɔn; mma hom nnyɛ edwumadzen biara.
Eso nduadzewakan da no mu, sɛ hom dze edziban fofor afɔr rebrɛ EWURADZE wɔ hom adapɛn afahyɛ mu a, hom nyɛ nhyiamu krɔnkrɔn; mma hom nnyɛ edwumadzen biara: mbom hom mbɔ ɔhyew afɔr a oyi nka huanhuam mma EWURADZE; anantwisaa mburwa ebien, oguannyin kor, nguambaanyin esuon a woedzi afrenhyia afrenhyia; na n’edziban afɔr, isiam pa a wɔdze ngo afrɔw, ebupɛn du mu ebiasa nka ɔnantwisaa kor ho, ebupɛn du mu ebien nka oguannyin kor no ho, ebupɛn du mu nkorkor nka eguambaa esuon no mu eguambaa biara ho; apɔnkyenyin kor, ma wɔmfa mpata mma hom.
Hom nyɛ mfa nka daa ɔhyew afɔr no, nye n’edziban afɔr no, nye no nom afɔr no ho.
Totorobɛnto Afahyɛ Afɔrbɔ Ho Nhyehyɛɛ Na bosoom a otsia esuon no mu, bosoom no ne da a odzi kan no, hom nyɛ nhyiamu krɔnkrɔn; mma hom nnyɛ edwumadzen edwuma: ɔyɛ totorobɛntohɛn da ma hom.
Na hom mbɔ ɔhyew afɔr a oyi nka huanhuam mma EWURADZE; ɔnantwisaa eburwa kor, oguannyin kor, nguambaanyin esuon a woedzi afrenhyia afrenhyia a wonndzii dzɛm; na n’edziban afɔr, isiam pa a wɔdze ngo afrɔw, ebupɛn du mu ebiasa nka oguannyin no ho, na ebupɛn du mu nkorkor nka eguambaa esuon no mu eguambaa biara ho: na bɔn ho afɔr apɔnkyenyin kor, ma wɔmfa mpata mma hom: mfa nka bosoom fofor ɔhyew afɔr, nye n’edziban afɔr, nye no nom afɔr ho, dɛ mbrɛ no ho mbra tsetsee, nyɛ ogya afɔr a oyi nka huanhuam mma EWURADZE.
Akɔnkyen Afɔrbɔ Ho Nhyehyɛɛ Na bosoom a otsia esuon no ara mu da a otsia du no hom nyɛ nhyiamu krɔnkrɔn; na hom mfa akɔnkyen; eso mma hom nnyɛ edwuma biara: na hom mbɔ ɔhyew afɔr a oyi nka huanhuam mma EWURADZE; ɔnantwisaa eburwa kor, oguannyin kor, nguambaanyin esuon a woedzi afrenhyia afrenhyia; a wonndzii dzɛm: na n’edziban afɔr, isiam pa a wɔdze ngo afrɔw, ebupɛn du mu ebiasa nka ɔnantwisaa no ho, ebupɛn du mu ebien nka oguannyin kor no ho, ebupɛn du mu nkorkor nka nguambaa esuon no mu eguambaa biara ho: bɔn ho afɔr apɔnkyenyin kor; mfa nka mpata bɔn ho afɔr, nye daa ɔhyew afɔr, nye n’edziban afɔr, nye no nom afɔr no ho.
Na bosoom a otsia esuon no ne da a otsia duenum no hom nyɛ nhyiamu krɔnkrɔn; mma hom nnyɛ edwumadzen biara, na hom nhyɛ fa nda esuon mma EWURADZE.
Hom mbɔ ɔhyew afɔr, ogya afɔr a oyi nka huanhuam mma EWURADZE; anantwisaa mburwa duebiasa, nguannyin ebien, nguambaanyin duanan a woedzi afrenhyia afrenhyia; a wonndzii dzɛm: na n’edziban afɔr, isiam pa a wɔdze ngo afrɔw, ebupɛn du mu ebiasa ebiasa nkeka anantwisaa du ebiasa no mu ɔnantwisaa biara ho, ebupɛn du mu ebien ebien nkeka nguannyin ebien no mu kor ho, na ebupɛn du mu nkorkor nka nguambaa duanan no mu eguambaa biara ho: na bɔn ho afɔr apɔnkyenyin kor; mfa nka daa ɔhyew afɔr, n’edziban afɔr, nye no nom afɔr no ho.
Na da a otsia ebien no hom mfa anantwisaa mburwa duebien, nguannyin ebien, nguambaanyin duanan a woedzi afrenhyia afrenhyia a wonndzii dzɛm mbra: na n’edziban afɔr nye no nom afɔr nka anantwisaa, nguannyin nye nguambaa no ho, dɛ mbrɛ hɔn dodow tse, wɔ mbra kwan: nye bɔn ho afɔr apɔnkyenyin kor; mfa nka daa ɔhyew afɔr, nye n’edziban afɔr, nye no nom afɔr no ho.
Na da a otsia ebiasa no anantwisaa dubiako, nguannyin ebien, nguambaanyin duanan a woedzi afrenhyia afrenhyia a wonndzii dzɛm; na n’edziban afɔr nye no nom afɔr nka anantwisaa, nguannyin, nye nguambaa no ho, dɛ mbrɛ hɔn dodow tse, wɔ mbra kwan: nye bɔn ho afɔr apɔnkyenyin kor; mfa nka daa ɔhyew afɔr, nye n’edziban afɔr, nye no nom afɔr no ho.
Na da a otsia anan no anantwisaa du, nguannyin ebien, nguambaanyin duanan a woedzi afrenhyia afrenhyia a wonndzii dzɛm: n’edziban afɔr nye no nom afɔr nka anantwisaa, nguannyin, nye nguambaa no ho, dɛ mbrɛ hɔn dodow tse, wɔ mbra kwan: nye bɔn ho afɔr apɔnkyenyin kor; mfa nka daa ɔhyew afɔr, n’edziban afɔr, nye no nom afɔr no ho.
Na da a otsia enum no anantwisaa akron, nguannyin ebien, nguambaanyin duanan a woedzi afrenhyia afrenhyia a wonndzii dzɛm: na n’edziban afɔr nye no nom afɔr nka anantwisaa, nguannyin, nye nguambaa no ho, dɛ mbrɛ hɔn dodow tse, wɔmbra kwan: nye bɔn ho afɔr apɔnkyenyin kor; mfa nka daa ɔhyew afɔr, n’edziban afɔr, nye no nom afɔr no ho.
Na da a otsia esia no anantwisaa awɔtwe, nguannyin ebien, nguambaanyin duanan a woedzi afrenhyia afrenhyia a wonndzii dzɛm: na n’edziban afɔr nye no nom afɔr nka anantwisaa, nguannyin, nye nguambaa ho, dɛ mbrɛ hɔn dodow tse, wɔ mbra kwan: nye bɔn ho afɔr apɔnkyenyin kor; mfa nka daa ɔhyew afɔr, n’edziban afɔr, nye no nom afɔr no ho.
Na da a otsia esuon no anantwisaa esuon, nguannyin ebien, nguambaanyin duanan a woedzi afrenhyia afrenhyia a wonndzii dzɛm: na n’edziban afɔr nye no nom afɔr nka anantwisaa, nguannyin, nye nguambaa no ho, dɛ mbrɛ hɔn dodow tse, wɔ mbrɛ kwan: nye bɔn ho afɔr apɔnkyenyin kor; mfa nka daa ɔhyew afɔr, n’edziban afɔr, nye no nom afɔr no ho.
Da a otsia awɔtwe no hom mbɔ ngua a no mu yɛ nwin: mma hom nnyɛ edwumadzen biara: mbom hom mbɔ ɔhyew afɔr, ogya afɔr a oyi nka huanhuam mma EWURADZE: ɔnantwisaa kor, oguannyin kor, nguambaanyin esuon a woedzi afrenhyia afrenhyia a wonndzii dzɛm: n’edziban afɔr nye no nom afɔr nka ɔnantwisaa, oguannyin, nye nguambaa no ho, dɛ mbrɛ hɔn dodow tse, wɔ kwan: nye bɔn ho afɔr apɔnkyenyin kor: mfa nka daa ɔhyew afɔr, nye edziban afɔr, nye no nom afɔr no ho.
Iyinom na hom mfa mbrɛ EWURADZE wɔ hom afahyɛ a wɔahyehyɛ no mu, mfa nka hom anohobadze nye hom ayamuyi afɔr ho, wɔ hom ɔhyew afɔr, nye hom edziban afɔr, nye hom ɔnom afɔr, nye hom asomdwee afɔr mu.
Na Moses kaa kyerɛɛ Israelmba no dɛ mbrɛ EWURADZE hyɛɛ Moses no nyinara.
Anohoba Ho Mbra Na Moses kasaa kyerɛɛ Israelmba ebusuakuw ebusuakuw mu etsitsir no dɛ, Iyi nye adze a EWURADZE ahyɛ.
Sɛ nyimpa bi bɔ EWURADZE anohoba, anaa ɔka ntam dze nkyehoma kyekyer ne kra a, mma ommbu n’asɛm do; ɔnyɛ dɛ mbrɛ dza ofi n’anomu nyinara tse.
Eso sɛ ɔbaa bi bɔ anohoba ma EWURADZE, na ɔdze nkyehoma kyekyer noho wɔ n’egya fie, ne nkataasiaber mu; na n’egya tse n’anohoba, nye ne nkyehoma a ɔdze akyekyer ne kra, na n’egya ennsiw no kwam a: ɔno n’anohoba nyinara ntsim hɔ, na nkyehoma biara a ɔdze akyekyer ne kra no ntsim hɔ.
Sɛ da a n’egya bɛtse no osiw no kwan dze a; ɔno n’anohoba, anaa ne nkyehoma a ɔdze akyekyer ne kra no mu biara rinntsim hɔ: na EWURADZE dze bɛkyɛ no, osiandɛ n’egya siiw no kwan.
Na sɛ ɔwɔ kun, wɔ aber a n’anohoba, anaa n’anosɛm hurutuhurutu a ɔdze akyekyer ne kra no, wɔ no do no; na no kun tse, na da a ɔtsee no oennsiw no kwan a: ɔno n’anohoba no ntsim hɔ na ne nkyehoma a ɔdze akyekyer ne kra no ntsim hɔ.
Sɛ no kun siw no kwan da a ɔtsee no dze a; ɔno ɔmma n’anohoba a ɔwɔ no do, nye n’anosɛm hurutuhurutu a ɔdze akyekyer ne kra no nyɛ kwa: na EWURADZE dze bɛkyɛr no.
Na okunafo, anaa nyia woegyaa no awar no n’anohoba dze, mekyerɛ adze biara a ɔdze kyekyer ne kra no, otsim no do.
Na sɛ ɔwɔ no kun fie na ɔbɔɔ anohoba, anaa ɔdze ntam dze nkyehoma kyekyeer ne kra, na no kun tsee, na ɔyɛɛ no komm, na oennsiw no kwan a; ɔno n’anohoba nyinara tsim hɔ, na nkyehoma biara a ɔdze akyekyer ne kra no tsim hɔ.
Sɛ no kun no ma ɔyɛ kwa wɔ da a ɔtsee no dze a; ɔno biribiara a ofii n’anomu do wɔ n’anohoba ho, anaa ne kra nkyehoma ho no, rinntsim hɔ: no kun no ama ayɛ kwa; na EWURADZE dze bɛkyɛ no.
Anohoba biara, nye ntam biara a wɔdze brɛ ɔkra adze no, no kun na ɔma otsintsim, anaa no kun na ɔma ɔyɛ kwa.
Na sɛ no kun yɛ no komm koraa fi da to da a; ɔno otsintsim n’anohoba nyinara, anaa ne nkyehoma nyinara a ɔwɔ no do no: oetsintsim no, osiandɛ ɔyɛɛ no komm wɔ da a ɔtsee no.
Sɛ ɔatse no ɔkyɛr ana ekyir no ɔama ayɛ kwa dze a; ɔno kun no nsoa yer no n’emumuyɛ.
Iyinom nye ahyɛdze a EWURADZE hyɛɛ Moses dɛ ɔnda banyin nye ne yer ntamu, ɔnda egya nye ne babaa a ɔwɔ ne nkataasiaber mu, wɔ n’egya fie ntamu.
Wotu Midianfo Do Sa Na EWURADZE kasaa kyerɛɛ Moses dɛ, Dzi Midianfo wer ma Israelmba ho: na n’ekyir no akɛka wo nkorɔfo ho wɔ nsamankyir.
Na Moses kasaa kyerɛɛ ɔman no dɛ, Hom mma hom mu mbanyin mmia mma ɔsa no, ama woeetu akɔ Midian do, na wɔmfa EWURADZE n’awerdzi nkɔ Midianfo do.
Hom mma Israel ebusuakuw ebusuakuw nyinara mu, ebusuakuw biara mu nyimpa apem nkɔ ɔsa no.
Nna woyiyii Israel mpempem mu mpemduebien a womiae maa ɔsa no, ebusuakuw biara mu apem.
Na Moses somaa hɔn, ebusuakuw biara mu apem no, ma wɔkɔr ɔsa no, hɔn nye ɔsɔfo Eleazar ne babanyin Finehas ɔdze ahotseweebea ndzɛmba no na ewubɔ ntotorobɛnto no wɔ ne nsamu na wɔkɔr ɔsa no.
Na wɔnye Midian kɔkoe dɛ mbrɛ EWURADZE hyɛɛ Moses no; na wokunkum mbanyin no nyinara.
Na wokunkum Midian ahemfo no kaa hɔn atɔfo nkaa no ho.
Evi, Rekem, Zur, Hur, nye Reba Midian ahemfo beenum no; na wɔdze nkrantsee kum Beor ne babanyin Balaam so.
Na Israelmba no faa Midian mbaa no nye hɔn mbofraba no ndɔmmum; na wɔfoom hɔn ofiembowa nyinara, nye hɔn nguankuw nyinara, nye hɔn ahodze nyinara.
Na wɔdze ogya hyehyeew hɔn nkurow nyinara wɔ mbeambea a wɔtsetsee no, nye hɔn nseraban nyinara.
Na wɔfaa asadze no nyinara, nye afonam no nyinara, nyimpa nye abowa nyina.
Na wɔdze ndɔmmum no, nye afonam no, nye asadze no, brɛɛ Moses, nye ɔsɔfo Eleazar, nye Israel mboanofo no; wɔ nseraban no mu wɔ Moab tɛtɛr a ɔda Jeriko Jordan ho no do.
Na Moses, nye ɔsɔfo Eleazar, nye mboanofo no mu mbapɔmba no nyinara fiir edzi kehyiaa hɔn wɔ nseraban no ekyir.
Na Moses no bo fuuw dɔm no hɔn asafohemfo no, apem apem do asafohemfo nye ɔha ɔha do asafohemfo a wofi asayɛ bae no.
Na Moses see hɔn dɛ, Ana hom agye mbaa no nyinara nkwa?
Hwɛ, iyinom, na ɔnam Balaam apam do, wɔmaa Israel yɛɛ bɔn tsiaa EWURADZE wɔ Peor asɛm no mu, na ɔmaa ɔyardɔm baa EWURADZE no mboanofo mu no.
Afei dɛm ntsi hom nkuku mbofraba no mu mbanyin nyinara, na wonku ɔbaa biara a oehu ɔbanyin dɛ ɔnye no ada.
Na mbaa mbofraba a wonnhun ɔbanyin dɛ wɔnye no ada no dze, hom ngye hɔn nkwa mma homho.
Na hom nkyer nsera wɔ nseraban no ekyir nda esuon: obiara a oeku nyimpa bi no, nye obiara a ɔaka ɔtɔfo bi no, hom ntsew homho da a otsia ebiasa no, nye da a otsia esuon no, hom nye hom ndɔmmumfo no.
Na atar biara dze, nye adze a wɔdze nwoma ayɛ nyinara, nye mpɔnkyenhwi edwuma nyinara, nye adze a wɔdze dua ayɛ nyinara, homara hom ntsew ho.
Na ɔsɔfo Eleazar see mbanyin akofo a wɔkɔr akono no dɛ, Iyi nye mbra a EWURADZE dze ahyɛ Moses no mu ahyɛdze: naaso sika nye dwetɛ, boran, dadze, seenyaa, nye sumbui no, adze biara a obotum ogya no, hom mma ɔnkɛfa ogya mu, na no ho ntsew; naaso hom mfa ahoguar nsu no ntsew ho: na adze a onnkotum ogya no nyinara, hom mma ɔnkɛfa nsu mu.
Na hom nhor hom ntar da a otsia esuon no, na hom ho ntsew, na n’ekyir no na hom mbra nseraban no mu.
Na EWURADZE kasaa kyerɛɛ Moses dɛ mbu, Ɔwo nye ɔsɔfo Eleazar nye mboanofo no egyanom efi mu etsitsir no, afonam a wɔfae no ano, nyimpa nye mbowa nyina, na kyɛ afonam no mu akyɛkyɛ ebien; ma mbanyin akofo a wɔkɔr akono no, nye mboanofo no nyinara: na gye mbanyin asayɛfo a wɔkɔr akono no hɔ tow ma EWURADZE: nyimpa, nye anantwi, nye nsoasopɔnkɔ, nye nguankuw mu ahaenum mu nkorkor: gye no wɔ hɔn ɔfa no mu, na fa ma ɔsɔfo Eleazar, dɛ EWURADZE ɔmado afɔr.
Na Israelmba ɔfa mu dze, gye nyimpa, anantwi, nsaso, nye nguankuw no, mekyerɛ ofiembowa nyinara mu eduonum eduonum mu nkorkor, na fa ma Levifo no a wɔhwɛ EWURADZE ntamadan ahwɛdodze do no.
Na Moses nye ɔsɔfo Eleazar yɛɛ dɛ mbrɛ EWURADZE hyɛɛ Moses no.
Afei afonam a ɔbor asadze a mbanyin asayɛfo no fae no do no, ɔyɛ nguan mpemahaesia eduosuon enum, nye anantwi mpemeduosuon ebien, nye nsoasopɔnkɔ mpemeduosia biako, nye nyimpa, mbaa a wonnhun ɔbanyin dɛ wɔnye no ada, nyinara wɔyɛ mpemeduasa ebien.
Na ɔfa no a ɔyɛ hɔn a wotui kɔr ɔsa no hɔn kyɛfa no, no dodow yɛ nguan mpemahaebiasa eduasa esuon nye ahaenum: na nguan no mu ɔtow a woyiyii maa EWURADZE no yɛ ahaesia eduosuon enum.
Na anantwi no yɛ mpemeduasa esia; hɔn mu ɔtow a woyiyii maa EWURADZE yɛ eduosuon ebien.
Na nsoasopɔnkɔ no yɛ mpemeduasa nye ahaenum; hɔn mu ɔtow a woyiyii maa EWURADZE yɛ eduosia biako.
Na nyimpa no yɛ mpemduesia; hɔn mu ɔtow a woyiyii maa EWURADZE yɛ nyimpa eduasa ebien.
Na Moses dze ɔtow a ɔyɛ EWURADZE ɔmado afɔr no maa ɔsɔfo Eleazar, dɛ mbrɛ EWURADZE hyɛɛ Moses no.
Na Israelmba hɔn ɔfa no a Moses gyee no wɔ akofo no hɔ no mu dze, nye Israelmba hɔn ɔfa no mu dze, Moses faa eduonum eduonum mu nkorkor, nyimpa nye mbowa nyina, na ɔdze maa Levifo no a wɔhwɛ EWURADZE ntamadan ahwɛdodze do no; dɛ mbrɛ EWURADZE hyɛɛ Moses no.
Na asafohemfo a wɔhwɛ dɔm mpempem do no, nye apem apem do asafohemfo, nye ɔha ɔha do asafohemfo no, baa Moses nkyɛn: na wɔbɛsee no dɛ, Wo nkowaa yeebu akofo a wɔwɔ hɛn nsamu no ano, na hɛn mu nyimpa kor mpo annyew.
Na yɛdze EWURADZE n’ayɛyɛdze aba, dza nyimpa biara enya no a, sika ndwindze, ananadze ntweaban, nye nsakɔnadze, nsɔwanonkaba, nsowamuadze, nye nkɔnmuadze, dɛ wɔmfa mpata mma hɛn akra wɔ EWURADZE enyim.
Na Moses nye ɔsɔfo Eleazar gyee hɔn hɔ sika no, mekyerɛ edwindze no nyinara.
Na ɔmado afɔr sika nyinara a wɔdze brɛ EWURADZE a ofi apem apem do asafohemfo, nye ɔha ɔha do asafohemfo hɔ no, ɔyɛ dwetɛbona mpemduesia ahaesuon eduonum.
Na akofo no hɔn afom asadze dze, hɔnankasa na wɔfefae.
Na Moses nye ɔsɔfo Eleazar gyee sika no wɔ apem apem nye ɔha ɔha do asafohemfo no hɔ, na wɔdze baa ehyiadzibuw no mu, dɛ ɔnyɛ Israelmba no nkaadze wɔ EWURADZE enyim.
