Jordan Esuogya Ebusuakuw Afei Reubenmba nye Gadmba no wɔ ofiembowa dodow a wɔdɔɔ so kɛsenara: na aber a wohun Jazer, nye Gilead asaase no, na hwɛ, bea no fata ofiembowa bea no; Wɔbae bɛkaa kyerɛɛ Moses, nye ɔsɔfo Eleazar, nye mboanofo no mu mbapɔmba no dɛ, Atarot, nye Dibon, nye Jazer, nye Nimra, nye Hesbon, nye Eleale, nye Sebam, nye Nebo, nye Beon, asaase a EWURADZE bɔɔ no wɔ Israel mboanofo no enyim no, yɛ asaase a oye ma mbowanyɛn, na wo nkowaa so wɔ ofiembowa.
Na wɔsee dɛ, Sɛ yeenya w’enyim enyimnyam a, ma wɔmfa asaase yi mma wo nkowaa ma yɛmfa; mma mmfa hɛn nntwa Jordan.
Na Moses see Gadmba nye Reubenmba no dɛ, Aso hom nuanom nkɔ ɔsa, na hom ntsena ha?
Na ɔyɛ dɛn ntsi na hom tu Israelmba akoma dɛ mma wonntwa nnkɔ asaase a EWURADZE dze ama hɔn no do yi?
Dɛm na hom egyanom yɛe, wɔ aber a mosomaa hɔn fii Kades-barnea dɛ wɔnkɔhwɛ asaase no.
Na aber a wɔfowee kɔr Eskol mbɔnsa mu, na wohun asaase no, wobotuu Israelmba no hɔn akoma dɛ mma wɔnnkɔ asaase a EWURADZE dze ama hɔn no do.
Na EWURADZE ebufuw dzɛɛw da no, na ɔkaa ntam dɛ, Ampaara mbanyin a wofi Egypt bae no a woedzi mfe eduonu nye ekyir no mu biara runnhu asaase a mekaa ho ntam mekyerɛɛ Abraham, nye Isaak, nye Jakob no; osiandɛ woennwie m’ekyir dzi: gyedɛ Keniznyi Jefune ne babanyin Kaleb, nye Nun ne babanyin Josua: osiandɛ hɔn na woedzi EWURADZE ekyir nokwar mu.
Na EWURADZE ebufuw dzɛɛw Israel do, na ɔmaa wokekyiin sar no do mfe eduanan, ma okodur dɛ ebusuasantsen no a wɔyɛɛ bɔn wɔ EWURADZE enyim no nyinara hyewee.
Na, hwɛ, hom asoɛr egyina hom egyanom ananmu, ndzebɔnyɛfo asefo, dɛ hom da ho araa dze EWURADZE n’ebufuhyew no reba Israel do.
Na sɛ hom dan fi n’ekyir a, ɔbɛda ho ara adan hɔn egya wɔ sar no do; na hom asɛɛ ɔman yi nyinara.
Na wɔbaa ne nkyɛn bɛsee dɛ, Nguamban na yɛbɛgyegye ama hɛn ofiembowa wɔ ha, na nkurow so yɛbɛkyekyer ama hɛn mbofraba: na hɛnankasa dze hɛn ho bɛyɛ har yeemia edzi Israelmba enyim, ekodu dɛ yɛdze hɔn bɔkɔ ekodu hɔn tsenabew ana: na hɛn mbofraba no ntsenatsena nkurow a wɔagye ho ban mu osian asaase no do atsefo no ntsi.
Yɛrennsan mmba hɛn efiefi, gyedɛ Israelmba ɔbanyin biara enya egyapadze edzi ana.
Na yɛnnye hɔn remmfa enyadze wɔ Jordan egya, ɔdze kɔ no; osiandɛ hɛn egyapadze ebefir hɛn Jordan nkyɛn ha boka afamu.
Na Moses see hɔn dɛ, Sɛ hom bɛyɛ iyi; sɛ hom bemia homho wɔ EWURADZE enyim akɔ ɔsa, na hom mu nyimpa biara a oemia botwa Jordan edzi EWURADZE enyim, ekodu dɛ ɔbɛpam n’atamfo efi n’enyim na wɔabrɛ asaase no adze wɔ EWURADZE enyim a: nna n’ekyir no hom bɛsan na hom edzi bem wɔ EWURADZE nye Israelmba ho; na asaase yi nyɛ hom enyadze wɔ EWURADZE enyim.
Na sɛ hom annyɛ dɛm a, hwɛ hom ayɛ bɔn etsia EWURADZE: na hom nhu dɛ hom bɔn beyi hom ama.
Hom nkyekyer nkurow mma hom mbofraba, na nguamban mma hom nguan; na hom nyɛ dza efi hom anomu epue no.
Na Gadmba nye Reubenmba no kasaa kyerɛɛ Moses dɛ, Wo nkowaa bɛyɛ dɛ mbrɛ mo wura ahyɛ no.
Hɛn mbofraba hɛn yernom hɛn nguankuw, nye hɛn ofiembowa nyinara, bɛtsena Gilead nkurow no mu hɔ: na wo nkowaa dze, ɔbanyin biara a oemia rokɔ ɔsa no, botwa mu wɔ EWURADZE enyim akɔko dɛ mbrɛ mo wura aka no.
Nna Moses dze hɔn ho mbra maa ɔsɔfo Eleazar, nye Nun ne babanyin Josua, nye Israelmba ebusuakuw ebusuakuw mu egyanom efi do etsitsir no.
Na Moses see hɔn dɛ, Sɛ Gadmba nye Reubenmba nye hom twa Jordan, ɔbanyin biara a oemia dzi EWURADZE enyim rokɔko no, na wɔbrɛ asaase no adze wɔ hom enyim a; ɔno hom mfa Gilead asaase mma hɔn ma wɔmfa: na sɛ woemmia nye hom enntwa a, ɔnodze wɔmma wonnya enyadze wɔ hom mu wɔ Keenan asaase do.
Na Gadmba nye Reubenmba no buaa dɛ, Dɛ mbrɛ EWURADZE aka akyerɛ wo nkowaa no, dɛmara na yɛbɛyɛ.
Yebemia wɔ EWURADZE enyim etwa mu akɔ Keenan asaase do, na hɛn egyapadze a yeenya no wɔ Jordan egya ha no ako hɛn hɔ.
Na Moses dze Amorifo hen Sihon n’ahendzi, nye Basanhen Ɔge n’ahendzi, asaase no, dɛ mbrɛ no do nkurow nye no ntoaado tsetsee no, mekyerɛ asaase no do nkurow a ehyia do no, maa hɔn, mekyerɛ Gadmba, nye Reubenmba, nye Josef ne babanyin Manaasɛ n’ebusuakuw ɔfa no a. Na Gadmba no kyekyeer Dibon, nye Atarot, nye Aroer; nye Atroth-sofan, nye Jazer, nye Jogbeha; nye Bɛt-nimra, nye Bɛt-haran: nkurow a wɔagyegye ho ban, nye nguamban.
Na Reubenmba no kyekyeer Hesbon, nye Eleale, nye Kiriataim; nye Nebo, nye Baal-meon, (hɔn edzin no sakyesakyeree), nye Sibma: na wɔdze edzin fofor totoo nkurow a wɔkyekyeree no.
Na Manaasɛ ne babanyin Makir mba no sii mu Gilead, na wɔkɛfae, na wotuu Amorifo a wɔwɔ mu hɔ no.
Na Moses dze Gilead maa Manaasɛ ne babanyin Makir; na ɔtsenaa mu.
Na Manaasɛ ne babanyin Jair sii mu kɛfaa no nkurow no na ɔfrɛɛ no Havot-jair.
Na Noba sii mu kɛfaa Kenat, nye no nkuroba, na ɔfrɛɛ no Noba, dɛ mbrɛ nankasa ne dzin no tse.
Israelfo Akwantu Iyinom nye Israelmba akwantu a wɔnam Moses nye Aaron nsa do fi Egypt asaase do tutui dɛ mbrɛ hɔn dɔm tsetsee.
Na Moses nam EWURADZE mbrasɛm do kyerɛɛw hɔn edzifir dɛ mbrɛ hɔn akwantu mu asoɛe no tse: na iyinom nye hɔn akwantu mu asoɛe dɛ mbrɛ hɔn edzifir tse.
Na bosoom a odzi kan no mu wotui fii Rameses, wɔ bosoom a odzi kan no mu da a otsia duenum no; apaho no ekyir adzekyee na Israelmba no dze ahosɛpɛw kɛse fiir edzi wɔ Egyptfo nyinara enyim, wɔ aber a Egyptfo risie sie hɔn mbakan nyinara a EWURADZE kunkum hɔn wɔ hɔn mu no: na hɔn enyame no so EWURADZE buu hɔn ntsɛn.
Na Israelmba no tui fii Rameses na wɔkɛkyeer nsera wɔ Sukɔt.
Na wotui fii Sukɔt, na wɔkɛkyeer nsera wɔ Etam a ɔwɔ sar no ano no.
Na wotui fii Etam, na wɔdanee baa Pi-hahirot a ɔwɔ Baal-zefon enyim no bio: na wɔkyeer nsera wɔ Migidɔl enyim.
Na wotui fii Hahirot enyim, na wokotwaa mu faa po no ne finimfin kɔr sar no do: na wɔnantseew ndaansa kwan wɔ Etam sar no do, na wɔkɛkyeer nsera wɔ Mara.
Na wotui fii Mara, na wɔbaa Elim: na Elim hɔ na nsunyiwa duebien, nye nkyiresua ndua eduosuon wɔ; na wɔkyeer hɔ nsera.
Na wotui fii Elim, na wɔkɛkyeer nsera wɔ Mbɛw Po a binom frɛ no Po kɔkɔɔ no ho.
Na wotui fii Mbɛw Po no ho, na wɔkɛkyeer nsera wɔ Sin sar do.
Na wotui fii Sin sar do, na wɔkɛkyeer nsera wɔ Dofka.
Na wotui fii Dofka, na wɔkɛkyeer nsera wɔ Alus.
Na wotui fii Alus, na wɔkɛkyeer nsera wɔ Refidim, mbrɛ ɔman no ennya nsu annom no a. Na wotui fii Refidim, na wɔkɛkyeer nsera wɔ Sinai sar do.
Na wotui fii Sinai sar do, na wɔkɛkyeer nsera wɔ Kibrot-hataava.
Na wotui fii Kibrot-hataava, na wɔkɛkyeer nsera wɔ Hazerot.
Na wotui fii Hazerot, na wɔkɛkyeer nsera wɔ Ritma.
Na wotui fii Ritma, na wɔkɛkyeer nsera wɔ Rimmon-perez.
Na wotui fii Rimmon-perez, na wɔkɛkyeer nsera wɔ Libna.
Na wotui fii Libna, na wɔkɛkyeer nsera wɔ Rissa.
Na wotui fii Rissa, na wɔkɛkyeer nsera wɔ Kehelata.
Na wotui fii Kehelata, na wɔkɛkyeer nsera wɔ bepɔw Sefer do.
Na wotui fii bepɔw Sefer do, na wɔkɛkyeer nsera wɔ Harada.
Na wotui fii Harada, na wɔkɛkyeer nsera wɔ Makhelot.
Na wotui fii Makhelot na wɔkɛkyeer nsera wɔ Tahat.
Na wotui fii Tahat, na wɔkɛkyeer nsera wɔ Tera.
Na wotui fii Tera, na wɔkɛkyeer nsera wɔ Mitka.
Na wotui fii Mitka na wɔkɛkyeer nsera wɔ Hasmona.
Na wotui fii Hasmona na wɔkɛkyeer nsera wɔ Maserot.
Na wotui fii Maserot, na wɔkɛkyeer nsera wɔ Bene-jaakan.
Na wotui fii Bene-jaakan, na wɔkɛkyeer nsera wɔ Hor-hagidgad.
Na wotui fii Hor-hagidgad, na wɔkɛkyeer nsera wɔ Jotbata.
Na wotui fii Jotbata, na wɔkɛkyeer nsera wɔ Abrona.
Na wotui fii Abrona, na wɔkɛkyeer nsera wɔ Ezion-geber.
Na wotui fii Ezion-geber, na wɔkɛkyeer nsera wɔ Zin sar do (ɔnoara nye Kades).
Na wotui fii Kades, na wɔkɛkyeer nsera wɔ bepɔw Hor do, wɔ Edom asaase ano.
Na ɔsɔfo Aaron nam EWURADZE mbrasɛm do fowee kɔr bepɔw Hor do na okowui wɔ hɔ, wɔ afe a Israelmba fi Egypt asaase do firii no ekyir dza otsia eduanan no mu, bosoom a otsia enum no mu da a odzi bosoom no ne kan no.
Na aber a Aaron wui wɔ bepɔw Hor do no na oedzi mfe ɔha eduonu ebiasa.
Na Keenannyi, Aradhen no a ɔtse Keenan asaase do wɔ Pomu afamu no tsee dɛ Israelmba no reba.
Na wotui fii bepɔw Hor ho, na wɔkɛkyeer nsera wɔ Zalmona.
Na wotui fii Zalmona, na wɔkɛkyeer nsera wɔ Punon.
Na wotui fii Punon, na wɔkɛkyeer nsera wɔ Obot.
Na wotui fii Obot, na wɔkɛkyeer nsera wɔ Iye-abarim, wɔ Moab ntoaado.
Na wotui fii Iyim, na wɔkɛkyeer nsera wɔ Dibon-gad.
Na wotui fii Dibon-gad, na wɔkɛkyeer nsera wɔ Almon-diblathaim.
Na wotui fii Almon-diblathaim, na wɔkɛkyeer nsera wɔ Abarim mbepɔw do, wɔ Nebo enyim.
Na wotui fii Abarim mbepɔw do, na wɔkɛkyeer nsera wɔ Moab tɛtɛr mu, wɔ Jeriko Jordan ho.
Na wɔkyeer Jordan ho nsera, fi Bɛt-jesimot araa kodur Abel-Sittim wɔ Moab tɛtɛr mu.
Ahyɛdze Wɔ Keenanfo Ho Na EWURADZE kasaa kyerɛɛ Moses wɔ Moab tɛtɛr mu wɔ Jeriko Jordan ho, dɛ, Kasa kyerɛ Israelmba, na se hɔn dɛ, Sɛ hom twa Jordan kɔ Keenan asaase do a, ɔno hom mpam asaase no do atsefo no nyinara mfi hom enyim, na hom nsɛɛ hɔn abo ehonyi nyinara, na hom nsɛɛ hɔn ehonyi a woegu no nyinara, na hom ndwurudwuruw mbea sorɔnsorɔm nyinara: na hom mfa asaase no mfa, na hom ntsena do: na hom na medze asaase no ama hom dɛ hom mfa.
Na hom ntwe tonto mfa nkyɛ asaase no dɛ mbrɛ hom ebusua ebusua tsetsee; hɔn a wɔso no hom mma hɔn egyapadze a ɔso, na hɔn a wosuar no ma hɔn egyapadze a osuar: beebiara mbrɛ tonto no abɔ nyimpa biara no hɔ na ɔnyɛ nedze; dɛ mbrɛ hom egyanom mbusuakuw tsetsee no na hom nyinya hom egyapadze.
Na sɛ hom ammpam asaase no do atsefo no wɔ hom enyim a; ɔno hɔn mu hɔn a hom ama wɔaka no bɛyɛ dɛ awowɔdze wɔ hom enyiwa mu, na ayɛ dɛ nsoɛ, wɔ hom mfe mu, na woehiahia hom ho wɔ asaase a hom tse do no do.
Na ɔbɛba dɛ, dɛ mbrɛ modween dɛ mebɛyɛ hɔn no, dɛmara na mebɛyɛ hom.
Asaase No Do Ahe Na EWURADZE kasaa kyerɛɛ Moses dɛ, Hyɛ Israelmba no mbra, na se hɔn dɛ, Sɛ hom du Keenan asaase no do a, (iyi nye asaase a ɔda hɔ ma hom dɛ egyapadze, mekyerɛ Keenan asaase no dɛ mbrɛ n’ahe tsetsee,) ɔno hom pomu afamu nkyɛn mfi Zin sar do wɔ Edom nkyɛn mu, na hom pomu ɔhe mfi Nkyen Epo ano wɔ boka afamu: na hom ɔhe no ndan mfa Akrabbim mfowee pomu afamu, na ontwa mu nkɔ Zin: na n’edzifir ndu Kades-barnea pomu afamu; na ɔnkɔ Hazar-adar, na ontwa mu nkɛfa Azmon: na ɔhe no mpon mfi Azmon nkɔ Egypt ɔwora ho, na n’edzifir ndu po no ano.
Na anee afamu ɔhe no dze, hom wɔ po kɛse no dze yɛ ne he: iyi na ɔnyɛ hom anee ɔhe.
Na iyi nyɛ hom kwaamu ɔhe: hom mfi po kɛse no ho nsan bepɔw Hor mfa: bepɔw Hor ho na hom mfi nsan mbrɛ wɔfa kɔ Hamat; na ɔhe no n’edzifir ndu Zedad: na ɔhe no mfir edzi nkɔ Zifron, na n’edzifir ndu Hazar-enan: iyi na ɔnyɛ hom kwaamu ɔhe.
Na hom nsan boka he mfa mfi Hazar-enan nkɔ Sefam: na ɔhe no mfi Sefam nsian nkɔ Ribla, wɔ Ain no boka afamu, na ɔhe no nsian araa nkodu Kinneret pomu afamu wɔ boka afamu: na ɔhe no nsian nkodu Jordan do, na n’edzifir ndu Nkyen Po ho: iyi nye hom asaase dɛ mbrɛ no ho ahe tsetsee.
Na Moses hyɛɛ Israelmba no mbra dɛ, Iyi nye asaase a hom ntwe ho tonto mfa nkyɛ no a EWURADZE ahyɛ dɛ wɔmfa mma mbusuakuw akron, nye ebusuakuw ɔfa no; nye Reubenmba ebusuakuw, dɛ mbrɛ hɔn egyanom efi tsetsee nye Gadmba ebusuakuw dɛ mbrɛ hɔn egyanom efi tsetsee, nye Manaasɛ ebusuakuw ɔfa no, woenya hɔn egyapadze: na mbusuakuw ebien no nye ebusuakuw ɔfa no enya hɔn egyapadze wɔ Jeriko Jordan egya wɔ boka afamu ɔdze kɔ wipuei no.
Na EWURADZE kasaa kyerɛɛ Moses dɛ, Iyinom nye mbanyin a wɔnkyɛ asaase no mu mma hom no hɔn edzin: ɔsɔfo Eleazar, nye Nun ne babanyin Josua.
Na hom nyi ebusuakuw biara mu ɔbapɔmba kor ma wɔnkyɛ asaase no mu.
Na mbanyin no hɔn edzin nye yi: Juda n’ebusuakuw mu, Jefune ne babanyin Kaleb.
Simeon ne mba ebusuakuw mu, Ammihud ne babanyin Semuel.
Benjamin n’ebusuakuw mu, Kislon ne babanyin Elidad.
Nye Dan ne mba ebusuakuw mu ɔbapɔmba, Jogli ne babanyin Bukki.
Josef ne mba mu: Manaasɛ ne mba ebusuakuw mu ɔbapɔmba, Efod ne babanyin Hanniel: nye Efraim ne mba ebusuakuw mu ɔbapɔmba, Siftan ne babanyin Kemuel.
Na Zebulun ne mba ebusuakuw mu ɔbapɔmba, Parnak ne babanyin Elizafan.
Na Isakar ne mba ebusuakuw mu ɔbapɔmba, Azzan ne babanyin Paltiel.
Na Aser ne mba ebusuakuw mu ɔbapɔmba, Selomi ne babanyin Ahihud.
Na Naftali ne mba ebusuakuw mu ɔbapɔmba, Ammihud ne babanyin Pedahel.
Iyinom nye hɔn a EWURADZE hyɛɛ hɔn dɛ wɔnkyɛ Keenan asaase no mu mma Israelmba no.
Levifo No Nkurow Na EWURADZE kasaa kyerɛɛ Moses wɔ Moab tɛtɛr mu wɔ Jeriko Jordan do dɛ, Hyɛ Israelmba no ma wɔmfa hɔn enyadze egyapadze no mu nkurow bi mma Levifo no ma wɔntsena mu; na nkurow no ho mfikyisaase no so hom mfa mma Levifo no.
Na nkurow no na wɔntsena mu: na no ho mfikyisaase no ndeda ho mma hɔn fiembowa, nye hɔn ahodze, nye hɔn mbowa nyinara.
Na nkurow no ho mfikyisaase a hom dze bɛma Levifo no, mfi kurow no fasu ekyir nkɔ basafa ahaenum ahaenum ntwa ho nhyia.
Na hom nsusu kurow no ekyir boka afamu basafa apem, nye pomu afamu basafa apem, nye anee afamu basafa apem, nye kwaamu afamu basafa apem, na kurow no nda ne finimfin.
Iyi na ɔnyɛ nkurow no ho mfikyisaase mma hɔn.
Na nkurow no a hom dze bɛma Levifo no nyɛ guansumabew nkurow esia no a, hom dze bɛma dɛ onyimpakumfo nguan nkɔ hɔ no: na hom mfa nkurow eduanan ebien nka ho.
Nkurow a hom dze bɛma Levifo no nyinara nyɛ nkurow eduanan awɔtwe: hom mfa nka ne mfikyisaase no ho mma hɔn.
Na nkurow a hom bɛgye no wɔ Israelmba enyadze mu ama Levifo no ho dze, hɔn a hɔndze dɔɔ so no hɔ na hom ngye dza ɔdɔɔ so: na hɔn a hɔndze suar no hɔ na hom ngye dza osuar: obiara dɛ mbrɛ n’egyapadze a oenya no tse no na ɔmfa no nkurow no mu bi mma Levifo no.
Guansumabew Nkurow Na EWURADZE kasaa kyerɛɛ Moses dɛ, Kasa kyerɛ Israelmba, na se hɔn dɛ, Sɛ hom twa Jordan kɔ Keenan asaase do a, ɔno hom nyiyi nkurow ma ɔnyɛ guansumabew nkurow mma hom; na onyimpakumfo a oku nyimpa bi wɔ ber a ɔannhyɛ da no oeeguan akɔ hɔ.
Na nkurow no nyɛ hom guansumabew wɔ ɔwerdzinyi no nsamu; amma onyimpakumfo no eennwu, ma eekodu dɛ obegyina mboanofo no enyim ma woeebu no atsɛn ana.
Na nkurow a hom beyi ama no nyɛ hom guansumabew nkurow esia.
Hom nyi nkurow ebiasa mma wɔ Jordan egya, na nkurow ebiasa so na hom nyi mma wɔ Keenan asaase do; ɔnyɛ guansumabew nkurow.
Na Israelmba, nye ɔhɔho, nye ɔkwantunyi a ɔwɔ hɔn mu, nye nkurow esia yi nyɛ hɔn guansumabew: na obiara a ne nsa apa no oeeguan akɔ hɔ.
Na sɛ obi dze dadze bi bɔ obi, ma owu a, ɔyɛ onyimpakumfo; oku na wonku onyimpakumfo no.
Na sɛ obi kitsa ɔbo a obotum eku nyimpa na ɔdze bɔ no, ma owu a, ɔyɛ onyimpakumfo: oku na wonku onyimpakumfo no.
Anaa sɛ okitsa dua a obotum eku nyimpa dze bɔ no, ma owu a, ɔyɛ onyimpakumfo: oku na wonku onyimpakumfo no.
Bɔgya ho ɔwerdzinyi no noara na onku onyimpakumfo no: sɛ ɔto no a, onku no.
Na sɛ ɔtan do na osun no, anaa ɔboapa tow biribi dze bɔ no ma owu; anaa enyitan do na ɔdze ne nsa dze bɔ no ma owu a: oku na wonku nyia ɔbɔ no no; ɔyɛ onyimpakumfo: bɔgya ho ɔwerdzinyi no nku onyimpakumfo no, sɛ ɔto no a. Na sɛ osun no awerɛfir mu na nnyɛ enyitan do, anaa ɔtow adze biara ma ɔbɔ no na ɔannhyɛ da, anaa ɔdze ɔbo biara a obotum eku nyimpa, na oennhu no, na ɔtow bɔ no, ma owu, na nnyɛ ne tamfo nkyii so ɔmmpɛ no bɔn bi a: ɔno mboanofo no mbu nyia ɔbɔe nye no bɔgyaa ho ɔwerdzinyi no ntamu atsɛn dɛ mbrɛ ntsɛmbu yi tsetsee: na mboanofo no nyi onyimpakumfo no mfi bɔgya ho ɔwerdzinyi no nsamu, na mboanofo no mfa no nsan nkɔ no guansumabew kurow no mu, mbrɛ oguanee kɔree no: na ɔnkɛtsena hɔ ma onkodu ɔsɔfopanyin a wɔdze ngo krɔnkrɔn asera no no wu.
Na sɛ onyimpakumfo no fir edzi aber biara tra no guansumabew kurow a oguanee kɔr hɔ no ne he do; na bɔgya ho ɔwerdzinyi no hu no wɔ no guansumabew kurow no ne he ekyir, na bɔgya ho ɔwerdzinyi no koku onyimpakumfo no a; onndzi bɔgya bi ho so: osiandɛ no guansumabew kurow no mu na ɔsɛ no dɛ nkyɛ ɔtsena kodu ɔsɔfopanyin no no wu do: na ɔsɔfopanyin no no wu ekyir no dze onyimpakumfo no nsan mbra n’enyadze asaase do bio.
Na iyi nyɛ atsɛmbu ahyɛdze mma hom wɔ hom ebusuasantsen nyina mu wɔ hom tsenabew nyinara mu.
Obiara a oku nyimpa biara no, adasefo enum na wɔmfa do nku onyimpakumfo no: na ɔdasefo kor dze mma onndzi dase nntsia nyimpa biara mma onnwu.
Nkyii so mma hom nngye onyimpakumfo a ɔsɛ owu no nkwa tsir mpata biara: na oku ara na wonku no.
Na mma hom nngye nyia oeguan kɔ no guansumabew kurow mu ne tsir mpata biara dɛ ɔnsan mbɛtsena asaase no do bio, nkodu ɔsɔfo no wu do.
Dɛm ntsi mma hom nngu asaase no a hom tse do no ho fi: na bɔgya ara na ogu asaase no ho fi: na wɔrennyɛ mpatadze biara mma asaase no wɔ bɔgya a woehue egu do no ntsi, gyedɛ nyia ɔkaa bɔgya gui no ara no bɔgyaa mu.
Na mma nngu asaase a hom tse do a mo so metse ne finimfin no do fi: na emi EWURADZE na metse Israelmba finimfin.
Mbabaa Awarfo Egyapadze Ho Na Gilead, Makir ne babanyin, Manaasɛ ne babanyin, a wofi Josef ne mbabanyin ebusua ebusua mu egyanom efi do etsitsir no bae, na wɔbɛkasae wɔ Moses, nye mbapɔmba no, Israelmba egyanom efi do etsitsir no enyim: na wɔsee dɛ, EWURADZE hyɛɛ mo wura dɛ ɔmfa tontotwe nkyɛ asaase no mu mma Israelmba ma wɔnyɛ no egyapadze: na mo wura na EWURADZE hyɛɛ no dɛ ɔmfa hɛn nua Zelofehad n’egyapadze mma ne mbabaa.
Na sɛ wɔwar hɔn ma Israelmba ebusuakuw bi mu mbabanyin biara a, ɔno wonyi hɔn egyapadze no mfi hɛn egyanom egyapadze mu, na wɔmfa nkɛka ebusuakuw kor a wɔakɛyɛ hɔndze no egyapadze ho: dɛm na wonyi mfi hɛn egyapadze kyɛfa no mu.
Na sɛ Israelmba ahosɛpɛw afe no du a, ɔno wɔmfa hɔn egyapadze no nkɛka ebusuakuw kor a wɔakɛyɛ hɔndze no egyapadze ho: ma woeyi hɔn egyapadze efi hɔn egyanom ebusuakuw egyapadze no mu.
Na Moses hyɛɛ Israelmba no dɛ mbrɛ EWURADZE n’asɛm tse, dɛ, Josef ne mbabanyin ebusuakuw no aka no tsenn.
Iyi nye adze a EWURADZE hyɛe wɔ Zelofehad mbabaa no ho no, dɛ, Wɔmma wɔnwarwar hɔn a wɔdwen hɔn dɛ woye no: hɔn egya n’ebusuakuw mu ebusua no ara nko na wɔnwarwar wɔ mu.
Amma Israelmba egyapadze biara eemmfi ebusuakuw kor mu annkɔ ebusuakuw fofor bi mu: na Israelmba no ntakyer hɔn egyanom ebusuakuw egyapadze ho.
Na ɔbabaa biara a onya egyapadze wɔ Israelmba ebusuakuw biara mu no, ɔnyɛ n’egya ebusuakuw mu ebusua no mu obi ne yer, ama Israelmba no eenyinya nyimpa biara n’egyanom egyapadze edzi.
Amma egyapadze biara eemmfi ebusuakuw kor mu annkɔ ebusuakuw kor so mu; na Israelmba ebusuakuw ebusuakuw no ntakyer hɔnankasa hɔn egyapadze ho.
Mekyerɛ dɛ mbrɛ EWURADZE hyɛɛ Moses no, dɛmara na Zelofehad ne mbabaa no yɛe: na Mahala, nye Tirza, nye Hogla, nye Milka, nye Noa, Zelofehad mbabaa no warwaar hɔn egya no nuanom mbabanyin no.
Wɔwarwaar hɔn kɔr Josef ne babanyin Manaasɛ mbabanyin ebusua ebusua mu, na hɔn egyapadze no kaa hɔn egya n’ebusua ebusuakuw no mu.
Iyinom nye mbransɛm nye ntsɛmbu a, EWURADZE nam Moses nsa do hyɛɛ Israelmba wɔ Moab tɛtɛr mu wɔ Jeriko Jordan do.
NHƐNMU Deuteronomi anaadɛ Mbra No Ne Ntsimu nwoma no mu nsɛm fa nsɛm ahorow a Moses kaa kyerɛɛ Israelmba wɔ ber a nna wɔwɔ Moab asaase do no ho.
Moses ne nsɛm ahorow yi wɔaboaboa ano ahyehyɛ no pɛpɛɛpɛr wɔ nwoma yi mu.
Israelfo fi Egypt kodur Moab.
Hɔ na hɔn sardo akwantu tsentsen no dze hɔn kodurii ma wɔgyee hɔn ahom.
Ha so na wofi boaboaa hɔnho dɛ wɔrokɔ akɛfa Keenan asaase no atsena do.
Nsɛm tsitsir a wɔakyerɛw wɔ nwoma no mu no bi nye yi: Moses kaakaa Israelfo no nsɛntsitsir bi a osisii wɔ mfe eduanan bi a etwa mu kɔ no.
Moses tu hɔn fo dɛ wɔmfa hɔn enyi nto dza Nyankopɔn ayɛ ama hɔn wɔ hɔn sardo akwantu no mu no do, na wontsie Nyankopɔn n’asɛm ndzi n’ekyir wɔ nokwar mu.
Moses san tsi mbrasɛm du no mu kyerɛ hɔn.
Ɔkyerɛkyerɛ hɔn mbrasɛm no mu, ne tsitsir nye mbrasɛm a odzi kan no.
Otu hɔn fo so dɛ EWURADZE nkotsee.
Afei otsi mbrasɛm ahorow a Nyankopɔn hyɛɛ hɔn dɛ sɛ wokodu anohoba asaase no do a, wondzi do no mu.
Moses kaa hɔn kyerɛɛ hɔn ahyɛmu a Nyankopɔn nye hɔn dzii no ase, na ɔhyɛɛ hɔn dɛ wɔnhwɛ ndzi n’ahyɛmu no do.
Wɔhyɛ Josua panyin dɛ ɔkandzifo fofor a ondzi Nyankopɔn ne man no enyim.
Moses tow ayɛyindwom dze kamfo Nyankopɔn no nokwardzi na ohyira Israelman no.
Iyi ekyir no, Moses wu wɔ Moab asaase do wɔ esutsen Jordan no boka afamu.
Asɛntsitsir a nwoma no gyina do no nye dɛ Nyankopɔn agye no nkorɔfo a ɔasan mu eyi hɔn na ɔdɔ hɔn no, wɔ ne nhyira a ohyiraa hɔn no ho.
Na ɔhyɛɛ hɔn ase dɛ ne man nkaa iyi, na hɔn so, wɔndɔ Nyankopɔn na wontsie n’asɛm na wondzi do.
Wɔyɛ dɛm a nna wobenya nkwa, na wɔakɔ do so enya nhyira.
Nsɛm a odzi mu wɔ nwoma no mu nye dza ɔwɔ .- mu no.
Ɔno mu na yehu nsɛm a Jesus too no dzin dɛ mbrasɛm no nyina mu kɛse no.
Ɔno na ɔka dɛ, Fa w’akoma nyinara, nye wo kra nyinara, na ɔnye w’ahoɔdzen nyinara dɔ EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn.
Dza Ɔwɔ Mu Moses ne nsɛm a ɔkae dzii kan .—.
Moses ne nsɛm a ɔkae a ɔtɔ do ebien .—.
.
Mbrasɛm Du no .—.
.
Ahyɛdze, nhyehyɛɛ na kɔkɔbɔ ho nsɛm .—.
Keenan asaase do kɔ ho nhyehyɛɛ .—.
Wɔhyɛ ahyɛmu no mu dzen .—.
Moses ne nsɛm odzi ekyir .—.
Moses no wu .-
Nsɛm A Moses Kae Iyinom nye nsɛm a Moses kaa kyerɛɛ Israel nyinara wɔ Jordan egya sar no do, wɔ Araba Suf tsentsendo, wɔ Paran, nye Tofel, nye Laban, nye Hazerot, nye Di-zahab ntamu.
Ofi Horeb wɔ bepɔw Seir kwan do kɔ Kades-barnea ɔyɛ nda dubiako kwan.
Na ɔbaa dɛ afe a otsia eduanan no mu, bosoom a otsia dubiako no ne da a odzi kan no, Moses kasaa kyerɛɛ Israelmba no dɛ mbrɛ EWURADZE hyɛɛ no dɛ ɔnka nkyerɛ hɔn no nyinara; wɔber a oeku Amorifo hen Sihon a ɔtse Hesbon, nye Basanhen Ɔge a ɔtse Astarot, wɔ Edrei no ekyir no.
Jordan egya wɔ Moab asaase do, na Moses hyɛɛ ase kyerɛkyerɛɛ mbra yi mu dɛ, EWURADZE hɛn Nyankopɔn kasaa kyerɛɛ hɛn wɔ Horeb dɛ, Hom atsena bepɔw yi ho akyɛr dodow: hom ndan homho, na hom ntu nkɔ Amorifo nkokodo nkurow mu, nye mbeambea a ɔbɛn ho hɔ nyinara, wɔ Araba, nkokodo nkurow mu, nye tɛtɛr mu, nye Pomu, nye mpoano, Keenanfo asaase do, nye Lebanon do, nkodu esutsen kɛse Eufrates no ho.
Hwɛ, medze asaase no ato hom enyim: hom nkɔ nkɛfa asaase a EWURADZE kaa ho ntam kyerɛɛ hom egyanom, Abraham, Isaak, nye Jakob, dɛ ɔdze bɛma hɔn nye hɔn asefo a wodzi hɔn ekyir no.
Moses Yiyi Atsɛmbuafo Na mekasaa kyerɛɛ hom aber no mu dɛ, Mara nkotsee runntum monnkora hom: EWURADZE hom Nyankopɔn ama hom adɔr, na hwɛ, ndɛ da yi hom dodow tse dɛ ɔsor nworaba.
EWURADZE hom egyanom Nyankopɔn, nyɛ hom dɛ mbrɛ hom tse yi mbɔho apem so nka ho, na onhyira hom, dɛ mbrɛ ɔabɔ hom anohoba no!
Mebɛyɛ dɛn monko metum asoa hom haw, nye hom adzesoa, nye hom aperper?
Hom nyiyi mbanyin enyansafo, nye enyimdzefo, na wɔda nsew, dɛ mbrɛ hom ebusuakuw no tsetsee, na menyɛ hɔn etsitsir wɔ hom do.
Na hom buaa me see dɛ, Dza aka no oye ma hɛn dɛ yɛyɛ.
Nna mefaa hom ebusuakuw ebusuakuw mu etsitsir no, mbanyin enyansafo wɔda nsew, na meyɛɛ hɔn etsitsir wɔ hom do, apem apem do asafohemfo, nye ɔha ɔha do asafohemfo, nye eduonum eduonum do asafohemfo, nye du du do asafohemfo, nye ahwɛdofo, dɛ mbrɛ hom ebusuakuw tsetsee.
Na mehyɛɛ hom atsɛmbuafo mbra aber no mu dɛ, Hom ntsie hom nuanom ntamu nsɛm, na hom mbu ntsɛn tsenenee wɔ nyimpa nye no nua, nye ɔhɔho a ɔnye no wɔ hɔ ntamu.
Mma hom nnhwɛ nyimpa enyim wɔ atsɛmbu mu; hom ntsie aketseaba nye ɔkɛse nyina pɛ; mma hom nnsuro nyimpa enyim; na atsɛmbu yɛ Nyankopɔn dze: na asɛm a ɔyɛ dzen dodow ma hom no na hom mfa mbrɛ me, na mintsie.
Na mehyɛɛ hom dza hom nyɛ no nyinara ho mbra aber no mu.
Wɔsoma Akwanserafo Fi Kades Na yetui fii Horeb, na yɛnantsewee faa sar kɛse a ɔyɛ hu a hom hunii no nyinara do wɔ Amorifo nkokodo nkurow kwan do, dɛ mbrɛ EWURADZE hɛn Nyankopɔn hyɛɛ hɛn no; na yedur Kades Barnea.
Na mesee hom dɛ, Hom edu Amorifo nkokodo nkurow a EWURADZE hɛn Nyankopɔn dze rema hɛn no ho.
Hwɛ, EWURADZE hom Nyankopɔn dze asaase no ato hom enyim: hom mfow kɔ, nkɛfa, dɛ mbrɛ EWURADZE, hom egyanom Nyankopɔn aka akyerɛ hom no; mma hom nnsuro, nkyii so mma hom akoma nntu.
Na hom baa me nkyɛn, hom nyinara; na wɔsee dɛ, Ma yɛnsoma mbanyin ma wondzi hɛn enyim nkɛsera asaase no mma hɛn, na wɔmbɛka ɔkwan kor a yɛbɛfa do, nye nkurow kor a yebodu do ho asɛm nkyerɛ hɛn.
Na asɛm no yɛɛ me enyisɔ dɛ: na mefaa hom mu nyimpa duebien, ebusuakuw biara mu nyimpa kor: na wɔdanee kɔfoow bepɔw no, na wokodur Eskol ɔbɔn mu, na wɔserae.
Na wɔfaa asaase no do aba bi kitsae, na wɔdze sanee baa hɛn nkyɛn, na wɔbɛkaa hɛn asɛm see dɛ, Asaase a EWURADZE hɛn Nyankopɔn dze rema hɛn no oye.
Naaso hom ammpɛ dɛ hom fow kɔ, na hom tseew EWURADZE hom Nyankopɔn mbrasɛm do etua: na hom hwinhwinii wɔ hom asesee mu see dɛ, Osiandɛ EWURADZE tan hɛn ntsi na oyii hɛn wɔ Egypt asaase do, dɛ ɔdze hɛn rebɛhyɛ Amorifo nsa, ma wɔaasɛɛ hɛn.
Henfa na yɛmfa nkɔ?
Hɛn enuanom etutu hɛn akoma, dɛ, Ɔman no wɔsoso na wɔwowar sen hɛn; nkurow no yɛ akɛse na wɔatotow ho afasu akɔ sor; na nkyii so yehun Anakfo mbabanyin wɔ hɔ.
Nna mesee hom dɛ, Mma hu nnka hom, nkyii so mma hom nnsuro hɔn.
EWURADZE hom Nyankopɔn a odzi hom enyim rokɔ no, ɔno na ɔbɔko ama hom, dɛ mbrɛ ɔyɛe maa hom wɔ Egypt wɔ hom enyiwa mu no nyinara; nye sar no do, beebi a hom hun mbrɛ EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn sii tuur hom, dɛ mbrɛ nyimpa tur ne babanyin, wɔ kwan a hom nantsewee no nyinara mu araa dze bodur dɛ hom dur ha yi.
Naaso iyi mu hom anngye EWURADZE hom Nyankopɔn enndzi, ɔno a odzii hom enyim wɔ ɔkwan no mu dɛ ɔrokɔhwehwɛ beebi a ma hom abɔ asesee, wɔ gya mu adzesaa, dɛ ɔkyerɛ hom ɔkwan a hom mfa do, nye mununkum mu adzekyee.
EWURADZE N’ebufuw Wɔ Israel Do Na EWURADZE tsee hom nsɛm, na no bo fuwii, na ɔkaa ntam dɛ, Ampaara ebusuasantsen bɔn yi mu nyimpa yi mu biara runnhu asaase pa a mekaa ho ntam dɛ medze bɛma hom egyanom no, gyedɛ Jefune ne babanyin Kaleb, ɔno na obohu; na ɔno na medze asaase a oetsia do no bɛma no, nye ne mba; osiandɛ oedzi EWURADZE ekyir koraa.
Eso hom ntsi EWURADZE nyaa no ho ebufuw, dɛ, Wo so ronnkɔ hɔ: Nun ne babanyin Josua a ogyina w’enyim no, ɔno na ɔbɔkɔ hɔ: hyɛ no dzen; na ɔno na ɔbɛyɛ ma Israel enya edzi.
Nkyii so hom mbofraba no a hom se dɛ wɔbɛyɛ afonam no, nye hom mba no a ndɛ da yi wonnyi papa anaa bɔn ho nyimdzee no, hɔn na wɔbɔkɔ hɔ, na hɔn na medze mebɛma hɔn, na wɔafa.
Na hom dze, hom ndan homho, na hom ntu nkɔ sar no do wɔ Mbɛw Po kwan do.
Nna hom buae na wɔsee me dɛ, Yɛayɛ bɔn etsia EWURADZE, yɛbɔfow akɔ akɔko, dɛ mbrɛ EWURADZE hɛn Nyankopɔn hyɛɛ hɛn no nyinara.
Na hom mu nyimpa biara dze n’akodze miamiae, na wodzii kan dɛ wɔrokɔfow akɔ bepɔw no do.
Na EWURADZE see me dɛ, Se hɔn dɛ, Mma wɔmmfow, nkyii so mma wɔnnko; na minnyi hom mu; bɛyɛ na hom akɔtotɔr wɔ hom atamfo enyim.
Na mekasaa mekyerɛɛ hom, na hom enntsie; na hom tseew EWURADZE mbrasɛm do etua, na hom tsitsii hom enyi ho ara fowee kɔr bepɔw no do.
Na Amorifo a wɔtse bepɔw no do no fiir edzi behyiaa hom, na wotsiiw hom, dɛ mbrɛ ndowa yɛ, na wokunkum hom wɔ Seir araa kodur Horma.
Na hom sanee na wobosui wɔ EWURADZE enyim; na EWURADZE enntsie hom ndze, na eso ɔannyɛ aso amma hom.
Nna hom tsenaa Kades dzii nda pii, dɛ mbrɛ nda a hom dze tsenaa hɔ tse no.
Sardo Akwantu Nna yɛdanee, na yetuu hɛn kwan kɔr sar no do wɔ Mbɛw Po kwan do, dɛ mbrɛ EWURADZE kaa kyerɛɛ me no: na yekyiin Seir bepɔw ho nda pii.
Na EWURADZE kaa kyerɛɛ me dɛ, Hom ekyin bepɔw yi ho akyɛr dodow: hom ndan homho wɔ kwaamu afamu.
Na hyɛ ɔman no dɛ, Hom rubotwa mu wɔ hom nuanom Esau mba a wɔtse Seir no ntoaado; na wobosuro hom: dɛm ntsi hom nhwɛ homho yie papa: mma wɔnnye hɔn nndzi aper; na meremmfa hɔn asaase no memma hom, oho, nnyɛ mbrɛ ɔnamɔn mpo betsia a: osiandɛ medze Seir bepɔw mama Esau dɛ ɔmfa.
Hom mfa sika ntɔ hɔn hɔ edziban, na hom eedzi; na hom mfa sika ntɔ hɔn hɔ nsu so, na hom aanom.
Na EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn ehyira wo wɔ wo nsaano edwuma nyinara mu: oehu wo nantsew wɔ sar kɛse yi do: mfe eduanan yi EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn edzi w’ekyir; ennhia wo biribiara.
Nna yetwae fi hɛn nuanom Esaumba a wɔtse Seir no ho, fi Araba kwan do fi Elat nye Ezion-geber.
Na yɛdanee, na yekotwaa mu wɔ Moab sar no do kwan do.
Na EWURADZE see me dɛ, Mma nnhiahia Moab ho, nkyii so mma nnye hɔn nndzi aper nnko: na meremmfa n’asaase mu bi memma wo mma emmfa; osiandɛ medze Ar ama Lotmba dɛ wɔmfa.
Emfo no na wɔtsenaa do nkan no, ɔman kɛse a wɔdɔɔ so, na wɔwowar dɛ Anakfo: iyinom so na wobu hɔn Refafo, dɛ Anakfo; na Moabfo dze wɔfrɛ hɔn Emfo.
Horfo so na nkyɛ nkan no wɔtsenaa Seir, na Esaumba no hyɛɛ hɔn ananmu; na wɔsɛɛ hɔn wɔ hɔn enyim, na wɔtsenaa hɔn ananmu dɛ mbrɛ Israel yɛɛ n’enyadze asaase a EWURADZE dze maa hɔn no.
Afei hom nsoɛr, na hom nkotwa ɔwora Zered.
Na yekotwaa ɔwora Zered.
Na mfe dodow a yɛdze nantsewee fi Kades-barnea bodur dɛ yebotwaa ɔwora Zered no, yɛ mfe eduasa awɔtwe; kodur dɛ akofo ebusuasantsen no nyinara wuwui wɔ nseraban no mu, dɛ mbrɛ EWURADZE kaa ho ntam no.
Nkyii so EWURADZE nsa tsiaa hɔn, dɛ ɔresɛɛ hɔn efi nseraban no mu, ekodu dɛ wɔbɛhyew.
Nna ɔbaa dɛ, aber a akofo no nyinara hyewee na wowuwui fii ɔman no mu no, EWURADZE kaa kyerɛɛ me dɛ, Ndɛ da yi na irubotwa mu wɔ Ar, Moab ntoaado no: na sɛ ikodu Ammonmba tsentsendo a, mma nnhiahia hɔn ho, na nnye hɔn nndzi aper so: na meremmfa Ammonmba asaase mu bi memma wo mma emmfa: osiandɛ medze mama Lotmba dɛ wɔmfa.
Ɔno so wobu no Refafo asaase; Refafo tsenaa do nkan no; na Ammonfo dze wɔfrɛ hɔn Zamzumfo; ɔman kɛse a, wɔdɔɔ so, na wɔwowar dɛ Anakfo; na EWURADZE sɛɛ hɔn wɔ hɔn enyim; na wɔhyɛɛ hɔn ananmu: dɛ mbrɛ ɔyɛe maa Esaumba a wɔtse Seir, aber a ɔsɛɛ Horfo wɔ hɔn enyim; na wɔhyɛɛ hɔn ananmu, na wɔtsenaa hɔn ananmu araa dze bodu ndɛ da yi; na Avifo a wɔtsenatsenaa nkuroba araa dze kodu Gaza mu no, Kaftorfo a, wofi Kaftor bae no, bɛsɛɛ hɔn, na wɔtsenaa hɔn ananmu.
Hom nsoɛr, wontu hom kwan, na wonkotwa Arnon bɔnsa; hwɛ, medze Amorinyi Sihon, Hesbon hen no, nye n’asaase ahyɛ wo nsa: hyɛ ase fa, na nye no ndzi aper nko.
Ndɛ da yi na mebɛhyɛ ase medze wo ho suro nye wo ho hu megu amanaman a wɔwɔ asaase nyina do a wɔbɛtse wo nka do, na hɔn ho apopo, na hɔn ho eguan hɔn wɔ wo ntsi.
Israel Dzi Sihon Do Konyim Na Kedamot sar do na mifi mosomaa abɔfo ma wɔdze asomdwee nsɛm kɔr Hesbon hen Sihon nkyɛn dɛ, Ma muntwa mu wɔ w’asaase do: ɔtsempɔn do ara na mebɛfa akɔ, merenndan mmfa enyimfa anaa abankum.
Tɔn me edziban gye sika, ma mindzi; na ma me nsu gye sika ma monnom: ma memfa m’anan kwa mumbotwa mu; dɛ mbrɛ Esaumba a wɔtse Seir, na Moabfo a wɔtse Ar, yɛɛ me no; ma onkodu dɛ mubotwa Jordan akɔ asaase a EWURADZE hɛn Nyankopɔn dze rema hɛn no do.
Na Hesbonhen Sihon amma hɛn kwan dɛ yentwa mu wɔ ne nkyɛn: osiandɛ EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn maa no asoɔdzen sunsum, na opiriim n’akoma, ama ɔdze no aahyɛ wo nsa, dɛ mbrɛ ɔtse ndɛ da yi.
Na EWURADZE see me dɛ, Hwɛ, mahyɛ ase meyi Sihon nye n’asaase mama wɔ w’enyim: hyɛ ase fa, na enya n’asaase no edzi.
Nna Sihon fiir edzi behyiaa hɛn, ɔno nye ne man nyinara, dɛ ɔrobɔko wɔ Jahaz.
Na EWURADZE hɛn Nyankopɔn yii no mae wɔ hɛn enyim; na yekunkum ɔno, nye ne mbabanyin, nye ne man nyinara.
Na yɛfaa no nkurow nyinara aber no mu, na yɛsɛɛ kurow biara a nyimpa tse mu no pasapasa, dze kaa mbaa nye mbofraba ho; yeenngyaa biara mma ɔannka: ofiembowa nko na hɛnara yɛfaa no afonam, dze kaa nkurow a yɛfae no mu asadze ho.
Ofi Aroer a ɔwɔ Arnon ɔbɔn no ano, na ofi kurow a ɔwɔ Arnon ɔbɔn no mu no do, araa dze kɔ Gilead, kurow biara nnyi hɔ a ɔyɛɛ dzen dodow maa hɛn: EWURADZE hɛn Nyankopɔn yii ne nyinara mae wɔ hɛn enyim: Ammonmba asaase no nko na ɔwo ammbɛn ho; esutsen Jabbok ne nkyɛn nyinara, nye nkurow a ɔwɔ nkokodo nkurow mu no, nye beebiara a EWURADZE hɛn Nyankopɔn amma hɛn ho kwan no.
Israelfo Dzi Ɔge Do Konyim Nna yɛdanee, na yɛfowee kɔr Basan kwan do: na Basan hen Ɔge fiir edzi behyiaa hɛn, ɔno nye ne man nyinara, dɛ ɔrobɔko wɔ Edrei.
Na EWURADZE see me dɛ, Mma nnsuro no: na meyi ɔno, nye ne man nyinara, nye n’asaase, ahyɛ wo nsa; na yɛ no dɛ mbrɛ ɔyɛɛ Amorifo hen Sihon a ɔtsenaa Hesbon no.
Dɛmara na EWURADZE hɛn Nyankopɔn yii Basanhen Ɔge so, nye ne man nyinara, hyɛɛ hɛn nsa: na yekum no araa kodur dɛ woenngyaa biara mma wɔannka amma no.
Na yɛgyee no nkurow nyinara aber no mu; kurow biara nnyi hɔ a yɛanngye no hɔn hɔ; nkurow eduosia, Argob mbew nyinara, Ɔge n’ahenman a ɔwɔ Basan.
Iyinom nyinara yɛ nkurow a no ho wɔ afasu atsentsen, mbotsen, nye adaban; ɔsor nkurow a ɔdɔɔ so piigyan a no ho nnyi afasu no.
Na yɛsɛɛ hɔn pasapasa, dɛ mbrɛ yɛyɛɛ Hesbonhen Sihon no, yɛsɛɛ kurow biara a nyimpa tse mu no pasapasa, dze kaa mbaa nye mbofraba ho.
Na ofiembowa nyinara, na nkurow no mu asadze no dze, hɛnara yɛfaa no afonam.
Na yɛgyee asaase no wɔ Amorifo ahemfo beenu no a wɔwɔ Jordan egya no nsamu aber no mu, fi Arnon ɔbɔn mu kodur bepɔw Hermon ho; (Hermon no Zidonfo frɛ no Sirion, na Amorifo frɛ no Senir;) tɛtɛr mu nkurow nyinara, nye Gilead nyinara, nye Basan nyinara, kodur Saleka nye Edrei, Ɔge n’ahenman nkurow a ɔwɔ Basan.
(Na Basanhen Ɔge nko na ɔkae wɔ Refafo nkaa no mu; hwɛ, nna ne mpadua ayɛ dadze mpadua; nnda ho nnsi Ammonmba Rabaa bi a?
Ne tsentsen yɛ basafa anan nye fa, na ne tɛtɛr basafa ebien, dɛ mbrɛ nyimpa basafa tse.)
Asaase No Ne Nkyekyɛmu Na asaase yi na yɛfae wɔ aber no mu: ofi Aroer a ɔwɔ Arnon ɔbɔn ho, nye Gilead nkokodo nkurow ɔfa, nye no nkurow, na medze maa Reubenfo nye Gadfo; na Gilead nkaa, nye Basan nyinara, Ɔge n’ahenman no, na medze memaa Manaasɛ ebusuakuw ɔfa no; Argob mbew nyinara, mekyerɛ Basan nyinara.
Na medze Gilead memaa Makir.
Na Reubenfo nye Gadfo na medze ofi Gilead araa dze kodu Arnon ɔbɔn ho, ɔbɔn no ne finimfin, nye no ntoaado memaa hɔn; mekyerɛ dze kodu esutsen Jabbok a ɔyɛ Ammonmba ɔhe no do; Araba so, nye Jordan nye no ntoaado, ofi Kinneret araa dze kodu Araba epo ho, Mbɛw Po no, wɔ Pisga ntserɛwee ase boka afamu.
Na mehyɛɛ hom aber no mu dɛ, EWURADZE hom Nyankopɔn dze asaase yi ama hom dɛ hom mfa: hom mmia ntwa mu ndzi hom nuanom Israelmba enyim, mbanyin a wɔyɛ ndam nyinara.
Hom yernom, nye hom mbofraba, nye hom fiembowa dze (minyim dɛ hom wɔ fiembowa piigyan) wɔntsena hom nkurow a medze mama hom no mu; nkodu dɛ EWURADZE bɛma hom nuanom ahomgye, dɛ hom, na hɔn so wɔaakɛfa asaase a EWURADZE hom Nyankopɔn dze rema hɔn wɔ Jordan egya no: n’ekyir no na hom mu nyimpa biara nsan mbra n’enyadze do, dza medze mama hom no a. Na mehyɛɛ Josua aber no mu dɛ, W’enyiwa ehu dza EWURADZE hom Nyankopɔn dze ayɛ ahemfo beenu yi nyinara: Mma hom nnsuro hɔn: na EWURADZE hom Nyankopɔn, ɔno nye nyia ɔroko ma hom.
Moses N’adzeserɛdze Na meserɛɛ EWURADZE aber no mu dɛ, Ao EWURADZE Nyankopɔn, ɔwo na ahyɛ ase dze wo kɛseyɛ, nye wo nsa dzendzen no akyerɛ w’akowaa: na onyame bɛn na ɔwɔ ɔsor anaa asaase do a obotum ayɛ dɛ mbrɛ wo ndwuma, nye mbrɛ w’akatakyidze tsetsee?
Mepa wo kyɛw, ma muntwa nkɔ, na monkɔhwɛ asaase pa a ɔwɔ Jordan egya no, bepɔw fɛɛfɛw no, nye Lebanon.
Na hom ntsi EWURADZE no bo fuuw me, na oenntsie me: na EWURADZE see me dɛ, Ma ɔndɔɔ wo so; mma nnye me nnkasa asɛm yi ho bio.
Fow kɔ Pisga etsifi, na ma w’enyiwa do wɔ anee afamu, nye kwaamu afamu, nye pomu afamu nye boka afamu, na fa w’enyiwa hwɛ; na ɔwo runntwa Jordan yi.
Mbom hyɛ Josua, na hyɛ no nsi, na hyɛ no dzen: na ɔno na obedzi ɔman yi enyim etwa, na ɔno na ɔbɛyɛ ma woeenya asaase a ibohu no edzi.
Nna yɛtsenaa ɔbɔn no mu wɔ Bɛt-peor tsentsendo.
Setsie Ho Kɔkɔbɔ Na afei, Israel, hom ntsie ahyɛdze nye atsɛmbu a mekyerɛkyerɛ hom dɛ hom nyɛ no; na hom eenya nkwa, na hom akɔ akɛfa asaase a EWURADZE, hom egyanom Nyankopɔn dze rema hom no.
Mma hom mmfa hwee nnka asɛm a merehyɛ hom yi ho, nkyii so mma hom nyi do bi, na hom eedzi EWURADZE hom Nyankopɔn mbransɛm a merehyɛ hom yi do.
Hom enyiwa ehu dza osian Baal-peor ntsi EWURADZE yɛe; na nyimpa a wodzii Baal-peor ekyir no nyinara, EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn asɛɛ hɔn efi hom mu.
Na hom a hom takyeer EWURADZE hom Nyankopɔn ho no dze, hom nyinara tse ase ndɛ da yi.
Hwɛ makyerɛkyerɛ hom ahyɛdze nye ntsɛmbu, dɛ mbrɛ EWURADZE me Nyankopɔn hyɛɛ me no ara, dɛ hom nyɛ dɛm wɔ asaase a hom rokɔ do akɛfa no mu.
Dɛm ntsi hom ndzi do na hom nyɛ; na iyi nye hom nyansaa nye hom ntseasee wɔ aman a wɔbɛtse ahyɛdze yi nyinara enyim, na wɔbɛse dɛ, Ampaara ɔman kɛse yi yɛ nyansa nye nyimdzee man.
Na ɔman kɛse bɛn na ɔwɔ hɔ a ɔwɔ nyame a ɔbɛn hɔn dɛm, dɛ mbrɛ EWURADZE hɛn Nyankopɔn tse wɔ aber biara a yɛfrɛ no no?
Na ɔman kɛse bɛn na ɔwɔ hɔ a ɔwɔ ahyɛdze nye atsɛmbu tsenenee dɛ mbrɛ mbra yi nyinara a medze risi hom enyim ndɛ da yi tse?
Hom ho yie ara na nhwɛ, na hom nsie hom kra yie, bɛyɛ na hom werɛ efir ndzɛmba a enyiwa hunii no, na bɛyɛ na efi hom akoma mu hom nkwa nda nyinara mu; mbom ma wo mba nye wo mba hɔn mba nhu; da a hom gyinaa EWURADZE hom Nyankopɔn enyim wɔ Horeb, aber a EWURADZE see me dɛ, Boaboa ɔman no ano ma me, na memma wontsie me nsɛm, na woeesuasua dɛ wosuro me wɔ nda a wɔdze tse ase wɔ asaase do nyinara, na wɔdze akyerɛkyerɛ hɔn mba no.
Na hom twee pinii na hom begyinaa bepɔw no ase; ber a bepɔw no dzɛɛw gya kɔr sor tɔnn, sum, mununkum, nye sum kebii.
Na EWURADZE fi gya no mu kasaa kyerɛɛ hom: hom tsee ne nsɛm ndze, na no su dze hom ennhu; ne ndze nko na hom tsee.
Na ɔkaa n’ahyɛmu a ɔhyɛɛ hom dɛ hom nyɛ no kyerɛɛ hom, mekyerɛ mbransɛm du no; na ɔkyerɛɛw no wɔ abopon ebien do.
Na EWURADZE hyɛɛ me aber no mu dɛ menkyerɛkyerɛ hom ahyɛdze nye ntsɛmbu, na hom aayɛ no wɔ asaase a hom rutwa mu akɛfa no do.
Abosonsɔr Ho Kɔkɔbɔ Dɛm ntsi hom nhwɛ homho yie papa; osiandɛ hom ennhu su biara da no a EWURADZE fi ogya no mu kasaa kyerɛɛ hom wɔ Horeb no: bɛyɛ na hom asɛɛ homho, na hom ayɛ ohonyi a wɔasen wɔ adze biara no su mu ama hom ho, ɔbanyin anaa ɔbaa saso, abowa biara a ɔwɔ asaase do ne saso, etubowa biara a otu wɔ wimu ne saso, adze biara a ɔwea famu ne saso, nam biara a ɔwɔ nsu mu wɔ asaase ase ne saso: na bɛyɛ na hom ama hom enyiwa do wɔ sor, na sɛ hom hu ewia nye bosoom, nye nworaba, mekyerɛ sor dɔm no nyinara a, wɔatwe hom ma hom akɔsɔr hɔn, na asom hɔn, dza EWURADZE hom Nyankopɔn ahyehyɛ ama aman nyinara wɔ asaase nyina do no.
Hom dze, EWURADZE afa hom, na oeyi hom efi dadze fononoo mu, efi Egypt dɛ hom mbɛyɛ n’egyapadze mma no, dɛ mbrɛ ɔtse ndɛ da yi.
Nkyii so hom ntsi EWURADZE nyaa me ebufuw, na ɔkaa ntam dɛ murunntwa Jordan, na moronnkɔ asaase pa no a EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn dze rema wo dɛ egyapadze no do.
Emi dze muruwu wɔ asaase yi do, murunntwa Jordan: na hom dze wobotwa, na wɔakɛfa asaase pa no.
Hom nhwɛ hom ho yie, bɛyɛ na hom werɛ efir EWURADZE hom Nyankopɔn ahyɛmu a ɔnye hom dzii no, na hom ayɛ ohonyi a wɔasen wɔ adze bi a EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn abra wo no su do ama woho.
Na EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn yɛ ogya a ɔmen, Nyame nyinkufo a. Sɛ hom wowo mba, na hom mba so wo mba, na hom kyɛr wɔ asaase no do, na hom sɛɛ homho, na wɔyɛ ohonyi a wɔasen wɔ adze biara no su do, na hom yɛ dza omuo wɔ EWURADZE hom Nyankopɔn enyiwa do, dze yi no ebufuw a: mefrɛ sor nye asaase dɛ wondzi hom dase ndɛ da yi, dɛ ɔhera na hom bɛhera ntsɛmara wɔ asaase a hom rutwa Jordan akɛfa no do; hom nda ronnwar wɔ do, mbom ɔsɛɛ na hom bɛsɛɛ pasapasa.
Na EWURADZE bɔbɔ hom apetse aman mu, na ɔbɛka hom nyimpa kakrabaabi wɔ amanaman mu mbrɛ EWURADZE begya hom akɔ no.
Na hɔ na hom bɔsom enyame, nyimpa nsaano edwuma, ndua nye abo a wonnhu, wɔnntse, wonndzidzi, wonnhua.
Na sɛ hom fi hɔ hwehwɛ EWURADZE hom Nyankopɔn a, hom bohu no, sɛ hom dze hom akoma nyinara nye hom kra nyinara hwehwɛ n’ekyir kwan a. Sɛ hom wɔ ahohia mu, na ndzɛmba yi nyinara ba hom do a, nda a odzi ekyir no mu no nsan mbra EWURADZE hom Nyankopɔn nkyɛn, na hom ntsie ne ndze: na EWURADZE hom Nyankopɔn yɛ mbɔbɔrhufo Nyankopɔn; ɔremmpa hom, nkyii so ɔrennsɛɛ hom, no werɛ rimmfir hom egyanom ahyɛmu a ɔkaa ho ntam kyerɛɛ hɔn no so.
Na afei hom nkaa tsetse nda a etwa mu kɔ no, fitsi da a Nyankopɔn bɔɔ nyimpa wɔ asaase do, na ofi ɔsor n’ano kor kodu kor so, kyerɛ dɛ biribi esi a ɔtse dɛ mbrɛ adze kɛse yi tse, anaa wɔatse dza ɔnye no sɛ?
Ana ɔman bi atse Nyankopɔn ndze dɛ ofi gya mu rekasa pɛn, dɛ mbrɛ hom atse no, na woenya nkwa?
Ana Nyankopɔn asɔ ahwɛ dɛ ɔbɔkɔ akɛfa ɔman bi efi ɔman kor so bi mu afa, wɔ nsɔhwɛ, nsɛnkyerɛdze, nye anwanwadze, nye ɔsa, nye nsa a ɔyɛ dzen, nye abasa a wɔatserɛw mu, nye suro akɛse mu, dɛ mbrɛ dza EWURADZE hom Nyankopɔn yɛe maa hom wɔ Egypt wɔ hom enyiwa mu no nyinara tsetsee a?
Hom na wɔdze kyerɛɛ hom, ma hom eehu dɛ EWURADZE nye Nyankopɔn; obi nnyi hɔ bio ka no ho.
Ofi sor maa hom tsee ne ndze, ma ɔaakyerɛkyerɛ hom: na asaase do na ɔmaa hun ne gya kɛse no; na ofi gya no mu na etsee ne nsɛm.
Na osiandɛ ɔdɔɔ hom egyanom ntsi, na ɔpaa hɔn asefo a wodzi hɔn ekyir no na ɔdze n’enyim nye no tum kɛse no, yii hom fii Egypt; dɛ orubotutu amanaman a wɔyɛ akɛse na wɔyɛ dzen sen hom efi enyim, dɛ ɔdze hom rokɔ mu, dze hɔn asaase akɛma hom dɛ ewungyadze, dɛ mbrɛ ɔtse ndɛ da yi.
Dɛm ntsi hom nhu ndɛ da yi, na hom mfa nto hom akoma mu, dɛ EWURADZE nye Nyankopɔn wɔ sor nye asaase do: na obi nnyi hɔ bio.
Na hom ndzi dzi n’ahyɛdze, nye ne mbransɛm a merehyɛ hom ndɛ da yi do, na eesi hom yie, na ɔnye hom mba a wodzi ekyir, na hom nda aawar wɔ asaase a EWURADZE hom Nyankopɔn dze rema hom no do daa.
Moses Yi Wipuei Guansumabew Ebiasa Nna Moses yiyii nkurow ebiasa wɔ Jordan egya a odzi ba wipuei no; dɛ onyimpakumfo a okum no nyɛnko awerɛfir mu, na ɔnntan no dada bi no, nguan nkɔ hɔ; na sɛ oguan kɔ nkurow yi kor mu a, oeenya nkwa: ɔno nye yi, oyii Bezer wɔ sar no do, wɔ ɔman tɛtɛr no mu maa Reubenfo; na Ramot wɔ Gilead, maa Gadfo; na Golan wɔ Basan maa Manaasɛfo.
Na iyi nye mbra a Moses dze too Israelmba enyim: iyinom nye dase, nye ahyɛdze, nye ntsɛmbu a Moses kaa kyerɛɛ Israelmba, wɔ aber a wofii Egypt bae no; wɔ Jordan egya, Bɛt-peor tsentsendo ɔbɔn no mu, wɔ Amorifo hen Sihon a ɔtsenaa Hesbon a Moses nye Israelmba kum no wɔ aber a wofii Egypt bae no, n’asaase do: na wɔfaa n’asaase no yɛɛ hɔndze, na Basan hen Ɔge asaase no Amorifo ahemfo beenu no a wɔwɔ Jordan egya a odzi ba wipuei no; ofi Aroer a ɔwɔ Arnon ano no araa dze kodu bepɔw Sion a ɔnoara nye Hermon no ho, nye Araba nyinara wɔ Jordan egya boka afamu, mekyerɛ ɔdze kodu Araba epo ho, wɔ Pisga ntserɛwee ase.
Mbrasɛm Du No Na Moses frɛɛ Israel nyinara, na ɔsee hɔn dɛ, Israel, hom ntsie ahyɛdze nye atsɛmbu a mereka no hom asomu ndɛ da yi, na hom eesua, na wɔaadwen do ayɛ.
EWURADZE hɛn Nyankopɔn nye hɛn dzii ahyɛmu wɔ Horeb.
Nnyɛ hɛn egyanom na EWURADZE nye hɔn dzii ahyɛmu yi, mbom hɛn a, hɛnara a ndɛ da yi hɛn nyinara tsetse ase ha yi a. EWURADZE fii ogya no mu nye hom kasaa enyim nye enyim wɔ bepɔw no ho.
Emi dze migyinaa EWURADZE nye hom ntamu aber no mu, dɛ merekyerɛ hom EWURADZE asɛm; na osian gya no ntsi hom suroi, na wɔammfow bepɔw no na ɔsee dɛ: Emi nye EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn a miyii wo fii Egypt asaase do, wɔ nkowaasom ofi mu no.
Mma nnya enyame bi so nnka mo ho.
Mma nnyɛ ohonyi bi, adze a ɔwɔ wimu ɔsor, anaa dza ɔwɔ asaase do famu, anaa dza ɔwɔ nsu mu wɔ asaase ase no su biara ne saso mma woho: mma mmbɔ wo mu adze mma hɔn, na nnsom hɔn: na emi EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn meyɛ Nyame nyinkufo a medze egyanom hɔn emumuyɛ mohwɛ mba kodu ebusuasantsen ebiasa nye anan a wɔtan me do; na muhu mpempem a wɔdɔ me na wodzi me mbransɛm do no mbɔbɔr.
Mma mmbɔ EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn dzin gyangyan na EWURADZE nnkɛma nyia ɔbɔ ne dzin gyangyan no afa noho tɔtrɔtɔ.
Dwen ahomgyeda no do sie no krɔnkrɔn, dɛ mbrɛ EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn hyɛɛ wo no.
Nda esia na yɛ edwuma na dzi wo dwuma nyinara: na da a otsia esuon no yɛ EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn ahomgyeda: mma nnyɛ edwuma biara wɔ mu, ɔwo o, wo babanyin o, wo babaa o, w’akowaa o, w’afonabaa o, wo nantwi o, w’asoaso o, wo fiembowa mu biara o, wo hɔhoe a ɔwɔ wo kuropon mu o; ama w’akowaa nye w’afonabaa aahom dɛ ɔwo.
Na kaa dɛ ɔwo yɛɛ akowaa wɔ Egypt asaase do, na EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn dze nsa a ɔyɛ dzen nye abasa a wɔatsɛw mu yii wo fii hɔ: dɛm ntsi na EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn hyɛɛ wo dɛ sie ahomgyeda no.
Dzi w’egya nye wo na nyi, dɛ mbrɛ wo Nyankopɔn hyɛɛ wo no: na wo nda aawar, na eesi wo yie, wɔ asaase a EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn dze rema wo no do.
Mma nndzi ewu.
Nkyii so nnto awar.
Nkyii so nnwia adze.
Nkyii so nngye wo nyɛnko ho dasewia.
Nkyii so mma w’enyi mmber wo nyɛnko yer; nkyii so mma wo kɔn nndɔ wo nyɛnko fi, ne haban, anaa n’akowaa, anaa n’afonabaa, ne nantwi, anaa n’asoaso, anaa adze biara a ɔyɛ wo nyɛnko dze.
Nsɛm yi na EWURADZE fi ogya, mununkum nye sum kebii no mu, dze ndze kɛse kaa kyerɛɛ hom baguaa no nyinara wɔ bepɔw no do: na wɔammfa bi annka ho.
Na ɔkyerɛɛw no wɔ abopon ebien do, na ɔdze maa me.
Ɔman No No Suro Na ɔbaa dɛ, aber a hom tsee ndze no wɔ sum no mu, wɔ aber a bepɔw no dzɛɛw gya no, hom twee piin me nkyɛn, mekyerɛ hom ebusuakuw mu etsitsir nyinara, nye hom mpanyimfo; na hom see dɛ, Hwɛ, EWURADZE hɛn Nyankopɔn eyi n’enyimnyam nye ne kɛseyɛ akyerɛ hɛn, na yɛatse ne ndze wɔ gya no mu: ndɛ da yi na yeehu dɛ Nyankopɔn nye nyimpa kasa, naaso ɔtsena ase.
Dɛm ntsi afei ebɛnadze ntsi na yenwu?
Osiandɛ gya kɛse yi rebɛhyew hɛn: sɛ yɛtse EWURADZE hɛn Nyankopɔn ndze bio a, ɔno yebowuwu.
Na honam nyinara mu woana na ɔatse Nyankopɔn tseasefo ndze dɛ ofi ogya mu rekasa, dɛ mbrɛ hɛn yɛatse yi, na ɔtsena ase?
Woara twe pin, na tsie dza EWURADZE hɛn Nyankopɔn bɛse nyinara: na woara bɛka dza EWURADZE hɛn Nyankopɔn bɛka akyerɛ wo nyinara kyerɛ hɛn; na yebetsie, na yɛayɛ.
Na EWURADZE tsee hom nsɛm no ndze, aber a hom kasaa kyerɛɛ me no; na EWURADZE see me dɛ, Matse ɔman yi nsɛm no a wɔaka akyerɛ wo no ndze: dza wɔaka no nyinara, wɔase no yie.
Ao kɛtseankyɛ woeenya dɛm akoma wɔ hɔn mu, dɛ wɔdze bosuro me, na woedzi me mbransɛm nyinara do daa daa, na eesi hɔn na ɔnye hɔn mba yie daa!
Kɔ kɛse hɔn dɛ, Hom nsan nkɔ hom asesee mu.
Na ɔwo dze, gyina me nkyɛn ha, na menka mbrasɛm, nye ahyɛdze, nye atsɛmbu a edze bɛkyerɛkyerɛ hɔn no nyinara menkyerɛ wo, na wɔnyɛ no wɔ asaase a medze rema hɔn dɛ wɔmfa no do.
Dɛm ntsi hom ndwen do nyɛ dɛ mbrɛ EWURADZE hom Nyankopɔn ahyɛ hom no: mma hom nndan mmfa enyimfa anaa abankum.
Hom nnantsew kwan no a EWURADZE hom Nyankopɔn ahyɛ hom no nyinara mu, na hom aatsena ase, na eesi hom yie, na hom nda aawar wɔ asaase a hom rekɛfa no do.
Mbrasɛm Kɛse No Afei iyi nye mbrasɛm, ahyɛdze, nye atsɛmbu a EWURADZE hom Nyankopɔn hyɛɛ dɛ wɔmfa nkyerɛkyerɛ hom, na hom nyɛ no wɔ asaase a hom rutwa mu akɛfa no do: na eesuro EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn, eedzi n’ahyɛdze nye ne mbransɛm a merehyɛ wo yi nyinara do, ɔwo, nye wo babanyin, nye wo babanyin ne babanyin, wo nkwa nda nyinara; na wo nda aawar.
Dɛm ntsi, Israel tsie, na dwen do yɛ; na eesi wo yie, na hom aadɔr pii, dɛ mbrɛ EWURADZE, w’egyanom Nyankopɔn abɔ wo anohoba no, wɔ asaase a numfonsu nye ewo pem wɔ do no do.
Israel, tsie: EWURADZE hɛn Nyankopɔn yɛ EWURADZE kor: na fa w’akoma nyinara, na ɔnye wo kra nyinara na ɔnye w’ahoɔdzen nyinara dɔ EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn.
Na nsɛm yi a merehyɛ wo ndɛ da yi, ɔnko w’akoma do; na fa kyerɛkyerɛ wo mba yie, na twetwe ho nkɔmbɔ aber a etse wo fie, nye aber a enam ɔkwan mu, nye aber a ereda, nye aber a erosoɛr.
Na fa yɛ asɛnkyerɛdze bɔ w’abaw do, na ɔnyɛ w’enyiwa ntamu nkaakyekyeree.
Na kyerɛw no wɔ wo fie mpondua ho, nye wo mbobotsen ho.
Asoɔdzen Ho Kɔkɔbɔ Na ɔbɛba dɛ, sɛ EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn dze wo du asaase a ɔkaa ho ntam kyerɛɛ w’egyanom, Abraham, Isaak nye Jakob, dɛ ɔdze rema wo no do; nkurow akɛse fɛɛfɛw a nnyɛ ɔwo na ekyekyeree, nye adan a ndzepa nyinara ahyɛ no amaama a nnyɛ ɔwo na edze hyɛɛ mu, nye mbura a woetutu a nnyɛ ɔwo na itutui, wenyin nture nye olive ndua a nnyɛ ɔwo na etsetsɛwee, na sɛ idzidzi na emee a; ɔno hwɛ yie bɛyɛ na wo werɛ efir EWURADZE a oyii wo fii Egypt asaase do, wɔ nkowaasom ofi mu no.
Suro EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn; na ɔno na som no, na ka ne dzin ho ntam.
Mma hom nndzi enyame fofor a wofi aman a woetwa hom ho ehyia no enyame mu ekyir; na EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn a ɔwɔ wo mu no yɛ Nyame nyinkufo; bɛyɛ na EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn ebufuw adzɛw wɔ wo do, na ɔasɛɛ wo efi asaase enyi.
Mma hom nnsɔ EWURADZE hom Nyankopɔn nnhwɛ, dɛ mbrɛ hom sɔɔ no hwɛe wɔ Massa no.
Hom ndzi EWURADZE hom Nyankopɔn ne mbransɛm, nye ne dasesɛm, nye n’ahyɛdze a ɔdze ahyɛ wo no do yie.
Na yɛ dza ɔtsen na oye wɔ EWURADZE enyiwa do; na eesi wo yie, na aakɔ akɛfa asaase pa a EWURADZE kaa ho ntam kyerɛɛ w’egyanom no, na eetu w’atamfo nyinara efi w’enyim, dɛ mbrɛ EWURADZE aka no.
Sɛ daakye bi wo babanyin bisa wo dɛ, Dasesɛm nye ahyɛdze, nye atsɛmbu a EWURADZE hɛn Nyankopɔn dze hyɛɛ hom yi ase nye dɛn a?
Ɔno se wo ba no dɛ, Nna yɛyɛ Farao no nkowaa wɔ Egypt; na EWURADZE dze nsa a ɔyɛ dzen yii hɛn fii Egypt: na EWURADZE kyerɛɛ nsɛnkyerɛdze nye anwanwadze, akɛse yayaayaw, wɔ Egypt, Farao, nye ne fi nyinara do, wɔ hɛn enyiwa mu: na oyii hɛn fii hɔ dɛ ɔdze hɛn reba, dze asaase a ɔkaa ho ntam kyerɛɛ hɛn egyanom abɛma hɛn.
Na EWURADZE hyɛɛ hɛn dɛ yɛnyɛ ahyɛdze yi nyinara, yensuro EWURADZE hɛn Nyankopɔn, wɔ hɛn yie ntsi, na ɔaagye hɛn nkwa, dɛ mbrɛ ɔtse ndɛ da yi.
Na ɔbɛyɛ tsenenee ama hɛn, sɛ yɛdwen do dzi mbrasɛm yi nyinara do wɔ EWURADZE hɛn Nyankopɔn enyim, dɛ mbrɛ ɔahyɛ hɛn no a.
EWURADZE Ne Man No No Krɔnkrɔnyɛ Sɛ EWURADZE hom Nyankopɔn dze hom du asaase a hom rokɔ akɛfa no do, na ɔpam amanaman pii wɔ hom enyim, Hitifo, Gergasfo, Amorifo, Keenanfo, Perizfo, Hivifo, nye Jebusfo, amanaman esuon a wɔyɛ akɛse na wɔyɛ dzen sen hom no; na sɛ EWURADZE hom Nyankopɔn yi hɔn ma wɔ hom enyim, na hom ku hɔn a; ɔno hom nsɛɛ hɔn pasapasa; mma hom nnye hɔn nndzi ahyɛmu, na mma hom nnhu hɔn mbɔbɔr so: nkyii so mma hom nnye hɔn nndzi awarwar; mma mmfa hom mbabaa mma hom mbabanyin, mma hom nngye hɔn mbabaa so awar mma hom mbabanyin.
Na wɔbɛdan hom mbabanyin enyi ma woeegyaa m’ekyir dzi, na waakɔsom enyame fofor; ma EWURADZE ebufuw adzɛw hom do, na ɔasɛɛ hom ntsɛm.
Mbom mbrɛ hom nye hɔn ndzi no nye yi; hom ndwuruw hɔn afɔrmbukyia na wombubu hɔn edum mu esinesin, na wontwitwa hɔn abosompɔw Aserim no ngu, na wɔmfa gya nhyew hɔn ehonyi a wɔasen no.
Na hom yɛ ɔman krɔnkrɔn ma EWURADZE hom Nyankopɔn: EWURADZE hom Nyankopɔn asan mu eyi hom dɛ bɛyɛ nankasa no soronko ɔman wɔ aman a wɔwɔ asaase enyi nyinara mu.
Nnyɛ dɛ hom dodow so sen ɔman biara ntsi na EWURADZE dze no dɔ sii hom do, na eso ɔsaan mu yii hom: na hom suar dodow wɔ aman nyinara mu.
Mbom osiandɛ EWURADZE dɔ hom, na ɔpɛ dɛ odzi ne ntam a ɔkaa kyerɛɛ hom egyanom no do ntsi, na EWURADZE dze nsa a ɔyɛ dzen eyi hom, na ɔapon hom efi no mu, wɔ Egypthen Farao nsamu.
Dɛm ntsi hom nhu dɛ EWURADZE hom Nyankopɔn, ɔno nye Nyankopɔn; Nyame nokwafo a osie ahyɛmu nye mbɔbɔrhu ma hɔn a wɔdɔ no na wodzi ne mbransɛm do dze kodu ebusuasantsen apem do; na otua hɔn a wɔtan no kaw dze bɔ hɔn enyim, dze sɛɛ hɔn: ɔrennyɛ nyaa mma nyia ɔtan no, obotua no kaw dze abɔ enyim.
Dɛm ntsi dzi mbrasɛm, nye atsɛmbu a merehyɛ wo ndɛ da yi do, na yɛ.
Setsie Do Nhyira Na ɔbɛba dɛ, osiandɛ hom tsie atsɛmbu yi, na wodzi do, na wɔyɛ no, EWURADZE hom Nyankopɔn so bedzi ahyɛmu nye mbɔbɔrhu a ɔkaa ho ntam kyerɛɛ hom egyanom no do ama hom: na ɔbɔdɔ hom, na oehyira hom, na ɔama hom adɔr: na so oehyira hom honam mu aba na hom asaase mu aba, hom eburow nye hom nsa hom wo ngo, hom anantwi mu ngu mu nye hom nguankuw mu mburwa, wɔ asaase a ɔkaa ho ntam kyerɛɛ hom egyanom dɛ ɔdze bɛma hom no do.
Wobehyira hom asen aman nyinara: ɔbanyin anaa ɔbaa anaa hom fiembowa biar rennyɛ ɔbɔnyin wɔ hom mu.
Na EWURADZE beyi yarba nyinara efi hom do; na ɔremmfa Egypt yarba bɔn a hom nyim no bi nnto hom do, na ɔdze bɔto hɔn a wɔtan hom nyinara do.
Na hom bɛhyew aman a EWURADZE hom Nyankopɔn beyi hɔn ama hom no nyinara; mma hom enyi nnhu hɔn mbɔbɔr: nkyii so mma hom nnsom hɔn enyame; na ɔno bɛyɛ efir ama hom.
Sɛ hom se wɔ hom akoma mu dɛ, Amanaman yi dɔɔ so sen hɛn; na yɛbɛyɛ dɛn na yeetum etu hɔn a, mma nnsuro hɔn: kaa dza EWURADZE hom Nyankopɔn dze yɛɛ Farao, nye Egypt nyinara no yie; nsɔhwɛ akɛse no a hom enyiwa hunii, nye nsɛnkyerɛdze, nye anwanwadze, nye nsa a ɔyɛ dzen, nye abasa a wɔatserɛw mu a EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn dze yii hom no: dɛmara na EWURADZE hom Nyankopɔn bɛyɛ aman a hom suro hɔn no nyinara.
Nkyii so EWURADZE hom Nyankopɔn bɔsoma nkotokrodo wɔ hɔn mu, ekodu dɛ hɔn a wɔaka, na woesuma hɔnho no, bɛhera wɔ hom enyim.
Mma hɔn ho nnyɛ hom hu: na EWURADZE hom Nyankopɔn wɔ hom finimfin, Nyame kɛse a no ho yɛ hu no a. Na EWURADZE hom Nyankopɔn bɛpam amanaman no efi hom enyim nkakrankakra: mma hom nnhyew hɔn prɛko, bɛyɛ na haban mu mbowa adɔɔ so hom wo do.
Na EWURADZE hom Nyankopɔn beyi hɔn ama wɔ hom enyim, na ɔdze ɔkogu kɛse bɛka hɔn egu, ekodu dɛ wɔbɛsɛɛ.
Na obeyi hɔn ahemfo ahyɛ hom nsa, na hom aama hɔn dzin ayera efi wiadze: nyimpa biara runntum nngyina hom enyim, ekodu dɛ hom asɛɛ hɔn.
Hom mfa gya nhyew hɔn enyame ehonyi a wɔasen no: mma hom enyi mmber hɔn ho dwetɛ anaa sika, na so mma hom nnyiyi mmfa, bɛyɛ na woesua hom efir wɔ mu: na ɔyɛ ekyiwadze ma EWURADZE hom Nyankopɔn: na mma hom mmfa ekyiwadze nnkɔ hom fie, na hom aannyɛ ebusudze dɛ ɔno: ma ɔnyɛ hom tantan koraa, na hom nkyir hɔn koraa: na ɔyɛ ebusudze.
Asetsena mu Ahwɛyie Mbransɛm a merehyɛ wo ndɛ da yi nyinara hom ndwen do nyɛ, na hom aatsena ase, na wɔaadɔr, na wɔaakɔ akɛfa asaase a EWURADZE kaa ho ntam kyerɛɛ hom egyanom no.
Na hom nkaa ɔkwan nyinara a EWURADZE hom Nyankopɔn egya wo wɔ mu mfe eduanan yi wɔ sar no do no, dɛ ɔrebrɛ hom adze, asɔ hom ahwɛ, ehu dza ɔwɔ hom akoma mu, dɛ hom bedzi ne mbransɛm do, anaa oho.
Na ɔbrɛɛ hom adze, na ɔmaa ɔkɔm dzee hom, na ɔdze manna a hom nnyim, na hom egyanom so nnyim maa hom dzii; na ɔaama hom ehu dɛ nnyɛ edziban nko bi na nyimpa nam do tsena ase, na asɛm biara a ofi EWURADZE anomu so nyimpa nam do tsena ase.
Hom nkataho ennsuw wɔ hom ho, nkyii so w’anan annhohon mfe eduanan yi mu.
Na dwen wɔ w’akoma mu dɛ, dɛ mbrɛ nyimpa tsea ne ba no, dɛmara so na EWURADZE hom Nyankopɔn tsea wo.
Na hom ndzi EWURADZE hom Nyankopɔn ne mbransɛm do, dɛ hom bɛnantsew n’akwan do, na hom esuro no.
Na EWURADZE hom Nyankopɔn dze hom rokɔ asaase pa do, asaase a no do wɔ nworansu, nsunyiwa nye ebun a ofifi abɔn nye akoko mu pem no; asaase a ewifua nye atoko, nye wenyinndua nye adɔmbandua nye pɔmegranate ekutu wɔ do; asaase a olive na ewo wɔ do no; asaase a irinndzi edziban a wɔ do, adze biara so rinnhia wo wɔ do; asaase a n’abo yɛ dadze, na n’akokoe mu na hom botu boran.
Na sɛ hom bedzidzi mee a, hom na nhyira EWURADZE hom Nyankopɔn wɔ asaase pa a ɔdze ama hom no ntsi.
Hom nhwɛ yie ɔno bɛyɛ na hom werɛ efir EWURADZE hom Nyankopɔn dɛ hom rinndzi ne mbransɛm, nye ne ntsɛmbu nye n’ahyɛdze a merehyɛ hom ndɛ da yi do: bɛyɛ so na hom edzidzi amee, na hom esisi adan fɛɛfɛw, atsenatsena mu; na sɛ hom anantwikuw nye hom nguankuw adɔr, na hom dwetɛ nye hom sika adɔɔ so, na adze a hom wɔ nyinara adɔɔ so a; nkyɛ hom akoma amema no ho do, na hom werɛ efir EWURADZE hom Nyankopɔn a oyii hom fii Egypt asaase do, wɔ nkowaasom ofi mu no; nyia ogyaa hom faa sar kɛse huhuhuhu no do, mbrɛ mbowatsena a bɔr wɔ hɔn ano nye nyankoma nketsebowa wɔ, nye asaase kwawee mbrɛ nsu nnyi; nyia oyi nsu fii ɔtwerɛbo botan mu maa hom; nyia ɔdze manna a hom egyanom nnyim nyɛɛn hom wɔ sar no do; dɛ ɔdze rebrɛ hom adze, na ɔasɔ hom ahwɛ, na ɔayɛ hom yie wɔ hom ewiei ekyir no mu: na sɛ wɔ hom akoma mu dɛ, Hɛn tum nye hɔn nsa ne dzen na wɔama yenya ahonya yi.
Na hom nkaa EWURADZE hom Nyankopɔn, na ɔno na ɔmaa hom tum dɛ hom mfa nya homho; na ɔaama n’ahyɛmu a ɔkaa ho ntam kyerɛɛ hom egyanom no etsim, dɛ mbrɛ ɔtse ndɛ da yi.
Na ɔbɛba dɛ, sɛ hom werɛ fir EWURADZE hom Nyankopɔn, na hom kedzi enyame fofor ekyir, na esom hɔn, na hom sɔr hɔn a, midzi hom dase ndɛ da yi, dɛ ɔsɛɛ na hom bɛsɛɛ.
Dɛ mbrɛ EWURADZE sɛɛ amanaman fi hom enyim no, dɛmara na hom bɛsɛɛ; osiandɛ hom enntsie EWURADZE hom Nyankopɔn ndze no.
Israelmba Hɔn Asoɔdzen Israel, tsie: rubotwa Jordan ndɛ da yi, akɔ akɛfa amanaman a wɔyɛ akɛse na wɔyɛ dzen sen ɔwoara, nkurow akɛse a wɔatotow ho afasu edu sor, ɔman a wɔyɛ akɛse na wɔwowaree, Anakfo mbabanyin a inyim hɔn, na atse dɛ wɔka no hɔn ho dɛ, Woana na obotum egyina Anak mbabanyin no enyim?
Dɛm ntsi hu ndɛ da yi, dɛ EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn nye nyia odzi w’enyim rukotwa dɛ ogya a ɔmemen; ɔbɛsɛɛ hɔn, na ɔabrɛ hɔn adze wɔ w’enyim ma eetu hɔn, na ama wɔaasɛɛ ntsɛm, dɛ mbrɛ EWURADZE aka akyerɛ wo no.
EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn enya etu hɔn efi w’enyim egu no, mma nnka wɔ w’akoma mu dɛ, Me ndzeyɛtsenenee ntsi na EWURADZE dze me aba dɛ mebɛfa asaase yi: naaso na amanaman yi hɔn ndzebɔnyɛ ntsi na EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn rutu hɔn efi w’enyim.
Nnyɛ wo ndzeyɛtsenenee, anaa w’akoma ne tsenenee ntsi na erokɔ akɛfa hɔn asaase: mbom amanaman yi hɔn ndzebɔnyɛ ntsi na EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn rutu hɔn efi w’enyim, na ɔaama asɛm a ɔkaa ho ntam kyerɛɛ w’egyanom, Abraham, Isaak, nye Jakob no etsim.
Dɛm ntsi hu dɛ nnyɛ wo ndzeyɛtsenenee bi ntsi na EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn dze asaase pa yi rema wo dɛ fa; na ɔman akɔnkyefo nye wo.
Kaa, mma wo werɛ mmfir, mbrɛ isii yii EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn ebufuw wɔ sar no do; ofi da a ifii Egypt asaase do edze bodur dɛ hom baa bea yi do yi, hom atsew etua wɔ EWURADZE do.
Na Horeb so hom yii EWURADZE ebufuw, na EWURADZE no bo fuuw hom dɛ nkyɛ ɔbɛsɛɛ hom.
Aber a mofoow bepɔw no dɛ merekɛgye abopon no, mekyerɛ ahyɛmu a EWURADZE nye hom dzii n’apon no, nna metsenaa bepɔw no do adaduanan adzekyee nye adzesaa; menndzi edziban mannom nsu so.
Na EWURADZE dze abopon ebien a wɔdze Nyankopɔn nsatseaba akyerɛw do no maa me; na no do na wɔakyerɛw nsɛm no nyinara a ofi gya mu wɔ bepɔw no do nye hom kasae wɔ nguabɔ da no mu no.
Na ɔbaa dɛ adaduanan adzekyee nye adzesaa n’ewiei no, EWURADZE dze abopon ebien no, mekyerɛ ahyɛmu apon no, maa me.
Na EWURADZE see me dɛ, Soɛr, fi ha sian ntsɛm; na wo man a ikeyii hɔn wɔ Egypt no asɛɛ hɔnho; wɔadan efi ɔkwan a mehyɛɛ hɔn no do ntsɛm; wɔayɛ ohonyi a woegu ama hɔnho.
Nkyii so EWURADZE kaa kyerɛɛ me dɛ, Mehu ɔman yi, na, hwɛ, wɔyɛ ɔman asoɔdzenfo: gyaa me ma mensɛɛ hɔn, na mempepa hɔn dzin mfi ɔsor ase: na menyɛ wo ɔman a ɔyɛ dzen na ɔso sen hɔn.
Nna medanee na mifii bepɔw no do sianee, na bepɔw no dzɛɛw gya: nna ahyɛmu apon ebien no kitsakitsa me nsamu.
Na mohwɛe, na, hwɛ, hom ayɛ bɔn etsia EWURADZE hom Nyankopɔn; hom ayɛ ɔnantwiba a woegu ama hom ho: hom adan efi ɔkwan a EWURADZE hyɛɛ hom no do afa nkyɛn ntsɛm.
Na musuoo apon ebien no mu, na motowee fii me nsa ebien no mu gui, na mobobɔɔ no wɔ hom enyim.
Na mohwee ase wɔ EWURADZE enyim, dɛ ahyɛse no, adaduanan adzekyee nye adzesaa; menndzi edziban, mannom nsu so; osian hom bɔn nyinara a hom yɛe no ntsi, dɛ wɔyɛɛ dza omuo wɔ EWURADZE enyi do, dze yii no ebufuw.
Na musuroo ebufuw nye ebufuhyew a EWURADZE nyaa no hom ho dɛ ɔdze rebɛsɛɛ hom no.
Na EWURADZE tsiee me aber no mu so.
Na EWURADZE nyaa Aaron ho ebufuw dodoodow dɛ nkyɛ ɔbɛsɛɛ no; na mepaa kyɛw maa Aaron so aber no ara mu.
Na mefaa hom bɔn a ɔyɛ ɔnantwiba no a hom yɛe no, ma medze gya hyeew no, na misiwii, nyaam no mokomoko kodur dɛ ɔyɛɛ fekɔfekɔ dɛ huntuma: na motoow no huntuma no guu ɔwora no a ofi bepɔw no do pem no mu.
Na Tabera, nye Massa, nye Kibrot-hataava so hom yii EWURADZE ebufuw.
Na aber a EWURADZE somaa hom fi Kades-barnea, dɛ, Hom mfow nkɛfa asaase a medze mama hom no, nna hom tseew etua wɔ EWURADZE hom Nyankopɔn mbrasɛm do, na hom anngye no enndzi, na woenntsie ne ndze so.
Hom ayɛ EWURADZE do etuatsewfo ara fi da a muhun hom no.
Dɛm ntsi na mohwee ase wɔ EWURADZE enyim adzekyee nye adzesaa adaduanan; osiandɛ EWURADZE ase dɛ ɔrebɛsɛɛ hom.
Na mepaa EWURADZE kyɛw, see dɛ, Ao EWURADZE Nyankopɔn, mma nnsɛɛ wo man nye w’egyapadze a enam wo kɛseyɛ do apon hɔn a edze nsa a ɔyɛ dzen eyi hɔn wɔ Egypt no.
Kaa wo nkowaa, Abraham, Isaak, nye Jakob; mma nnhwɛ ɔman yi hɔn asoɔdzen, nye hɔn ndzeyɛbɔn, nye hɔn bɔn so: ɔno bɛyɛ na asaase a iyii hɔn fii do no ase dɛ, Osiandɛ EWURADZE enntum ammfa hɔn annkɔ asaase a ɔbɔɔ hɔn ho anohoba no do, na osiandɛ ɔtan hɔn ntsi, na ɔdze hɔn efir edzi dɛ orukokuku hɔn wɔ sar no do.
Naaso wɔyɛ wo man nye w’egyapadze a enam wo tum kɛse nye w’abasa a wɔatsɛw mu do eyi hɔn.
Abopon No Ho Asɛm Aber no mu na EWURADZE see me dɛ, sen abopon ebien a ɔtse dɛ kan dze no ma woho, na fow bra me nkyɛn wɔ bepɔw no do, na yɛ duadaka ma woho.
Na mebɛkyerɛw nsɛm a ɔwɔ nkan no apon a ebobɔɔ no no do no, wɔ apon no do, na fa hyɛ adaka no mu.
Nna meyɛɛ akeesia duadaka, na meseen abopon ebien a ɔtse dɛ kan dze no, na mofoow bepɔw no, na apon ebien no kitsa me nsamu.
Na EWURADZE kyerɛɛw apon no do, dɛ mbrɛ kan no nkyerɛwee no tse, mbransɛm du no a ɔnoara fi gya no mu kaa kyerɛɛ hom wɔ bepɔw no do nguabɔ da no: na ɔdze maa me.
Na medanee fii bepɔw no do sianee, na medze apon no bɛhyɛɛ adaka a meyɛe no mu; na hɔ na ɔwɔ dɛ mbrɛ EWURADZE hyɛɛ me no.
Na Israelmba tui fii Beerot Bene-jaakan kɔr Mosera: hɔ na Aaron wui, na hɔ na wosiee no; na ne babanyin Eleazar hyɛɛ n’ananmu dzii ɔsɔfo.
Wofi hɔ tui kɔr Gudgoda; na wofi Gudgoda kɔr Jotbata, asaase a nworansu wɔ do.
Aber no mu na EWURADZE yii Levi ebusuakuw, dɛ wɔnsoa EWURADZE ahyɛmudaka no, wongyina EWURADZE enyim nsom no, na wonhyira wɔ ne dzin mu, a wɔayɛ araa dze ebodu ndɛ da yi.
Dɛm ntsi na Levi ennya kyɛfa nye egyapadze wɔ no nuanom mu; EWURADZE nye n’egyapadze, dɛ mbrɛ EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn kaa kyerɛɛ no no.
Na misiankae wɔ bepɔw no do, dɛ asɔpɔn no, adzekyee nye adzesaa adaduanan: na EWURADZE tsiee me aber no mu so; na EWURADZE ammpɛ dɛ ɔsɛɛ wo.
Na EWURADZE see me dɛ, Soɛr, tu wo kwan kedzi ɔman no enyim; ma wɔnkɔ nkɛfa asaase a mekaa ho ntam kyerɛɛ hɔn egyanom dɛ medze mebɛma hɔn no.
EWURADZE N’apɛdze Na afei, Israel, ebɛnadze na EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn rohwehwɛ wɔ wo hɔ, kyɛn dɛ ibosuro EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn, ebɛnantsew n’akwan nyinara do, na adɔ no, na edze w’akoma nyinara nye wo kra nyinara asom EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn, na edzi EWURADZE mbransɛm, nye n’ahyɛdze a merehyɛ wo ndɛ da yi do wɔ wo yieyɛ ntsi?
Hwɛ, ɔsor dzi wɔ EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn, nye ɔsor no sor, asaase, nye dza ɔwɔ mu nyinara.
W’egyanom nko na EWURADZE nyaa hɔn ho enyika dɛ ɔbɔdɔ hɔn, na ɔsaan mu yii hɔn asefo a wodzi hɔn ekyir no, mekyerɛ homara, wɔ aman nyinara mu, dɛ mbrɛ ɔtse ndɛ da yi.
Dɛm ntsi hom ntwitwa hom akoma twatsia na mma wɔnnyɛ asoɔdzen bio.
Na EWURADZE hom Nyankopɔn, ɔno nye enyame mu Nyame, nye ewuradze mu EWURADZE, Nyame kɛse no, Otumfo a no ho yɛ hu a ɔnnhwɛ nyimpa enyim, na onndzi mboaba.
Odzi egyanka nye okunafo hɔn asɛm, na ɔdɔ ɔhɔho, ɔma no edziban nye akataho.
Dɛm ntsi hom ndɔ ahɔho: osiandɛ ho so hom yɛɛ ahɔho wɔ Egypt asaase do.
Suro EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn; ɔno na som no; na ɔno na takyer no ho, na ne dzin ho na ka ntam.
Ɔno nye w’ayɛyi, na ɔno nye wo Nyankopɔn a ɔayɛ ndzɛmba akɛse a ɔyɛ hu a w’enyiwa ehu yi ama wo.
Nyimpa eduosuon na w’egyanom dze sianee kɔr Egypt; na afei EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn ayɛ wo ɔdodow dɛ ɔsor nworaba.
EWURADZE Ne Kɛseyɛ Dɛm ntsi dɔ EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn, na sie n’ahwɛdodze, nye n’ahyɛdze, nye ne atsɛmbu, nye ne mbransɛm dabaa.
Na hom nhu ndɛ da yi: na mennkasa nnkyerɛ hom mba a wonnyim, na wonnhun EWURADZE hom Nyankopɔn ntsea, ne kɛseyɛ, ne nsa a ɔyɛ dzen, nye n’abasa a wɔatserɛw mu, nye ne nsɛnkyerɛdze, nye no ndwuma a ɔyɛe no wɔ Egypt tsiaa Egypthen Farao, nye n’asaase nyinara; nye dza ɔdze yɛɛ Egyptdɔm, nye hɔn mpɔnkɔ, nye hɔn ntseaseanam; mbrɛ ɔmaa Mbɛw Po nsu praam hɔn do aber a woritsiw hom, na mbrɛ EWURADZE asɛɛ hɔn ebodu ndɛ da yi; nye dza ɔdze yɛɛ hom wɔ sar no do, bodur dɛ hom baa bea yi do; na dza ɔdze yɛɛ Datan nye Abiram, Reuben ne babanyin Eliab mbabanyin no; mbrɛ asaase buee n’ano, na ɔmeen hɔn, nye hɔn efifo, nye hɔn asesee, nye enyikandze biara a odzii hɔn ekyir, wɔ Israel nyinara finimfin no: na hom enyiwa ehu edwuma kɛse a EWURADZE yɛe no nyinara.
Dɛm ntsi hom ndzi mbrasɛm a merehyɛ wo ndɛ da yi nyinara do, na hom ho aayɛ dzen, na hom aakɛfa asaase a hom rutwa mu akɔ do akɛfa no; na hom nda aawar wɔ asaase a EWURADZE kaa ho ntam kyerɛɛ hom egyanom dɛ ɔdze bɛma hɔn na hɔn asefo no do, asaase a numfonsu nye ewo pem wɔ do.
Na asaase no, mbrɛ irutwa mu akɔ do akɛfa no, ɔnntse dɛ Egypt asaase, mbrɛ hom fi bae no, mbrɛ epe w’aba, na edze w’anan petse do nsu, dɛ fan ture no: na asaase no, mbrɛ hom rutwa mu akɛfa no, yɛ akoko nye abɔn asaase, na ɔnom ɔsor nyankom mu nsu; asaase a EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn hwɛ do; EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn n’enyiwa wɔ do dabaa, ofi afe n’ahyɛse araa kodu afe n’ewiei.
Na ɔbɛba dɛ, sɛ hom tsie me mbransɛm a merehyɛ hom ndɛ da yi yie, dɛ hom dze hom akoma nyinara nye hom kra nyinara bɔdɔ EWURADZE hom Nyankopɔn, na hom asom no a, ɔno mebɛma hom asaase do nsɔ atɔ wɔ n’aber mu, esusow nye ɔbɛsɛ, ma aaboaboa w’eburow, nye wo nsa, nye wo ngo ano.
Na mebɛma wo haban mu aba nkyɛkyɛr ama wo fiembowa, na eedzidzi amee.
Hom nhwɛ homho yie, ma wɔanndaadaa hom akoma, na hom aanndan ammfa nkyɛn, na hom aannkɔsom enyame fofor, na hom aannsɔr hɔn; na EWURADZE n’ebufuw aanndzɛw wɔ hom do, na ɔaanntow ɔsor mu, dɛ nsu nntɔ, na asaase mma no ndɔbaa; na hom aannhera ntsɛmara wɔ asaase pa a EWURADZE dze rema hom no do.
Dɛm ntsi hom mfa me nsɛm yi nsie hom akoma nye hom kra mu; na hom mfa nyɛ asɛnkyerɛdze mbɔ hom abaw do, na ɔnyɛ nkaakyekyeree wɔ hom enyiwa ntamu.
Na hom mfa nkyerɛkyerɛ hom mba, twetwe ho nkɔmbɔ aber a etse wo fie, nye aber a enam ɔkwan mu, nye aber a ereda, nye aber a erosoɛr.
Na kyerɛw no wɔ wo fi mpondua ho, na wo mbotsen ho: ama hom nda, nye hom mba nda aadɔɔ so wɔ asaase a EWURADZE kaa ho ntam kyerɛɛ hom egyanom dɛ ɔdze bɛma hɔn no do, dɛ ɔsor nda wɔ asaase do.
Na sɛ hom bɔdɔ EWURADZE hom Nyankopɔn, hom anantsew n’akwan nyinara do, na hom atakyer no ho a; ɔnodze EWURADZE botutu amanaman yi nyinara efi hom enyim, na hom afa amanaman akɛse a wɔyɛ dzen sen homara.
Beebiara a hom anamɔn betsia no bɛyɛ homdze: ofi sar no do, nye Lebanon, ofi esutsen Eufrates ho ara kodu ekyirekyir epo no ho bɛyɛ hom he.
Nyimpa biara runntum nngyina hom enyim: EWURADZE hom Nyankopɔn dze hom ho suro nye hom ho hu bogu asaase a hom betsia do nyinara do, dɛ mbrɛ ɔaka akyerɛ hom no.
Nhyira Na Ndom Hwɛ, medze nhyira nye ndom mirisi hom enyim ndɛ da yi; nhyira no, sɛ hom tsie EWURADZE hom Nyankopɔn mbransɛm a merehyɛ hom ndɛ da yi a; na ndom no, sɛ hom enntsie EWURADZE hom Nyankopɔn mbransɛm, na hom dan fi ɔkwan a merehyɛ hom ndɛ da yi do fa nkyɛn dɛ worikedzi enyame fofor a hom nnyim hɔn ekyir a. Na ɔbɛba dɛ, sɛ EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn dze wo du asaase a erokɔ akɛfa no do a, ibesi nhyira no wɔ bepɔw Gerizim do, na ndom no wɔ bepɔw Ebal do.
Ana wonnyi Jordan egya, witɔree kwan no ekyir, wɔ Keenanfo a wɔtse Araba do no asaase do, Gilgal tsentsendo, wɔ More nsudur ho bi a?
Na hom rubotwa Jordan akɔ akɛfa asaase a EWURADZE hom Nyankopɔn dze rema hom no, na hom bɛfa, na hom atsena do.
Na hom ndwen do nyɛ ahyɛdze nye atsɛmbu a medze mirisi hom enyim ndɛ da yi nyinara.
Beebi a Wɔnsom Nyankopɔn Iyinom nye ahyɛdze nye ntsɛmbu a hom ndwen do nyɛ wɔ asaase a EWURADZE, w’egyanom Nyankopɔn dze ama wo dɛ fa no do, nda a hom dze tse asaase do nyinara.
Ɔsɛɛ na hom nsɛɛ mbeambea nyinara a amanaman a hom rekɛfa no som hɔn enyame, mbepɔw atsentsen do, nye akoko do, nye dua momon biara ase; na hom ndwuruw hɔn afɔrmbukyia, na wombubu hɔn edum mu esinesin, na wɔmfa gya nhyew hɔn Aserim; na hom ntwitwa hɔn enyame ehonyi a woesinsian no mu ngu, na hom nsɛɛ hɔn dzin mfi bea no do.
Mma hom nnyɛ dɛm mma EWURADZE hom Nyankopɔn.
Mbom beebi mbrɛ EWURADZE hom Nyankopɔn bɛsan mu eyi wɔ hom ebusuakuw nyinara mu dɛ ɔdze ne dzin bɔto hɔ no, mekyerɛ ne tsenabew no na hom nhwehwɛ, na hɔ na hom kɔ; na hɔ na hom mfa hom ɔhyew afɔr, nye hom okum afɔr, nye hom ebupɛn du du nye hom nsamu ɔmado afɔr, nye hom anohobadze, nye hom ayamuyi afɔr, nye hom anantwikuw nye hom nguankuw mu mbakan nkɔ: na hɔ na hom ndzidzi wɔ EWURADZE hom Nyankopɔn enyim, na hom nye hom efifo, hom enyi ngye wɔ adze nyinara a hom dze hom nsa ka a EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn ehyira wo wɔ mu no mu.
Mma hom nnyɛ dɛ mbrɛ ndzɛmba a yɛreyɛ wɔ ha ndɛ da yi mu biara tse yi a nyimpa biara yɛ dza ɔtsen wɔ nankasa n’enyiwa do no: na hom nnyae nndur ahomgye nye egyapadze a EWURADZE hom Nyankopɔn dze rema hom no mu.
Mbom sɛ hom nya twa Jordan, na hom kɛtsena asaase a EWURADZE hom Nyankopɔn rema hom enya edzi no do, na ɔma hom ahomgye fi hom atamfo nyinara a woetwa hom ho ehyia ho, na hom tsena dwudwoodwo a; ɔno ɔbɛba dɛ beebi mbrɛ EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn bɛsan mu eyi ma ne dzin atsena hɔ no, hɔ na hom mfa dza merehyɛ hom no nyinara nkɔ; hom ɔhyew afɔr, nye hom okum afɔr, hom ebupɛn du du, nye hom nsamu ɔmado afɔr, nye hom soronko anohobadze a hom bɔ ma EWURADZE no nyinara: na hom mma hom enyi ngye wɔ EWURADZE hom Nyankopɔn enyim, hom, nye hom mbabanyin, nye hom mbabaa, nye hom nkowaa, nye hom mfonabaa, nye Levinyi a ɔwɔ hom kuropon mu, susuampa dɛ onnyi kyɛfa anaa egyapadze wɔ hom mu no.
Hom nhwɛ hom ho yie mma hom aammbɔ hom hyew afɔr wɔ beebiara a hom hu; gyedɛ beebi mbrɛ EWURADZE bɛsan mu eyi wɔ hom ebusuakuw kor mu, hɔ na hom mbɔ hom hyew afɔr, na hɔ na hom nyɛ dza merehyɛ hom nyinara.
Naaso ku na dzi nam wɔ wo kuropon nyinara mu, dɛ mbrɛ wo kra no kɔn dɔ nyinara, dɛ mbrɛ nhyira a EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn dze ehyira wo no tse: nyia no ho nntsew nye nyimpa no ho tsew ndzi bi, dɛ adoa, nye dɛ ɔtrɔm.
Bɔgya no nko na mma hom nndzi; hue gu famu dɛ nsu.
Mma nndzi w’eburow, anaa wo nsa, anaa wo ngo mu ebupɛn du du wɔ wo kuropon mu, anaa w’anantwikuw anaa wo nguankuw mu mbakan, nye w’anohobadze biara a ebɔ ho anohoba, nye w’ayamuyi afɔr, nye wo nsamu ɔmado afɔr: mbom dzi no wɔ EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn enyim wɔ beebi mbrɛ EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn bɛsan mu eyi no, ɔwo, nye wo babanyin, nye wo babaa, nye w’akowaa, nye w’afonabaa, nye Levinyi a ɔwɔ wo kuropon mu: na ma w’enyi ngye wɔ EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn enyim wɔ dza wo nsa ka nyinara ho.
Hwɛ woho yie amma aammpow Levinyi aber tsentsen nyina a edze tse w’asaase do nyinara mu.
Sɛ EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn trɛw wo he mu, dɛ mbrɛ ɔabɔ wo anohoba no, na ese dɛ, mibedzi nam, osiandɛ wo kra no kɔn dɔ dɛ obedzi nam a, dzi nam, dɛ mbrɛ wo kra no kɔn dɔ nyinara.
Sɛ beebi mbrɛ EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn bɛsan mu eyi dze ne dzin ato hɔ no ɔnye wo ntamu twe dodow a, ɔno ku w’anantwikuw nye wo nguankuw a EWURADZE dze ama wo no mu bi, dɛ mbrɛ mahyɛ wo no, na dzi wɔ wo kuropon mu, dɛ mbrɛ wo kra no kɔn dɔ nyinara.
Mekyerɛ dɛ mbrɛ wodzi adoa nye ɔtrɔm no, dɛmara so na dzi bi: nyia no ho nntsew nye nyia no ho tsew nyina ndzi bi.
Nsew ara na hyɛ mma enndzi bɔgya no: na mma mmfa nam no nnka bɔgya no ho nndzi.
Mma nndzi; hue gu famu dɛ nsu.
Mma nndzi; ma onsi ɔwo, nye wo mba a wodzi w’ekyir yie, aber a ereyɛ dza ɔtsen wɔ EWURADZE enyiwa do no.
Wo ndzɛmba krɔnkrɔn a ewɔ no nko, nye w’anohobadze, na fa kɔ beebi mbrɛ EWURADZE bɛsan mu eyi no: na bɔ wo hyew afɔr, nam nye bɔgya no, wɔ EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn afɔrmbukyia no do: na wo kum afɔr bɔgyaa no wonhue ngu EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn afɔrmbukyia no do, na nam no na dzi.
Dwen do tsie nsɛm a merehyɛ wo yi nyinara, ma eesi ɔwo, nye wo mba a wodzi w’ekyir yie daa, aber a ereyɛ dza oye na ɔtsen wɔ EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn enyiwa do no.
Sɛ EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn twitwa amanaman fi w’enyim, mbrɛ erokɔ akɛfa hɔn no, na efa hɔn, na etsena hɔn asaase do a; hwɛ woho yie amma wɔasɛɛ hɔn efi w’enyim n’ekyir no, hɔn ekyirdzi aannyɛ wo efir; na eemmbisa hɔn enyame ekyir kwan, dɛ, Amanaman yi dua dɛn som hɔn enyame, na mo so menyɛ dɛmara?
Mma nnyɛ EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn dɛm: na EWURADZE n’ekyiwadze a okyir no nyinara na wɔayɛ ama hɔn enyame; na hɔn mbabanyin nye hɔn mbabaa mpo na wɔdze gya hyew hɔn ma hɔn enyame.
Adze biara a merehyɛ hom no, na hom ndwen do nyɛ: mma mmfa bi nnka ho, na mma nnyi do bi so.
Kɔkɔbɔ Wɔ Ehonyisom Ho Sɛ nkɔnhyɛnyi bi, anaa ɔdaasonyi bi soɛr wɔ wo mu, na ɔma wo asɛnkyerɛdze anaa anwanwadze bi, na asɛnkyerɛdze anaa anwanwadze a ɔkasaa ho kyerɛɛ wo no ba mu, dɛ, Ma yɛnkɔ nkedzi enyame fofor a ɔwo nnyim hɔn no ekyir, na yɛnkɔsom no a; mma nntsie nkɔnhyɛnyi no anaa ɔdaasonyi no nsɛm no: na EWURADZE hom Nyankopɔn rosɔ hom ahwɛ, dze ehu kyerɛ dɛ hom dze hom akoma nyinara nye hom kra nyinara dɔ EWURADZE hom Nyankopɔn.
Hom nnantsew ndzi EWURADZE hom Nyankopɔn ekyir, na hom nsuro no, na hom ndzi ne mbransɛm do, na hom ntsie ne ndze, na hom nsom no; na hom ntakyer no ho.
Na nkɔnhyɛnyi no, anaa ɔdaasonyi no, wonku no; osiandɛ wɔaka etuatsew ho asɛm etsia EWURADZE hom Nyankopɔn a oyii hom fii Egypt asaase do, na ɔpoon wo fii nkowaasom ofi mu no, dɛ ɔdze rotwetwe wo efi ɔkwan a EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn hyɛɛ wo dɛ nantsew mu no do esi nkyɛn.
Ama eetu bɔn no efi wo mu.
Sɛ wo nuabanyin, wo na ne babanyin, anaa wo babanyin, anaa wo babaa, anaa wo yer a ɔda wo bo mu, anaa wo nyɛnko a ɔtse dɛ wankasa wo kra, daadaa wo nsumaa mu, dɛ, Ma yɛnkɔ nkɔsom enyame fofor a ɔwo nye w’egyanom nnyim no; aman a woetwa hom ho ehyia a wɔbɛn wo, anaa wɔnye wo ntamu twe, ofi asaase ano kor ara kodu asaase ano kor so hɔn enyame mu bi a; mma mmpen no, na nntsie no so; nkyii so mma w’enyiwa nnhu no mbɔbɔr, na nkora no do, na nnhuntsa no do so; na oku na ku no; wo nsa na ondzi kan ntɔ no do dɛ woboku no, na n’ekyir no na ɔman no nyinara nsa.
Na siw no abo ma onwu; osiandɛ ɔhwehwɛɛ dɛ ɔtwetwe wo fi EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn a oyii wo fii Egypt asaase do, wɔ nkowaasom ofi mu no ho.
Na Israel nyinara ntse, na wonsuro, na wɔannda ho ara annyɛ dɛm ndzebɔn a ɔtse dɛ mbrɛ iyi tse yi wɔ wo mu.
Na sɛ etse dɛ wɔreka wɔ wo nkurow a EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn dze rema wo dɛ tsena mu hɔ no kor bi ho, dɛ, Ebusuyɛfo bi efi wo mu asoɛr, na wɔadaadaa hɔn kurow mu atsefo dɛ, Hom mma yɛnkɔ nkɔsom enyame fofor a hom nnyim hɔn a; ɔno hwehwɛ mu, na bisabisa mu yie; na hwɛ, sɛ ɔyɛ nokwar, na asɛm no yɛ ampa dɛ dɛm ekyiwadze yi wɔayɛ no wɔ wo mu a: oku na fa nkrantsee ano ku kurow no mu atsefo no, na fa nkrantsee ano sɛɛ no, nye dza ɔwɔ mu nyinara nye no mu fiembowa so pasapasa.
Na boaboa no mu asadze nyinara ano wɔ no brɔn finimfin, na fa gya hyew kurow no, nye no mu asadze no nyinara dɛ ɔhyew afɔr mu, fa ma EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn: na ɔnyɛ ɔmamfo daa; mma wɔnnkyekyer no bio.
Na mma ebusudze no mu bi mmfam wo nsa ho: ama EWURADZE aadan efi n’ebufuhyew no ho, na oeehu wo mbɔbɔr, na oennya ayamuhyehye ama wo, na ɔaama adɔr dɛ mbrɛ ɔaka ntam akyerɛ w’egyanom; sɛ a itsie EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn ndze, dɛ idzi ne mbransɛm a merehyɛ wo ndɛ da yi nyinara do, na eyɛ dza ɔtsen wɔ EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn enyiwa do a.
Mbowa A Hom Ndzi Na Dza Mma Hom Nndzi Hom yɛ EWURADZE hom Nyankopɔn ne mba: mma hom mmbobɔ homho akam, na mma hom nnyɛ hom momapɔw do ahyɛnsewdze mma ewufo.
Na ɔwo yɛ ɔman krɔnkrɔn ma EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn, na EWURADZE asan mu eyi wo dɛ ebɛyɛ noara no soronko ɔman, wɔ aman a wɔwɔ asaase enyi nyinara mu.
Mma nndzi ekyiwadze biara.
Iyinom nye mbowa a hom ndzi: ɔnantwi, ɔkɔsɔw, nye apɔnkye, ɔtrɔm, nye adoa, nye ɔwansan, nye iwi, nye ɔtwe, nye eko, nye ɔwɛr.
Na abowa biara a ɔwɔ anansa a no mu apae, na n’anansa no mu apae ebien koraa, na ɔkosa adzepuwii, wɔ mbowa mu no, ɔno na hom ndzi.
Naaso iyinom na mma hom nndzi wɔ hɔn a wɔkosa adzepuwii mu, anaa hɔn a hɔn anansa mu apae koraa mu: efupɔnkɔ, nye asokɛtɛ, nye etwabowa, osiandɛ wɔkosa adzepuwii dze na hɔn anansa mu mmpaae, hɔn ho nntsew mma hom: na preko, osiandɛ n’anansa mu apae dze na ɔnnkosa adzepuwii, no ho nntsew mma hom: hɔn nam no mma hom nndzi bi, na hɔn efun no mma hom nnka.
Iyinom na hom ndzi wɔ dza ɔwɔ nsu mu nyinara mu: dza ɔwɔ tɛterɛ nye abon no hom ndzi: na biara a onnyi tɛterɛ nye abon no mma hom nndzi; no ho nntsew mma hom.
Nnoma a hɔn ho tsew no nyinara hom ndzi.
Na iyinom nye hɔn a mma hom nndzi bi: ɔkɔr, nye ɔkɔrbia, nye nsukɔr; nye ɔkom pɛtɛ, nye ɔkom, nye ɔsansaa n’ahorow; nye akonkoran biara n’ahorow; nye sohor, na anadwe krɔma, nye epo akokɔ, nye akrɔma n’ahorow; patu ketseaba, nye patu kɛse, nye ambɛn patu; na nantwinoma, nye ɔpɛtɛ, nye epo akonkoran; nye esukɔnkɔn, nye bakanoma n’ahorow, nye esuakwa nye apan.
Na ntumbowa a wɔwea nyinara hɔn ho nntsew mma hom: mma wonndzi.
Ntumbowa a hɔn ho tsew no nyinara hom ndzi.
Mma hom nndzi biribi a noara oewu: fa ma ɔhɔho a ɔwɔ wo kuropon mu ma ondzi; anaa tɔn ma ɔnanaben: na ɔwo yɛ ɔman krɔnkrɔn ma EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn.
Mma nnoa apɔnkyeba wɔ ne na no numfonsu mu.
Ebupɛn Du Du W’aba a idua no ndɔbaa a ofi wo haban mu ba afrenhyia afrenhyia no, yiyi do ebupɛn du du.
Na dzi wɔ EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn enyim, wɔ beebi mbrɛ ɔbɛsan mu eyi dɛ ne dzin ntsena hɔ no, w’eburow, nye wo nsa, nye wo ngo do ebupɛn du du, nye w’anantwikuw, nye wo nguankuw mu mbakan; ama eesua dɛ isuro EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn dabaa.
Na sɛ EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn hyira wo na sɛ ɔkwan no war dodow ma wo ma irunntum nnsoa, osiandɛ beebi mbrɛ EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn asan mu eyi dɛ ɔdze ne dzin bɔto no nye wo ntamu twe dodow, ɔno dan no sika mu, na kyekyer sika no kitsa, na kɔ beebi mbrɛ EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn asan mu eyi no.
Fa sika no tɔ adze biara a wo kra no kɔn dɔ, ɔnantwi, anaa oguan, anaa wenyin, anaa nsa dzendzen, anaa adze biara a wo kra pɛ no: na dzi no wɔ hɔ ara wo EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn enyim, na ma w’enyi ngye, ɔwo nye wo fifo: na Levinyi a ɔwɔ wo kuropon mu no, mma nngya no ekyir; osiandɛ onnyi kyɛfa nye egyapadze ka wo ho.
Mfe ebiasa biara n’ewiei no, yiyi afe no ara mu ndɔbaa do ebupɛn du du no nyinara, na fa gu wo kuropon mu: na Levinyi, osiandɛ onnyi kyɛfa nye egyapadze biara dɛ mbrɛ ewɔ, na ɔhɔho, nye egyanka, nye okunafo a wɔwɔ wo kuropon mu, mbra, na wombedzidzi mmee; na EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn eehyira wo wɔ wo nsaano edwuma a eyɛ nyinara mu.
Mfe Esuon Ho Mbra Mfe esuon biara n’ewiei no yɛ akwangya.
Na mbrɛ wonsi ngya kwan nye yi: ɔdzefɛmfo biara dza ɔdze fɛm ne nyɛnko no ɔmfa nkyɛ no; mma ɔnnhyɛ ne nyɛnko nye no nua no nngye.
Ɔnanaben dze hyɛ no gye: na adze biara a ewɔ wɔ wo nua hɔ dze fa kyɛ no.
Naaso mma ohianyi bi mmba wo mu; (na nhyira na EWURADZE behyira wo wɔ asaase a EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn dze rema wo dɛ egyapadze a kɛfa no do;) sɛ iritsie EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn ndze ara yie, dɛ erodwen do ayɛ ahyɛdze yi a merehyɛ wo da yi nyinara a. Na EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn behyira wo, dɛ mbrɛ ɔbɔɔ wo anohoba no: na edze afemfɛm amanaman pii, na ɔwo dze erennkɛfɛm: na ɔwo bɔhom amanaman pii do, na hɔn dze, wɔronnhom wo do.
Sɛ wo nuanom mu obi yɛ ohianyi wɔ wo nkyɛn, wɔ wo kuropon biara mu wɔ asaase a EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn dze rema wo no do a, mma mmpirim w’akoma, na mma mmua wo nsa so wɔ wo nua ohianyi no do: na obue na bue wo nsa ma no, na ɔfɛm na fɛm no dza ɔbɔso ne hia a ehia no no.
Hwɛ yie ma adwen huhuw ammba w’akoma mu dɛ, Afe a otsia esuon no, akwangya afe no abɛn; na annyɛ bɔn enntsia wo nua ohianyi no, dɛ eremma no hwee; ma ɔaanntsea mu ammfrɛ EWURADZE enntsia wo, na aannyɛ bɔn amma wo.
Ɔma na ma no, na mma ɔnnyɛ w’akoma mu yaw dɛ ebɛma no: osiandɛ dɛm adze yi ntsi na EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn behyira wo wɔ w’edwuma nyinara mu, nye dza edze wo nsa bosuo mu nyinara mu.
Na ohianyi remmpa wɔ asaase no do: dɛm ntsi na merehyɛ wo dɛ, Bue na bue wo nsa ma wo nua, wo kɔhweaban, nye wo hianyi, wɔ w’asaase do.
Sɛ wɔtɔn wo nua Hebriwnyi ɔbanyin, anaa ɔbaa, ma wo, na ɔsom wo mfe esia a; ɔno afe a otsia esuon no gya no kwan na omfi wo nkyɛn mfa noho ndzi nkɔ.
Na sɛ irigya no kwan ma oeefi wo nkyɛn afa noho edzi akɔ a, mma ɔmmfa nsapan nnkɔ: fa wo nguankuw mu bi, nye w’ewuporoweebea do bi, nye wo wenyintwer mu bi ma no kwa: dɛ mbrɛ EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn ehyira wo no na ma no.
Na kaa dɛ eyɛɛ akowaa wɔ Egypt asaase do, na EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn poon wo: dɛm ntsi na merehyɛ wo asɛm yi ndɛ.
Na ɔmbra dɛ, sɛ ɔse wo dɛ, Mirimmfi wo nkyɛn nnkɔ; osiandɛ ɔdɔ wo nye wo fi ntsi, wɔ dɛ ɔtse no yie wɔ wo nkyɛn ntsi a; ɔno fa fitsii, na fa fitsi n’asowa mu suo abow mu, na ɔnyɛ w’akowaa daa.
Na w’afonabaa no so yɛ no dɛmara.
Mma ɔnnyɛ dzen mma wo, dɛ ibegya no kwan ma oeefi wo nkyɛn afa noho edzi akɔ; na ɔasom wo mfe esia ayɛ ɔpaanyi akatua mbɔho ebien ho adze: na EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn behyira wo wɔ dza eyɛ nyinara mu.
W’anantwikuw nye wo nguankuw mu mbakan enyin a wɔbɔwo hɔn no tu hɔn si nkyɛn ma EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn: mma mmfa wo nantwi abakan nnyɛ edwuma, na nnsusua wo nguankuw mu abakan ho nhwi so.
Dzi no wɔ EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn enyim afrenhyia afrenhyia wɔ beebi mbrɛ EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn bɛsan mu eyi no, ɔwo nye wo fifo.
Na sɛ ɔwɔ dzɛm bi wɔ no ho dɛ ɔyɛ apakye anaa n’enyi efura, dzɛm bɔn biara wɔ no ho a, mma mmfa mmbɔ EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn afɔr.
Dzi no wɔ wo kuropon mu: nyia no ho nntsew nye nyia no ho tsew nyina ndzi, dɛ mbrɛ wodzi ɔwansan nye ɔforote.
No bɔgyaa nko na mma nndzi; hue gu famu dɛ nsu.
Afahyɛ Ahorow No Ho Mbra Hyɛ bosoom Abib nsew, na dzi apaho no ma EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn; na bosoom Abib mu na EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn yii wo wɔ Egypt anadwe.
Na bɔ apaho okum afɔr no ma EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn, nguankuw nye anantwikuw mu, wɔ beebi mbrɛ EWURADZE bɛsan mu eyi dɛ ne dzin ntsena hɔ no.
Mma mmfa mbɔrkaw boodoo nnka ho nndzi; nda esuon na fa epitsi boodoo ka ho dzi, mekyerɛ amandzehu boodoo no; osiandɛ ɔhar mu na ifiir edzi fii Egypt asaase do: ama aakaa da a edze fiir edzi fii Egypt asaase do no wo nkwa nda nyinara.
Na mma wonnhu wo nkyɛn mbɔrkaw wɔ w’ahe nyinara do nda esuon; nkyii so mma nam a iku hɔn da a odzi kan ewimbir no bi nnka anadwe no nyinara mma onnkodu anapa.
Mma nnku apaho no wɔ wo kuropon a EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn dze rema wo no biara mu: gyedɛ beebi mbrɛ EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn bɛsan mu eyi dɛ ne dzin ntsena hɔ no, hɔ na ku apaho no ewimbir, wi rokɔtɔ no, wɔ wo Egypt fi aber no mu.
Na toto na dzi no wɔ beebi mbrɛ EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn bɛsan mu eyi no: na anapa no san, na kɔ w’asesee mu.
Nda esia na dzi epitsi boodoo: na da a otsia esuon no nyɛ asomdwee nguabɔ mma EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn; mma nnyɛ edwuma wɔ mu.
