Adapɛn esuon na kan ma woho: da a erehyɛ ase dze kantankrankye aka eburow a osisi hɔ no na fi kan adapɛn esuon.
Na hyɛ adapɛn afahyɛ no ma EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn fa ka wo nsa mu ayamuyi afɔr ntoboa a edze rema no no ho, dɛ mbrɛ EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn ehyira wo no: na ma w’enyi ngye wɔ EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn enyim, ɔwo, nye wo babanyin, nye wo babaa, nye w’akowaa, nye w’afonabaa, nye Levinyi a ɔwɔ wo kuropon mu, nye ɔhɔho, nye egyanka, nye okunafo a wɔwɔ wo mu, wɔ beebi mbrɛ EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn bɛsan mu eyi dɛ ne dzin ntsena hɔ no.
Na kaa dɛ eyɛɛ akowaa wɔ Egypt: na dwen do yɛ ahyɛdze yi.
Hyɛ ntamadan afahyɛ nda esuon, aber a aboaboa w’ewuporoweebea do nye wo wenyintwer mu adze ano no: na ma w’enyi ngye wɔ w’afahyɛ no mu, ɔwo, nye wo babanyin, nye wo babaa, nye w’akowaa, nye w’afonabaa, nye Levinyi, nye ɔhɔho, nye egyanka, nye okunafo a wɔwɔ wo kuropon mu.
Nda esuon na hyɛ fa ma EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn wɔ beebi mbrɛ EWURADZE bɛsan mu eyi no: osiandɛ EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn behyira wo wɔ wo ndɔbaa nyinara mu, na wo nsaano edwuma nyinara mu, na w’enyi bɛgye ara.
Afrenhyia kor mu mpɛn ebiasa na wo mbanyin nyinara nkefir EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn enyim wɔ beebi mbrɛ ɔbɛsan mu eyi no; wɔ epitsi boodoo afahyɛ no mu, nye adapɛn afahyɛ no mu, nye ntamadan afahyɛ no mu: na mma wɔmmfa nsapan mmbefir EWURADZE enyim: nyimpa biara mma dza obotum, dɛ mbrɛ EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn nhyira a ɔdze ehyira wo no tse.
Atsɛmbuafo Na Atsɛntsenenee Hyɛ ntsɛmbuafo nye mpanyimfo wɔ wo nkuropon a EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn dze rema wo dɛ mbrɛ w’ebusuakuw tsetsee nyinara mu: na wɔmfa ntsɛn tsenenee mbu ɔman no ntsɛn.
Mma nndan atsɛmbu enyi; mma mmfɛr nyimpa: nkyii so mma nngye akyɛdze; na akyɛdze fura enyansafo enyi, na ɔdan atseneneefo nsɛm enyi.
Dza ɔtsen ara na dzi ekyir, ama eenya nkwa, na eenya asaase a EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn dze rema wo no edzi.
Mma nntsɛw dua biara mmfa nnyɛ abosompɔw Asera wɔ EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn afɔrmbukyia a ebɛyɛ ama woho no nkyɛn.
Nkyii so mma nnsi dum a EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn kyir mma woho.
Mma mmfa ɔnantwi, anaa oguan a no ho wɔ dzɛm, anaa adzebɔn biara, mmbɔ okum afɔr mma EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn na ɔyɛ ekyiwadze ma EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn.
Sɛ wohu wɔ wo mu, wɔ wo nkuropon a EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn dze rema wo no biara mu, ɔbanyin anaa ɔbaa bi a ɔyɛ dza omuo wɔ EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn enyi do dɛ ɔto n’ahyɛmu, na ɔkɔ kɔsom enyame fofor bi, ɔsɔr dɛ, ewia, bosoom, anaa ɔsor dɔm no mu biara a mennhyɛɛ ho mbra no, na wɔka kyerɛ wo, ma etse a, ɔno hwehwɛ mu yie na hwɛ, sɛ ɔyɛ nokwar, na asɛm no wɔ mu ampa, dɛ ɔayɛ dɛm ekyiwadze yi wɔ Israel a; ɔno fa ɔbanyin anaa ɔbaa no a ɔayɛ dɛm adze bɔn yi fir edzi kɔ wo kuropon ho, na wonsiw no abo ma onwu.
Adasefo beenu, anaa adasefo baasa anomu do na wɔmfa nku nyia ɔsɛ owu no; mma wɔmmfa ɔdasefo kor anomu do nnku no.
Adasefo no nsa na ondzi kan wɔ no do nku no, na n’ekyir no ɔman no nyinara hɔn nsa.
Ama eeyi mbusu no efi wo mu.
Sɛ asɛm bi ho atsɛmbu yɛ dzen dodow ma wo, wɔ ewudzi nye nsa a apa ntamu, mansosɛm mu, na opira no, dɛ ɔyɛ akasakasa bi wɔ wo kuropon mu a, ɔno soɛr, na kɔ beebi mbrɛ EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn bɛsan mu eyi no; na kɔ asɔfo Levifo, nye nda no mu ɔtsɛmbufo a ɔwɔ do no nkyɛn na kebisa; na wɔnkyerɛ wo asɛm no n’atsɛmbu: na yɛ dɛ mbrɛ asɛm a wɔbɛkyerɛ wo wɔ beebi mbrɛ EWURADZE bɛsan mu eyi no tse no ara; na dwen do yɛ dɛ mbrɛ wɔbɛkyerɛkyerɛ wo no nyinara: dɛ mbrɛ mbra a wɔbɛkyerɛkyerɛ wo, na mbrɛ atsɛmbu a wɔbɛka akyerɛ wo no tse no ara, na yɛ: mma nndan mmfi asɛm a wɔbɛkyerɛ wo no ho nnkɔ enyimfa anaa abankum.
Na nyimpa a obedzi nkontompɔsɛm, dɛ orinntsie ɔsɔfo a ogyina hɔ som wɔ EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn enyim, anaa ɔtsɛmbufo no, dɛm nyimpa no onwu: na yi mbusu no fi Israel.
Na ɔman no nyinara ntse, na wonsuro, na wonndzi nkontompɔsɛm bio.
Ahensi Na Ɔhen N’asɛdze Sɛ idu asaase a EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn dze rema wo no do, na efa, na etsena do, na ese dɛ, Mibesi mo do hen, dɛ amanaman a wotwa mo ho hyia nyinara no a; nyia EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn bɛsan mu eyi no no noara na fa no si wo do hen: wo nuanom mu bi na fa no si wo do hen: mma mmfa ɔnanaben bi a ɔnnyɛ wo nua nnsi wo do.
Mma ɔhen no mma no mpɔnkɔ nndɔɔ so mma no, nkyii so mma ɔmma ɔman no nnsan nnkɔ Egypt, nnkɛpɛ no mpɔnkɔ dodow: mber dodowara a EWURADZE ase hom dɛ ɔdzekɔr yi mma hom nnsan mmfa ɔkwan no do bio no.
Nkyii so mma ɔmma ne yernom nndɔɔ so.
Na ɔmbra dɛ, sɛ ɔtse n’ahendzi ahengua do a, onsusu mbra yi a ɔwɔ asɔfo Levifo no enyim no do nkyerɛw bi wɔ nwoma mu mma noho: na ɔnko ne nkyɛn, na ɔnkenkan mu no nkwa nda nyinara: na oeesua dɛ obosuro EWURADZE no Nyankopɔn, na odzi mbra yi mu nsɛm nyinara nye ahyɛdze yi do, na ɔyɛ: na n’akoma aamma noho do annsen no nuanom, na ɔaanndan emmfi mbrasɛm no ho ammfa enyimfa, anaa abankum: ama ne nda aawar wɔ n’ahendzi mu, ɔno nye ne mba wɔ Israel.
Asɔfo Na Levifo Kyɛfa Levifo Asɔfo nye Levi ebusuakuw nyinara rinnya kyɛfa nye egyapadze wɔ Israel mu: EWURADZE ogya afɔr nye n’egyapadze na wondzi.
Na worinnya egyapadze wɔ hɔn nuanom mu: EWURADZE nye hɔn egyapadze, dɛ mbrɛ ɔaka akyerɛ hɔn no.
Na iyi nyɛ asɔfo no hɔn ndzinoa mfi ɔman no hɔ, mfi hɔn a wɔbɔ afɔr no hɔ, ɔnantwi o, oguan o, wɔmfa abasa, nye adadaw ebien no, nye efur no mma ɔsɔfo no.
W’eburow, wo nsa, nye wo ngo mu nduadzewakan, nye wo nguan ho nhwi a woesusua no kan no, fa ma no.
Osiandɛ ɔno na EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn asan mu eyi no wɔ w’ebusuakuw nyinara mu, dɛ ongyina nsom wɔ EWURADZE ne dzin mu, ɔno na ne mbabanyin daa nyina.
Na sɛ Levinyi bi fi wo nkuropon no biara mu, fi Israel mu beebiara mbrɛ ɔakɔsoɛ, na ɔdze ne kra ne pɛ nyinara ba beebi mbrɛ EWURADZE asan mu eyi no a; ɔno ɔnsom wɔ EWURADZE ne Nyankopɔn ne dzin mu, dɛ mbrɛ no nuanom Levifo no a wogyina EWURADZE enyim hɔ no nyinara yɛ no.
Wonnya kyɛfa dɛ hɔndze no ndzi, mfa nka dza ofi n’egyanom adzetɔn mu ba no ho.
Amanaman Ndzeyɛɛ A Ɔyɛ Ekyiwadze Sɛ inya du asaase a EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn dze rema wo no do a, mma nnsua amanaman no hɔn ndzeyɛɛ a ɔyɛ ekyiwadze no yɛ.
Mma wonnhu wo mu obi a ɔma ne babanyin anaa ne babaa fa ogya mu, nyia ɔhyɛ mbusunkɔm, nyia ɔyɛ abayidze, anaa adzebisafo, anaa osumantunyi, anaa kaberkyernyi, anaa nyia ɔfrɛfrɛ esunsum, anaa anyɛn, anaa ɔsamamfrɛnyi.
Osiandɛ obiara a ɔyɛ iyinom no yɛ ekyiwadze ma EWURADZE: na osian ekyiwadze yi ntsi na EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn tutuu hɔn fii w’enyim yi.
Enye EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn ntsena no emudzi mu.
Na amanaman yi a erekɛfa yi wotsie hɔn a wɔyɛ abayidze, na mbusunkɔnhyɛfo: na ɔwo dze, EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn mmaa wo kwan dɛ yɛ dɛm.
Nyankopɔn No Nkɔnhyɛnyi No Nkɔnhyɛnyi a ofi wo mu, ofi wo nuanom mu a ɔtse dɛ emi, na EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn bɛma no do ama wo; ɔno na hom ntsie no; dɛ mbrɛ dza ibisae wɔ EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn hɔ wɔ Horeb, wɔ nguabɔ da no tse nyinara, dɛ, Mma menntse EWURADZE me Nyankopɔn ndze bio, nkyii so mma munnhu ogya kɛse yi bio, na meennwu.
Na EWURADZE see me dɛ, Dza wɔaka no, wɔaka no yie.
Mebɛma nkɔnhyɛnyi do ama hɔn wɔ hɔn nuanom mu tse dɛ ɔwo; na medze me nsɛm bɛhyɛ n’anomu, na ɔaka dza mebɛhyɛ no nyinara akyerɛ hɔn.
Na ɔbɛba dɛ obiara a onnketsie me nsɛm a ɔbɛka wɔ me dzin mu no, mibebisa noara.
Na nkɔnhyɛnyi a ɔbɛka asɛm bi nkontompɔ mu wɔ me dzin mu a, mennhyɛɛ no dɛ ɔnka no, anaa nyia ɔbɛkasa wɔ enyame fofor bi dzin mu no, nkɔnhyɛnyi kor no bowu.
Bi a nna ase wɔ w’akoma mu dɛ, Yɛbɛyɛ dɛn bohu asɛm a EWURADZE nnkae no?
Ɔno nye dɛ, sɛ nkɔnhyɛnyi bi kasa wɔ EWURADZE ne dzin mu, na sɛ asɛm no annyɛ hɔ anaa ammba mu so a, nna asɛm a EWURADZE nnkae no nye no: nkɔnhyɛnyi no aka no ator mu, mma nnsuro no.
Guansumabew Nkurow Sɛ EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn twitwa amanaman a ɔdze hɔn asaase rema wo gu, na itu hɔn, na etsena hɔn nkurow, nye hɔn adan mu a; yiyi nkurow ebiasa si hɔ ma woho wɔ asaase a EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn dze rema wo dɛ fa no mu.
Siesie ɔkwan no ma woho, na paapaa asaase a EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn rema enya edzi no n’ahe mu ebiasa na onyimpakumfo biara eeguan akɔ hɔ.
Na onyimpakumfo a onguan nkɔ hɔ na onnya nkwa no n’asɛm nye yi: nyia oku ne nyɛnko awerɛfir mu, na ɔnntan no dada bi; dɛ nyimpa nye ne nyɛnko kɔ kwaa mu rukotwa dua, na ne nsa ma abɔndua do dze eetwa dua no, na ne tsidadze no hɔn fi no kura mu, na ɔka ne nyɛnko no, ma owu a; onguan nkɔ nkurow yi kor mu na onnya nkwa: amma bɔgya ho ɔwerdzinyi no eenntsiw nyimpakumfo no, aber a n’akoma ayɛ hyew no, na osiandɛ ɔkwan no war ntsi ɔaannkɔto no, na ɔaammbɔ no ɔbɔtɔr; naaso na nyimpakumfo no nnsɛ wu, susuampa dɛ ɔnntan no dada bi no.
Dɛm ntsi na merehyɛ wo dɛ yiyi nkurow ebiasa si hɔ ma woho.
Na sɛ EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn tserɛw wo he mu, dɛ mbrɛ ɔaka ntam akyerɛ w’egyanom, na ɔdze asaase no a ɔbɔɔ anohoba dɛ ɔdze bɛma w’egyanom no nyinara ma wo: sɛ idzi mbrasɛm yi nyinara a merehyɛ wo ndɛ da yi do eyɛ, dɛ ebɔdɔ EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn, na anantsew n’akwan do daa a; ɔno yiyi nkurow ebiasa so ka ebiasa yi ho si hɔ ma woho: na wɔaannka bɔgya a onndzi so enngu wɔ w’asaase a EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn dze rema wo dɛ egyapadze no mu, na bɔgya eengu wo do.
Na sɛ nyimpa bi tan ne nyɛnko, na ɔkɔ no atsɛwee, na ɔsoɛr no do, na ɔbɔ no ɔbɔtɔr ma owu; na oguan kɔ nkurow yi kor mu a: ɔno no kurow no mu mpanyimfo nsoma ma wɔnkɛfa no wɔ hɔ na wɔmfa no nhyɛ bɔgya ho ɔwerdzinyi no nsa, ma onwu.
Mma w’enyiwa nnhu no mbɔbɔr, na yi bɔgya a onndzi so fi Israel, na eesi wo yie.
Adasefo Ho Asɛm Mma nntwe wo nyɛnko n’asaasehe a tsetsefo no dze esi, wɔ w’egyapadze a ibenya edzi wɔ asaase a EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn dze rema wo dɛ fa no do.
Ɔdasefo baako nnsoɛr nntsia nyimpa bi wɔ emumuyɛ biara, anaa bɔn biara ho, wɔ bɔn biara a ɔyɛ ho: adasefo beenu anomu, anaa adasefo baasa anomu na wɔmfa do nsi asɛm gyinae.
Sɛ ɔdasekrumfo bi soɛr tsia nyimpa bi dzi no mfom ho dase a; ɔno nyimpa beenu nyina a ɔham no da hɔn ntamu no, mbegyina EWURADZE enyim, wɔ asɔfo nye ntsɛmbufo a wɔwɔ hɔ nda no mu no enyim; na ntsɛmbufo no nhwehwɛ mu yie: na, hwɛ, sɛ ɔdasefo no yɛ ɔdasekrumfo, na oedzi no nua dasekrum a; ɔno hom nyɛ no dɛ mbrɛ ɔdween dɛ nkyɛ ɔbɛyɛ no nua no: ama eeyi mbusu no efi wo mu.
Na hɔn a wɔaka no ntsi, na wonsuro na ɔdzekɔr yi wɔaammbɔ mbusu biara a ɔtse dɛm wɔ wo mu bio.
Na mma w’enyiwa nnhu mbɔbɔr; nkwa nhyɛ nkwa ananmu, enyiwa nhyɛ enyiwa ananmu, ese nhyɛ ese ananmu, nsa nhyɛ nsa ananmu, anan nhyɛ anan ananmu.
Sɛ itu ɔsa nye w’atamfo aakɔko, na ihu mpɔnkɔ, nye ntseaseanam, nye ɔman a wɔdɔɔ so sen wo a, mma nnsuro hɔn: na EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn a ɔdze wo fi Egypt asaase do bae no ka wo ho.
Na ɔmbra dɛ sɛ hom rehɛn akono a, ɔsɔfo no ntwe mpin na ɔmbɛkasa nkyerɛ ɔman no, na ɔnse hɔn dɛ, Israel, hom ntsie, hom rebɛn akono ndɛ da yi nye hom atamfo akɔko: mma hom akoma nntu, mma hom nnsuro, na hom ho mmpopo, nkyii so mma hɔn ho nnyɛ hom hu; na EWURADZE hom Nyankopɔn nye nyia ɔnye hom rokɔ, nye hom atamfo rokɔko ama hom, na ɔaagye hom nkwa.
Na ahwɛdofo no nkasa nkyerɛ ɔman no, dɛ, Nyimpa mmuana na oesi dan fofor, na ommbuei?
Wɔmma ɔnsan nkɔ ne fie, ma ɔaanntɔ wɔ ɔko mu, na nyimpa fofor eennkobue.
Na nyimpa mmuana na ɔatsew wenyin ture, na onnyae nnyii n’aba bi?
Wɔmma ɔnsan nkɔ ne fie, na ɔaanntɔ wɔ ɔko mu, na nyimpa fofor eennkeyi n’aba no.
Na nyimpa biara a ɔagye basia bi dɛ yer, na onnyae nnhyiaa no no, wɔmma ɔnsan nkɔ ne fie, ma ɔaanntɔ wɔ ɔko mu, na nyimpa fofor bi annkɛfa no dɛ ɔyer.
Na ahwɛdofo no nwɔw do nkasa nkyerɛ ɔman no, na wɔnse dɛ, Nyimpa mmuana na osuro na n’akoma apa?
Wɔmma ɔnsan nkɔ ne fie, amma no nuanom hɔn akoma eenntu dɛ n’akoma.
Na ɔmbra dɛ, sɛ ahwɛdofo no wie ɔman no kasa kyerɛ a, wɔnhyehyɛ asafohemfo wɔ ɔman no ne tsir.
Sɛ ebɛn kurow bi dɛ enye no rokɔko a, ɔno bɔ asomdwee ho dawur kyerɛ no.
Na ɔmbra dɛ, sɛ ɔma wo asomdwee mbuae, na obue wo a, ɔno, ma nkorɔfo a ibohu hɔn wɔ mu no nyinara mbɛyɛ ɔtowyiman mma wo, na wɔnsom wo.
Na sɛ ɔnnye wo ennsiesie, na otu wo do sa a, ɔno kɔ no ntoa: na sɛ EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn yi no hyɛ wo nsa a, ɔno fa nkrantsee ano bobɔ no mu mbanyin nyinara: na mbaa nye mbofraba, nye ofiembowa, nye dza ɔwɔ kurow no mu nyinara dze, mekyerɛ no mu asadze nyinara, fa no afonam fa ma woho; na dzi w’atamfo asadze a EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn dze ama wo no.
Dɛm na yɛ nkurow a wɔnye wo ntamu twe dodow nyinara a wɔnnyɛ amanaman yi nkurow bi no.
Na aman yi nkurow a EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn dze rema wo dɛ egyapadze no dze, mma nngye biribiara a ogu ahom no nkwa: mbom sɛɛ hɔn pasapasa; Hetfo, nye Amorifo, Keenanfo, nye Perizfo, nye Hivifo, nye Jebusfo; dɛ mbrɛ EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn ahyɛ wo no: amma wɔaannkyerɛ wo mma aannyɛ hɔn ekyiwadze nyinara a wɔyɛ ma hɔn enyame no bi; na hom aannyɛ bɔn enntsia EWURADZE hom Nyankopɔn.
Sɛ itua kurow bi ma ɔkyɛr, dɛ ereyɛ ho sa afa a, mma mmfa abɔndua nnsɛɛ no ho ndua; na no do aba bi na ibedzi, na mma nntwitwa nngu; ana haban mu dua yɛ nyimpa, na asɛɛ no?
Ndua a inyim dɛ ɔnnyɛ ndua a wodzi no nko, na sɛɛ no na twitwa gu; na sisi nduaban wɔ kurow a ɔnye wo dzi ako no ho araa ma onkodu dɛ ɔbɔhwe ase.
Nsumaa mu Ewudzi Sɛ wohu obi a woeku no da haban mu, wɔ asaase a EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn dze rema wo dɛ fa no do, na wonnyim nyia okum no a: ɔno wo mpanyimfo nye wo atsɛmbufo mfir edzi, na wonkosusu nkodu nkurow a etwa ehyia nyia woeku no no ho no do: na ɔmbra dɛ, kurow a ɔbɛn nyimpa a woeku no no nkyɛn no, mekyerɛ kurow no mu mpanyimfo no mfa anantwikuw mu ɔnantwiber a wɔmmfaa no nnyɛɛ edwuma, na ɔnntwee kɔndua pɛn; ɔnantwiber no nsian nkɔ ɔbɔn a nsu pem wɔ do a wɔnndɔwee na wonnduaa mu adze mu, na wombu ɔnantwiber no no kɔn wɔ ɔbɔn no mu: na Levi mbabanyin asɔfo no mbra ho; na hɔn na EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn asan mu eyi hɔn dɛ wɔnsom no, na wonhyira wɔ EWURADZE ne dzin mu; na hɔn anomu asɛm do na wɔmfa ndzi ɔham biara nye ɔbɔ biara ho asɛm: na kurow no mu mpanyimfo a wɔbɛn nyimpa a woku no no, nhohor hɔn nsa ho ngu ɔnantwiber a wobuu no kɔn mu wɔ ɔbɔn no mu no do: na wombua nse dɛ, Nnyɛ hɛn nsa bi kaa bɔgya gui, nkyii so hɛn enyiwa ennhu.
EWURADZE, fa fir wo man Israel a apon hɔn no, na mma bɔgya a onndzi so nnka wo man Israel mu.
Na bɔgya no wɔdze bɛkyɛ hɔn.
Ama eeyi bɔgya a onndzi so no efi wo mu, aber a ereyɛ dza ɔtsen wɔ EWURADZE enyiwa do no.
Mbasiafo A Wɔafa Hɔn Ndɔmmum Sɛ itu sa nye w’atamfo kɔko, na EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn yi hɔn hyɛ wo nsa, na efa hɔn ndɔmmum, na ihu ndɔmmum no mu ɔbaa fɛɛfɛw bi, na inya no ho akɔndɔ, na epɛ dɛ efa no yɛ wo yer a; ɔno fa no bra fie; na onyi ne tsir na ombubu n’awerɛw; na onyi no ndɔmmum akataho no mfi noho, na ɔnka wo fie, na ongyam n’egya nye ne na bosoom ara mu: na n’ekyir no akɔ ne nkyɛn, na ayɛ no kun, na ɔayɛ wo yer.
Na ɔmbra dɛ, sɛ emmpɛ no a, ɔno ma ɔnkɔ beebi mbrɛ ɔpɛ; na ɔtɔn dze, mma nntɔn no nngye sika, mma nnye no nndzi dɛ afonabaa, osiandɛ abrɛ no adze.
Abakan Ne Ndzinoa Sɛ ɔbanyin bi wɔ yernom beenu na, ɔdɔ kor, na ɔtan kor, na hɔn beenu no nyina awowo mba ama no; na sɛ abakan no nye nyia ɔtan no ne babanyin a: ɔno ɔmbra dɛ, da a ɔkyɛ n’adze a ɔwɔ mu ma ne mbabanyin no mma ɔmmfa nyia ɔdɔ no no ne babanyin nnyɛ abakan nndzi nyia ɔtan no ne babanyin a ɔyɛ abakan no enyim: mbom ɔngye abakan no nto mu, nyia ɔtan no no ne babanyin no, ɔmma no dza ɔwɔ nyinara mu kyɛfa mbɔho ebien: na ɔno nye n’ahoɔdzen ahyɛse; abakan ndzinoa yɛ nedze.
Ɔba Otuatsewnyi Sɛ nyimpa wɔ babanyin ɔsoɔdzennyi nye etuatsewnyi a onntsie n’egya ne ndze, anaa ne na ne ndze, na wɔtsea no so, na onntsie hɔn a: ɔno n’egya nye ne na nkyer no, na wɔmfa no mfir edzi nkɔ no kurow mu mpanyimfo nkyɛn wɔ no kuropon ano; na wɔnse no kurow no mu mpanyimfo no dɛ, Hɛn babanyin yi yɛ ɔsoɔdzennyi nye otuatsewnyi, onntsie hɛn ndze.
Ɔyɛ ɔkɔhwinyi, nye ɔsabokwanyi.
Na no kurow no mu mbanyin nyinara nsiw no abo, ma ɔntɔ: ama eeyi mbusu no efi wo mu; na Israel nyinara ntse, na wonsuro.
Mbra Ahorow Bi So Na sɛ nyimpa bi yɛ bɔn a ɔsɛ owu, na woku no, na edze no sɛn dua bi do a; mma ne nyimpadua no nnka dua no do anadwe no nyinara, na osie na sie no da no ara; na nyia wɔasɛn no no Nyame apa no; amma eenngu w’asaase a EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn dze rema wo dɛ egyapadze no ho fi.
Mma nnhu wo nua ne nantwi anaa no guan dɛ ɔatɔ gon, na mmfi hɔn ho nnkosuma: fa hɔn san brɛ wo nua.
Na sɛ wo nua no mmbɛn wo, anaa sɛ innyim no a, ɔno fa no bra wo fie wo, na ɔnko wo nkyɛn nkodu dɛ wo nua no bɔhwehwɛ no, na aadan no ama no bio.
Na dɛmara so na fa yɛ n’asoaso; anaa wo nua n’adze biara a ayew no a ehu no: mma nnguan mmfi ho.
Mma nnhu wo nua n’asoaso anaa ne nantwi dɛ ɔahwe ase wɔ ɔkwan mu, na mmfi ho nnkosuma: boa no ma ɔmma hɔn do bio.
Mma ɔbaa nnhyɛ adze a ɔyɛ ɔbanyin dze, nkyii so ɔbanyin nnhyɛ ɔbaa n’atar: na obiara a ɔyɛ iyinom no ɔyɛ ekyiwadze ma EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn.
Sɛ ikopue anoma ne birebuw bi do awerɛfir mu wɔ ɔkwan mu, wɔ dua biara do anaa famu, mba anaa nkyirefuwa wɔ mu, na na no butuw na mba no, anaa nkyirefuwa no do a, mma nnkyer na no nnka mba no ho; ɔno ma na no nkɔ, na fa mba no; na eesi wo yie, na ama wo nda aawar.
Sɛ isi dan fofor a, ɔno gye wo dan etsifi ban, ama sɛ obi fi do hwe ase a, aammfa bɔgya ammba wo dan no do.
Mma mmfa aba horow ebien nndua wo wenyin ture mu: amma aannhwer nduadzewa no nyina, aba a edua no, nye wenyin ture no ndɔbaa no nyina.
Mma mmfa ɔnantwi nye asoaso mmbɔ mu mmfuntum.
Mma mmfura tam a wɔdze kuntu nye ndwera afora awen.
Tu wo tam a edze kata wo do no ntoado anan no do ndwow.
Sɛ ɔbanyin bi hyia yer, na ɔkɔ ne nkyɛn, na ɔtan no, na ɔdze enyimguasesɛm to no do, na ɔbɔ no dzin bɔn, se dɛ, Mihyiaa ɔbaa yi, na mokɔr ne nkyɛn no, mennhu no ho mbaabunyɛ nsɛnkyerɛdze no a: ɔno akataasia no n’egya nye ne na mfa akataasia no ne mbaabunyɛ nsɛnkyerɛdze no na wɔmfa mbra kurow no mu mpanyimfo nkyɛn wɔ kuropon no mu; na akataasia no n’egya nse mpanyimfo no dɛ, Medze me babaa maa ɔbanyin yi awar, na ɔtan no; na, hwɛ, ɔdze enyimguasesɛm ato no do, dɛ, Mennhu mbaabunyɛ nsɛnkyerɛdze wɔ wo babaa yi ho; naaso me babaa ne mbaabunyɛ nsɛnkyerɛdze nye yi.
Na wɔntserɛw tam no mu wɔ kurow no mu mpanyimfo no enyim.
Na kurow no mu mpanyimfo no mfa ɔbanyin no na wɔntwe n’aso; na wɔngye no mbratodze dwetɛ ɔha, na wɔmfa mma akataasia no n’egya, osiandɛ ɔabɔ Israel ɔbaabun dzin bɔn: na nwar no; mma ɔnnko no wɔ ne nda nyinara mu.
Na sɛ asɛm yi yɛ nokwar, dɛ woennhu mbaabunyɛ nsɛnkyerɛdze wɔ akataasia no ho dze a: ɔno wonyi akataasia no mbra n’egya ne fi abowano, na no kurow no mu mbanyin nsiw no abo ma onwu: osiandɛ ɔayɛ nkwaseadze wɔ Israel, dɛ ɔagor ndwamangor wɔ n’egya fie: ama eeyi mbusu no efi wo mu.
Sɛ wohu ɔbanyin bi dɛ ɔnye ɔbaa a ɔwɔ kun da a, ɔno hɔn beenu nyina nwu, ɔbanyin a ɔnye ɔbaa no dae no, nye ɔbaa no: ama eeyi mbusu no efi Israel.
Sɛ wɔdze akataasia bi a ɔyɛ ɔbaabun ma banyin bi awar, na banyin bi hu no wɔ kurow mu, na ɔnye no da a; ɔno hom mfa hɔn emu ebien nyina mfir edzi nkɔ kurow no n’abotsen ekyir, na hom nsiw hɔn abo ma wonwuwu; akataasia no, dɛ ɔwɔ kurow mu na ɔannkeka mu ntsi; na ɔbanyin no, dɛ ɔabrɛ ne nyɛnko ne yer adze ntsi: ama eeyi mbusu no efi wo mu.
Na sɛ banyin bi hu akataasia ɔwarfo bi yer no wɔ haban mu, na ɔbanyin no kyer no, na ɔnye no da a; ɔno ɔbanyin a ɔnye no dae no nko na onwu: na akataasia no dze mma nnyɛ no hwee; bɔn a ɔsɛ owu nnyi akataasia no do: na dɛ mbrɛ nyimpa soɛr ne nyɛnko do, na oku no no, dɛmara so na asɛm yi tse: na haban mu na ohun no; na akataasia a wɔagye no yer no kekaa mu, na nna obi nnyi hɔ a ɔbɛgye no.
Sɛ banyin bi hu akataasia a ɔyɛ ɔbaabun a wɔnngyee no yer, na ɔkyer no, na ɔnye no da, na wohu hɔn a; ɔno banyin a ɔnye no dae no, mfa dwetɛ dwetɛbona eduonum mma akataasia no n’egya, na ɔnyɛ ne yer, osiandɛ ɔabrɛ no adze; mma ɔnnko no ne nda nyinara.
Ɔbanyin bi nnwar n’egya ne yer, na onnyi n’egya n’akatado.
Nyia Ɔmfata EWURADZE Ne Bagua Nyia no ntɔhwɛbo abɔ, anaa ne banyin etwa no, mma ɔnnhɛn EWURADZE ne baguaa mu.
Nyia wɔawo no wɔ edwaman bi nnhɛn EWURADZE ne baguaa mu; n’ebusuasantsen a otsia du mpo mu biara nnhɛn EWURADZE ne baguaa mu.
Ammonnyi anaa Moabnyi nnhɛn EWURADZE ne baguaa mu; hɔn ebusuasantsen a otsia du mpo mu biara nnhɛn EWURADZE ne baguaa mu ara da: osiandɛ wɔammfa edziban na ɔnye nsu emmbehyia hom wɔ ɔkwan no mu, aber a hom fi Egypt reba no; na dɛ wɔkɔbɔɔ Beer ne babanyin Balaam a ofi Petor a ɔwɔ Mesopotemia no paa dɛ ɔmbɔdom wo ntsi.
Naaso EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn ammpɛ dɛ otsie Balaam; na EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn daan ndom no nhyira maa wo, osiandɛ EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn dɔɔ wo.
Mma nnhwehwɛ hɔn asomdwee nye hɔn eyiedzi wo nda nyinara daa.
Mma nnkyir Edomnyi; na ɔyɛ wo nua: mma nnkyir Egyptnyi; osiandɛ ekɛyɛɛ n’asaase do ɔhɔho.
Ebusuasantsen a otsia ebiasa mba a wɔbɔwo hɔn ama hɔn no na wɔnhɛn EWURADZE ne baguaa mu.
Ahotsew Wɔ Nseraban Mu Sɛ ifir edzi kɛkyer w’atamfo ho nsera a, ɔno sie woho yie wɔ adze bɔn biara ho.
Sɛ ɔbanyin bi wɔ hom mu a no ho nntsew wɔ no ha a ɔsen anadwe bi ntsi a, ɔno omfi nseraban no mu nkɔ ekyir, mma ɔmmba nseraban no mu; na ɔmbra dɛ orudu ewimbir no, onguar noho wɔ nsu mu: na sɛ wi kɔtɔ a, ɔmbra nseraban no mu.
Nya beebi so wɔ nseraban no ekyir, mbrɛ ibefir edzi akɔ: na nya ɔsɔsɔw wɔ wo ndadzedze mu; na ɔmbra dɛ, sɛ ekɔkotow ekyir hɔ a, edze eefun, na aasan ekyir akata dza ofi wo mu ba no do: na EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn nenam wo nseraban mu, dɛ ɔregye wo, na ɔdze w’atamfo ama wɔ w’enyim; dɛm ntsi wo nseraban nyɛ krɔnkrɔn: amma oeennhu efifidze bi wɔ wo mu, na ɔaanndan emmfi wo nkyɛn.
Mbra Bi So Mma nnyi akowaa a oefi no wura nkyɛn eguan aba wo hɔ mma no wura: ma ɔnye wo ntsena, wɔ wo mu, wɔ beebi mbrɛ ɔbɛsan mu eyi no wɔ wo nkuropon no kor mu, mbrɛ ɔpɛ no dodow no: mma nnhyɛ no do.
Mma Israel mbabaa mu biara nnyɛ edwaman, nkyii so mma Israel mbabanyin mu biara nndan edwaman.
Mma mmfa ɔbaa edwaman apaabɔdze, anaa ɔkraman (banyin edwaman) n’akatua, mmba EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn fie wɔ anohoba biara mu: na ebien yi nyina yɛ ekyiwadze ma EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn.
Mma mmbɔ wo nua bosa nngye nsiho: ɔnanaben na bɔ no bosa gye nsiho; na wo nua dze, mma mmbɔ no bosa nngye nsiho: na EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn eehyira wo adze a edze wo nsa bɛka nyinara mu, wɔ asaase a erokɔ akɛfa no do.
Sɛ ebɔ EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn anohoba a, mma nnyɛ nyaa dɛ ebɔpon: na ampaara EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn bɔhwehwɛ no wɔ wo hɔ; na ɔbɛdan wo bɔn.
Na sɛ ema anohoba no ka a, ɔnnyɛ bɔn mma wo.
Dza efi w’anofamfa do epue no dwen do na yɛ; dɛ mbrɛ abɔ EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn anohoba, ayamuyi afɔr a edze w’ano aka no.
Sɛ idu wo nyɛnko no wenyin ture mu a, ɔno dzi esikyireamba no bi mee; mbom mma mmfa bi nngu w’adze mu.
Sɛ idu wo nyɛnko n’eburow a osisi hɔ mu a, ɔno fa wo nsa pempan mbɛtsem no bi; mbom mma mma dadze do wɔ wo nyɛnko n’eburow a osisi hɔ do.
Awar Na Awargyaa Sɛ ɔbanyin bi fa ɔbaa na ɔwar no, na ɔba dɛ, ɔbaa no nnya n’enyin enyimnyam, osiandɛ oehu no ho enyitodze bi ntsi a, ɔnkyerɛw awargyaa krataa mma no, na ɔmfa nhyɛ ne nsa, na ongya no kwan ma omfi ne fie nkɔ.
Na sɛ ofi ne fie kɔ a, ɔnkɔ nkɛyɛ ɔbanyin fofor bi ne yer.
Na sɛ kun fofor no so tan no, na ɔkyerɛw awargyaa krataa ma no, na ɔdze hyɛ ne nsa, na ogya no kwan ma ofi ne fie kɔ; anaa sɛ ekyir kun no a ɔfaa no yɛɛ ne yer no wu a; mma no kun a odzi kan no a ogyaa no kwan no, mmfa no nnyɛ ne yer bio, wɔ no ho fi a ogui no ekyir no; na ɔyɛ ekyiwadze wɔ EWURADZE enyim: na mma nnyɛ ma asaase a EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn dze rema wo dɛ egyapadze no do nnyɛ bɔn.
Mbra No Bi So Sɛ ɔbanyin bi hyia yer fofor a, mma ɔnnkɔ sa, nkyii so mma wɔmmfa edwuma biara nnto no do: ondzi noho wɔ fie afrenhyia, na ɔmma ne yer a oehyia no no akomatɔmu.
Mma nyimpa bi nngye ewuyambo anaa ewuyambobaa a ɔda do no ahoba: nna tserɛ ɔregye nyimpa no nkwa dɛ ahoba.
Sɛ wohu nyimpa a owia no nuanom Israel mu bi, na ɔtseetsee no, anaa ɔtɔn no a; ɔno owifo no nwu; ama eeyi mbusu no efi wo mu.
Hwɛ yie wɔ kwata owuyar ho, na aadwen do yie ayɛ dɛ mbrɛ asɔfo Levifo no bɛkyerɛkyerɛ hom no nyi nara: dɛ mbrɛ mehyɛɛ hɔn no, dɛmara so na hom ndwen do nyɛ.
Kaa dza EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn dze yɛɛ Miriam wɔ ɔkwan no mu aber a hom fi Egypt reba no.
Sɛ ebɔ wo nyɛnko bosa biara a, mma nnkɔ ne fie nnkɛgye n’ahobadze.
Abow enyim na gyina, na nyimpa a ebɔ no bosa no mfa ahobadze no mfir edzi mbrɛ wo wɔ abow enyim.
Na sɛ ɔyɛ ohianyi a, mma mmfa n’ahobadze no nnda: sɛ wi kɔtɔ a, fa ahobadze no san kɛma no, na ɔnda wɔ n’atar mu, na onhyira wo: na ɔnyɛ tsenenee mma wo wɔ EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn enyim.
Mma nnhyɛ ɔpaanyi a ɔyɛ ɔbɔbɔnyi nye ohianyi no do, sɛ ofi wo nuanom mu o, ofi w’ahɔhoe a wɔwɔ w’asaase do wɔ wo nkuropon mu o: ne da mu na ma no n’apaadze, nkyii so mma wi nnkɔtɔ do; osiandɛ ɔyɛ ɔbɔbɔnyi, na ɔdze n’akoma esi do: amma ɔaannka mu ammfrɛ EWURADZE enntsia wo, na aannyɛ bɔn amma wo.
Mma wonnku egyanom wɔ mba hɔn bɔn ntsi, nkyii so mma wonnku mba wɔ egyanom hɔn bɔn ntsi: nyimpa biara nankasa no bɔn ntsi na wonku no.
Mma nndan ɔhɔho, anaa egyanka n’atsɛmbu enyi na nngye okunafo akataho ahoba: na kaa dɛ eyɛɛ akowaa wɔ Egypt, na EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn poon wo wɔ hɔ: dɛm ntsi na merehyɛ wo dɛ yɛ iyi yi.
Sɛ itwa wo ndɔbaa wɔ wo haban mu, na wo werɛ fir ifi bi wɔ haban no mu a, mma nnsan nnkɔ nnkɛfa mmba: ma ɔnyɛ ɔhɔho, egyanka, nye okunafo dze: na EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn eehyira wo wɔ wo nsaano edwuma nyinara mu.
Sɛ eporow wo ngodua a, mma nnkɔ n’abaw no do bio: ma dza aka no nyɛ ɔhɔho, egyanka, nye okunafo dze.
Sɛ etsew wo wenyin ture mu esikyireamba a, mma nnkedzi w’ekyir mpɛpɛw: ma ɔnyɛ ɔhɔho, egyanka, nye okunafo dze.
Na kaa dɛ eyɛɛ akowaa wɔ Egypt asaase do: dɛm ntsi na merehyɛ wo dɛ yɛ iyi yi.
Sɛ ɔham ba mbanyin ntamu, na wɔba asɛndzii, na ntsɛmbuafo rubua hɔn atsɛn a; ɔno wombu ɔtseneneenyi no bem, na wombu ɔdzebɔnyɛnyi no fɔ; na ɔmbra dɛ, sɛ ɔdzebɔnyɛnyi no sɛ hwe a, ɔtsɛmbuafo no mma ɔnda famu, na wɔnhwe no wɔ n’enyim, dodow dɛ mbrɛ no bɔn no tse.
Mbaa eduanan na ɔsɛ no a, mma ɔmmbor: ɔno bɛyɛ na sɛ ɔbor, na ɔhwe no mbaa pii sen iyi a, wo nua no adan w’enyi do ɔhorohoraanyi.
Mma nnkata ɔnantwi ano aber a oritsia ewu.
Onua Asodzii Wɔ Onua Ho Sɛ enuanom bɔ mu tsena, na hɔn mu baako wu, na onnyi ɔbabanyin a, mma owufo no ne yer nnkɔ ehuw mu nnkɔwar ɔhɔho: no kun no no nua na ɔnkɔ ne nkyɛn, na ɔmfa no nyɛ ne yer, na ɔnyɛ okun no nua asɛdze no mma no.
Na ɔmbra dɛ, abakan a ɔbɔwo no no nhyɛ no nua a oewu no ne dzin ananmu, na ne dzin aammpepa emmfi Israel.
Na sɛ ɔbanyin no mmpɛ dɛ ɔfa no nua yer no a, ɔno no nua ne yer no nkɔ mpanyimfo nkyɛn wɔ kuropon no ano, na ɔnse dɛ, Mo kun no nua pow dɛ ɔma dzin do ma no nua wɔ Israel, ɔmmpɛ dɛ ɔyɛ kun no nua asɛdze no ma me.
Ɔno no kurow no mu mpanyimfo no mfrɛ no, na wɔnkasa nkyerɛ no: na sɛ ogyina hɔ, na ɔse dɛ, Memmpɛ dɛ mefa no a; ɔno no nua ne yer no mbra ne nkyɛn wɔ mpanyimfo no enyim, onyi banyin no n’ananadze mpaboa na onhima n’enyi do ntafi; na ɔnse dɛ, Dɛm na wɔnyɛ ɔbanyin a ɔnnkyekyer no nua ne fi.
Na wɔmfrɛ ne dzin wɔ Israel dɛ, Nyia ne mpaboa efi n’ananadze no ne fi.
Sɛ mbanyin beenu roko, na ɔbaako ne yer twe bɛn dɛ ɔrebɛgye no kun efi nyia ɔrohwe no ne nsamu, na basia no tsen ne nsa suo banyin kor no ne banyin mu a: ɔno twa ɔbaa no ne nsa, mma w’enyi nnhu no mbɔbɔr.
Mma nnya wo foto mu abrambo ahorow, kɛse nye kakraba.
Mma nnya wo fi mu esusudze ahorow, kɛse nye kakraba.
Abrambo kwan mu a ɔtsen na nya; esusudze kwan mu a ɔtsen na nya: na wo nda aawar wɔ asaase a EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn dze rema wo no do.
Na hɔn a wɔyɛ dɛm ndzɛmba nyinara, mekyerɛ hɔn a wɔyɛ dza ɔmmfa kwan mu nyinara, yɛ ekyiwadze ma EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn.
Wɔnsɛɛ Amalek Kaa dza Amalek dze yɛɛ wo wɔ ɔkwan no mu aber a hom fi Egypt reba no; mbrɛ osii behyiaa wo wɔ ɔkwan no mu, na ɔbɔɔ w’ekyirfo, hɔn a wɔyɛ mberɛw wɔ w’ekyir nyinara, aber a atɔ bahaw na aberɛ; na oennsuro Nyankopɔn.
Dɛm ntsi ɔmbra dɛ, sɛ EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn ma wo ahomgye fi w’atamfo a woetwa wo ho ehyia nyinara nsamu wɔ asaase a EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn dze rema wo dɛ fa yɛ egyapadze no do a, pepa Amalek nkaa fi ɔsor ase; mma wo werɛ mmfir.
Nduadzewakan Afɔrbɔ Na ɔmbra dɛ, sɛ idu asaase a EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn dze rema wo dɛ egyapadze no do, na efa, na etsena do a; fa asaase no do nduadzewa a ibenya no wɔ asaase a EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn dze rema wo no do no, no nduadzewa a odzi kan no nyinara mu bi; na fa gu kɛntsɛn mu, na fa kɔ beebi mbrɛ EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn bɛsan mu eyi dɛ ne dzin ntsena hɔ no.
Na kɔ ɔsɔfo a ɔbɛtsena hɔ nda no mu no nkyɛn, na se no dɛ ndɛ da yi mepaa mu meka kyerɛ EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn, dɛ medu asaase a EWURADZE kaa ho ntam kyerɛɛ hɛn egyanom dɛ ɔdze rema hɛn no do.
Na ɔsɔfo no ngye kɛntsɛn no wɔ wo nsamu, na ɔmfa nsi EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn n’afɔrmbukyia no enyim.
Na bua na ka no wɔ EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn enyim dɛ, Sirianyi a ɔreyɛ ahera nye m’egya, na osianee kɔr Egypt, na ɔkɛtsenaa hɔ, ne nyimpa kumaabi; na ɔyɛɛ ɔman kɛse a wɔyɛ dzen, na wɔdɔree wɔ hɔ: na Egyptfo no yɛɛ hɛn bɔn, na wohiahiaa hɛnho, na wɔdze nkowaasom dzendzen too hɛn do: na yɛkekaa mu frɛɛ EWURADZE, hɛn egyanom Nyankopɔn, na EWURADZE tsiee hɛn ndze, na ohun hɛn ahohiahia, nye hɛn fona, nye hɛn su: na EWURADZE dze nsa a ɔyɛ dzen, nye abasa a wɔatserɛw mu, nye suro akɛse, nye nsɛnkyerɛdze, nye anwanwadze yii hɛn fii Egypt firii: na ɔdze hɛn aba bea yi do, na ɔdze asaase yi ama hɛn, asaase a numfonsu nye ewo pem wɔ do.
Na afei, hwɛ, medze asaase a ɔwo, EWURADZE, dze ama me no do nduadzewa a odzi kan no aba.
Na fa si EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn enyim, na sɔr wɔ EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn enyim: na gye w’enyi wɔ adzepa a EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn dze ama ɔwo, nye wo fi nyinara mu, ɔwo, nye Levinyi, nye ɔhɔho a ɔwɔ wo mu no.
Sɛ iwie wo ndɔbaa mu ebupɛn du du nyinara yiyi wɔ afe a otsia ebiasa no a ɔyɛ ebupɛn du du yiyi afe no mu a, ɔno fa ma Levinyi, nye ɔhɔho, nye egyanka, nye ekunafo, ma wondzi wɔ wo kuropon mu, mmee; na se wɔ EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn enyim dɛ, Meyi ndzɛmba krɔnkrɔn no efi me fie, na afei so medze ama Levinyi, nye ɔhɔho, nye egyanka, nye okunafo, dɛ mbrɛ wo mbrasɛm a edze ahyɛ me no nyinara tse monntoo wo mbransɛm mu biara, nkyii so mo werɛ mmfirii.
Minndzii bi wɔ m’eyiyɛ mu, nkyii so minnyii bi nnkyenee dɛ no ho nntsew ntsi, na memmfaa bi memmaa ewufo so: metsie EWURADZE me Nyankopɔn ndze, mayɛ dɛ mbrɛ edze ahyɛ me no nyinara.
Fi wo tsenabew krɔnkrɔn no, wɔ ɔsor, hwɛ famu, na hyira wo man Israel, nye asaase a edze ama hɛn no, dɛ mbrɛ ekaa ntam kyerɛɛ hɛn egyanom no, asaase a numfonsu nye ewo pem wɔ do no.
Ndɛ da yi EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn rehyɛ wo dɛ yɛ ahyɛdze nye atsɛmbu yi: dɛm ntsi fa w’akoma nyinara nye wo kra nyinara dzi do na yɛ.
Ndɛ da yi, aka ato gua dɛ edze EWURADZE bɛyɛ wo Nyankopɔn, na anantsew n’akwan mu, na edze n’ahyɛdze, nye ne mbransɛm, nye ne ntsɛmbu do, na etsie ne ndze: na EWURADZE aka ato gua ndɛ da yi dɛ ebɛyɛ nankasa no soronko man, dɛ mbrɛ ɔabɔ wo anohoba no, na eedzi ne mbransɛm nyinara do; na ɔaama wo do akyɛn amanaman a ɔayɛ nyinara, wɔ ayɛyi mu, nye dzin mu, nye enyidzi mu; na aayɛ ɔman krɔnkrɔn ama EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn, dɛ mbrɛ ɔaka no.
Mbra No Wɔ Abopon Do Na Moses nye Israel mpanyimfo no hyɛɛ ɔman no dɛ, Hom ndzi mbrasɛm a merehyɛ hom ndɛ da yi nyinara do.
Na ɔmbra dɛ, da a hom botwa Jordan akɔ asaase a EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn dze rema wo no do no, fa abo akɛse sisi hɔ, na fa ntarho tetar ho: na kyerɛw mbra yi mu nsɛm nyinara wɔ do, aber a etwa no; na aakɔ asaase a EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn dze rema wo no do, asaase a numfonsu nye ewo pem wɔ do no, dɛ mbrɛ EWURADZE, w’egyanom Nyankopɔn, abɔ wo anohoba no.
Na ɔmbra dɛ aber a hom etwa Jordan no, hom mfa abo yi a merehyɛ hom ndɛ da yi, nsisi hɔ wɔ bepɔw Ebal do, na fa ntarho tetar ho.
Na hɔ na si afɔrmbukyia ma EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn, abo afɔrmbukyia a: mma emma dadze edwindze do wɔ do.
Abo a wonntwae na fa si EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn afɔrmbukyia no: na bɔ ɔhyew afɔr wɔ do ma EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn: na bɔ asomdwee afɔr, na dzidzi wɔ hɔ; na gye w’enyi wɔ EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn enyim.
Na kyerɛw mbra yi mu nsɛm nyinara petee wɔ abo no do.
Na Moses nye Levifo asɔfo no kasaa kyerɛɛ Israel nyinara dɛ, Israel, hom nyɛ dzinn, na hom ntsie; ndɛ da yi abɛyɛ EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn ne man.
Dɛm ntsi tsie EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn ne ndze, na dzi ne mbransɛm na n’ahyɛdze a merehyɛ wo ndɛ da yi do.
Koko Ebal Do Mpaa Na Moses hyɛɛ ɔman no da no ara, dɛ, Iyinom na wongyina bepɔw Gerizim do nhyira ɔman no, aber a hom etwa Jordan no; Simeon, Levi, Juda, Isakar Josef, nye Benjamin: na iyinom ngyina bepɔw Ebal do mpaa; Reuben, Gad Aser, Zebulun, Dan, nye Naftali.
Na Levifo no mfa ndze kɛse ntsea mu, na wɔnse Israelfo no nyinara dɛ: Mpaa nka nyimpa a ɔbɛyɛ ohonyi a wɔasen anaa woegu, EWURADZE ekyiwadze, odwimfo nsaano edwuma, na ɔdze besi kokoa mu.
Na ɔman no nyinara mbua nse dɛ, Amen.
Mpaa nka nyia ɔyaw n’egya anaa ne na.
Na ɔman no nyinara nse dɛ, Amen.
Mpaa nka nyia ɔtwe ne nyɛnko n’asaasehe.
Na ɔman no nyinara nse dɛ, Amen.
Mpaa nka nyia ɔma onyifurafo fi ɔkwan do kyin.
Na ɔman no nyinara nse dɛ, Amen.
Mpaa nka nyia ɔdan ɔhɔho, egyanka, nye okunafo atsɛmbu enyi.
Na ɔman no nyinara nse dɛ, Amen.
Mpaa nka nyia ɔnye n’egya yer da; osiandɛ oeyi n’egya n’akataho.
Na ɔman no nyinara nse dɛ, Amen.
Mpaa nka nyia ɔnye abowa biara da.
Na ɔman no nyinara nse dɛ, Amen.
Mpaa nka nyia ɔnye n’akyerɛbaa da, n’egya ne babaa, anaa ne na ne babaa.
Na ɔman no nyinara nse dɛ, Amen.
Mpaa nka nyia ɔnye n’asew da.
Na ɔman no nyinara nse dɛ, Amen.
Mpaa nka nyia ɔbɔ ne nyɛnko adze nsumaa mu.
Na ɔman no nyinara nse dɛ, Amen.
Mpaa nka nyia ɔgye mboaba dɛ oboku nyimpa a odzi bem.
Na ɔman no nyinara nse dɛ, Amen.
Mpaa nka nyia ɔnnhyɛ mbra yi mu nsɛm dzen dɛ ɔbɛyɛ.
Na ɔman no nyinara nse dɛ, Amen.
Setsie Do Nhyira Na ɔbɛba dɛ, sɛ itsie EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn ne ndze yie, dɛ ebɔdwen do ayɛ ne mbransɛm a merehyɛ wo ndɛ da yi nyinara a, EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn bɛma wo do akɔ sor asen asaase do amanaman nyinara: na nhyira yi nyinara bɛba wo do, na wɔabɔto wo, osiandɛ itsie EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn ndze.
Nhyira bɛka wo wɔ kurow mu, na nhyira aka wo wɔ haban mu.
Nhyira bɛka wo honam mu aba, na w’asaase do aba, na wo fiembowa mu aba, w’anantwi ndɔree, nye wo nguankuw mu mburwa.
Nhyira bɛka wo kɛntsɛn nye wo mbɔrkorow.
Nhyira bɛka wo wɔ wo fie ba mu, na nhyira bɛka wo wɔ w’edzifir mu.
EWURADZE bɛma w’atamfo a wɔsoɛr wo do no edzi nkogu wɔ w’enyim: wɔnam ɔkwan kor do bɛba wo do, na wɔnam akwan esuon do eguan wɔ w’enyim.
EWURADZE bɛhyɛ ma nhyira aba wo do wɔ w’asan do, na dza edze wo nsa bɛka nyinara mu; na obehyira wo wɔ asaase a EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn dze rema wo no do.
Sɛ idzi EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn ne mbransɛm do, na enantsew n’akwan do a EWURADZE dze wo betsim hɔ ma aayɛ ɔman krɔnkrɔn ama noara, dɛ mbrɛ ɔaka ntam akyerɛ wo no.
Na asaase do aman nyinara bohu dɛ wɔdze EWURADZE dzin afrɛ wo; na wobosuro wo.
Na EWURADZE bɛma yie ebu wo do, wɔ wo honam mu aba mu, nye wo fiembowa aba mu, nye w’asaase aba mu, wɔ asaase a EWURADZE kaa ho ntam kyerɛɛ w’egyanom dɛ ɔdze bɛma wo no do.
EWURADZE bobue ɔsor n’adzepa korabea no ama wo na ɔaama w’asaase do nyankom atɔ wɔ n’aber mu, na oeehyira wo nsaano edwuma nyinara do: na edze bɛfɛm amanaman pii, na ɔwo remmfɛm.
sɛ itsie EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn ne mbransɛm a merehyɛ wo ndɛ da yi dɛ ebɔdwen do ayɛ a, EWURADZE bɛma akɔ kan na ennkɛka ekyir; na ɔwo bɔbɔ do ara nko, na eremmba ase.
Ne dɛm ntsi mma nndan mmfi nsɛm a merehyɛ wo ndɛ da yi ho, mmfa enyimfa, anaa abankum, nnkɔ nnkedzi enyame fofor ekyir nnkɔsom hɔn.
Asoɔdzen No Nsunsuando Na ɔbɛba dɛ, sɛ enntsie EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn ne ndze dɛ ebɔdwen do edzi ne mbransɛm nye n’ahyɛdze a merehyɛ wo ndɛ da yi nyinara do a; mpaa yi nyinara bɛba wo do, na wɔabɛmen wo.
Mpaa bɛka wo wɔ kurow mu, na mpaa aka wo wɔ haban mu.
Mpaa bɛka wo kɛntsɛn, nye wo mbɔrkorow.
Mpaa bɛka wo honam mu aba, nye w’asaase mu aba, nye w’anantwi mu ndɔree, nye wo nguankuw mu mburwa.
Mpaa bɛka wo wɔ wo fie ba mu, na mpaa bɛka wo wɔ w’edzifir mu.
EWURADZE bɛma mpaa, nkogu, nye adapaabɔ aba wo do, wɔ dza edze wo nsa bɛka ayɛ nyinara mu, dze ekodu dɛ ebɛsɛɛ, na ayew ntsɛm; osian wo ndzeyɛɛ a enam do apow me ntsi.
EWURADZE bɛma ɔyardɔm afam wo ho, dze ekodu dɛ ɔahyew wo efi asaase a erokɔ do akɛfa no do.
EWURADZE dze asasawaw, nye etsiridii, nye ahohur, nye ahohyehye kɛse, nye nkrantsee, nye ɔhow, nye ɔpo bɔbɔ wo; na wobetsiw wo araa ekodu dɛ ebɛsɛɛ.
Na ɔsor bɛyɛ dɛ boran ama wo, na asaase adan dadze ama wo.
EWURADZE bɛma etudur na huntuma atɔ dɛ nsu egu wo do araa ekodu dɛ wɔbɛsɛɛ wo.
EWURADZE bɛma edzi w’atamfo enyim ɔkogu: enam ɔkwan kor do befir edzi ekehyia hɔn, na enam akwan esuon do eguan wɔ hɔn enyim: na wobedzi wo akɔnaaba wɔ asaase do ahendzi nyinara mu.
Na wo fun bɛyɛ wimu ntumbowa nyinara, nye asaase do mbowa edziban, na obiara rennka hɔn.
EWURADZE dze Egypt pɔmpɔ, tukuruw, satwem, nye ntwem a worunntum wo eduyɛ bɔbobɔ wo.
EWURADZE dze abɔdam, nye enyifura, nye akoma mu ahodwuruw bɔbɔ wo; na ebɛkeka ewiaber ketee, dɛ ofurafo rekeka wɔ sum mu, na w’akwan mu rennyɛ wo yie: na ɔhyɛ nko na wɔbɛhyɛ wo na wɔafow wo dabaa, na obiara renngye wo.
Ebɛgye ayewar, na ɔbanyin fofor bi nye no ada: ibesi dan, na erenntsena mu: ebɛtsɛw wenyin ture, na erenntsew n’aba bi.
Woboku wo nantwi wɔ w’enyim, na irinndzi bi: wɔbɛfa w’asoaso enyimpi do wɔ w’enyim, na wɔrenndan mma wo: wɔdze wo nguan bɛma w’atamfo na innkenya obi ma ɔaagye wo.
Wɔdze wo mbabanyin nye wo mbabaa bɛma ɔman fofor bi na w’enyiwa bɔhwɛ, na hɔn ho enyigyinae egura wo daa nyinara: na tum biara nnyi wo nsamu.
W’asaase do aba, nye w’edwumadze nyinara, na ɔman a innyim hɔn bedzi; na ɔhyɛ nko na wɔbɛhyɛ wo na wɔadwerew wo dabaa: dɛm ntsi w’enyiwa do adze a ibohu no bɔbɔ wo dam.
EWURADZE dze pɔmpɔ bɔn bɔbɔ wo wɔ anankoroma, nye aserɛ do a worunntum wo eduyɛ, efi w’ananadze ekodu w’etsifipampamu.
EWURADZE dze ɔwo, nye wo hen a ibesi no wo do no, bɔkɔ ɔman a ɔwo nye w’egyanom nnyim no mu; na hɔ na ebɔsom enyame fofor, ndua nye abo.
Na ebɛdan ahodwuruwdze, akasabɛbu, nye ifen, wɔ aman a EWURADZE bɛma akɔ no nyinara mu.
Ebɔsoa aba pii akɔ haban mu, na kakrabaabi na ebɔboa ano aba fie; na mbɛbɛw bedzi.
Ebɛtsetsɛw wenyin nture na esiesie mu, na ne nsa dze eronnom, na erenntsew esikyireamba no so; na mbowaba bedzi.
Ibenya ngodua wɔ wo ntoado nyinara, na ngo no dze erennsera woho bi; na wo ngodua no bɔporow n’aba.
Ebɔwo mbabanyin nye mbabaa, na wɔrennyɛ wodze; na wɔbɔkɔ ndɔmmum mu.
Wo ndua nyinara nye w’asaase do aba no mbɛbɛw bɛfa.
Ɔhɔho a ɔwɔ wo mu bɛkyɛn wo akɔ sorsorsor; na ɔwo dze ibesian aba famufamu.
Ɔno na ɔdze bɛfɛm wo, na ɔwo dze, irinnya mmfɛm no: ɔno na ɔbɔkɔ kan, na ɔwo aka ekyir.
Na mpaa yi nyinara bɛba wo do, na woetsiw wo, na wɔamen wo, ekodu dɛ ebɛsɛɛ; osiandɛ enntsie EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn ndze, dɛ ibedzi ne mbransɛm nye n’ahyɛdze a ɔhyɛ wo no do: na ɔbɛyɛ asɛnkyerɛdze nye anwanwadze, wɔ ɔwo nye w’asefo do daa: osiandɛ ammfa enyigye, nye akoma pa annsom EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn, wɔ adze nyinara no dodow mu ntsi: dɛm ntsi ebɔsom w’atamfo a EWURADZE bɔsoma hɔn ma wɔaaba wo do no, wɔ ɔkɔm, nsukɔm, adagyaw, nye ndzɛmba nyinara ho hia mu: na ɔdze dadze kɔndua bɔto wo kɔn do, ekodu dɛ ɔbɛsɛɛ wo.
EWURADZE dze ɔman bi befi ekyirekyir efi asaase ano aba wo do, dɛ mbrɛ ɔkɔr tu; ɔman a enntse hɔn kasaa; ɔman a hɔn enyim yɛ hu a wɔmmfɛr akɔdaa enyim, na wɔnnkyerɛ enyimtsewee wɔ aberantsɛ do so: na obedzi wo fiembowa mu aba, na w’asaase do aba, ekodu dɛ wɔbɛsɛɛ wo: eso orinngya wo eburow, nsa, anaa ngo, w’anantwi mu ndɔree, anaa wo nguankuw mu mburwa, ekodu dɛ ɔbɛma asɛe.
Na ɔbɔkɔ wo ntua wɔ wo nkuropon nyinara mu, ekodu dɛ w’afasu atsentsen a ɔyɛ dzen no a edze wo werɛ hyɛ mu no bodwuruw egu famu, wɔ w’asaase nyina do: na ɔbɔkɔ wo ntua wɔ wo nkuropon nyinara a ɔwɔ w’asaase a EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn dze ama wo no nyinara do.
Na ibedzi woara wo honam mu aba, wo mbabanyin nye wo mbabaa a EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn dze ama wo no hɔn nam; wɔ ntua nye ahokyer a w’atamfo bɛma wo ho akyer wo no mu.
Ɔbanyin a ɔdwe na ɔwɔ tsema wɔ hom mu no n’enyiwa bɛyɛ bɔn wɔ no nua, nye ne yer a ɔda no bo mu, nye ne mba nkaa a wɔama wɔaka no ho: dɛ ɔremma hɔn mu biara ne mba nam a oridzi no bi, osiandɛ biribiara annka amma no; wɔ ntua nye ahokyer a wo tamfo bɛma wo ho akyer wo wɔ wo nkuropon nyinara mu no mu.
Hom mu ɔbaa so a ɔdwe na ɔsonsɔn no ho na ɔnam mberɛwyɛ ntsi ɔnnsɔe nnhwɛɛ pɛn dɛ ɔdze n’ananadze bɛka famu no, bɛyɛ nyimpa bɔn wɔ no kun a ɔda no bo mu, nye ne babanyin, nye ne babaa ho; na ɔbɔwe ne mba a ɔbɔwo hɔn no nye ekyiradze no wɔ nsumaa mu: wɔ ahohia a ofi ntua nye ahokyer a wo tamfo bɛma aba wo do wɔ wo nkuropon mu no ntsi.
Sɛ eronndwen do nnyɛ mbra yi mu nsɛm nyinara a wɔakyerɛw no wɔ nwoma yi mu, na ennsuro enyimnyam dzin a no ho yɛ hu yi, EWURADZE WO NYANKOPƆN no a, ɔno EWURADZE bɛma wo yardɔm, nye w’asefo yardɔm ayɛ nwanwa; mekyerɛ ɔyardɔm akɛse a ɔkyɛr, nye yarba bɔn a ɔkyɛr.
Na ɔdze Egypt yarba no a isuro no nyinara bɛba wo do bio; na ɔabɛfemfam wo ho.
Eso yarba biara, nye ɔyardɔm biara a wɔnnkyerɛɛw no wɔ mbra yi no nwoma mu no, ɔno na EWURADZE dze bɛba wo do, ekodu dɛ wɔbɛsɛɛ wo.
Na ɔbɛka hom nyimpa kakrabaabi, naaso nna nkyɛ hom dodow tse dɛ ɔsor nworaba; osiandɛ hom enntsie EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn ne ndze.
Na ɔbɛba dɛ, dɛ mbrɛ EWURADZE n’enyi gye hom ho dɛ ɔbɛyɛ hom yie, na ɔama hom adɔr no; dɛmara so na EWURADZE n’enyi bɛgye hom ho dɛ ɔbɛma hom ase etu, na ɔasɛɛ hom: na wɔbɛpempan hom efi asaase a hom rokɔ do akɛfa no do.
Na EWURADZE bɔbɔ wo apetse aman nyinara mu, efi asaase ano kor araa ekodu asaase ano kor so; na hɔ na ebɔsom enyame fofor a ɔwo nye w’egyanom nnyim hɔn, mekyerɛ ndua nye abo.
Na amanaman iyinom mu irinnya ahotɔ, na w’ananadze rinnya ahomgye: na EWURADZE bɛma wo ahopopo akoma, nye enyiwa a ayɛ siamoo, nye ɔkra a etwintwam wɔ hɔ: na wo nkwa bɛsɛn ehihim wɔ w’enyim; na ibosuro adzesaa nye adzekyee, na irinnya wo nkwa ho gyedzi biara: anapa ebɛse dɛ, Kɛtseankyɛ ewimbir a: na ewimbir so ebɛse dɛ, Kɛtseankyɛ anapa a: wɔ w’akoma mu suro a ibosuro, nye w’enyiwa do adze a ibohu no ntsi.
Na EWURADZE dze ahɛn dze wo bɛsan akɔ Egypt, wɔ ɔkwan a mekaa wo ho asɛm dɛ irunnhu bio no do: na hɔ na hom bɔtontɔn homho ama hom atamfo ayɛ nkowaa nye mfonabaa, na nyimpa biara ronntɔ hom.
EWURADZE Nye Israel Dzi Ahyɛmu Wɔ Moab Iyi nye ahyɛmu a EWURADZE hyɛɛ Moses dɛ ɔnye Israelmba ndzi wɔ Moab asaase do, nka ahyɛmu a ɔnye hɔn dzii wɔ Horeb no ho no, no mu nsɛm.
Na Moses frɛɛ Israel nyinara, na ɔsee hɔn dɛ, Hom ehu adze nyinara a EWURADZE dze yɛɛ Farao, nye no nkowaa nyinara, nye n’asaase nyinara, wɔ hom enyiwa mu, wɔ Egypt asaase do; nsɔhwɛ akɛse a w’enyiwa hunii, nsɛnkyerɛdze, nye anwanwadze akɛse no: naaso obodu ndɛ da yi, EWURADZE mmaa wo dɛm akoma a onyim dze, enyiwa a wɔdze hwɛ, nye asowa a wɔdze tsie.
Na medzi hom enyim ma hom anantsew mfe eduanan wɔ sar no do; hom ntar nnsuwii wɔ hom ho, na wo mpaboa nntsetsewee wɔ w’ananadze.
Hom nndzii paanoo, nkyii so hom nnoom wenyin anaa nsa dzendzen: ama hom eehu dɛ emi nye EWURADZE hom Nyankopɔn.
Na aber a hom dur bea yi do no, Hesbonhen Sihon, nye Basenhen Ɔge, fiir edzi baa hɛn do nye hɛn bɔkoe, na yekum hɔn; na yɛfaa hɔn asaase, na yɛdze maa Reubenfo, nye Gadfo, nye Manaasɛfo ebusuakuw ɔfa no, dɛ egyapadze.
Dɛm ntsi hom ndzi ahyɛmu yi mu nsɛm do, na hom nyɛ, na hom aayɛ prɔmprɔm wɔ dza hom yɛ nyinara mu.
Ndɛ da yi hom nyinara hom ngyina EWURADZE hom Nyankopɔn enyim; hom etsitsir, hom ebusuakuw ebusuakuw, hom mpanyimfo, nye hom ahwɛdofo, mekyerɛ Israel mbanyin nyinara, hom mbofraba, hom yernom, nye wo hɔhoe a ɔwɔ wo nseraban mu, ofi wo duatwafo do dze kodu wo nsusawfo do: ama aahɛn EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn n’ahyɛmu, nye ne nsew a Ɔnye wo ridzi ndɛ da yi mu: ama ɔdze wo eesi hɔ ndɛ da yi dɛ ɔman ama noho, na ɔno so aayɛ Nyankopɔn ama wo, dɛ mbrɛ ɔkaa kyerɛɛ wo, na dɛ mbrɛ ɔkaa ntam kyerɛɛ w’egyanom, Abraham, Isaak, nye Jakob no.
Nkyii so nnyɛ hom nko na menye hom ridzi ahyɛmu yi nye nsew yi: mbom menye nyia ɔnye hɛn gyina EWURADZE hɛn Nyankopɔn enyim ha ndɛ da yi, na eso menye nyia ɔnnye hɛn nnyi ha ndɛ da yi: Na hom nhwɛ yie amma hom mu ɔbanyin bi, anaa ɔbaa bi, anaa ebusua bi, anaa ebusuakuw bi n’akoma anndan ndɛ da yi emmfi EWURADZE hɛn Nyankopɔn ho, dɛ ɔrokɔ akɔsom amanaman no hɔn enyame no: na ndwow bi aammba hom mu a ɔsow bɔr nye ɔbɔwen; na aammba dɛ, sɛ ɔtse mpaa yi mu nsɛm a, oeennhyira noho wɔ n’akoma mu, dɛ, mibenya asomdwee, kaansa menam m’akoma no sorow mu mpo a, amma wɔaannsɛɛ dza afɔw annka dza awow ho.
EWURADZE remmfa nnkyɛ no, na mbom EWURADZE n’ebufuw nye ne nyinkuntwe bopun nyimpa no, na mpaa a wɔakyerɛw no wɔ nwoma yi mu no nyinara bodwir no do, na EWURADZE bɛpepa ne dzin efi asaase do.
Na EWURADZE beyi no efi Israel ebusuakuw nyinara mu esi hɔ ama mbusu, dɛ mbrɛ ahyɛmu a wɔakyerɛw no wɔ mbra nwoma yi mu mpaa no tse nyinara.
Na ebusuasantsen a wɔbɛba no, hom mba a wɔbɔsoɛr edzi hom ekyir no, nye ɔnanaben a ofi ekyirekyir asaase do bɛba no, sɛ wohu asaase no do yardɔm, nye nyarbanyarba a EWURADZE dze ama wɔayar no a, wɔbɛse dɛ; n’asaase nyinara ayɛ sɔɔfee nye nkyen, nye nkyewee, wonndua do adze, ɔnnsow, nkyɛkyɛr mpo mmfir do, ɔtse dɛ Sodom nye Gomora, Adma nye Zeboim mbutuwii a EWURADZE nam n’ebufuw nye n’ebufuhyew mu butuwii no: mekyerɛ amanaman nyinara bɛse dɛ, Ebɛnadze ntsi na EWURADZE ayɛ asaase yi dɛm yi?
Ebufuw kɛse hyeehyew yi ase nye dɛn?
Nna nkorɔfo bɛse dɛ, Osiandɛ wɔpoow EWURADZE, hɔn egyanom Nyankopɔn ahyɛmu a oyii hɔn wɔ Egypt asaase do no ɔnye hɔn dzii no; na wɔkɔree kɔsoom enyame fofor, na wɔsɔɔr hɔn, enyame a wonnyim hɔn, na ɔammfa hɔn amma hɔn: dɛm ntsi na EWURADZE ebufuw dzɛwee wɔ asaase yi do, ma ɔdze mpaa a wɔakyerɛw no wɔ nwoma yi mu nyinara aba do; na EWURADZE tutuu hɔn ase fii hɔn asaase do wɔ ebufuw, nye ebufuhyew, nye ahohyehye kɛse mu, na wɔatow hɔn egu asaase bi so do, dɛ mbrɛ ɔtse ndɛ da yi.
Ndzɛmba a osuma yɛ EWURADZE hɛn Nyankopɔn dze: na ndzɛmba a wɔada no edzi no dze ɔyɛ hɛn nye hɛn mba dze daa, ama yeedzi mbra yi mu nsɛm nyinara do.
Nnuho Ho Ekyir Nhyira Na ɔbɛba dɛ, sɛ ndzɛmba iyinom nyinara ba wo do, nhyira nye mpaa a, medze esi w’enyim yi, na ekaakaa no wɔ amanaman nyinara mu mbrɛ EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn apam wo akɔ no, na sɛ ɔwo, nye wo mba san ba EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn nkyɛn, na edze w’akoma nyinara, na ɔnye wo kra nyinara tsie ne ndze na eyɛ dza merehyɛ wo ndɛ da yi nyinara a; ɔno na EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn bɛdan wo ndɔmmumkɔ no, na oenya ayamuhyehye ama wo, na ɔasan aboa w’ano efi aman a ɔnoara EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn abɔ wo apetse mu no nyinara mu.
Sɛ wo nyimpa a wɔapam hɔn no bi wɔ ɔsor ano no ho mpo a, ofitsi hɔ na EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn bɔboa w’ano, na hɔ na ɔbɛfa wo efi: na EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn dze wo bɛba asaase a w’egyanom nyaa no do, na aafa; na ɔbɛyɛ wo yie, na ɔama adɔr akyɛn w’egyanom.
Na EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn bɛma ɔwo nye w’asefo akoma, a ɔdwe, na edze w’akoma nye wo kra nyinara, aadɔ EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn, na eenya nkwa.
Na EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn dze mpaa yi nyinara bogu w’atamfo, nye hɔn a wokyir wo a wohiahia wo ho no do.
Na ɔwo dze, ebɛsan ebetsie EWURADZE ndze, na edzi ne mbransɛm a merehyɛ wo ndɛ da yi nyinara do.
Na EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn bɛma yie ebu wo do wɔ wo nsaano edwuma nyinara mu, wɔ wo honam mu aba mu, nye wo fiembowa aba mu, nye w’asaase do aba mu, wɔ wo yieyɛ ntsi: na EWURADZE n’enyi bɛsan agye wo ho wɔ wo yieyɛ ntsi, dɛ mbrɛ n’enyi gyee w’egyanom ho no: sɛ ibetsie EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn ndze, dɛ ibedzi ne mbransɛm nye n’ahyɛdze a wɔakyerɛw no wɔ mbra nwoma yi mu no do, dɛ edze w’akoma nyinara, na ɔnye wo kra nyinara bɛsan aba EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn nkyɛn a. Na mbrasɛm yi a merehyɛ wo ndɛ da yi, ɔnnyɛ dzendzen dodow mma wo, nkyii so onnyi ekyirekyir.
Onnyi sor, na aase dɛ, Woana na ɔbɔfow akɔ sor ama hɛn, na ɔakɛfa abrɛ hɛn, na ɔama yɛatse, na yɛayɛ.
Nkyii so onnyi po n’egya, na aase dɛ, Woana na obotwa po ama hɛn, na ɔakɛfa abrɛ hɛn, na ɔama yɛatse, ma yaayɛ.
Na asɛm no bɛn wo dodoodow, ɔwɔ w’anomu, na ɔwɔ w’akoma mu, ama aayɛ.
Hwɛ, ndɛ da yi medze nkwa nye papa, nye owu nye bɔn, esi w’enyim; wɔ dɛ merehyɛ wo ndɛ da yi dɛ dɔ EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn, nantsew n’akwan do, na dzi ne mbransɛm nye n’ahyɛdze nye ne ntsɛmbu do, na aatsena ase na aadɔr, na EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn ehyira wo wɔ asaase a erokɔ do akɛfa no do.
Mbom sɛ w’akoma dan, na enntsie, na ema wɔtwe wo kɔ, na ekɔsɔr enyame fofor, na esom hɔn a; mepaa mu meka kyerɛ hom ndɛ da yi, dɛ ɔsɛɛ na hom bɛsɛɛ; na hom remma hom nda nnwar wɔ asaase mbrɛ irutwa Jordan akɔ do akɛfa no do.
Mefrɛ ɔsor nye asaase dɛ wondzi hom dase ndɛ da yi, dɛ medze nkwa nye owu, nhyira nye mpaa esi w’enyim: dɛm ntsi fa nkwa, ma ɔwo, nye w’asefo nnya nkwa: na dɔ EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn, tsie ne ndze, na takyer no ho: na ɔno nye wo nkwa, nye wo nda ne tsentsen: ama aatsena asaase a EWURADZE kaa ho ntam kyerɛɛ w’egyanom, Abraham, Isaak, nye Jakob dɛ ɔdze bɛma hɔn no do.
Josua Si Moses N’ananmu Na Moses kɔree kɛkaa asɛm yi kyerɛɛ Israel nyinara.
Na ɔsee hɔn dɛ, Ndɛ yi, medzi mfe ɔha eduonu; emi a munntum nnkɔ, emi so a munntum mmba: na eso EWURADZE ase me dɛ, Irunntwa Jordan yi.
EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn, ɔno na odzi w’enyim rukotwa; ɔno na ɔbɛsɛɛ amanaman yi efi w’enyim, na afa hɔn: na Josua na oridzi w’enyim ekotwa, dɛ mbrɛ EWURADZE aka no.
Na EWURADZE bɛyɛ hɔn dɛ mbrɛ ɔyɛɛ Amorifo ahemfo, Sihon nye Ɔge a ɔsɛɛ hɔn, nye hɔn asaase no.
EWURADZE beyi hɔn ama wɔ hom enyim, na hom ayɛ hɔn dɛ mbrɛ mbransɛm a mahyɛ hom nyinara tse.
Hom nhyɛ dzen na hom nnya akokodur, mma hom nnsuro, mma hɔn ho nnyɛ hom hu so; na EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn no, ɔno na ɔnye wo rokɔ, ɔremmpa wo, na ɔrommpow wo so.
Na Moses frɛɛ Josua, na ɔsee no wɔ Israel nyinara enyim dɛ, Hyɛ dzen na nya akokodur; na ɔwo na edze ɔman yi bɔkɔ asaase a EWURADZE aka ho ntam akyerɛ hɔn egyanom dɛ ɔdze bɛma hɔn no do; na ɔwo na ebɛma woenya edzi.
Na EWURADZE, ɔno nye nyia oridzi w’enyim akɔ; obedzi w’ekyir, ɔremmpa wo, nkyii so ɔrommpow wo; mma nnsuro, nkyii so mma w’akoma nntu.
Mfe Esuon Biara Wɔnkenkan Mbra No Na Moses kyerɛɛw mbra yi, na ɔdze maa asɔfo Levi mbabanyin no a wɔsoa EWURADZE ahyɛmudaka no, nye Israel mpanyimfo nyinara.
Na Moses hyɛɛ hɔn dɛ, Mfe esuon biara n’ewiei, akwangya afe n’aber a wɔahyɛ no mu, ntamadan afahyɛ no mu, aber a Israel nyinara rubopue wɔ EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn enyim wɔ beebi mbrɛ ɔbɛsan mu eyi no, kenkan mbra yi wɔ Israel nyinara enyim ma wɔntse.
Boaboa ɔman no ano, mbanyin nye mbaa nye mbofraba, nye wo hɔhoe a ɔwɔ wo nkuropon mu, ma wontsie, na wonsua, na wonsuro EWURADZE hom Nyankopɔn, na wɔndwen do ndzi mbra yi mu nsɛm nyinara do; na hɔn mba a wonnyim no ntsie, na wonsua dɛ wonsuro EWURADZE hom Nyankopɔn, aber tsentsen nyina a hom tse asaase no do mbrɛ hom rukotwa Jordan akɛfa no.
EWURADZE Ka Asoɔdzen A Israel Bɛyɛ No Ho Asɛm Na EWURADZE see Moses dɛ, Hwɛ, wo nda a ibowu abɛn: frɛ Josua, na wonkeyi homho nkyerɛ wɔ ehyiadzibuw no mu, ma menhyɛ no mbra.
Na Moses nye Josua kɔree, na wokeyii hɔnho kyerɛe wɔ ehyiadzibuw no mu.
Na EWURADZE nam mununkum dum mu yii noho edzi wɔ Buw no mu: na mununkum dum no begyinaa Buw no n’abowano.
Na EWURADZE see Moses dɛ, Hwɛ, ɔwo, iribetsiw wo nananom wɔ samanadze na ɔman yi bɔsoɛr, na woekedzi asaase no do enyame ekyir wɔ ndwamangor mu, wɔ mbrɛ wɔrokɔ akɔforafora hɔn mu no, na wɔbɔpow me na wɔato m’ahyɛmu a menye hɔn edzi no.
Ɔno na m’ebufuw bɛdzɛw wɔ hɔn do wɔ da no mu, na mapow hɔn, na medze m’enyim esuma hɔn, na wɔamen hɔn, na mbusu nye ɔfona pii bɛba hɔn do; ama wɔaaka wɔ da no mu dɛ, Ana nnyɛ hɛn Nyankopɔn a onnyi hɛn mu ntsi na mbusu yi aba hɛn do bi a?
Na suma ara na medze m’enyim mubosuma wɔ da no mu wɔ mbusu a wɔabɔ no nyinara ntsi, wɔ dɛ wɔadan akɔ enyame fofor nkyɛn ntsi.
Dɛm ntsi afei hom nkyerɛw ndwom yi mma hom ho, na fa kyerɛkyerɛ Israelmba: fa hyɛ hɔn anomu, ma ndwom yi ndzi me dase ntsia Israelmba.
Na sɛ minya dze hɔn du asaase a mekaa ho ntam kyerɛɛ hɔn egyanom no a numfonsu nye ewo pem wɔ do no do a wobedzidzi amee, na wɔayɛ abran.
Ɔno nna afei wɔbɛdan akɔ enyame fofor nkyɛn, na wɔakɔsom hɔn, na woebu me enyimtsia, na wɔato m’ahyɛmu.
Na ɔbɛba dɛ, aber a mbusu nye ɔfona pii aba hɔn do no, ndwom yi bɛyɛ dɛ ɔdasefo edzi dase wɔ hɔn enyim; osiandɛ ɔnnkɛpa hɔn asefo anomu: na minyim hɔn adwendwen a wɔrodwendwen no seseiara mpo, ansaana medze hɔn bodu asaase a mekaa ho ntam no do.
Nna Moses kyerɛɛw ndwom yi da no ara, na ɔdze kyerɛkyerɛɛ Israelmba.
Na ɔhyɛɛ Nun ne babanyin Josua mbra, na ɔsee dɛ, Hyɛ dzen na nya akokodur: na ɔwo na edze Israelmba bɔkɔ asaase a mekaa ho ntam kyerɛɛ hɔn no do; na mibedzi w’ekyir.
Moses Dze Mbra No Hyɛ Levifo Nsa Na ɔbaa dɛ aber a Moses wiee mbra yi mu nsɛm kyerɛw wɔ nwoma mu no, Moses hyɛɛ Levifo a wɔsoa EWURADZE n’ahyɛmudaka no, dɛ, Hom mfa mbra nwoma yi, na hom mfa nto EWURADZE hom Nyankopɔn n’ahyɛmudaka no ho, ma ɔnko hɔ nyɛ dase ntsia hom.
Na minyim hom etuatsew, nye hom asoɔdzen: hwɛ, meda ho ara menye hom tse ase ndɛ da yi mpo, na hom ayɛ etuatsewfo wɔ EWURADZE do yi; na afei mo wu ekyir ɛ?
Hom mboaboa hom ebusuakuw ebusuakuw mu mpanyimfo nyinara, nye hom ahwɛdofo ano mbra me nkyɛn, ma menka nsɛm yi wɔ hɔn aso mu, na memfrɛ ɔsor nye asaase ma wondzi hɔn dase.
Na minyim dɛ mo wu ekyir no ɔsɛɛ na hom bɛsɛɛ homho, na hom adan efi ɔkwan a mahyɛ hom no do; na mbusu bɛba hom do nda a odzi ekyir no mu; osiandɛ hom bɛyɛ dza omuo wɔ EWURADZE enyi do, dze nam hom nsaano edwuma do eyi no ebufuw.
Na Moses kaa ndwom yi mu nsɛm wɔ Israel bagua no nyinara asomu dze kodur dɛ owiei.
Moses No Ndwom Ɔsor, hom nyɛ aso, na merebɛkasa; Na wɔmma asaase ntsie m’anomu nsɛm: Me nkyerɛkyerɛ bɔsosɔ dɛ nyankom, Me kasaa bogugu dɛ ɔbɔsu; Dɛ nkyɛkyɛr do nsumpetsema, Nye haban do nsutɔree: Na mobɔbɔ EWURADZE dzin akyerɛ: Hom mfa kɛseyɛ mma hɛn Nyankopɔn, Ɔbotan no, n’edwuma dzi mu; Na n’akwan nyinara yɛ atsɛmbu: Nyankopɔn nokwardzifo a, na onnyi emumuyɛ, Ɔyɛ pɛrpɛr na ɔtsen.
Woedzi no asɛmbɔn, wɔnnyɛ ne mba, hɔn dzɛmdzi a; Ebusuasantsen kɔntɔnkye a wɔakyea a. Ana EWURADZE na hom nye no dzi no dɛm yi, Ɔman nkwasea a wɔnnyɛ enyansafo?
Ana nnyɛ ɔno nye w’egya a ɔawo wo bi a?
Ɔno na ɔayɛ wo na oetsintsim wo.
Kaa tsetsentserdee nda no, Dwen ebusuasantsen pii no hɔn mfe ho: Bisa w’egya, na ɔnkyerɛ wo; Wo mpanyimfo, na wɔnka nkyerɛ wo.
Aber a Ɔsorsornyi no memaa amanaman hɔn egyapadze no, Aber a ɔpaapaa nyimpa mba mu no, Osisii aman hɔn ahe Dɛ mbrɛ Israelmba hɔn dodow tse.
Na EWURADZE ne kyɛfa nye ne man; Jakob nye n’egyapadze kyɛfa.
Ohun no wɔ sar asaase do, Na kwaa tuntum sar predede do nkekabowa mu; Otwaa no ho hyiae, ɔhwɛɛ no do yie, Ɔkoraa no do dɛ n’enyiwa kyesua: Dɛ mbrɛ ɔkɔr huenyan ne birebuw, Na otu bɔ ne ba do faafaa no, Ɔtserɛɛw ne ntsaban mu faa hɔn no, Ɔsoaa hɔn wɔ ne ntɛkyerɛ do: EWURADZE nkotoo na ogyaa no Na onyame fofor bi annka no ho, Ɔmaa ɔfaa asaase mbea sorɔnsorɔm do tutui kɔree, Na odzii haban mu ndɔbaa; Na ɔmaa ohwieew ewo fii ɔbotan mu, Nye ngo fii ɔtwerɛbo botan mu; Anantwi numfonsungo, nye nguan numfonsu, Nye nguambaa seradze, Nye Basan nnyɛmbowa mu nguannyin, nye mpɔnkye, Nye ewifua ntan mu seradze; Na enoom esikyireamba mu bɔgya wenyin.
Na Jesurun yɛɛ ɔbran, na ɔtoow ntsia: Ayɛ bran, ayɛ kɛse, wo mu ayɛ dur: Nna ɔpoow Nyankopɔn a ɔyɛɛ no no, Na obuu no nkwagye botan no tootooba.
Wɔdze enyame nanaben yii no nyinkun, Wɔdze ekyiwadze yii no ebufuw.
Wɔbɔɔ afɔr maa abosom a wɔnnyɛ Nyame, Dze maa enyame a wonnyim hɔn, Dze maa enyame fofor a wɔbaa nkyinkyirii, Dza hom egyanom ennsuro hɔn no.
Ɔbotan a ɔwoo wo no anndwen no ho, Na wo werɛ efir Nyame a ɔkyeem wo no.
Na EWURADZE hunii, na okyiir hɔn, Wɔ ne mbabanyin nye ne mbabaa ho ehi ntsi.
Na ɔsee dɛ, Mibeyi m’enyim esuma hɔn, Mobɔhwɛ mbrɛ hɔn ewiei bɛyɛ: Na wɔyɛ ebusuasantsen kɔntɔnkye, Mba a hɔn mu nnyi gyedzi.
Wɔdze dza ɔnnyɛ Onyame eyi me nyinkun: Wɔdze hɔn egyangyandze eyi me ebufuw: Na medze hɔn a wɔnnyɛ ɔman biara no mibeyi hɔn nyinkun; Medze ɔman nkwasea bi mibeyi hɔn ebufuw.
Na ogya adzɛw wɔ m’ebufuw mu, Na ɔrehyew ekodu samanadze ase, Na ɔremen asaase nye no ndɔbaa, Na ɔato mbepɔw mfapem mu ogya.
Mobɔboa mbusu ano megu hɔn do; Mobɔhwer m’egyen menaba wɔ hɔn do: Ɔkɔm bɔfɔn hɔn, na ahohyehye yaayaw Nye ɔsɛɛ wenwen bɛmen hɔn; Na mobɔsoma mbowa se ma wɔaaba hɔn do, Nye huntuma mu nweaweambowa bɔr.
Abɔntsen do na nkrantsee bohwim, Adankyir so nketsenketse a; Ɔbɛsɛɛ aberantsɛ nye ɔbaabun nyina, Enumfoanoba nye nyimpa a oefuw gon nyina.
Mesee dɛ nkyɛ mobɔbɔ hɔn apetse ekyirekyir, Nkyɛ mebɛma hɔn nkaa tun do etwa efi nyimpa mu: Sɛ nnyɛ ɔtamfo ehiyi na musuroi a, Bɛyɛ na hɔn ayɛfo anntse m’akwan ase, Bɛyɛ na wɔase dɛ, Hɛn nsa na akrɔn, Na nnyɛ EWURADZE na ɔayɛ iyi nyinara.
Na wɔyɛ aman a egyinatu abɔ hɔn, Na ntseasee bi nnyi hɔn mu.
Ao kɛtseankyɛ woeehu nyansa, na wɔaatse iyi ase, Na nkyɛ wɔaadwen hɔn ewiei ekyir no ho!
Ɔbaako bɛyɛ dɛn etsiw apem, Na beenu aka mpemdu egu, Gyedɛ hɔn Ɔbotan atɔn hɔn ana, Na EWURADZE eyi hɔn ama ana?
Na hɔn ɔbotan nntse dɛ hɛn Ɔbotan, Na hɛn atamfo ankasa mpo nye atsɛmbuafo.
Na hɔn wenyindua fi Sodom wenyindua mu, Na ofi Gomora haban mu: Hɔn esikyireamba yɛ bɔr esikyireamba, Hɔn esiaw yɛ wenwen: Hɔn nsa yɛ sasabɔnsam bɔr, Nye nhurutsia owubɔr dzendzen.
Ana wɔnnkora iyi do wɔ me nkyɛn, Wɔnnsɔw ano wɔ m’akoradze mu bi a?
Awerdzi yɛ medze, akatua so, Aber a hɔn anan bɛpatser: Na hɔn mbusu da abɛn, Na ndzɛmba a ɔwɔ dɛ ɔba hɔn do no bɛba ntsɛntsɛm.
Na EWURADZE bobu ne man atsɛn, Na oenu noho wɔ no nkowaa ntsi; Aber a obohu dɛ hɔn ahoɔdzen asa, Na ɔdehye anaa akowaa biara nnyi hɔ bio, Na ɔbɛse dɛ, Henfa na hɔn enyame no wɔ, Ɔbotan a wɔdze hɔn werɛ hyɛɛ mu no; Hɔn a wodzi hɔn okum afɔr seradze, Na wɔnom hɔn ɔnom afɔr nsa no a?
Ma wɔnsoɛr mbɔboa hom, Ma wɔnyɛ hom ntwitwagye.
Afei hom nhu dɛ emi, mara nye no, Na onyame bi nnka mo ho: Emi na muku, na mema nkwa; Mipira, na mesa yarba: Na obi nnyi hɔ a obotum agye efi me nsamu.
Na mema me nsa do wɔ ɔsor, Na mese dɛ, Dɛ metse ase daa yi, Sɛ mesew me nkrantsee nyinamnyinam no, Na me nsa suo atsɛmbu mu a; Mibedzi hɔn a wɔnye me dzi esi do wer, Na metua hɔn a wɔtan me kaw.
Mebɛma bɔgya abow m’egyen menaba, Na me nkrantsee edzi nam; Atɔfo nye ndɔmmumfo bɔgyaa, Ofi ɔtamfo Edzikamfo tsir do.
Amanaman, hom nye ne man ndzi dɛw: Na obedzi no nkowaa bɔgyaa ho wer, Na ɔdze awerdzi etua n’ayɛfo kaw, Na ɔapata ama n’asaase ama ne man.
Na Moses baa bɛkaa ndwom yi mu nsɛm nyinara wɔ ɔman no asomu, ɔno, nye Nun ne babanyin Josua.
Na Moses wiee nsɛm yi nyinara ka kyerɛɛ Israel nyinara: na ɔsee hɔn dɛ, Hom mfa hom akoma nsi nsɛm a miridzi hom ho dase ndɛ da yi nyinara do; ɔno na hom mfa nhyɛ hom mba, dɛ wɔndwen do ndzi mbra yi mu nsɛm nyinara do.
Na mma ɔnnyɛ asɛnhun mma hom; osiandɛ ɔyɛ hom nkwa, na asɛm yi do na hom nam bɛma hom nda awar wɔ asaase a hom rukotwa Jordan akɛfa no do.
Nyankopɔn Soma Moses Wɔ Nebo Na EWURADZE kasaa kyerɛɛ Moses da no ara dɛ, Kɔfow bepɔw Abarim yi, kɔ bepɔw Nebo a ɔwɔ Moab asaase do, wɔ Jeriko tsentsendo no; na hwɛ Keenan asaase a medze merema Israelmba dɛ enyadze no: na wu wɔ bepɔw no a erofow akɔ do no do, na kɛka wo nananom ho wɔ samanadze; dɛ mbrɛ wo nua Aaron wui wɔ bepɔw Horeb do, na ɔkɛkaa ne nananom ho no; osiandɛ hom foom me wɔ Israelmba mu wɔ Meriba nsu a ɔwɔ Kades, wɔ Zin sar do no ho; osiandɛ hom annyɛ me krɔnkrɔn wɔ Israelmba mu.
Na ibohu asaase no wɔ w’enyim; na mbom eronnkɔ asaase a medze rema Israelmba no do hɔ.
Moses Hyira Israel Na iyi nye nhyira a Onyame nyimpa Moses dze hyiraa Israelmba ansaana oruwu.
Na ɔsee dɛ, EWURADZE fi Sinai bae, Na ɔsoɛree fi Seir maa hɔn; Ɔhyerɛɛn fi bepɔw Paran do, Na ofi akrɔnkrɔmfo mpedu mpedu mu bae: Na n’enyimfa wɔ mbra a ɔyɛ ogya ma hɔn.
Nyew, ɔdɔ aman; N’ahotseweefo nyinara wɔ wo nsamu: Na wɔtsenatsenaa famu wɔ w’anan ho; Obiara bɛgye wo nsɛm ato mu.
Moses hyɛɛ hɛn mbra, Jakob bagua egyapadze.
Na ɔyɛɛ ɔhen wɔ Jesurun, Aber a ɔman no mu etsitsir hyiae, Israel ebusuakuw ebusuakuw nyinara bɔ mu no.
Ma Reuben nnya nkwa, na mma onnwu; Na eso mma n’ase nnhyew.
Na iyi nye Juda nhyira: na ɔsee dɛ, EWURADZE, tsie Juda ne ndze, Na fa no kɔ fie no nkorɔfo nkyɛn: Ma ne nsa nso no so, Na yɛ ɔboafo fa tsia n’ayɛfo.
Na Levi ho dze ɔsee dɛ, Wo Tummim nye wo Urim wɔ wo nyamesuronyi no hɔ, Nyia esɔɔ no hwɛe wɔ Massa no, Nye no hamee wɔ Meriba nsu ho no; Nyia ɔsee wɔ n’egya, nye ne na ho dɛ, Munnhun hɔn; Nkyii so ɔammpen no nuanom do no, Na woennhu nankasa ne mba so no: Na wɔadwen w’asɛm do: Na woedzi w’ahyɛmu do.
Wɔdze w’atsɛmbu bɛkyerɛ Jakob, Na wo mbra akyerɛ Israel: Wɔdze eduhuam bɔto w’enyim, Na ɔhyew afɔr mu ato w’afɔrmbukyia do.
EWURADZE, hyira n’ahoɔdzen, Na ma ne nsaano edwuma nsɔ w’enyi: Bobɔ hɔn a wɔsoɛr tsia no no hɔn ndwonku, Na hɔn a wɔtan no, amma wɔaannsoɛr bio.
Benjamin ho dze ɔsee dɛ, EWURADZE no dɔfo bɛtsena ne nkyɛn dwudwoodwo; Ɔkata no do adzekyee tsentsen nyinara, Na ɔtse n’abatsir ntamu.
Na Josef ho dze, ɔsee dɛ EWURADZE nhyira n’asaase; Ɔmma ɔsor ndzepa, ɔbɔsu, Nye bun a ɔda daadzetsirmu ne dze, Nye ewia no nduadzewa mu ndzepa, Nye dza abosoom ma ofifir mu ndzepa, Nye tsetse mbepɔw do adze tsitsir, Nye daa daa nkoko do ndzepa, Nye asaase nye ne mayɛ mu ndzepa, Nye nyia ɔtsenaa kwaa mu n’enyisɔ: Ma nhyira no ɔmbra Josef n’etsifi, Nye no nuanom mu nyia woeyi no esi nkyɛn no n’etsifi pampamu.
Ne nantwisaa abakan, tumdzi dzi wɔ no; Na n’ambɛn yɛ eko ambɛn: Ɔno na ɔdze bosunsun aman nyinara, mekyerɛ asaase n’ano n’ano: Na hɔn nye Efraim mpedu mpedu no, Na hɔn nye Manaasɛ mpempem no, Na Zebulun, ho dze ɔsee dɛ, Zebulun, ma w’enyi ngye wɔ w’edzifir mu; Na, Isakar, wɔ w’asesee mu.
Wɔbɛfrɛ aman akɔ bepɔw do; Hɔ na wɔbɔbɔ tsenenee okum afɔr: Na woehwiew epo no mbordo no, Nye anhwea mu akoradze a ohuntsa no.
Na Gad ho dze ɔsee dɛ, Nhyira aka nyia ɔtserɛw Gad mu: Ɔtsena hɔ dɛ ogyataber, Ɔtsetsew abasa, nyew, etsifi pampamu.
Na osiesiee dza odzi kan no maa noho, Na hɔ na wɔakora mbrahyɛfo ne kyɛfa; Na ɔnye ɔman no mu etsitsir bae, Na ɔyɛɛ EWURADZE ne tseneneedze, Nye ne ntsɛmbu wɔ Israel nkyɛn.
Na Dan ho dze ɔsee dɛ, Dan yɛ ogyata ne ba a Ohuruw fi Basan.
Na Naftali ho dze ɔsee dɛ, Naftali a enyisɔ amee no, EWURADZE ne nhyira ahyɛ no ma: Fa anee nye pomu afamu asaase no fa, Na Aser ho dze ɔsee dɛ, Wɔmfa mba nhyira Aser; Wɔmma ɔnyɛ nyia ɔsɔ enyi mma no nuanom, Na wɔmma ɔmfa n’anan mbɔ ngo mu.
W’adaban nyɛ dadze nye boran; Na dɛ mbrɛ wo nda tse no, dɛmara so na w’ahoɔdzen nyɛ.
Jesurun, obi nnyi hɔ a ɔtse dɛ Onyame a Otutu nam sor dzi boa wo, Na n’akɛseyɛ wɔ wimu.
Ɔdomankoma Nyankopɔn nye wo tsenabew: Na n’ase na daa daa abasa wɔ: Na ɔpaam ɔtamfo no wɔ w’enyim, Na ɔsee dɛ, Sɛɛ hɔn.
Na Israel retsena dwudwoodwo, Jakob nsubura no nkotoo, Wɔ eburow nye nsa asaase do; Nyew, no sor so sosɔw ɔbɔsu.
Osiarfo nye wo, Israel: Woana na ɔnye wo sɛ, ɔman a EWURADZE agye no nkwa, Wo mboa akokyɛm, Na ɔno nye wo kɛseyɛ nkrantsee!
Na w’atamfo bɛbrɛ hɔnho adze ama wo; Na ibetsiatsia hɔn mbea sorɔnsorɔm no do.
Moses No Wu Na Moses fii Moab tɛtɛr mu fowee kɔr bepɔw Nebo do, wɔ Pisga etsifi a ɔwɔ Jeriko tsentsendo.
Na EWURADZE kyerɛɛ no Gilead asaase nyinara, ɔdze kodu Dan: nye Naftali nyinara, nye Efraim nye Manaasɛ asaase, nye Juda asaase nyinara, ɔdze kodu ekyirekyir epo no ho; nye Epomu, nye Tɛtɛrmu, nkyiresua kurow Jeriko ɔbɔn no, ɔdze kodu Zoar.
Na EWURADZE see no dɛ, Iyi nye asaase a mekaa ho ntam mekyerɛɛ Abraham, Isaak, nye Jakob dɛ, W’asefo na medze mebɛma hɔn no: mama wo kwan dɛ fa w’enyiwa hwɛ, na hɔ dze eronnkɔ.
Nna EWURADZE n’akowaa Moses wuu hɔ wɔ Moab asaase do, dɛ mbrɛ EWURADZE n’asɛm tse.
Na osiee no wɔ ɔbɔn no mu wɔ Moab asaase do wɔ Bɛt-peor tsentsendo na n’adakamona dze nyimpa biara nnyim dze bodu ndɛ da yi.
Na aber a Moses wui no na oedzi mfe ɔha eduonu: n’enyiwa annyɛ kusukusu, na n’ahoɔdzen so do ennhuan.
Na Israelmba sui maa Moses wɔ Moab tɛtɛr mu adaduasa: nna Moab n’eyiyɛ mu osu nda no bɔɔ adze.
Na nyansa sunsum hyɛɛ Nun ne babanyin Josua ma: na Israelmba tsiee no, na wɔyɛɛ dɛ mbrɛ EWURADZE hyɛɛ Moses no.
Na ofitsi aber no nkɔnhyɛnyi biara nnsoɛree wɔ Israel mu bio a ɔtse dɛ Moses a EWURADZE nye no nyaa nkitahodzi a no mu dɔ yie Dɛm Moses yi ara so na EWURADZE somaa no wɔ nsa a ɔyɛ dzen do kɔr Egypt ma ɔkɛyɛɛ nsɛnkyerɛdze nye anwanwadze pii wɔ Farao nye no nkowaa nye n’asaase nyinara do no.
Afei so, ɔnam Moses do na ndzɛmba akɛse a ɔyɛ hu na tum wɔ mu daa edzi wɔ Israel nyinara enyim.
NHƐNMU Josua nwoma no mu nsɛm no fa dzi a odzii Israelmba no enyim kɔtoaa Keenanfo nye hɔn kɔkoe no.
Dɛm Josua yi na odzii Moses n’adze.
Nsɛm tsitsir a wɔka ho asɛm no bi nye esutsen Jordan no ntwae, Jeriko ne nsɛe, Ai ko no na Nyankopɔn n’ahyɛmu a ɔnye ne mamfoo dzii no ne ntsimu no.
Asɛm a wonyim no yie papaapa wɔ dɛm nwoma yi mu nye, “Ndɛ da yi, hom nsan mu nyi nyia hom bɔsom no; sɛ enyame a hom egyanom somee a wɔwɔ Esu no egya no o, Amorifo a hom tse hɔn asaase do yi enyame o: na emi na me fi dze yɛbɔsom EWURADZE”.
Dza Ɔwɔ Mu Wodzi Keenanfo do konyim .—.
Wɔkyɛ asaase no mu .—.
.
Asaase a ɔda Jordan boka afamu .- .
Asaase a ɔda Jordan anee afamu .—.
.
Guansumabew nkurow no .- .
Levifo nkurow .- Ebusuakuw a wɔwɔ boka afamu no san kɔ hɔn asaase do .- Josua ne nkradzi nsɛm .- Wɔhyɛ ahyɛmu no mu dzen wɔ Sekem .-
EWURADZE Kyerɛ Josua Dza Ɔnyɛ EWURADZE n’akowaa Moses wui n’ekyir no, EWURADZE kasaa kyerɛɛ Nun ne babanyin Josua a nna ɔyɛ Moses no somfo no dɛ, M’akowaa Moses ewu; dɛm ntsi afei soɛr, twa Jordan yi, ɔwo, nye ɔman yi nyinara, kɔ asaase a medze rema hom, mekyerɛ Israelmba no do.
Beebiara a hom anamɔn betsia no, medze ama hom, dɛ mbrɛ mekaa kyerɛɛ Moses no.
Ofi sar no do, nye Lebanon yi ho araa dze kodu esutsen kɛse Eufrates no ho, Hitifo asaase nyinara, na ɔdze kodu po kɛse no ho wɔ witɔree afamu no, na ɔnyɛ hom he.
Nyimpa biara runntum nngyina w’enyim wɔ wo nkwa nda nyinara mu: na dɛ mbrɛ midzii Moses n’ekyir no, dɛmara so na mibedzi w’ekyir: meremmpa wo, na morommpow wo so.
Hyɛ dzen na nya akokodur: na ɔwo na ebɛma ɔman yi ekenya asaase a mekaa ho ntam kyerɛɛ hɔn egyanom dɛ medze mebɛma hɔn no edzi.
Dzen ara na hyɛ na nya akokodur papaapa, na dwen do dzi mbra a m’akowaa Moses hyɛɛ wo no nyinara do: mma mmfi ho mmfa enyimfa anaa abankum, ama eesi wo yie wɔ beebiara a ebɔkɔ.
Mma mbra nwoma yi mmpa w’anomu, na mbom dwen ho adzekyee nye adzesaa, ama aadwen do ayɛ dɛ mbrɛ wɔakyerɛw wɔ mu no nyinara tse no: na ɔno na ebɛma wo kwan ayɛ dwudwoodwo, na ɔno na ibenya no yie.
Ana mennhyɛɛ wo bi a?
Hyɛ dzen na nya akokodur; mma mmbɔ hu, nkyii so mma w’abaw mu nntu: na EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn dzi w’ekyir wɔ beebiara a ebɔkɔ.
Josua Kyerɛ Ɔman Ahwɛdofo No Dza Wɔnyɛ Nna Josua hyɛɛ ɔman no hɔn ahwɛdofo no, dɛ, Hom ndɔ nseraban no mu na hom nhyɛ ɔman no dɛ, Hom nsiesie edzidzidze mma homho, na aka ndaansa hom botwa Jordan yi akɔ akɛfa asaase a EWURADZE hom Nyankopɔn dze rema hom dɛ wɔnkɛfa no.
Na Josua kasaa kyerɛɛ Reubenfo, nye Gadfo, nye Manaasɛ ebusuakuw ɔfa no dɛ, Hom nkaa asɛm a EWURADZE n’akowaa Moses hyɛɛ hom no, dɛ, EWURADZE hom Nyankopɔn rema hom ahomgye, na ɔdze asaase yi ama hom no.
Hom yernom, hom mbofraba, nye hom fiembowa, ntsena asaase a Moses dze maa hom wɔ Jordan egya yi do; na homara dze, hom mmia ndzi hom nuanom enyim ntwa, hom mu mbarimba akatakyi nyinara, na hom nkɔboa hɔn; ma onkodu dɛ EWURADZE bɛma hom nuanom ahomgye, dɛ mbrɛ ɔdze ama hom yi, na hɔn so woeenya asaase a EWURADZE hom Nyankopɔn dze rema hom no afa: na n’ekyir no hom asan abɛfa hom enyadze asaase a EWURADZE n’akowaa Moses dze maa hom wɔ Jordan egya ɔdze kɔ wipuei afamu no.
Na wobuaa Josua, dɛ, Dza edze ahyɛ hɛn nyinara yɛbɛyɛ, na beebiara a ebɔsoma hɛn no, yɛbɔkɔ.
Dɛ mbrɛ yetsiee Moses wɔ adze nyinara mu no, dɛmara so na yebetsie wo: w’ekyir ara na EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn ndzi, dɛ mbrɛ odzii Moses ekyir no.
Nyimpa biara a ɔbɛtsew etua wɔ wo mbrasɛm do, na onnketsie wo nsɛm wɔ dza edze hyɛ no nyinara mu no, ɔtse dɛ woana ara a wonku no: dzen ara na hyɛ na nya akokodur.
Rahab Gye Akwanserafo No Nna Nun ne babanyin Josua somaa mbanyin beenu nsumaa mu fi Sittim dɛ aserafo dɛ wɔnkɔ nkɔhwɛ asaase no, nye Jeriko.
Na wɔkɔree, na wɔkɔr ɔbaa huhunyi bi a ne dzin dze Rahab ne fie, na wɔkɔsoɛɛ hɔ.
Na binom kaa kyerɛɛ Jerikohen no, dɛ, Hwɛ, mbanyin bi fi Israelmba mu baa ha anadwe yi dɛ wɔrebɛsera asaase yi.
Na Jerikohen no somae ma wɔkɔr Rahab hɔ, dɛ, Fa mbanyin no a wɔaba abɛhɛn wo fie no pue: na wɔaba rebɛsera asaase no nyinara.
Na ɔbaa no faa mbanyin beenu no, na ɔdze hɔn sumae; na ɔsee dɛ, Ɔyɛ nokwar, mbanyin no baa me nkyɛn, na mbom, minnyim mbrɛ wofi: na ɔbaa dɛ aber a wɔdze tow kuropon no mu no durii no, nna mbanyin no fii me nkyɛn: na mbrɛ wɔkɔree no dze, minnyim: hom ntsiw hɔn ntsɛm; na hom bɔto hɔn.
Nna ɔnoara dze hɔn akɔ ɔdan etsifi na ɔdze hɔn ekosuma asaaba a wɔmmpaae bi a ɔaboaboa no yie wɔ ɔdan etsifi no mu.
Na ɔhen no n’asomafo no faa Jordan kwan do tsiiw hɔn araa dze kodur esutwaree: na hɔn a wotsiiw hɔn no kɔree no ara, na wɔtoow kuropon no mu.
Na wonnyae nnkɛdae no, Rahab fowee kɔr hɔn nkyɛn wɔ dan no etsifi hɔ: na ɔsee mbanyin no dɛ, Minyim dɛ EWURADZE dze asaase yi ama hom, na hom ho hu atɔ hɛn do, na asaase yi do atsefo nyinara hɔn ho mbowa eguan wɔ hom ntsi.
Na yɛatse mbrɛ EWURADZE sii maa Mbɛw Po (Mbɛw Po) no no nsu wewee wɔ hom enyim, aber a hom fi Egypt firii no; na dza hom dze yɛɛ Amorifo ahemfo beenu, Sihon nye Ɔge a wɔwɔ Jordan egya no, na mbrɛ hom sii sɛɛ hɔn pasapasa no nyinara.
Na yɛtsee no ara na hɛn akoma tui, nkyii so ahom biara annka nyimpa biara mu bio, osian hom ntsi: na EWURADZE hom Nyankopɔn no, ɔno nye Nyankopɔn wɔ sor, nye asaase do.
Dɛm ntsi afei, mepa hom kyɛw, hom mfa EWURADZE ndzi nsew nkyerɛ me dɛ, ɔnam dɛ mayɛ hom yie ntsi, hom so bɛyɛ m’egya fie yie, hom mma me nokwar asɛnkyerɛdze: dɛ hom bɛgye m’egya, nye me na, nye mo nuanom mbanyin nye mbaa, na adze a wɔwɔ nyinara nkwa, na woeyi hɛn efi owu mu.
Na mbanyin no see no dɛ, Hɛn nkwa nhyɛ homdze ananmu, sɛ hom annka hɛn nsɛm yi annkyerɛ a; ɔno ɔbɛba dɛ, sɛ EWURADZE dze asaase yi ma hɛn a, yɛnye wo bedzi no yie nye nokwar mu.
Nna ɔdze ntampee duaa tokura mu gogoow hɔn sisii famu: osiandɛ ne dan no si kurow no ho fasu no do, na fasu no do na ɔtse.
Na ɔsee hɔn dɛ, Hom nkɔ bepɔw no do, amma etsiwfo no aannto hom; na hom nsuma homho wɔ hɔ, ndaansa, nkodu dɛ etsiwfo no bɛsan: na n’ekyir no hom bɔkɔ hom kwan a, hom aakɔ.
Na mbanyin no see no dɛ, Yennkedzi so wɔ wo ntam a ama yɛaka yi ho.
Hwɛ, sɛ yɛreba asaase yi do a, fa serdaa ahoma yi kyekyer tokura a edze hɛn duaa mu sisii famu no mu: na boa w’egya, nye wo na, nye wo nuanom, nye w’egya ne fifo nyinara ano wɔ wo nkyɛn wɔ fie no mu.
Na ɔbɛba dɛ, obiara a obefi wo fi mbobow ano akɔ abɔntsen do no, no bɔgyaa bogu ɔnoara n’etsifi, na yennkedzi so: na obiara a ɔwɔ wo nkyɛn wɔ fie no, sɛ obi dze ne nsa ka no a, no bɔgyaa ngu hɛn etsifi.
Na sɛ eka hɛn asɛm yi kyerɛ a, ɔnodze, yennkedzi so wɔ wo ntam a ama yɛaka yi ho.
Na ɔsee dɛ, Dɛ mbrɛ hom nsɛm yi tse no ara, wɔmma ɔnyɛ hɔ.
Na ogyaa hɔn kwan, na wosii mu kɔree: na ɔdze serdaa ahoma no kyekyeer tokura no mu.
Na wɔkɔree kodur bepɔw no do, na wɔtsenaa hɔ ndaansa, kodur dɛ etsiwfo no sanee: na etsiwfo no hwehwɛɛ hɔn wɔ kwan no mu nyina, na woennhu hɔn.
Nna mbanyin beenu no sanee, na wofii bepɔw no do sianee, na wotwae baa Josua, Nun ne babanyin no, ne nkyɛn.
Na wɔsee Josua dɛ, Ampaara, EWURADZE dze asaase no nyinara ahyɛ hɛn nsa; na nkyii so asaase no do atsefo no nyinara hɔn akoma etu kɛsenara wɔ hɛn enyim.
Israelmba No Twa Jordan Na Josua soɛɛr ahanamakye, na wotui fii Sittim, ɔno na Israelmba nyinara; na wɔbaa Jordan do, na wɔkyeer nseraban wɔ hɔ ansaana worutwa.
Na ɔbaa dɛ odzii ndaansa no, ahwɛdofo no tui dɔɔ nseraban no mu; na wɔhyɛɛ ɔman no, dɛ, Sɛ hom hu EWURADZE hom Nyankopɔn n’ahyɛmudaka no, na Levifo asɔfo a wɔso no a, ɔno hom ntu mfi hom ananmu na hom ndzi ekyir nkɔ; ama hom eehu kwan kor a ɔwɔ dɛ hom fa do; osiandɛ hom mmfaa kwan yi do da gyedɛ ndɛ.
Mbom, hom mma ɔkwan a wosusu a ɔbɛyɛ basafa apem nda hom nye ahyɛmudaka no ntamu: na mma hom mmbɛn no.
Na Josua see ɔman no dɛ, Hom ntsew homho: na ɔkyena EWURADZE bɛyɛ hom mu anwanwadze.
Na Josua kaa kyerɛɛ asɔfo no, dɛ, Hom mma ahyɛmudaka no do, na hom ntwa mu nkedzi ɔman no enyim.
Na wɔmaa ahyɛmudaka no do, na wokedzii ɔman no enyim.
Na EWURADZE see Josua dɛ, Ndɛ da yi na mebɛhyɛ ase mama wo do wɔ Israel nyinara enyi do, na woeehu dɛ, dɛ mbrɛ midzii Moses ekyir no, dɛmara so na mibedzi w’ekyir.
Na hyɛ asɔfo a wɔso ahyɛmudaka no, dɛ, Sɛ hom du Jordan nsu no no nkɔkɔnoa a, hom ngyina dzinn wɔ Jordan no mu.
Na Josua see Israelmba no dɛ, Hom mbra ha mbetsie EWURADZE hom Nyankopɔn ne nsɛm.
Na Josua see dɛ, Ɔnam iyi do na hom dze bohu dɛ tseasefo Nyankopɔn no wɔ hom mu, na dɛ ɔpam ara na ɔbɛpam Keenanfo, Hitifo, Hivifo, Perizfo, Girgasfo, Amorifo, nye Jebusfo no nyinara efi hom enyim.
Hwɛ, asaase nyinara Wura ahyɛmudaka no rutwa mu edzi hom enyim akɔ Jordan mu.
Dɛm ntsi afei hom nyiyi Israel ebusuakuw ebusuakuw mu mbanyin duebien, ebusuakuw biara mu nyimpa baako.
Na ɔbɛba dɛ, aber a asɔfo a wɔso EWURADZE, asaase nyinara Wura no, n’adakaa no, hɔn anamɔn besi Jordan no nsu mu no, Jordan no nsu no botwa, mekyerɛ nsu a ɔpem fi etsifi ba no a; na wɔabɔ kuw kor egyina hɔ.
Na ɔman no tui fii hɔn asesee mu a nna asɔfo no a wɔso ahyɛmudaka no dzi hɔn enyim.
Nna Jordan yir kata no nsukɔn nyinara do buber nyinara naaso, aber a asɔfo a wɔso adaka no dur Jordan do, na hɔn anan sii nsu no nkɔkɔnoa no ara pɛr, nna nsu a ɔpem fi etsifi ba no gyinae, na ɔbɔɔ kuw kor, wɔ ekyirkyiikyir, wɔ Adam, kurow no a ɔwɔ Zaretan ne nkyɛn no noho: na dza ɔpem kɔ Araba po a ɔnoara nye Nkyen Epo no mu no twaa koraa: na ɔman no twae faa Jeriko tsentsendo.
Na asɔfo a wɔso EWURADZE n’ahyɛmudaka no gyinaa daadze kɛsɛɛ do pintsinn wɔ Jordan ne finimfin, na Israel nyinara nam daadze kɛsɛɛ do twae araa dze kodur dɛ ɔman no nyinara wiee Jordan twa.
Wosisi Nkaabo Na ɔbaa dɛ, aber a ɔman no nyinara wiee Jordan twa no, EWURADZE kaa kyerɛɛ Josua dɛ, Hom nyiyi ɔman no mu mbanyin duebien, ebusuakuw biara mu nyimpa baako, na hom nhyɛ hɔn dɛ, Hom mfa abo duebien wɔ Jordan mu wɔ mbrɛ asɔfo no hɔn anan gyinaa pintsinn no, na hom nsoa nkɔ, na wɔmfa nkogu asoɛe, mbrɛ hom bɔsoɛ anadwe yi no.
Nna Josua frɛɛ mbanyin duebien no a oesiesie hɔn wɔ Israelmba no mu no, ebusuakuw biara mu nyimpa baako: na ɔsee hɔn dɛ, Hom ntwa mu nkedzi EWURADZE hom Nyankopɔn n’adakaa no enyim nkɔ Jordan ne finimfin, na hom mu nyimpa baako biara mfa ɔbo kor nto no kɔn ho, dɛ mbrɛ Israelmba ebusuakuw ebusuakuw no dodow tse: ama iyi aayɛ hom mu asɛnkyerɛdze, na sɛ ndaamba bi hom mba bisa hom dɛ, Abo yi hom kyerɛ ase dɛn a, ɔno hom nse hɔn dɛ, Osiandɛ Jordan nsu no twae wɔ EWURADZE ahyɛmudaka no enyim; aber a ahyɛmudaka no twaa Jordan no, hwɛ, Jordan no nsu no, otwaa koraa: na abo yi na ɔyɛ nkaadze ma Israelmba daa.
Na Israelmba no yɛɛ dɛ mbrɛ Josua hyɛe no, na wɔfaa abo duebien wɔ Jordan mu, dɛ mbrɛ EWURADZE kaa kyerɛɛ Josua no, dɛ mbrɛ Israelmba ebusuakuw ebusuakuw no dodow tse; na wɔsoae dze kɔr beebi mbrɛ wɔkɔsoɛe no, na wɔdze guu hɔ.
Na Josua so dze abo duebien sisii Jordan finimfin, wɔ beebi mbrɛ asɔfo a wɔso ahyɛmudaka no dze hɔn anan sisii no: na ɔwɔ hɔ dze bodu ndɛ da yi.
Na asɔfo a wɔso adaka no gyinaa Jordan mu araa ma okodur dɛ wowiee adze biara a EWURADZE hyɛɛ Josua dɛ ɔnka nkyerɛ ɔman no yɛ, dɛ mbrɛ Moses dze hyɛɛ Josua no nyinara: na ɔman no yɛɛ ntsɛm twae.
Na ɔbaa dɛ, aber a ɔman no nyinara wiee twa no, na EWURADZE n’adakaa no so twae, na asɔfo no kedzii ɔman no enyim.
Na Reubenmba, Gadmba, nye Manaasɛ ebusuakuw ɔfa no, miae twae kedzii Israelmba no enyim, dɛ mbrɛ Moses kaa kyerɛɛ hɔn no: mbarimba bɛyɛ mpemeduanan a woemia prɛko dɛ wɔrokɔ sa twae kedzii EWURADZE enyim kɔr akono, wɔ Jeriko tɛtɛr mu.
Da no ara na EWURADZE maa Josua do wɔ Israel nyinara enyi do; na wosuroo no, dɛ mbrɛ wosuroo Moses no, wɔ no nkwa nda nyinara mu.
Na EWURADZE kaa kyerɛɛ Josua, dɛ, Hyɛ asɔfo a wɔso dasedaka no, ma womfi Jordan mu mbra.
Dɛm ntsi Josua hyɛɛ asɔfo no, dɛ, Hom mfi Jordan mu mbra.
Na ɔbaa dɛ, asɔfo a wɔso EWURADZE n’ahyɛmudaka no fi Jordan mu fowee, na asɔfo no hɔn anamɔn besii daadze kɛsɛɛ do ara, na Jordan no nsu no sanee kɔr n’anamu, na ɔkɛkataa no nsukɔn nyinara do, dɛ mbrɛ nkan no nna ɔtse no.
Na ɔman no fii Jordan mu fowee wɔ bosoom a odzi kan no mu da a otsia du no mu, na wɔkɛkyeer nsera wɔ Gilgal, wɔ Jeriko no boka afamu ɔhe do.
Na abo duebien no a woyiyii no wɔ Jordan mu no, Josua dze hyɛɛ siw wɔ Gilgal.
Na ɔkaa kyerɛɛ Israelmba, dɛ, Sɛ ndaamba bi hom mba bisa hɔn egyanom dɛ, Abo yi ase nye dɛn a, ɔnodze, hom mma hom mba nhu dɛ, Asaase kɛsɛɛ do na Israel nam twaa Jordan yi.
Na EWURADZE hom Nyankopɔn weew Jordan mu nsu no wɔ hom enyim, na hom twae ana, dɛ mbrɛ EWURADZE hom Nyankopɔn yɛɛ Mbɛw Po (Mbɛw Po) no a ɔwewee no wɔ hɛn enyim, ma yɛtwae ana no: ama asaase do aman nyinara eehu dɛ EWURADZE n’abasa mu yɛ dzen; ama hom eesuro EWURADZE hom Nyankopɔn daa.
Na ɔbaa dɛ aber a Amorifo ahemfo a wɔwɔ Jordan egya anee afamu nyinara, nye Keenanfo ahemfo a wɔwɔ po ho no nyinara, tsee mbrɛ EWURADZE sii na ɔweew Jordan no nsu wɔ Israelmba no enyim ma wotwae ana no, hɔn akoma tui, nkyii so nna ahom bi nnyi hɔn mu bio, osian Israelmba no ntsi.
Twatsiatwa Na Apaho Wɔ Gilgal Aber no mu na EWURADZE see Josua dɛ, ɔwoara yɛ ɔtwerɛbo asekan, na twitwa Israelmba no twatsia bio ne mprɛnu.
Na Josua noara yɛɛ ɔtwerɛbo asekan, na otwitwaa Israelmba no twatsia wɔ Gibeat Haaralot.
Na dza osian ntsi ma Josua twitwaa twatsia no nye yi: ɔman no a wofi Egypt bae no nyinara a wɔyɛ mbanyin no, mekyerɛ mbarimba akofo no nyinara, wuwuu kwan mu wɔ sar no do, ber a wofi Egypt firii n’ekyir no.
Nna ɔman no a wofiir edzi no nyinara woetwitwa hɔn twatsia: na ɔman no a wofi Egypt firii no a wɔwoo hɔn kwan mu wɔ sar no do nyinara dze, wonntwitwaa hɔn twatsia.
Na Israelmba no nantsewee wɔ sar no do mfe eduanan, kodur dɛ ɔman no nyinara, mekyerɛ mbarimba akofo no a wofi Egypt firii no, hɔn ase kumii, osiandɛ woenntsie EWURADZE ne ndze: woyinom na EWURADZE kaa ntam dɛ ɔnnkɛma woehu asaase a ɔno EWURADZE kaa ho ntam kyerɛɛ hɔn egyanom dɛ ɔdze bɛma hɛn no, asaase a numfonsu nye ewo pem wɔ do no.
Na hɔn mba no, hɔn a ɔmaa wɔsoɛree hyɛɛ hɔn ananmu no, nna wɔyɛ monomonomfo, osiandɛ woenntwa hɔn twatsia wɔ kwan no mu na hɔn na Josua twitwaa hɔn twatsia no.
Na ɔbaa dɛ, aber a wowiee ɔman no nyinara twatsia twitwa no, wɔtsenatsenaa hɔn ananmu wɔ nseraban no mu ma wɔtsee apɔw ana.
Na EWURADZE see Josua dɛ, Ndɛ da yi na meyi Egypt enyimguase no efi hom do.
Dɛm ntsi wɔfrɛɛ bea no ne dzin Gilgal dze bodu ndɛ da yi.
Na Israelmba no kyeer nsera wɔ Gilgal, na wodzii apaho wɔ bosoom no ne da a otsia duanan no n’ewimbir wɔ Jeriko tɛtɛr mu.
Na wodzii apaho no n’adzekyee no nna wodzii asaase no do eburow dadaw, epitsi tatar nye eburow kyewee.
Na da a wodzii asaase no do eburow dadaw no, adzekyee no ara nna manna no siankae; na Israelmba no ennya manna bio; mbom wodzii Keenan asaase no do ndɔbaa wɔ afe no mu.
Josua Hyia EWURADZE No Bɔfoe Na ɔbaa dɛ aber a Josua wɔ Jeriko ho no, ɔmaa n’enyiwa do na ohun banyin bi a ɔatwe n’afona kitsa ne nsamu dɛ ogyina n’enyim tsentsendo: na Josua kɔr ne nkyɛn, na obisaa no dɛ, Ewɔ hɛn afa, anaa ewɔ hɛn atamfo afa?
Na obuaa dɛ, Oho, nnyɛ no mu biara, na mbom dɛ EWURADZE no dɔm safohen panyin no, na afei maba.
Na Josua dze n’enyim butuuw famu, na ɔsɔɔr no, na ɔsee no dɛ, Na mo wura ese n’akowaa dɛn?
Na EWURADZE no dɔm safohen panyin no see Josua dɛ, Yiyi wo mpaboa wɔ w’anan; na beebi mbrɛ igyinae no yɛ krɔnkrɔn.
Na Josua yɛɛ dɛm.
Jeriko N’asehwe Na ɔnam Israelmba no ntsi, wɔtoow Jeriko mu twitwiitwi a obi mmfi mu mmpue, na obi nntum mmba mu.
Na EWURADZE see Josua dɛ, Hwɛ, medze Jeriko, nye ne hen, nye ne mbarimba akatakyi a wɔyɛ ndam no nyinara ahyɛ wo nsa.
Na hom nkyin kurow no ho, mbarimba akofo nyinara mbɔ kurow no ho aprɔw prɛko.
Yɛ no dɛm nda esia.
Na asɔfo beesuon mfa nguannyin mmbɛn mbɛn esuon ndzi adaka no enyim: Na da a otsia esuon no hom nkyin kurow no ho mpɛn esuon, na asɔfo no nhɛn mbɛn no.
Na ɔbɛba dɛ, sɛ wɔhɛn oguannyin abɛn no ma ɔkyɛr a, na sɛ hom tse abɛn no ne ndze a, ɔman no nyinara mfa huro kɛse mbɔ ose; na kurow no ho fasu no bodwuruw egu famu dɛfɛɛ, na ɔman no mu obiara ndua n’enyim tsentsendo mfow nkɔ.
Na Josua, Nun ne babanyin no, frɛɛ asɔfo no, na ɔsee hɔn dɛ, Hom mma ahyɛmudaka no do, na wɔmma asɔfo beesuon mfa nguannyin mmbɛn mbɛn esuon ndzi EWURADZE n’adakaa no enyim.
Na wɔsee ɔman no dɛ, Hom ntwa mu nkɔbɔ kurow no ho aprɔw, na wɔmma mbarimba a woemia no ntwa mu nkedzi EWURADZE n’adakaa no enyim.
Na wɔyɛɛ dɛm, aber a Josua kasaa kyerɛɛ ɔman no, asɔfo beesuon no a wɔdze nguannyin mmbɛn mbɛn esuon dzi EWURADZE enyim no twaa mu, na wɔhɛɛn mbɛn no: na EWURADZE n’ahyɛmudaka no toaa hɔn do.
Na mbarimba a woemia no dzii asɔfo a wɔhɛn mbɛn no enyim, na nkyidɔm no dzii adaka no ekyir.
Wɔnam rokɔ no nna asɔfo no rehɛn mbɛn no.
Na Josua hyɛɛ ɔman no dɛ, Mma hom mmbɔ ose, mma wɔnntse hom ndze so, mma asɛm bi mmfi hom anomu mmpue, kyerɛ da a mebɛse hom dɛ wɔmbɔ ose no; nna hom mbɔ ose.
Nna ɔmaa EWURADZE n’adakaa no kekyiin kurow no ho, kɔbɔɔ ho aprɔw prɛko: na wɔbaa nseraban no mu, na wɔbɛdaa nseraban no mu.
Na Josua soɛɛr anapaatu, na asɔfo no maa EWURADZE n’adakaa no do.
Na asɔfo beesuon no a wokitsakitsa nguannyin mmbɛn mbɛn esuon no nantsewee dzii EWURADZE n’adakaa no enyim, na wɔhɛɛn mbɛn no.
