Na Israelmba mboanofo man mu nyinara hwinhwiin Moses nye Aaron ho wɔ sar no do: na Israelmba no see hɔn dɛ, Mbom nkyɛ EWURADZE mma yenwuwu ne nsaano wɔ Egypt asaase do, aber a yɛtsetse nam nkutu ho no, aber a yedzi edziban mee no; osiandɛ hom dze hɛn efir edzi aba sar yi do, dɛ hom dze akɔmfun rubokuku mboanofo man mu yi nyinara.
Nna EWURADZE see Moses dɛ, Hwɛ, mebɛma edziban efi sor atɔ ama hom; na ɔman no befir edzi akɛtase dza ɔbɔso hɔn ano da kor wɔ ne da mu, ma maasɔ hɔn mahwɛ kyerɛ dɛ wobedzi me mbra do anaa wonnkedzi do.
Na ɔbɛba dɛ da a otsia esia no, wobesiesie dza wɔdze ba no, na ɔbɛyɛ dza wɔtase no daa no no mbɔho ebien.
Na Moses nye Aaron see Israelmba no nyinara dɛ, Ewimbir nna hom bohu dɛ EWURADZE eyi hom efi Egypt asaase do: na anapa nna hom bohu EWURADZE n’enyimnyam; osiandɛ ɔtse hom ehwinhwin a hom hwinhwin EWURADZE ho no: na hɛn dze, ebɛnadze nye hɛn, na hom hwinhwin hɛn ho?
Na Moses see dɛ, Iyi bɛba, EWURADZE bɛma hom nam ewimbir ma woeedzi, na edziban anapa ma wɔaamee, osiandɛ EWURADZE tse hom ehwinhwin a hom dze hwinhwin no ho: na ebɛnadze nye hɛn?
Nnyɛ hɛn ho na hom hwinhwin, mbom EWURADZE ho a. Na Moses see Aaron dɛ, Se Israelmba mboanofo no nyinara dɛ, Hom ntwe mpin EWURADZE enyim: na ɔatse hom ehwinhwin no.
Na ɔbaa dɛ Aaron rekasa kyerɛ Israelmba mboanofo nyinara no, wɔdandaan hɔn enyi kɔr sar no do, na hwɛ, EWURADZE enyimnyam puei wɔ mununkum no mu.
Na EWURADZE kaa kyerɛɛ Moses dɛ, Matse Israelmba ehwinhwin no: ka kyerɛ hɔn dɛ, Ewimbir hom bedzi nam, na anapa hom edzi edziban amee; na hom ehu dɛ emi nye EWURADZE hom Nyankopɔn.
Na ɔbaa dɛ ewimbir no Nkokɔhwerɛw bae, na wɔbɛkataa nseraban no do: na anapa no ɔbɔw tɔr nseraban no ho hyiae.
Na ɔbɔw a ɔtɔree no kɔr sor no, hwɛ, adze bi nkorkorba nketsenketse deda sar no enyi, nketsenketse dɛ famu ɔbɔsu kyenkyenee.
Na aber a Israelmba hunii no, wɔsesee hɔnho nkorkor dɛ, Ebɛnadze nye yi?
Osiandɛ wonnyim adze kor no.
Na Moses see hɔn dɛ, Iyi nye edziban a EWURADZE dze ama hom dɛ hom ndzi.
Iyi nye adze a EWURADZE ahyɛ, Hom ntase bi dɛ mbrɛ nyimpa biara n’edzidzi tse; olonka nkorkor, dɛ mbrɛ hom nyimpa dodow tse, nna hom mfefa, nyimpa biara mfa mma hɔn a wɔwɔ n’asesee mu no.
Na Israelmba no yɛɛ dɛm, na wɔtasee, binom dze so, binom dze suar.
Na wɔdze olonka susui no, nyia ɔtasee pii no oennya bi ammbor do, na nyia ɔtasee kumaabi no annka no bi: wɔtasee dɛ mbrɛ nyimpa biara n’edzidzi tse.
Na Moses see hɔn dɛ, Mma obi nngya bi ma adze nnkye do.
Naaso woenntsie Moses; mbom hɔn mu binom gyaa bi ma adze kyee do, na ɔdɔɔ mbowaba, na ɔbɔnee; na Moses no bo fuuw hɔn.
Na wɔtasee no anapa anapa, nyimpa biara dɛ mbrɛ n’edzidzi tse: na ewia ano yɛɛ dzen no, ɔnanee.
Na ɔbaa dɛ, da a otsia esia no wɔtasee edziban no mbɔho, ɔbaako dze yɛ olonka ebien: na mboanofo no mu mpanyimfo nyinara baa bɛkaa kyerɛɛ Moses.
Na ɔsee hɔn dɛ, Iyi nye dza EWURADZE aka no, Ɔkyena yɛ awɔse ahomgye, ahomgyeda krɔnkrɔn ma EWURADZE: hom nto dza hom bɔto, na hom nnoa dza hom bɔnoa; na dza ɔka no nyinara hom mfa nsie ma adze nkye do.
Na wɔdze siee ma okodur anapa, dɛ mbrɛ Moses hyɛe no: na ɔammbɔn, nkyii so abowaba bi nnyi mu.
Na Moses see dɛ, Hom ndzi ɔno ndɛ; na ndɛ ɔyɛ ahomgyeda ma EWURADZE: ndɛ hom nnkohu bi wɔ haban mu.
Nda esia na hom ntase; na da a otsia esuon no dze ɔyɛ ahomgyeda, ɔno mu bi nnkɛba hɔ.
Na ɔbaa dɛ da a otsia esuon no, ɔman no mu bi fiir edzi dɛ wɔrekɛtase, na woennhu bi.
Na EWURADZE see Moses dɛ, Hom ropow dɛ wodzi me mbransɛm nye me mbra do ma ekodu dabɛn?
Hom nhwɛ, osiandɛ EWURADZE ama hom ahomgyeda ntsi, na da a otsia esia no ɔma hom nda ebien edziban: hom mu nyimpa biara ntsena ne tsenabew, mma obiara mmfir edzi mmfi ne tsenabew wɔ da a otsia esuon no mu.
Nna ɔman no hoom da a otsia esuon no.
Na Israel fi frɛɛ ne dzin Manna: nna ɔtse dɛ wusa aba, fitaa, na ne dɛw tse dɛ tatar ntrɛtraba a wɔdze ewo ayɛ.
Na Moses see dɛ, Iyi nye adze a EWURADZE ahyɛ, Wɔmfa bi nhyɛ esusudze olonka ma mfa nsie hom ebusuasantsen; ama woeehu edziban a medze menyɛɛn hom wɔ sar no do, aber a miyii hom fii Egypt asaase do no.
Na Moses see Aaron dɛ, Fa kutu bi, na fa manna esusudze olonka kor gu mu, na fa si EWURADZE enyim, ma wɔmfa nsie hom ebusuasantsen.
Dɛ mbrɛ EWURADZE hyɛɛ Moses no, dɛmara so na Aaron dze sii Adasehyɛdze no enyim, ma wɔdze eesie.
Na Israelmba dzii manna no mfe eduanan, dze kodur dɛ wɔbaa asaase a nyimpa tse do do; wodzii manna no, dze kodur dɛ wɔbaa Keenan asaase no ntoaado.
Afei esusudze olonka yɛ efa mu ebupɛn du mu kor.
Nsu Fi Bobaa Mu Ba Na Israelmba mboanofo no nyinara tui fii Sin sar no do, wɔ hɔn akwantu mu, dɛ mbrɛ EWURADZE mbrasɛm tse, na wɔkɛkyekyeer nsera wɔ Refidim: na nsu nnyi hɔ mma ɔman no dɛ wɔbɔnom.
Dɛm ntsi ɔman no nye Moses hamee, na wɔsee dɛ, Ma hɛn nsu ma yɛnnom.
Na Moses see hɔn dɛ, Ebɛnadze ntsi na hom nye me reham?
Ebɛnadze ntsi na hom rosɔ EWURADZE ahwɛ yi?
Na nsukɔm dzee ɔman no wɔ hɔ; na ɔman no hwinhwiin Moses ho, na wɔsee dɛ, Ebɛnadze ntsi na iyii hɛn fii Egypt bae, dɛ edze nsukɔm ruboku hɛn nye hɛn mba nye hɛn mbowa yi?
Na Moses sui frɛɛ EWURADZE see dɛ, Ebɛnadze na menyɛ memma ɔman yi?
Aka kakra ma woeesiw me abo.
Na EWURADZE see Moses dɛ, Pa ho kedzi ɔman no enyim, na fa Israel mpanyin no bi ka woho; na wo poma a edze bɔɔ esutsen no, fa kitsa wo nsamu, na kɔ.
Hwɛ, mibegyina w’enyim wɔ hɔ wɔ Horeb ɔbotan no do; na bɔ ɔbotan no, na nsu befi mu aba, ma ɔman no aanom.
Na Moses yɛɛ dɛm wɔ Israel mpanyin no enyim.
Na ɔfrɛɛ bea no ne dzin Massa, nye Meriba, osian Israelmba hɔn ham no ntsi, na EWURADZE a wɔsɔɔ no hwɛe see dɛ, Ana EWURADZE wɔ hɛn mu, anaa onnyi mu ntsi a?
Israel nye Amalek Ko Nna Amalek bae, na ɔnye Israel bɔkoe wɔ Refidim.
Na Moses see Josua dɛ, San mu yiyi mbanyin ma hɛn, na fir edzi kɔ, nye Amalek nkɔko: ɔkyena medze Nyankopɔn poma no bekitsa me nsamu mekegyina koko no etsifi.
Nna Josua yɛɛ dɛ mbrɛ Moses see no no, na ɔnye Amalek kɔkoe: na Moses, Aaron, nye Hur fowee kɔr koko no etsifi.
Na ɔbaa dɛ, sɛ Moses ma ne nsa do a, nna Israel edzi nyim: na sɛ ɔto ne nsa famu a, nna Amalek edzi nyim.
Na Moses ne nsa gyenee; na wɔfaa ɔbo, na wɔdze too n’ase, na ɔtsenaa do; na Aaron nye Hur susuoo ne nsamu gyinae, ɔbaako dze afa, na ɔbaako so dze afa so; na ne nsa gyinaa dzinn kodur witɔree.
Na Josua dwereew Amalek nye ne man afona ano.
Na EWURADZE see Moses dɛ, Kyerɛw iyi wɔ nwoma mu fa yɛ nkaa, na ka hyɛ Josua n’asomu: dɛ pepa ara na mebɛpepa Amalek ho nkaa mefi ɔsor ase.
Na Moses sii afɔrmbukyia, na ɔfrɛɛ ne dzin Yahweh-nissi, (a ase nye, EWURADZE nye me frankaa), na ɔsee dɛ, EWURADZE esua: EWURADZE nye Amalek bedzi ako fi ebusuasantsen do ekodu ebusuasantsen do.
Jetro Kɛsera Moses Afei Jetro, Midian ɔsɔfo no, Moses n’asew no, tsee dza Nyankopɔn ayɛ ama Moses, nye ne man Israel no nyinara, mbrɛ EWURADZE esi eyi Israel efi Egypt.
Na Jetro, Moses n’asew no, faa Zipora, Moses yer a ɔama ɔasan kɔ no, nye ne mbabanyin beenu a ɔbaako ne dzin dze Gersom; osiandɛ ɔkaa dɛ, Mayɛ amanandze hɔho: na kor no so ne dzin dze Eliezer, osiandɛ ɔsee dɛ, M’egya ne Nyankopɔn yɛɛ mo mboa, na oyii me fii Farao n’afona anomu: na Jetro, Moses n’asew no, dze ne mbabanyin no nye ne yer no baa Moses nkyɛn wɔ sar no do mbrɛ ɔkɛkyeer nsera no, wɔ Nyankopɔn bepɔw no ho: na ɔsee Moses dɛ, Emi w’asew Jetro, nye wo yer, nye wo mbabanyin beenu no ka no ho, aba wo nkyɛn.
Na Moses fiir edzi kehyiaa n’asew, na ɔkotowee, na ɔfeew n’ano; na wobisabisaa hɔn apɔwmu; na wɔbaa asese mu.
Na Moses kaa dza osian Israel ntsi EWURADZE dze ayɛ Farao nye Egyptfo nyinara kyerɛɛ n’asew, awoko a ɔbaa hɔn do wɔ ɔkwan no mu nyinara, na mbrɛ EWURADZE sii yii hɔn no.
Na Jetro dzii dɛw wɔ papa a EWURADZE ayɛ ama Israel, wɔ dɛ oyii hɔn fii Egyptfo nsamu no nyinara ho.
Na Jetro see dɛ, Nhyira nka EWURADZE a oeyi hom efi Egyptfo nsamu, na woefi Farao nsamu; ɔno a oeyi ɔman no efi Egyptfo nsaadze.
Afei na mehu dɛ EWURADZE yɛ kɛse kyɛn enyame nyinara: nyew, adze a wɔdze dzi hɔn do nkontompɔsɛm no ara mu a. Na Jetro, Moses n’asew no, faa ɔhyew afɔr nye okum afɔr kɛmaa Nyankopɔn: na Aaron nye Israel mpanyin nyinara baa dɛ wɔnye Moses n’asew no ribedzidzi wɔ Nyankopɔn enyim.
Moses Yi Atsɛmbuafo Na ɔbaa dɛ adze kyee no, Moses tsenaa famu dɛ orubu ɔman no atsɛn: na ɔman no gyinaa Moses do tsentsen fi anapa kodur ewimbir.
Na aber a Moses n’asew hun dza ɔyɛe maa ɔman no nyinara no, ɔsee dɛ, Ebɛnadze na ereyɛ ma ɔman yi?
Ɔyɛ dɛn ntsi na woara nko etse hɔ, na ɔman no nyinara gyinagyina wo do tsentsen fi anapa ebodu ewimbir yi?
Na Moses see n’asew no dɛ, Osiandɛ ɔman no ba me nkyɛn Nyankopɔn hɔ ebisa: sɛ wonya asɛm bi a, wɔba me nkyɛn; na mubu nyimpa nye ne nyɛnko ntamu atsɛn, na mema wohu Nyankopɔn n’ahyɛdze, nye ne mbra.
Na Moses n’asew no see no dɛ, Adze a eyɛ yi onnye.
Ampa ebɛberɛ, ɔwo nye ɔman a wɔka wo ho yi nyina, osiandɛ adze no yɛ dur dodow ma wo; ɔwo woara nko irunntum nnyɛ.
Afei tsie me ndze, mebɛma wo apam, na Nyankopɔn ndzi w’ekyir; ɔwo gyina Nyankopɔn afamu ma ɔman no, na fa nsɛm no brɛ Nyankopɔn: na kyerɛkyerɛ hɔn ahyɛdze no nye mbra no, na ma wonhu ɔkwan kor a ɔwɔ dɛ wɔnantsew mu, na edwuma a ɔwɔ dɛ wɔyɛ.
Afei so yiyi ɔman no nyinara mu mbanyin a wotum a wosuro Nyankopɔn a wɔyɛ anokwafo a wokyir enyikaber, na fa hɔn sisi hɔn do, ma wɔnyɛ apem apem do mpanyin, ɔha ɔha do mpanyin, eduonum eduonum do mpanyin, nye du du do mpanyin; na ma wombu ɔman no ntsɛn aber nyinara mu: na ɔmbra dɛ asɛnkɛse biara dze wɔmfa mbrɛ wo, na nsɛnketseaba nyinara dze, hɔnara wondzi: ama aayɛ wo do har, na wɔnye wo aasoa adzesoa no.
Sɛ eyɛ dɛm adze yi, na Nyankopɔn hyɛ wo dɛm a, ɔno na ibotum asɔw, na ɔman yi nyinara so bɔkɔ hɔn tsenabew dwudwoodwo.
Nna Moses tsiee n’asew ne ndze, na ɔyɛɛ dza ɔsee no nyinara.
Na Moses yiyii Israel nyinara mu nyimpa a wotum, na ɔyɛɛ hɔn etsitsir wɔ ɔman no do, apem apem do mpanyin, ɔha ɔha do mpanyin, eduonum eduonum do mpanyin, nye du du do mpanyin.
Na wobuu ɔman no ntsɛn aber nyinara mu: nsɛm a ɔyɛ dzen no wɔdze brɛɛ Moses, na nsɛnketseaba dze hɔnara wodzii.
Na Moses gyaa n’asew no kwan; na ɔfaa no kwan kɔr nankasa n’asaase do.
Israelmba No Ba Sinai Bosoom a otsia ebiasa a Israelmba sii mu fii Egypt asaase do no, da no ara na wɔbaa Sinai sar do.
Na aber a wotui fii Refidim, na wɔbaa Sinai sar do no, wɔkyeer nsera wɔ sar no do; na hɔ na Israel kyeer nsera wɔ bepɔw no enyim.
Na Moses fowee kɔr Nyankopɔn nkyɛn, na EWURADZE fii bepɔw no do frɛɛ no see dɛ, Dɛm na se Jakob fi, na ka kyerɛ Israelmba; Hom ehu dza medze mayɛ Egyptfo, na mbrɛ mosoaa hom nkɔr ntsaban do, na medze hom baa mara me nkyɛn.
Dɛm ntsi afei, sɛ hom betsie me ndze ara ampa, na woedzi m’ahyɛmu do a, ɔnodze, hom bɛyɛ egyapadze a ɔsom bo efi aman nyinara mu ama me: osiandɛ asaase nyinara yɛ medze: na hom bɛyɛ asɔfo ahendzi, nye ɔman krɔnkrɔn ama me.
Iyinom nye nsɛm a fa ka kyerɛ Israelmba no.
Na Moses bae na ɔbɛfrɛɛ ɔman mpanyimfo no, na ɔdze nsɛm yi a EWURADZE dze hyɛɛ no nyinara too hɔn enyim.
Na ɔman no nyinara bɔɔ mu buae, na wɔsee dɛ, Dza EWURADZE aka nyinara, yɛbɛyɛ.
Na Moses kɛkaa ɔman no hɔn nsɛm no kyerɛɛ EWURADZE.
Na EWURADZE see Moses dɛ, Hwɛ, mereba wo nkyɛn wɔ mununkum kebii mu, ama sɛ menye wo kasa a ɔman no aatse, na eso wɔaagye wo edzi daa.
Na Moses kaa ɔman no hɔn nsɛm no kyerɛɛ EWURADZE.
Na EWURADZE see Moses dɛ, Kɔ ɔman no nkyɛn, na tsew hɔn ho ndɛ nye ɔkyena, na ma wɔnhohor hɔn ntar, na wonsiesie hɔnho nsie da a otsia ebiasa no: na da a otsia ebiasa no EWURADZE besian wɔ ɔman no nyinara enyim aba bepɔw Sinai do.
Na bɔ ɔman no ho ɔheban hyia, se dɛ, Hom nhwɛ homho yie, ma hom aammfow bepɔw no, anaa hom annkɛka ne he: obiara a ɔbɛka bepɔw no oku na woboku no: nsa biara nnka no, mbom abo na wonsiw no, anaa tow na wɔntow no ma onhwira mu; sɛ abowa o, nyimpa o, orinnya nkwa: sɛ abɛn no hɛn kyɛr a, wɔmfow bepɔw no.
Na Moses sianee fi bepɔw no do kɔr ɔman no nkyɛn, na ɔtseew ɔman no ho; na wɔhohoor hɔn ntar.
Na ɔsee ɔman no dɛ, Hom nsiesie homho nsie da a otsia ebiasa no: mma wɔnnkɔ ɔbaa biara ho.
Na ɔbaa dɛ da a otsia ebiasa no, anapa no, asenaman nye enyinam, nye mununkum kebii baa bepɔw no do, na abɛn ndze dzendzen mbordo; na ɔman a wɔwɔ nseraban no mu nyinara ho popoe.
Na Moses dze ɔman no fir edzi fii nseraban no mu dɛ worikehyia Nyankopɔn; na wokegyinagyinaa bepɔw no ase afamu.
Na bepɔw Sinai no nyinara rupun wusiw, osiandɛ EWURADZE nam gya mu sianee baa do: na no wusiw no tui kɔr sor dɛ fononoo mu wusiw, na bepɔw no nyinara wosoow kɛsenara.
Na abɛn no ne ndze yɛɛ dzendzenndzen dodow no, Moses kasae, na Nyankopɔn dze ndze gyee no do.
Na EWURADZE sianee baa bepɔw Sinai do, wɔ bepɔw no etsifi: na EWURADZE frɛɛ Moses dɛ ɔnkɔ bepɔw no etsifi: na Moses fowee kɔree.
Na EWURADZE see Moses dɛ, Sian famu behyia ɔman no, amma wɔaanntsetsew mu ammba EWURADZE nkyɛn ammbɔhwɛ, ma hom mu pii aanntotɔ.
Na ma asɔfo no so a wɔba EWURADZE nkyɛn no ntsew hɔnho, amma EWURADZE eenntu annhyɛ hɔn do.
Na Moses see EWURADZE dɛ, Ɔman no runntum mmfow mmba bepɔw Sinai do: osiandɛ woara hyɛɛ hɛn dɛ, Bɔ bepɔw no ho ɔheban hyia, na tsew ho.
Na EWURADZE see no dɛ, Kɔ, sian famu; na fow bra, ɔwo, nye Aaron ka wo ho: na mma asɔfo no nye ɔman no nntsetsew mu mmfow mmba EWURADZE nkyɛn, amma oeenntu annhyɛ hɔn do.
Nna Moses sianee kɔr ɔman no nkyɛn, na ɔkɛkaa kyerɛɛ hɔn.
Mbrasɛm Du No Na Nyankopɔn kaa nsɛm yi nyinara, see dɛ, Emi nye EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn a miyii wo wɔ Egypt asaase do, wɔ nkowaasom fi mu no.
Mma nnya enyame fofor nnka mo ho.
Mma nnyɛ ohonyi bi, anaa adze a ɔwɔ wimu wɔ sor, anaa dza ɔwɔ asaase do wɔ famu, anaa dza ɔwɔ nsu mu wɔ asaase ase, ne saso mma woho: mma mmbɔ wo mu adze mma hɔn, na nnsom hɔn: na emi EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn meyɛ Nyame nyinkufo a medze egyanom hɔn emumuyɛ bɔhwɛ mba, ekodu ebusuasantsen ebiasa nye anan a wɔtan me do; na muhu mpempem a wɔdɔ me na wodzi me mbransɛm do mbɔbɔr.
Mma mmbɔ EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn dzin gyangyan, na EWURADZE nnkɛma nyia no a ɔbɔ ne dzin gyangyan afa noho tɔtrɔtɔ.
Kaa ahomgyeda no na sie no krɔnkrɔn.
Nda esia na yɛ edwuma, na dzi wo dwuma nyinara: na da a otsia esuon no yɛ EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn ahomgyeda: mma nnyɛ edwuma biara wɔ mu, ɔwo o, wo babanyin o, wo babaa o, w’akowaa o, w’afonabaa o, wo mbowa o, wo hɔho a ɔwɔ wo kuropon mu o: na nda esia na EWURADZE bɔɔ sor nye asaase, po, nye dza ɔwɔ mu nyinara, na ɔhoom da a otsia esuon no: dɛm ntsi na EWURADZE hyiraa ahomgyeda no, na ɔyɛɛ no krɔnkrɔn.
Dzi w’egya nye wo na nyi: ama wo nda aawar wɔ asaase a EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn dze rema wo no do.
Mma nndzi ewu.
Mma nnto awar.
Mma nnwia adze.
Mma nngye wo nyɛnko ho dasewia.
Mma w’enyi mmber wo nyɛnko fi, mma w’enyi mmber ne yer, anaa n’akowaa, anaa n’afonabaa, anaa ne nantwi, anaa n’asoaso, anaa biribiara a ɔyɛ wo nyɛnko dze.
Suro Ka Ɔman No Na aber a ɔman no nyinara hun asenaman no, nye enyinam no, nye bepɔw a orupun wusiw no, na wɔtsee abɛn ndze no, hɔn ho popoe, na wokegyinaa ekyirekyir.
Na wɔsee Moses dɛ, Woara nye hɛn nkasa, na yebetsie: na mma Nyankopɔn nnye hɛn nnkasa, ɔno yebowuwu.
Na Moses see ɔman no dɛ, Mma hom nnsuro: na Nyankopɔn aba dɛ ɔrobɔsɔ hom ahwɛ, ama no ho suro aaba hom enyi do, ma hom aannyɛ bɔn.
Na ɔman no gyinaa ekyirekyir, na Moses twee bɛɛn sum kadoo no mbrɛ Nyankopɔn wɔ no.
Afɔrmbukyia Ho Mbra Na EWURADZE see Moses dɛ, Mbrɛ se Israelmba nye yi, Homara hom ehu dɛ mifi ɔsor na menye hom akasa.
Mma hom nnyɛ me saso enyame bi mma hom ho; dwetɛ enyame, anaa sika enyame o, mma hom nnyɛ.
Dɛtse afɔrmbukyia na yɛ ma me, na dze wo hyew afɔr, nye w’asomdwee afɔr, wo nguan, nye w’anantwi no bɔ do afɔr: beebiara a mebɛma wɔakaa me dzin no, mebɛba wo nkyɛn na mebehyira wo.
Na sɛ ereyɛ abo afɔrmbukyia ama me: mma mmfa abo a woetwa nnsia osiandɛ sɛ ema w’edwindadze do bɔ do a, egu ho fi.
Nkyii so mma mmfow atwer nnkɔ afɔrmbukyia do, amma w’adagyaw aannda edzi wɔ do.
Nkowaa Ho Mbra Na iyinom nye ntsɛmbusɛm a fa to hɔn enyim.
Sɛ etɔ akowaa a ɔyɛ Hebriwnyi a, mfe esia na ɔnsom: na dza otsia esuon no mu ɔmfa no ho ndzi nkɔ kwa.
Sɛ noara nko na ɔbae a, noara nko nkɔ: sɛ ɔawar a, ɔno ne yer nye no nkɔ.
Sɛ no wura ma no yer, na ɔwo mbabanyin anaa mbabaa ma no a, yer no nye ne mba nyɛ ɔbaa no no wura dze, na noara nko nkɔ.
Na sɛ akowaa no ka no petee dɛ, Modɔ mo wura, me yer, nye me mba; mennkɛfa moho edzi akɔ a: ɔno no wura no mfa no mbra Nyankopɔn enyim, na ɔmfa no mbra ɔpon ho, anaa ɔpon dua ho; na no wura no mfa fitsii mfitsi n’asomu; na ɔnsom no daa.
Na sɛ ɔbanyin bi tɔn ne babaa ma ɔkɛyɛ afonabaa a, ɔnodze mma ɔmmfa noho nndzi nnkɔ dɛ mbrɛ akowaa no yɛ.
Sɛ ɔnnsɔ no wura a noara ɔagye no ayewar no enyi a, ɔnodze wɔmma wɔmbɔpon no: onnyi tum dɛ ɔtɔn no ma ɔnanaben bi, osiandɛ ɔadaadaa no.
Na sɛ ɔgye no ayewar ma ne babanyin a, ɔnyɛ no dɛ mbrɛ wɔdze yɛ mbabaa.
Sɛ ɔgye yer fofor ma no a; mma onnkuw n’edziban, n’akataho, nye n’awar edwuma do.
Na sɛ ɔannyɛ iyinom ebiasa yi amma no a, ɔnodze ɔmfa noho ndzi nkɔ kwa, sika bi nnyi mu.
Basabasayɛ a Ɔdze Pira Anaa Owu Ba Nyia ɔbɔ nyimpa ma owu no, oku na wonku no.
Na sɛ nyimpa annkɔ atsɛwee, na Nyankopɔn na ɔama ne nsa apa dze a; ɔno mibeyi beebi mama wo na oeeguan akɔ hɔ.
Na sɛ nyimpa bi ba ne nyɛnko do enyidaho mu dze ndaadaa ku no a; yi no fi m’afɔrmbukyia ho, ma onwu.
Na nyia ɔbɔ n’egya, anaa ne na no, oku na wonku no.
Na nyia owia nyimpa, na ɔtɔn no no, anaa sɛ wohu no wɔ ne nsamu a, oku na wonku no.
Na nyia ɔdom n’egya, anaa ne na no, oku na wonku no.
Na sɛ nyimpa bi woridzi aper, na kor bɔ kor no ɔbo, anaa kutuku, na oennwu, na ɔka no to ne mpa do a: sɛ ɔsoɛr bio, na osuo no poma mu nantsew fir edzi a, ɔnodze nyia ɔbɔɔ no no no ho nyɛ no tɔtrɔtɔ: ne mber a asɛɛ no nko na ontua kaw, na ɔmma wɔnsa no yarba koraa.
Na sɛ nyimpa bobɔ n’akowaa, anaa n’afonabaa abaa, ma owu ne nsaano a; ɔno wondzi no wer.
Naaso sɛ ɔtsena hɔ da kor anaa nda ebien a, mma wonndzi no wer: osiandɛ ɔyɛ ne sika.
Na sɛ mbanyin roko, na wopira onyinsemfo, ma ɔpon ɔba, na mbusu bi ammba ekyir dze a: brabo na wɔngye no, dɛ mbrɛ ɔbaa no no kun dze bɔto no do no; na ontua no dɛ mbrɛ ntsɛmbuafo no bɛkyerɛ no.
Na sɛ mbusu bi ba ekyir a, ɔnodze fa nkwa hyɛ nkwa ananmu, enyiwa hyɛ enyiwa ananmu, se hyɛ se ananmu, nsa hyɛ nsa ananmu, anan hyɛ anan ananmu, hyehyew hyɛ hyehyew ananmu, ɔkam hyɛ ɔkam ananmu, mfemfem hyɛ mfemfem ananmu.
Na sɛ obi bɔ n’akowaa enyiwa, anaa n’afonabaa enyiwa na ɔsɛɛ no a, n’enyiwa no ntsi ɔmma ɔmfa noho ndzi nkɔ.
Na sɛ ɔbɔ n’akowaa ne se tu no, anaa n’afonabaa ne se a; ne se no ntsi ɔmma ɔmfa noho ndzi nkɔ.
Ewuranom Hɔn Asodzii Na sɛ ɔnantwi sɛ ɔbanyin anaa ɔbaa, ma owu a, ɔno ɔnantwi no wonsiw no abo, na mma wonndzi ne nam; na ɔnantwi no wura dze wongyaa no.
Na sɛ ɔnantwi no ɔtɔ sesɛ dada na wɔama no wura atse, na oennsie no fie, na oekoku ɔbanyin anaa ɔbaa dze a; ɔnantwi no wonsiw no abo, na no wura no so wonku no.
Sɛ wɔbɛgye no mpata a, ɔno ɔmma adze biara a wɔbɛgye no no mfa ntɔ no nkwa.
Sɛ ɔbabanyin na ɔasɛ no o, ɔbabaa na ɔasɛ no o, atsɛmbu yi ara na wɔmfa mbu no.
Sɛ ɔnantwi no sɛ akowaa anaa afonabaa a; ɔno ɔmma hɔn wura dwetɛ dwetɛbona eduasa, na wonsiw ɔnantwi no abo.
Na sɛ nyimpa bi kobue amona do, anaa sɛ nyimpa bi kotu amona na ɔannkata do, na ɔnantwi anaa asoaso kɔhwe mu a, ma no wura no nhyɛ ananmu; ɔmfa sika mma hɔn wura no, na mbowafun no nyɛ nedze.
Na sɛ nyimpa kor bi ne nantwi pira kor nedze ma owu a; ɔno wɔntɔn nantwi nyikan no, na wɔnkyɛ ne tsiadze no; na fun no so wɔnkyɛ.
Mbom sɛ wonyim dɛ ɔnantwi no ɔtɔ sesɛ dada, na no wura no ammfa no ennsie fie a; ɔno ɔmfa ɔnantwi nhyɛ ɔnantwi ananmu, na abowafun no nyɛ noara nedze.
Kaw No Ntuae Ho Mbra Sɛ nyimpa bi kowia nantwi, anaa guan, na oku no, anaa ɔtɔn no a; ɔmfa anantwi enum nhyɛ nantwi kor ananmu, na nguan anan nhyɛ guan kor ananmu ntua kaw.
Sɛ wohu owifo no dɛ oebubu mu reba, na wɔbɔ no adze ma owu a, bɔgya asodzi nnyi hɔ mma no.
Sɛ ewia pue no do a, bɔgya asodzi wɔ hɔ ma no: ahyɛnanmu na ɔnyɛ; sɛ onnyi hwee a, ɔno n’adzewia ntsi wɔntɔn no.
Sɛ wohu adzewiadze no wɔ ne nsamu enyikan a, sɛ ɔyɛ ɔnantwi o, asoaso o, oguan o, ontua kaw mbɔho.
Sɛ nyimpa bi ma wodzi haban anaa wenyin ture mu adze, na ogyaa n’abowa ma okedzi nyimpa kor so ne haban mu adze a, ɔmfa nankasa ne haban mu ndzepa, nye nankasa no wenyin ture mu ndzepa bi nhyɛ ananmu.
Sɛ ogya pue, na ɔkɔsɔ nsoɛ mu ma eburow ekuwekuw, anaa eburow a ogyinagyina hɔ, anaa haban no hyew a; ɔhyɛ na nyia ɔsɔɔ gya no nhyɛ ananmu.
Sɛ nyimpa bi dze sika anaa efidze ma ne nyɛnko esie, na wowia no wɔ nyimpa no ne fie a; sɛ wohu owifo no a, ontua kaw mbɔho.
Sɛ woennhu owifo no a, ɔno fiwura no ntwe mbɛn Nyankopɔn nhwɛ kyerɛ dɛ ɔnntsen ne nsa nnka ne nyɛnko n’adze no a. Na mbrato ho asɛm biara, sɛ ɔyɛ ɔnantwi dze o, asoaso dze o, oguan dze o, anaa adze a ayew biara a obi bɛse wɔ ho dɛ, Ɔno nye yi o, wɔmfa hɔn beenu nyina hɔn asɛm mbra Nyankopɔn enyim; nyia Nyankopɔn bobu no fɔ no, ontua kaw mbɔho mma ne nyɛnko no.
Sɛ nyimpa bi dze asoaso, anaa nantwi, anaa guan, anaa abowa biara ma ne nyɛnko esie; na owu anaa opira, anaa wɔka no to hamu, na nyimpa bi ennhu a: EWURADZE ntam mbra hɔn beenu no ntamu, kyerɛ dɛ ɔnntsen ne nsa nnka ne nyɛnko no n’adze no a: na adze no wura no ɔmpen do, na mma ɔnnhyɛ ananmu.
Sɛ wowia no wɔ ne nkyɛn dze a, ɔnhyɛ adze no wura ananmu.
Sɛ wɔatsetsew no esinesin a, ɔmfa mbra mbedzi dase; dza wɔatsetsew no no mma ɔnnhyɛ ananmu.
Na sɛ nyimpa bi kɛfɛm biribi wɔ ne nyɛnko hɔ, na ɔsɛɛ, anaa owu, dɛ adze no wura no no ho nnyi mu a, ɔhyɛ na ɔnhyɛ ananmu.
Sɛ adze no wura no no ho wɔ mu a, mma ɔnnhyɛ ananmu: sɛ ɔyɛ apaabɔ adze a, na ogyina n’apaabɔdze do.
Abrabɔ Na Nyamesom Ho Mbra Na sɛ nyimpa bi kɛdaadaa ɔbaabun a wɔnngyee no yer, na ɔnye no da a, ɔno ɔmma ne tsiadze ma ɔnyɛ ne yer.
Sɛ n’egya pow koraa dɛ ɔdze no ma no a, onker sika mma, dɛ mbrɛ mbaabun tsiadze tse.
Mma mma ɔbaa anyɛn kwan ma ɔntsena ase.
Obiara a ɔnye abowa bɛda no, oku na wonku no.
Nyia ɔbɔbɔ afɔr ama onyame biara, na nnyɛ EWURADZE nko no, wɔnsɛɛ no koraa.
Na ɔhɔho dze mma nnyɛ no bɔn, nkyii so mma nnhaw no: osiandɛ hom yɛɛ ahɔho wɔ Egypt asaase do.
Mma hom nntseetsee ɔbaa kunafo biara, anaa egyankaba.
Sɛ etseetsee hɔn ɔkwan biara mu, na wosu frɛ me dze a, otsie ara na mibetsie hɔn sufrɛ no; na m’ebufuw ano bɛyɛ dzen, na medze afona boku hom; na hom yernom bɛyɛ ekunafo na hom mba ayɛ ngyanka.
Sɛ efɛm me man mu ohianyi biara a ɔnye wo wɔ hɔ sika a, mma nnyɛ dɛ ɔpempensinyi; nkyii so mma hom nngye no nsiho.
Sɛ egye wo nyɛnko tam ahoba a, wi rotɔ no fa san ma no: osiandɛ ɔnoara nko nye n’akataho, no honam ho tam a: ebɛnadze na ɔmfa nda?
Na ɔbɛba dɛ, sɛ osu frɛ me a, mibetsie: osiandɛ mbɔbɔrhufo nye me.
Mma nnyeyaw Nyankopɔn, anaa nndom wo man mu ɔpanyin.
Mma nnkyinkyim dɛ edze wo ndɔbaa anaa wo nsa mu bi bɔbɔ afɔr.
Wo mbabanyin mu abakan no fa ma me.
Dɛmara na yɛ w’anantwi, na ɔnye wo nguan: nda esuon na ɔnye ne na ntsena; da a otsia awɔtwe no fa no brɛ me.
Na hom bɛyɛ nyimpa krɔnkrɔn ama me: dɛm ntsi mma hom nndzi bɔnam bi a abowa atsetsew mu wɔ haban mu; hom ntow nkyen mbɔdɔm.
Pɛrpɛryɛ Mma nntsie atorsɛm: mma nnye omumuyɛfo nndzi nsawosow dɛ ebɛyɛ ɔdasefo ɔkontompɔnyi.
Mma nndzi ɔdodow ekyir nnkɛyɛ bɔn; nkyii so mma nnkasa asɛm bi mu nnkedzi ɔdodow ekyir nndan atsɛmbu enyi: nkyii so mma nndzi nnkɔ ohianyi afa wɔ n’asɛm mu.
Sɛ ekɔto wo tamfo ne nantwi anaa n’asoaso dɛ ɔatɔ gon a, fa no san ekyir brɛ no bio.
Sɛ ihu nyia okyir wo n’asoaso dɛ ɔhyɛ n’adzesoa ase, na nkyɛ ennkɛpɛ dɛ eboa no a, boa na nye no mboa no.
Mma nndan wo hianyi n’atsɛmbu enyi wɔ n’asɛm mu.
Twe woho fi atorsɛm ho kɔ ekyirekyir; na mma nnku nyia odzi bem na ɔtsen: osiandɛ murummbu omumuyɛfo bem.
Na mma nngye akyɛdze: osiandɛ akyɛdze ma hɔn a wɔwɔ enyiwa fura, na ɔkyeakyea atseneneefo nsɛm.
Na mma nnhaw ɔhɔho: osiandɛ hom nyim ɔhɔho n’akoma, ɔnam dɛ hom yɛɛ ahɔho wɔ Egypt asaase do ntsi.
Afe Esuon No Na Nda Esuon No Na mfe esia na pe w’asaase do aba, na boaboa no ndɔbaa ano sie: na afe a otsia esuon no dze ma ɔngye n’ahom na ɔnda hɔ kwa; ma wo man mu ehiafo ndzi: na dza wobegya no, hamu abowa ebedzi.
Dɛmara na yɛ wo wenyin ture, nye wo ngodua ture.
Nda esia na fa yɛ w’edwuma, na da a otsia esuon no fa hom: na wo nantwi nye w’asoasopɔnkɔ eenya ahomgye: na w’afonabaa ba, nye ɔhɔho no so eenya ahomgye.
Na hom nhwɛ yie wɔ ndzɛmba a maka akyerɛ hom nyinara ho: na mma hom mmbobɔ enyame afofor bi dzin, nkyii so mma mma wɔnntse no wɔ w’anomu.
Afahyɛ Akɛse Ebiasa No Mpɛn ebiasa na hyɛ fa ma me wɔ afrenhyia mu.
Sie epitsi afahyɛ no: nda esuon na dzi epitsi boodoo, dɛ mbrɛ mehyɛɛ wo no, wɔ mber a wɔahyɛ no wɔ bosoom Abib mu no (osiandɛ no mu na ifii Egypt bae); na mma obiara mmfa nsapan mmbefir m’enyim: na otwaber afahyɛ no, w’edwumadze a eyɛ no wɔ haban mu no mu nduadzewakan no: na anoboaboa afahyɛ no wɔ afe no ewiei, aber a eboaboa wo ndwumadze ano fi haban mu no.
Wo mbanyin nyinara mbefir EWURADZE Nyankopɔn enyim mpɛn ebiasa wɔ afrenhyia mu.
Mma mmfa mbɔrkaw nnka m’afɔrbɔ bɔgya no ho mmbɔ afɔr; nkyii so mma m’afahyɛ mu seradze no ɔnnko hɔ anadwe nyinara ma onnkodu adzekyee.
Wo daadze mu nduadzewakan mu kan dze no fa bra EWURADZE wo Nyankopɔn fie.
Mma nnoa apɔnkyeba wɔ ne na no numfonsu mu.
EWURADZE N’anohoba Na Mboa Hwɛ, morosoma ɔbɔfo ma oeedzi w’enyim akɔhwɛ wo wɔ ɔkwan no mu, na ɔdze wo ekodu bea a mesiesie no do.
Hom nhwɛ yie wɔ no ho, na wontsie ne ndze; mma wonnyi no ebufuw: na ɔnnkɛfa hom mbrato akyɛ hom; osiandɛ me dzin wɔ no mu.
Na sɛ itsie ne ndze ara ampa, na eyɛ dza meka nyinara a; ɔnodze, mebɛyɛ ɔtamfo ama w’atamfo, nye ɔhohiahianyi mama w’ahohiahiafo.
Na mo bɔfoe no bedzi w’enyim akɔ, na ɔdze wo ekodu Amorifo, Hitifo, Perizfo, Keenanfo, Hivifo, nye Jebusfo nkyɛn: na mubotwa hɔn egu.
Mma mmbɔ wo mu adze mma hɔn enyame, na nnsom hɔn, na nnyɛ hɔn ndzeyɛɛ so: na butuw na butuw hɔn, na bubu hɔn edum mu esinesin.
Na hom nsom EWURADZE hom Nyankopɔn, na obehyira w’edziban, nye wo nsu do; na mibeyi yarba mefi wo mu.
Obiara nnkɔpon ɔba, na ɔnnkɛyɛ ɔbɔnyin so, wɔ w’asaase do: mebɛma wo nda no dodow ano edu.
Mebɛma mo ho hu edzi w’enyim, na mebɛka aman a ebɛba hɔn do nyinara megu, na mama w’atamfo nyinara adan hɔn ekyir ama wo.
Na mobɔsoma nkotokrodo ma woeedzi w’enyim, apam Hivifo, Keenanfo, nye Hitifo no wɔ w’enyim.
Mennkɛpam hɔn wɔ w’enyim wɔ afe kor mu; ɔno bɛyɛ na asaase no adan amamfo, na hamu mbowa adɔɔ so wɔ wo do.
Nkakrankakra na mebɛpam hɔn wɔ w’enyim, ekodu dɛ ebɔdɔr, na enya asaase no.
Na mubotwa wo he efi Mbɛw Po no ho araa ekodu Filistiafo po no ho, na medze mefi sar no ano ekodu Esutsen no ho: na mibeyi asaase no do mba mahyɛ wo nsa; na ebɛpam hɔn wɔ w’enyim.
Mma nnye hɔn nye hɔn enyame so nndzi ahyɛmu.
Mma wɔnntsena w’asaase do, ɔno bɛyɛ na wɔama ayɛ bɔn etsia me: na sɛ esom hɔn enyame a, ampaara ɔbɛyɛ efir ama wo.
Ahyɛmu No No Nsɔwano Na ɔsee Moses dɛ, Fow bra EWURADZE nkyɛn, ɔwo, nye Aaron, Nadab, nye Abihu, nye Israel mpanyimfo mu eduosuon; na hom nkɔsɔr wɔ ekyirekyir: na Moses nko ntwe mbɛn EWURADZE; na hɔn dze, mma wɔnntwe mmbɛn; nkyii so mma ɔman no nnye no mmfow nnkɔ.
Na Moses bae bɛkaa EWURADZE ne nsɛm no nyinara kyerɛɛ ɔman no, na atsɛmbu no nyinara: na ɔman no nyinara dze ndze kor buae, na wɔsee dɛ, Nsɛm a EWURADZE aka no nyinara yɛbɛyɛ.
Na Moses kyerɛɛw EWURADZE ne nsɛm no nyinara, na ɔsoɛɛr anapaatu, na osii afɔrmbukyia wɔ bepɔw no ase, nye edum duebien, dɛ mbrɛ Israel ebusuakuw duebien no ano tse.
Na ɔsomaa Israelmba no mu mberantsɛ a wɔdze anantwi kɔbɔɔ ɔhyew afɔr, nye asomdwee afɔr maa EWURADZE.
Na Moses faa bɔgya no ne fa guguu mbɛɛsen mu, na ɔdze bɔgya fa no petsee afɔrmbukyia no do.
Na ɔfaa ahyɛmu nwoma no, na ɔkenkaan no wɔ ɔman no asomu: na wɔsee dɛ, Dza EWURADZE aka no nyinara yɛbɛyɛ, na yɛayɛ setsie.
Na Moses faa bɔgya no, na ɔdze petsee ɔman no do, na ɔsee dɛ, Hwɛ ahyɛmu a EWURADZE nye hom edzi wɔ nsɛm yi nyinara ho no no bɔgyaa nye yi.
Nna Moses, nye Aaron, Nadab, nye Abihu, nye Israel mpanyimfo mu eduosuon no fowee kɔree: na wohun Israel Nyankopɔn no; n’anan ase tse dɛ wɔdze hoabo ataa hɔ, na n’enyi tsew dɛ ɔsor noara.
Na ɔammfa ne nsa annto Israelmba mu ekunyin no do: na wɔhwɛɛ Nyankopɔn, na wodzidzii na wɔnomee.
Moses Kɔ Bepɔw Sinai Do Na EWURADZE see Moses dɛ, Fow bra me nkyɛn wɔ bepɔw no do, na tsena hɔ: na medze abopon, nye mbrasɛm a makyerɛw no mebɛma wo, ma aakyerɛkyerɛ hɔn.
Na Moses soɛree, ɔnye no somfo Josua: na Moses fowee kɔr Nyankopɔn ne bepɔw no do.
Na ɔsee mpanyimfo no dɛ, Hom ntsintsim ha ntweɔn hɛn ma onkodu dɛ yɛbɛba hom nkyɛn bio: na hwɛ, Aaron nye Hur nye hom wɔ ha: obiara a ɔwɔ asɛm bi no, wɔmma ɔntwe mbɛn hɔn.
Na Moses fowee kɔr bepɔw no do, na mununkum no bɛkataa bepɔw no do.
Na EWURADZE n’enyimnyam bɛtsenaa bepɔw Sinai do, na mununkum no kataa do nda esia: na da a otsia esuon no, ofi mununkum no mu frɛɛ Moses.
Na EWURADZE n’enyimnyam no hwɛbea ɔtse dɛ gya a ɔhyew adze wɔ bepɔw no etsifi wɔ Israelmba no enyiwa mu.
Na Moses kɛhɛɛn mununkum no ne finimfin, na ɔfowee kɔr bepɔw no do: na Moses dzii bepɔw no do adaduanan adzekyee nye adzesaa.
Ehyiadzibuw Ho Afɔrbɔdze Na EWURADZE kasaa kyerɛɛ Moses dɛ, Ka kyerɛ Israelmba ma wɔmfa ayɛyɛdze mbrɛ me: nyimpa biara a n’akoma pɛ no no hɔ na hom ngye m’ayɛyɛdze.
Na iyi nye ayɛyɛdze a hom ngye no wɔ hɔn hɔ; sika, nye dwetɛ, nye boran; nye bibir, nye ɔberdum, nye serdaa, nye ndwera fɛɛfɛw, nye mpɔnkyenhwi; nye nguannyin nwoma a wɔahyɛ no memen, nye nsukraman nwoma; nye akeesia dua; kandzea ho ngo, ɔserango ho nduhuam, nye nduhuam a wɔhyew ho edur; abo a no su tse dɛ epopobibir, nye abo a wɔdze besisi egugudo no, nye akatabo no mu no.
Na ma wɔnyɛ krɔnkrɔnbea mma me; ma maatsena hɔn mu.
Dɛ mbrɛ merekyerɛ wo no nyinara, ntamadan no saso, nye no mu ndzɛmba nyinara ne saso, dɛmara pɛ na hom nyɛ no.
Ahyɛmudaka Ho Nhyehyɛɛ Na wɔnyɛ akeesia dua adaka: ne tsentsen nyɛ bɛyɛ basafa kor na fa, na ne tɛtɛr bɛyɛ anamɔn ebien na fa, na no krɔn so bɛyɛ anamɔn ebien na fa.
Na fa sika mapa dura ho, no mu nye n’ekyir na fa dura, na yɛ ho sika hankra twa ho hyia.
Na gu no ho sika nkaba anan, na fa tuatua n’anan anan no ho; na nkaba ebien ndzi n’afa fakor, na nkaba ebien ndzi n’afa no ho.
Na fa dua sian mpoma, na fa sika dura ho.
Na fa mpoma no hyehyɛ nkaba no mu wɔ adaka no ne nkyɛn mu, ma wɔmfa nsoa adaka no.
Mpoma no nhyehyɛ adaka no ne nkaba no mu: mma wonnyiyi mmfi mu.
Na fa dase a medze mebɛma wo no to adaka no mu.
Na fa sika mapa yɛ mbɔbɔrhu egua: ne tsentsen nyɛ bɛyɛ basafa kor nye fa, na ne tɛtɛr bɛyɛ anamɔn ebien nye fa.
Na yɛ sika kerubim ebien; ɔbor edwuma na fa yɛ, wɔ mbɔbɔrhu egua ne tsir ebien no do.
Na yɛ kerubim kor wɔ ne tsir kor, nye kerubim kor wɔ ne tsir kor so: mbɔbɔrhu egua no mu na hom mma kerubim ebien no mfi wɔ ne tsir ebien no do.
Na kerubim no ntserɛtserɛw hɔn ntsaban mu wɔ ɔsor, mfa hɔn ntsaban no nkata mbɔbɔrhu egua no do, hɔn enyim ndzi abɔenyim; mbɔbɔrhu egua no do na kerubim no hɔn enyim mbedzi.
Na fa mbɔbɔrhu egua no si adaka no do sor; na adaka no mu na fa dase a medze mebɛma wo no to.
Na hɔ na menye wo behyia, na mefi mbɔbɔrhu egua no do wɔ kerubim ebien a wɔwɔ dasedaka no do no ntamu maka wo ndzɛmba a mebɛhyɛ wo dɛ fa kyerɛ Israelmba no nyinara ho nsɛm.
Pon No Ho Nhyehyɛɛ Na fa akeesia dua pon: ne tsentsen nyɛ basafa kor, ne tɛtɛr anamɔn kor nye fa, na no krɔn bɛyɛ anamɔn ebien nye fa.
Na fa sika mapa dura ho, na yɛ ho sika hankra hyia.
Na yɛ ho ntotoano a ɔbɛyɛ nsatseama hyia, na yɛ ntotoano no ho sika hankra hyia.
Na yɛ ho sika nkaba anan, na fa nkaba no sisi nkutuw anan a ɔwowɔ n’anan anan no ho no do.
Ntotoano no nkyɛn papaapa na nkaba no ndzi, ma ɔnyɛ beebi mbrɛ wɔdze mpoma no bɛhyehyɛ dze asoa ɔpon no.
Na fa akeesia dua sinsian mpoma no, na fa sika duradura ho, ama wɔdze aasoa pon no.
Na yɛ do mboyaa, nye ntser, nye nkɔɔpow, nye nkorbaa a wɔdze bohue: sika mapa na fa yɛ.
Na fa kyerɛpaanoo si pon no do wɔ m’enyim daa.
Kandzeadua Ho Nhyehyɛɛ Na fa sika mapa yɛ kandzeadua: ɔbor edwuma na fa yɛ kandzeadua no, n’anan, nye no dua; no ho mpokuwa, no nkukuduuduw, nye ne nhyiren, mfi sin kor no ara mu: na abaw esia mfifi ne nkyɛn mu; kandzeadua n’abaw ebiasa mfi n’afa fakor, na kandzeadua no n’abaw ebiasa so mfi n’afa kor so: mpokuwa ebiasa a wɔayɛ no dɛ almɔnd nhyiren wɔ abaw kor ho, kukuduuduw nye nhyiren; na mpokuwa ebiasa a wɔayɛ no dɛ almɔnd nhyiren wɔ abaw kor no so ho, kukuduuduw nye nhyiren: dɛm na yɛ wɔ abaw esia a efifir wɔ kandzeadua no ho no ho: na kandzeadua no ho mpokuwa anan a wɔayɛ no dɛ almɔnd nhyiren, no kukuduuduw nye ne nhyiren: na kukuduuduw nhyɛ abaw ebien a otuatua ho no ase, na kukuduuduw nhyɛ abaw ebien a otuatua ho no ase, na kukuduuduw nhyɛ abaw ebien a otuatua ho no ase wɔ abaw esia a efifir kandzeadua no mu no ase.
No ho nkukuduuduw nye no ho abaw no mfi mu ara, ne nyinara sika mapa na wɔmfa nyɛ no ɔbor edwuma kor.
Na yɛ ne nkandzea no esuon: na wɔnsosɔ ne nkandzea no, ma ɔngyegye wɔ n’enyim.
Na no ho adabaa, nye no ho nsompokuwa nyɛ sika mapa.
Sika mapa kyɛpɛn kor na wɔmfa nyɛ, ɔnye no ho ndzɛmba yi nyinara.
Na hwɛ na yɛ no dɛ mbrɛ no nsusudo a wɔdze akyerɛ wo wɔ bepɔw no do no tse.
Ntamadan No Ho Nhyehyɛɛ Nkyii so fa nsensɛnho atam du yɛ ntamadan no; ndwera fɛɛfɛw a woefira, nye bibir, nye ɔberdum, nye serdaa na fa yɛ me kerubim a ɔyɛ odwimfo pa edwinsa.
Nsensɛnho tam kor ne tsentsen nyɛ basafa duanan, na nsensɛnho tam kor ne tɛtɛr nyɛ basafa ebien: nsensɛnho atam no nyinara no nsusui ngyina kor.
Wɔmfa nsensɛnho atam enum ntoatoa do kor ntoa kor so do; na nsensɛnho atam enum no so ntoatoa do kor ntoa kor so do.
Na fa bibir bobɔ nsensɛnho tam kor mbuano do etokur wɔ ano wɔ ntoae no do; na dɛmara na yɛ wɔ nsensɛnho tam a odzi ekyir no no mbuano do wɔ ntoae a otsia ebien no do.
Etokur eduonum na bobɔ wɔ nsensɛnho tam kor mu, na etokur eduonum so na bobɔ wɔ nsensɛnho tam a ɔwɔ ntoae a otsia ebien no so ano; etokur no ndzi abɔenyim nkorkor.
Na yɛ sika nkɔtɔkorba eduonum, na fa nkɔtɔkorba no yɛ ma nsensɛnho atam no kor ntoae kor so do: na ntamadan no nyɛ kor.
Na fa mpɔnkyenhwi yɛ nsensɛnho atam fa si buw wɔ ntamadan no do: yɛ no nsensɛnho atam dubiako.
Nsensɛnho tam kor ne tsentsen nyɛ basafa duenum, na nsensɛnho tam kor ne tɛtɛr nyɛ basafa ebien: nsensɛnho atam dubiako no no nsusui ngyina kor.
Na fa nsensɛnho atam enum toatoa yɛ no kor, na yɛ nsensɛnho atam esia so kor, na boka nsensɛnho tam a otsia esia no ma ɔnkata buw no do wɔ n’enyim.
Na yɛ etokur eduonum wɔ nsensɛnho tam kor a odzi ekyir no mbuano do wɔ ntoae no do, nye etokur eduonum so wɔ ntoae a otsia ebien no ne nsensɛnho tam no mbuano do.
Na yɛ mboran nkɔtɔkorba eduonum, na fa nkɔtɔkorba no susuo etokur no mu, na yɛ ma buw no ntoae mu, ma ɔnyɛ kor.
Na buw no ne nsensɛnho atam a aka sensɛn hɔ no, nsensɛnho tam fa no a aka no, nsensɛn ntamadan no ekyir.
Na buw no ne nsensɛnho atam no ne tsentsen mu anamɔn kor nye fa a abor do wɔ afa ha, nye anamɔn kor nye fa a abor do wɔ afa hɔ no nsensɛn ntamadan no ne nkyɛn nkyɛn wɔ afa ha nye afa ha nkata do.
Na fa nguannyin nwoma a wɔahyɛ no memen yɛ buw no ne nkatado; na fa nsukraman nwoma yɛ no sor akatado.
Na fa akeesia dua yɛ ntamadan no ne ntaabow a osisi hɔ.
Basafa enum nyɛ taabow ne tsentsen, na bɛyɛ anamɔn ebien nye fa nyɛ taabow kor ne tɛtɛr.
Anan ebien ntuatua taabow kor mu, nsusuo kor mu mfam kor so ho: dɛm na yɛ ma ntamadan no ne ntaabow nyinara.
Na yɛ ntamadan no ne ntaabow no, ntaabow eduonu ndzi pomu afamu nkyerɛ pomu.
Na yɛ ntaabow eduonu no n’ase dwetɛ ngyinado eduanan; ngyinado ebien nhyehyɛ taabow kor ase mma anan ebien no, na ngyinado ebien nhyehyɛ taabow kor so ase mma n’anan ebien no: na ntamadan no n’afa a otsia ebien no, odzi kwaamu afamu no, ntaabow eduonu: na no dwetɛ ngyinado eduanan no; ngyinado ebien nhyehyɛ taabow ase, na ngyinado ebien nhyehyɛ taabow kor so ase.
Na ntamadan no n’ekyir a odzi anee afamu no yɛ hɔ ntaabow esia.
Na yɛ ntaabow ebien ma ntamadan no no kutuw do wɔ n’ekyir afamu.
Na ɔmpam ho wɔ ase, na ɔnyɛ mu dɛmara nkodu no sor nkaba kor ho: dɛm na n’ebien nyina nyɛ; wondzi kutuw ebien no do.
Na ɔnyɛ ntaabow awɔtwe, nye no dwetɛ ngyinado, ngyinado duesia; ngyinado ebien nhyehyɛ taabow kor ase, na ngyinado ebien nhyehyɛ taabow kor so ase.
Na fa akeesia dua yɛ mbeabeamu; enum nyɛ ntamadan no ne nkyɛn kor ntaabow no dze, na mbeabeamu enum so nyɛ ntamadan no ne nkyɛn kor no ne ntaabow no dze, na mbeabeamu enum so nyɛ ntamadan no ne nkyɛn ekyir wɔ anee afamu ntaabow no dze.
Na finimfin mbeamu a ɔwɔ ntaabow no ne finimfin no ntwa mu mfi tsir nkodu tsir.
Na fa sika duradura ntaabow no ho, na fa sika yɛ no ho nkaba no ma ɔnyɛ mbeabeamu no hyehyɛbea: na fa sika duradura mbeabeamu no ho.
Na si ntamadan no dɛ mbrɛ ne nyɛbea a woeyi akyerɛ wo wɔ bepɔw no do no tse.
Na fa bibir, nye ɔberdum, nye serdaa nye ndwera fɛɛfɛw a woefira yɛ ntwamutam: yɛ me kerubim a ɔyɛ odwimfo pa edwinsa: na fa sensɛn akeesia edum anan a woeduradura ho sika do, no nkwaba nyɛ sika, nsisi dwetɛ ngyinado anan do.
Na fa ntwamutam no sensɛn nkɔtɔkorba no ase, na fa dasedaka no bra ntwamutam no mu: na ntwamutam no ntwa bea krɔnkrɔn no nye krɔnkrɔn mu krɔnkrɔn no mu mma wo.
Na fa mbɔbɔrhu egua no si dasedaka no do wɔ krɔnkrɔn mu krɔnkrɔnbea no mu.
Na fa ɔpon no si ntwamutam no ekyir, na kandzeadua no ndzi ɔpon no tsentsendo wɔ ntamadan no nkyɛn mu wɔ pomu afamu: na fa ɔpon no si kwaamu afamu.
Na fa bibir, nye ɔberdum, nye serdaa, nye ndwera fɛɛfɛw a woefira, wen nkyermu fa yɛ ntamadan no n’abowano nkataano.
Na yɛ akeesia edum enum fa ma nkataano no, na fa sika duradura ho; no nkwaba nyɛ sika: na gu boran ngyinado enum wɔ ase.
